Kṣemendra Avadānakalpalatā
kṣemendraviracitā

bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatā ।

namaḥ sarvajñāya ।

prabhāsāvadānam ।

cittaṃ yasya sphaṭikavimalaṃ naiva gṛhṇāti rāgaṃ
kāruṇyārdre manasi nikhilāḥ śoṣitā yena doṣāḥ ।
akrodhena svayamabhihato yena saṃsāraśatruḥ
sarvajño asau bhavatu bhavatāṃ śreyase niścalāya ।।

sacchāyaḥ sthiradharmamūlavalayaḥ puṇyālavālasthitir
dhīvidyākaruṇāmbhasā hi vilasadvistīrṇaśākhānvitaḥ ।
saṃtoṣojjvalapallavaḥ śuciyaśaḥpuṣpaḥ sadāsatphalaḥ
sarvāśāparipūrako vijayate śrībuddhakalpadrumaḥ ।।

jāyate jagaduddhartuṃ saṃsāramakarākarāt ।
matirmahānubhāvānāmatrānuśrūyate yathā ।।

asti prabhāvatī nāma hemaharmyagṛhairvṛtā ।
purī prabhāvatīva dyaurvimānaiḥ puṇyakarmaṇām ।।

vidyādharavatī siddhagandharvagaṇasevitā ।
gāṃ śritā śakranagarī sukṛtena satāmiva ।।

sevitā satataṃ satyavratadānadayāmayaiḥ ।
rājadhānīva dharmasya puṇyāvasathaśālinī ।।

abhūdbhūtilakastasyāṃ prabhāso nāma bhūpatiḥ ।
saprabhā sādarairyasya kīrtirabhyarcyate suraiḥ ।।

guṇasaurabhasaṃbhārāḥ sarvāsāṃ hariṇīdṛśām ।
yadyaśaḥpuṣpamañjaryo yātāḥ karṇavataṃsatām ।।

upāyajñasya yasyājñāṃ suvaṇakusumojjvalām ।
mālāmiva mahīpālā maulicakreṣu cakrire ।।

taṃ kadācitsamāsīnamabhyetya bhuvaneśvaram ।
uvāca kṣitivinyastajānurnāgavanādhipaḥ ।।

deva divyadyutirdantī gṛhīto asmābhiradbhutaḥ ।
tvatkīrtiśravaṇādbhūmimairāvaṇa ivāgataḥ ।।

dvāri sthito asau dviradastridaśārhaḥ pradṛśyatām ।
bhṛtyānāṃ prabhunāṃ dṛṣṭaḥ saphalo hi pariśramaḥ ।।

etadākarṇya nṛpatirnirgatyāmātyasaṃmataḥ ।
dadarśa dviradaṃ dvāri kailāsamiva jaṅgamam ।।

uddāmasaurabhāhūtairbhramarairgaṇḍaḍiṇḍimaiḥ ।
śṛṅgārābharaṇodāraṃ vasantamiva sevitam ।।

dantaparyantaviśrāntakaraṃ mīlitalocanam ।
smarantaṃ vindhyakadalīsallakīkānanaśriyaḥ ।।

agastyaśāsanād yātaṃ bhuvi kuñjararājatām ।
sphuratsaptacchadāmodaṃ vindhyācalamivonnatam ।।

taṃ vilokya kṣitipatirdantastambhavibhūṣitam ।
lakṣmīvilāsabhavanaṃ vismayādityacintayat ।।

aho navanavotkarṣā nirmāṇāścaryaśālinām ।
karmaṇāmanavacchinnā saṃsārasargasaṃtatiḥ ।।

amanthena sudhāmbhodheranāyāsena vāsukeḥ ।
anākarṣeṇa śailasya kenāyaṃ janito gajaḥ ।।

atha hastimahāmātraṃ saṃyātaṃ nāma bhūpatiḥ ।
ādideśārcitādeśaṃ gajo ayaṃ damyatāmiti ।।

tadādiśya mahīpāle yāte antaḥpuramandiram ।
nāgaṃ jagrāha saṃyātaḥ sarvaśikṣābharakṣamam ।।

sa sacchiṣya iva prājñaḥ prāgjanmābhyāsayantritaḥ ।
nītastena prayatnena sarvaśikṣāvinītatām ।।

bahudānanirudvegaḥ śaktyutsāhayutaḥ kṣamī ।
ripupraghātasugatiḥ sa rājñastulyatāṃ yayau ।।

damyakriyāsamuttīrṇaṃ tatastaṃ kuñjareśvaram ।
nareśvarāya saṃyātaḥ kṛtakṛtyo nyavedayat ।।

dṛṣṭvā tamaṅkuśāyattaṃ nirvikārabalodayam ।
utsāhaśikharārūḍhaṃ mene rājā jayaśriyam ।।

sa saṃjātapraharṣotthadākṣyaśikṣādidṛkṣayā ।
tamāruroha sotsāhaḥ sahasrāṃśurivodayam ।।

saṃyāto atha gajendrasya mantrīva vaśavartinaḥ ।
sarvamaṇḍalasaṃcāracāturthaṃ samadarśayat ।।

gajaprekṣāprasaṅgena mṛgayākelilālasaḥ ।
rājā nijotsāhamiva vyagāhata vanaṃ mahat ।।

sa yayau ratnakeyūrakiraṇairdūrasarpībhiḥ ।
sallakīpallavavarairdignāgānāhvayanniva ।।

vrajantaṃ tatra dadṛśustaṃ vane vanadevatāḥ ।
praharṣavismayākīrṇakarṇapūrīkṛtekṣaṇāḥ ।।

śabarīkabarīpāśapuṣpasaurabhanirbharāḥ ।
vaindhyā vasuṃdharādhīśaṃ marutastaṃ siṣevire ।।

atha vindhyopakaṇṭheṣu svacchandasukhaśākhiṣu ।
smṛtvā vilāsavṛttāntaṃ gajaḥ sotkaṇṭhatāṃ yayau ।।

kariṇyāḥ premabaddhāyā gandhamāghrāya sa dvipaḥ ।
nītiṃ nṛpa ivotsiktastatyājāṅkuśayantraṇām ।।

savegaṃ dhāvatastasya rāgākṛṣṭasya daṇḍinaḥ ।
vimūḍhasyeva saṃsāre nābhavadviratiḥ kkacit ।।

dṛṣṭvā prabhañjanajavaṃ kuñjaraṃ rājakuñjaraḥ ।
vrajantaṃ jātasaṃdehaḥ saṃyātamidamabravīt ।।

aho batāyaṃ bhavatā vinayaṃ grāhito gajaḥ ।
dṛṣṭaḥ prayāto vaimukhyaṃ gurorasyāṅkuśasya yaḥ ।।

bhramatīva diśāṃ cakramanuyāntīva pādapāḥ ।
pādanyāsabhareṇāsya kṣībeṇādhūrṇate kṣitiḥ ।।

asmin deva ivākāle prayāte pratikūlatām ।
sarvāḥ puruṣakārasya niṣphalā yatnavṛttayaḥ ।।

vacaḥ śrutveti saṃyātaḥ prabhorāyātasādhvasaḥ ।
śikṣāpavādavailakṣyāduvāca racitāñjaliḥ ।।

deva sarvakriyāyattaḥ kuñjaro ayaṃ mayā kṛtaḥ ।
kariṇīgandhamāghrāya yātaḥ kiṃ tvadya vikriyām ।।

nopadeśaṃ na niyamaṃ na dākṣiṇyaṃ na sādhutām ।
smaranti jantavaḥ kāmaṃ kāmasya vaśamāgatāḥ ।।

kena ratirasotsiktā viṣayābhimukhī matiḥ ।
adabhraśvabhravibhraṣṭaśaolakulyeva vāryate ।।

śarīraśramaśikṣāyāṃ damakāḥ kuśalā vayam ।
manoniyamaśikṣāyāṃ munayo api na paṇḍitāḥ ।।

rāgādagaṇitāyāsaḥ skhalitākhilasaṃyamaḥ ।
eṣa dhāvatyamāreṇa mūrkhaḥ khala iva dvipaḥ ।।

vṛkṣaśākhāṃ samālambya tyajemaṃ pṛthivīpate ।
vyasanī patitaḥ satyaṃ pātayatyeva durjanaḥ ।।

saṃyātasya vacaḥ śrutvā tatkālasadṛśaṃ nṛpaḥ ।
tenaiva sahitaḥ śākhāmālalambe mahātaroḥ ।।

avatīrya taroraśvamāruhya nṛpatau gate ।
prāpyāliliṅga kariṇīṃ vigāhya gahanaṃ gajaḥ ।।

tataḥ śāntasmaro hastī dinairabhyetya saptabhiḥ ।
svayamālānasaṃbaddhastasthau bhuktvā yathāsukham ।।

śikṣāsaṃyamayantritaṃ taṃ dṛṣṭvā svayamāgatam ।
saṃyātaḥ kauśalotkarṣaharṣādrājñe nyavedayat ।।

rāgavāgurayākṛṣṭaḥ prayayau yaḥ smarāturaḥ ।
śikṣāyāmavisaṃvādī so ayaṃ prāptaḥ svayaṃ gajaḥ ।।

saṃketayantrito vaśyo rasajñaḥ sallakībhuvām ।
saṃtaptalohakavalaṃ gṛhṇāti vinaye sthitaḥ ।।

eṣa kāmarasākṛṣṭaḥ kaṣṭāṃ vikṛtimāyayau ।
punaḥ prakṛtimāpannaḥ praśāntamadanajvaraḥ ।।

śakyā damayituṃ deva siṃhavyāghragajādayaḥ ।
na tu rāgāsavakṣībaviṣayābhimukhaṃ manaḥ ।।

etadākarṇya bhūpālastattatheti vicintayan ।
uvāca satyamucitaṃ saṃyāta kathitaṃ tvayā ।।

apyasti kaścilloke asmin yena cittamadadvipaḥ ।
nītaḥ praśamaśīlena saṃyamālānalīnatām ।।

ityukte de vatāviṣṭaḥ saṃyātastamabhāṣata ।
deva santi jagatkleśaniḥśeṣonmūlanodyatāḥ ।।

vivekālokitā loke vairāgyajanitāgrahāḥ ।
śamasaṃtoṣaviśadā buddhā eva prabodhinaḥ ।।

iti buddhābhidhāṃ śrutvā samyaksaṃbodhicetasaḥ ।
rājñaḥ prāgjanmajābhyāsapraṇidhānamajāyata ।।

vinimajjajjagadidaṃ saṃsāre makarākare ।
saṃtārayeyaṃ saṃbodhimuktaḥ kuśalasetunā ।।

athocurdevatā vyonmastaṃ śuddhāvāsakāyikāḥ ।
samyaksaṃbodhisaṃbuddho bhaviṣyasi mahāmate ।।

iti tadvacanaṃ śrutvā rājā virajasāṃ varaḥ ।
jātismaro divyacakṣuḥ prayayau bodhisattvatām ।।

atha sa vipulasattvastattvanikṣiptacakṣur
bhavajalanidhimajjatsarvabhūtānukampī ।
abhavadabhinavodyatsaṃvuditsāhayogād
dalitakuśalasetuḥ sattvasaṃtāraṇāya ।।

iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ prabhāsāvadānaṃ nāma prathamaḥ pallavaḥ samāptaḥ ।।

śrīsenāvadānam ।

te jayanti jagatyasjin puṇyacandanapādapāḥ ।
chedanirgharṣadāhe api ye parārtheṣu nirvyathāḥ ।।

gaṇanīyā guṇagaṇairastyariṣṭābhidhā purī ।
spardhayā śakranagarī yasyā na syādgarīyasī ।।

tasyāṃ babhūva bhūpālaḥ śrīsena iti viśrutaḥ ।
samagraguṇaratnānāṃ ratnākara ivākaraḥ ।।

paropakāraśaktasya caturasya prabhāvataḥ ।
anuraktā diśaḥ sarvāḥ sūryasyeva prabhāvataḥ ।।

yaśobhi śobhitaṃ yena dhanadānasugandhibhiḥ ।
gajaiśca bhūtidhavalairjagatkalpadrumairiva ।।

kalālayo api saralaḥ saralo api mahāmatiḥ ।
yo babhūva prajāpuṇyairmatimānapyavañcakaḥ ।।

yāvattapati tigmāṃśuryāvadvahati mārutaḥ ।
tāvadājñā ca kīrtiśca yasyāpratihatābhavat ।।

śamavyāyāmaviduṣāṃ ṣasṅguṇajñānacakṣuṣām ।
yaṃ dvādaśasahasrāṇi mantriṇāṃ paryupāsate ।।

tasmindharmapare rājñi babhūva sukṛtī janaḥ ।
bhartṛtulyā bhavantyeva guṇaiḥ striya iva prajāḥ ।।

tasya puṇyādhivāsena janāstridivagāminah ।
vimānaiḥ śakranagarīṃ niḥsaṃcārāḥ pravakrire ।।

dṛṣṭvā manujalokena suralokasamāvṛtim ।
jātavairaḥ kṣitiopatau śatakraturacintayat ।।

seneva lakṣmī vasudheṣu cārasyāścaryakartavya ca dattanityam ।
kalyāṇaśīlena ca sa rvacetanyapravyahāsāmana asmakāśca ।।

tasyākhaṇḍitacetasaḥ daddhidvalyānubhāvapām ।
kartavyā dhairyājijñāsā mayā māyāvidhāyinā ।।

iti saṃcintya suciraṃ sarvairanugataḥ suraiḥ ।
rūpaṃ śakraḥ parāvartya martyalokamavātarat ।।

atrāntare prajākāryaparyālocanatatparaḥ ।
rājyarakṣāgururmantrī nṛpamūce mahāmatiḥ ।।

rājan virajasā rājyarājamānena nirjitaḥ ।
nirvyājadānairbhavatā lajjate tridaśeśvaraḥ ।।

parasya pūrṇaguṇatāmātmanastadvihīnatām ।
dṛṣṭvā ko nāma nāyāti mātsaryasya vidheyatām ।।

īrṣyālavaḥ parotkarṣasaṃgharṣasya juṣo janāḥ ।
prāyeṇodvegamāyānti mahatām sukṛteṣvapi ।।

sarvasvadānamaryādādānavyasanino astu te ।
putradārātmadāne tu saṃkalpo hyatisāhasaḥ ।।

dṛśyante dāruṇāste te svapnāḥ sādhvasahetavaḥ ।
jagataḥ sūcyate tīvraṃ yaiścūḍāmaṇikhaṇḍanam ।।

daivajñānāṃ pravādaśca śrūyate tattvavādinām ।
śarīraṃ pṛthivīpālo dāsyatīti suduḥsahaḥ ।।

śarīradānaṃ sarvārthisārthanaiṣphalyakāraṇam ।
sarvaprado bhavatyeva tiṣṭhan kalpamahīruhaḥ ।।

tasmādasmānmahīpāla virama tyāgasāhasāt ।
rakṣāratnaṃ hi jagataḥ prajāyattaṃ vapustava ।।

iti mantrireṇoktamākarṇya vasudhādhipaḥ ।
tamūce sattvadhavalasmitaghautādharadyutiḥ ।।

uktaṃ hitaṃ mhāmātya bhavatā sacivocitam ।
kiṃ tvarthinavaimukhyasaṃtāpaṃ nāhamutsahe ।।

dehīti vādiṣu giro niṣedhaparuṣākṣarāḥ ।
sphuranti vadane yeṣāṃ sajīvāste gatāsavaḥ ।।

idamasmādavāpsyāmītyādhāya hṛdi yācakaḥ ।
prāpyaḥ prayāti vaimukhyaṃ yasmin kiṃ tena jīvatā ।।

dhigjanma puṇyahīnasya tasya niṣkaruṇātmanaḥ ।
yasyārtajanasaṃtāpaśravaṇe śītalaṃ manaḥ ।।

etadarthamayaṃ kāyaḥ sāpāyo api satāṃ priyaḥ ।
yatkasyacit kkacid yāti kadācidupakāritām ।।

śrutveti nṛpatervākyamamātyaḥ sattvaśālinaḥ ।
novāca kiṃcidacalāṃ vicintya bhavitasyatām ।।

tataḥ kadācidbhūbhartustasya līlāvihāriṇaḥ ।
jāyāṃ jayaprabhāṃ nāma ratiṃ ratipateriva ।।

dūrād yadṛcchayāyātāṃ cittasāsaṅgavāgurām ।
muniradhyāpakaḥ kāntām dadarśa vinimeṣadṛk ।।

prāgjanmābhyāsasaṃbandhasnehātparicitāmiva ।
tāṃ dṛṣṭvā sa dhṛteḥ prāpa dhairyarāśiranīśatām ।।

tasya vītaspṛhasyāpi vāsanollasitaṃ manaḥ ।
utsṛjya bhavavaimukhyamabhilāṣabhuvaṃ yayau ।।

iyaṃ hi satatasyūtā saṃtataprītitantubhiḥ ।
nāpaiti sarvajantūnāṃ prāgjanmābhyāsavāsanā ।।

tadāśramapadaṃ prāptaḥ samāptādhyayanavrataḥ ।
śiṣyo māṇavakaḥ prāha dakṣiṇā gṛhyatāmiti ।।

sa tamūce na me vatsa vane vṛttiḥ prayojanam ।
tathāpi yadi nirbandhaḥ śrūyatāṃ yadabhīpsitam ।।

śrīsenasya kṣitipateyadi devī jayaprabhā ।
labhyate bhavatā dātuṃ tadasau mama dakṣiṇā ।।

ityuktaṃ guruṇā śrutvā śiṣyaḥ kampitamānasaḥ ।
aśakyaprārthanālābhe saṃśayākulito abhavat ।।

sa gatvā satatasvecchāvivṛtadvāramarthinām ।
viveśa svairaviśrambhabhavanaṃ bhūbhṛtāṃ prabhoḥ ।।

alabhyārthārthanādainyacintātikliṣṭamānasaḥ ।
namrānano ativailakṣyād vīkṣamāṇa iva kṣitim ।।

taṃ dṛṣṭvārthinamāyātaṃ prahṛṣṭo abhūnmahīpatiḥ ।
sudhāpradānasannaddhasamudbhūtirivāmbudhiḥ ।।

kiṃ tavepsitamityuktvā pūjitaḥ sa mahībhujā ।
uvācānucitākhyānavailajjaskhalitākṣaraḥ ।।

anarthitaparaḥ pūrvamarthikalpatarostava ।
garvarthamarthitāṃ yātaḥ sudurlabhapade apyaham ।।

mama vidyāvrate pūrṇe dakṣiṇābhimatā guroḥ ।
rājan jayaprabhā devī dīyatā yadi śakyate ।।

ityukre muniśiṣyeṇa sahasaiva mahīpateḥ ।
snehadānasāviddhaṃ dvidhābhūtamabhūnmanaḥ ।।

sa jagād vijaṃ dantajyotiṣāgravisāriṇā ।
gṛhyatāṃ dayitā svacchavāsasācchādayanniva ।।

avicārya mayā deyamīpsitaṃ tava yadguroḥ ।
viyogacakitaṃ cetaḥ satyaṃ na gaṇayāmyaham ।।

ityuktvāhūya dayitām rājā rājīvalocanām ।
sadā hṛdayasaṃsaktām jīvavṛttimivāparām ।।

nivārito api guruṇā viyogavyasanāgninā ।
niṣiddho apyativṛddhena snehena smarabandhunā ।।

pradadau muniśiṣyāya sahasā hariṇīmiva ।
kimetaditi sāyāsasaṃtrāsataralekṣaṇām ।।

dattāyāṃ tyāgaśīlena priyāyāṃ pṛthivībhujā ।
cakampe tyāgabhīteva bhūmirlolābdhimekhalā ।।

yatkṛte durdaśāṃ dehe sehire duḥsahāmapi ।
indracandrādayo devāstāh priyāḥ kasya na priyāḥ ।।

śīlaṃ keciddhanaṃ keciddharmaṃ kecittapaḥ pare ।
lajjāṃ kecittanuṃ kecittyajanti yoṣitāṃ kṛte ।।

yadeva rāgasarvasvaṃ puṃsāṃ jīvitajīvitam ।
tadeva sphīṭasattvānām dāne tṛṇalavāyate ।।

tāmādāya gate tasmin virahākulito nṛpaḥ ।
viraheṇa sukhadveṣī manobhava ivābhavat ।।

śiṣyeṇa munirānītām dṛṣṭvā bhūpativallabhām ।
rahitāṃ jīviteneva paralokabhuvaṃ gatām ।।

gāḍhānuśayasaṃtaptaḥ paraṃ lajjānimīlitaḥ ।
acintayadanaucityamātmanaḥ karmavuplavāt ।।

aho nu bālakeneva mayā kevalacāpalāt ।
niḥśankamayaśaḥpaṅke svayamātmā nipatitaḥ ।।

iyaṃ prajānāṃ jananī bharmyāṇāṃ dharmakāriṇā ।
varṇāśramagurorjāyām mayā duḥkhānale arpitā ।।

kiṃ tu nākalitaṃ śīlaṃ na smṛtaḥ saṃyamo mayā ।
gaṇitaṃ naiva vairāgyaṃ viveko nāvalokitaḥ ।।

aho atra nirvicārāṇāṃ sanmārgavimukhaṃ manaḥ ।
asaṃyamāsavakṣībamapatheṣveva dhāvati ।।

iti saṃcitya sa munirvailakṣyakṣapitadyutiḥ ।
abhyetya rājadayitāmuvāca vinatānanaḥ ।।

samāśvasihi he mātarna śokaṃ kartukarhasi ।
bhavitavyatayaivāyaṃ kleśaste durnayaśca me ।।

tyaktvā hi śramasaṃtāpamasya tīrataroradhaḥ ।
adhunaiva nijaṃ dhāma sahāsmābhirgamiṣyasi ।।

ityukte muninā devī sīktevāmṛtavṛṣṭibhiḥ ।
avāptajīvitadhṛtistatyāja bhayasaṃbhramam ।।

śrutvaitat tridivavyāpi dātuścaritamadbhutam ।
rājñaḥ sattvadayām jñātuṃ vāsavaḥ samupāyayau ।।

bhakṣitādhaḥśarīrārdho vyāghreṇa vijane vane ।
putraiścaturbhirākrandairgṛhīto brāḥmaṇākṛtiḥ ।।

prasravadbhūrirūdhiro lambamānāntramaṇḍalah ।
kṛccheṣvapagataprāṇaḥ pāpairiva dṛḍhīkṛtaḥ ।।

pratyagrāmiṣyāgandhena kravyādairbhṛśamanvitaḥ ।
lubdhapārthivacaurotthairanarthairarthavāniva ।।

nagarāntaramāsādya sa yayau puravāsinām ।
kāruṇyadainyaduḥkhārto smayāvismayahetutām ।।

sa śoka iva sākāraḥ sa trāsa iva duḥsahaḥ ।
vidadhe sādhvasāyāsaṃ sahasā paurayoṣitām ।।

so arthisaṃdarśanasthānasthitasyātha mahīpateḥ ।
putrarūpaiścaturbhistairnyasto agre mañcikārpitah ।।

taṃ dṛṣṭvā vaiśasāveśaviṣamakleśavihvalam ।
niṣkūṇitānanavano jano abhūnmīlitekṣaṇah ।।

sa kampavihvalaṃ vakṣo muktamudyamya dakṣiṇam ।
bhujaṃ jagāda bhūpālaṃ vyathāśithilitākṣaraḥ ।।

svasti tubhyaṃ mahīpate brāhmaṇo ahamimāṃ daśām ।
tīvrapāpa iva prātaḥ paśya māṃ karuṇānidhe ।।

saṃsāreghoragahane vane vyāghreṇa bhakṣitaḥ ।
jīvāmyavaśyabhogyatvādduḥkhasyāsya garīyasaḥ ।।

asminnapi vipattāpe tīvrakleśasahiṣṇavaḥ ।
vimuñcanti na māṃ prāṇāḥ sahṛdaḥ sajjanā iva ।।

dadāti yadi te kaścit chittvā dehārdhamātmanaḥ । tatte jīvitamastīti māmūce vyomadevatā ।।

ko dadāti jagatyasmin jīvitaṃ karuṇānidhe ।
prāyeṇa svasukhānveṣī parārthavimukho janaḥ ।।

sarvadā sarvadātāraṃ dīnavyasanabāndhavam ।
dehadāne apyavimukhaṃ tvāmasmi śaraṇaṃ gataḥ ।।

ekastvameva loke asmin jātaḥ sukṛtapādapaḥ ।
nirvyājamādarodāraṃ dānaṃ yasya phalodgatiḥ ।।

kimanyairvā vadānyasya kīrtitairbhavato guṇaiḥ ।
dānamevāhato yasya loke sukṛtaḍiṇḍimaḥ ।।

āpannārtiparitrāṇapavitracaritavratāḥ ।
prāyante puṇyapaṇyena vipatkāle bhavadvidhāḥ ।।

amandānandasuhṛdo haricandanaśītalāḥ ।
haranti santaḥ saṃtāpaṃ dakṣiṇāḥ pavanā iva ।।

pūrṇendusundarādasmāduditā vadanāttava ।
jyoptsneva jīvayatyeva vāṇī pīyūṣavarṣiṇī ।।

ityuktastena sahasā hṛdi saṃkrāntatadvyathaḥ ।
saṃmohamūrcchitaṃ rājā tamūce vācamākulam ।।

samāśvasihi muñca tvaṃ bahyaṃ prāṇaviyogajam ।
prayacchāmi śarīrārdhamavicāryaiva te dvija ।।

dhanyasy ayātyayaṃ kāyaḥ paropakṛtaye kṣatim ।
kṣaṇakṣayī hi deho ayaṃ rakṣyamāṇo api nākṣayaḥ ।।

ityuktavati bhūpāle samutkampitamānasaḥ ।
vajrāhata ivovāca mahāmātyo mahāmatiḥ ।।

aho nu sāhasābhyāsādāyāsavyasanī prabhuḥ ।
hitaṃ na gaṇayatyeva prajāpuṇyaparikṣayāt ।।

prajānāṃ bhūtaye śaktaḥ ko anyastvatsadṛśo guṇī ।
yadbhaktimukharo bhṛtyaḥ śrotā kartā ca bhūpatiḥ ।।

na karoti hitaṃ svāmī gajalīlānimīlitaḥ ।
gaṇanīyāḥ subhṛtyānāmiyatyo bhogasaṃpadaḥ ।।

bhānti t e suciraṃ karṇe yaiḥ kṛtā madhumañjarī ।
kalyāṇakarṇikākīrṇā vāṇī vinayavādinām ।।

rākṣaso ayaṃ piśāco ca chadmanā brāhmaṇākṛtiḥ ।
rakṣāratnasya jagatāṃ śarīrairarthitām gatah ।।

yadi nāma na māyeyaṃ kṛtā tena mahīyasī ।
tatkathaṃ kṛttadehasya kṣaṇamapyasti jīvitam ।।

avicāryaiva sukṛtaṃ kriyate durgraheṇa yat ।
tadātmapīḍāoparuṣaṃ paraloke api niḥsukham ।।

śakyameva sadā dadyādaśakyaṃ dīyate katham ।
sarvasvadehadānādipravāda eva śobhanaḥ ।।

karṇāmṛtamidaṃ dūrādyanmahārthimaṇipradaḥ ।
saṃprāptānāṃ punastatra pānamasyānyato arthinām ।।

rakṣyaḥ sarvaprayatnena pareṣāmapi jīvitaiḥ ।
prajānāṃ jīvitaṃ rājannarthicintāmaṇirbhavān ।।

prasīda dayasvāsmāsu deva mā sāhasaṃ kṛthāḥ ।
n akācaśakalasyārthe kriyate cātmavikrayaḥ ।।

ityuktvā pādayoḥ patyuḥ papātāmātyapuṃgavaḥ ।
śarīradānasaṃkalpānnoccacāla ca bhūpatiḥ ।।

so avadat praṇayasmeracikasaddaśanadyutiḥ ।
jīvitasnehasaṃmohatamah pariharanniva ।।

kevalaṃ bhaktisaṃyuktamuktaṃ vyaktamidaṃ tvayā ।
na sahe ahaṃ mahāmātya viprasya prāṇasaṃśayam ।।

hāraistuṣāraiḥ kamalairmṛṇālairinducandanaiḥ ।
nivartate antaḥsaṃtāpo nārthivaimukhyaduḥkhajaḥ ।।

sarvathā sarvaduḥkhārtiharaṇodyatacetasaḥ ।
na bodherantarāyaṃ me sumate kartumarhasi ।।

janmāntare api dadato dehaṃ me na vyathābhavat ।
smarāmyatītavṛttasya samyaksaṃbodhicetasā ।।

purā dṛṣṭvodyatām vyāghrīṃ kṣutkṣāmāṃ potabhakṣaṇe ।
tadrakṣāyai mayā dattaṃ śarīramavikṣariṇā ।।

śibijanmani cāndhāya dattaṃ netrayugaṃ mayā ।
rakṣitaśca svadehena kapotaḥ śyenakādbhayāt ।।

candraprabhāvatāre ca raudrākṣāyārpitaṃ śiraḥ ।
sarvasvaputradārādi dattaṃ cānyeṣu janmasu ।।

ityukte bodhisattven abhūbhujāmātyapuṃgavaḥ ।
na sajīvo n anirjīva ivābhūdvyathitendriyaḥ ।।

alaṅghyaśāsanenātha rājñā krakacadhārayā ।
niyuktau palagaṇḍākhyau śarīracchedakarmaṇi ।।

tau tīvraśokavivaśau śakramāyāvimohitau ।
kathaṃcidiva bhūbharturdehacchede samudyatau ।।

nṛpaternirvikārasya krūrakrakacadhārayā ।
vidāryamāṇe dehārdhe pṛthivī samakampata ।।

bhraṣṭolkā raktavasanā virghātacyutatārakā ।
dyauḥ saśabdaṃ rurodeva kīrṇāśrukaṇasaṃtatiḥ ।।

vaiśasālokanedbhūtatīvraduḥkhāsahiṣṇunā ।
tūrṇaṃ rajaḥpaṭeneva raviṇā pihitaṃ mukham ।।

tasmin prajāh prajānāthe krakacākrāntavigrahe ।
cakranduḥ pūritākrandā digvadhūmiḥ pratisvanaiḥ ।।

akṣubdhasattvamālokya nṛpaṃ śakro dvihākṛtiḥ ।
vismayānuśayākrāntacittaściramacintayat ।।

aho mahāmaterasya karuṇākomalaṃ manaḥ ।
prāptaṃ parārthapīḍāsu vajrādapi kaṭhoratām ।।

sāgarādapi gambhīraṃ merorapi samunnatam ।
tridivādapi sāścaryamaho vṛttaṃ mahātmanām ।।

ahi prāṇapravāse api sattvaṃ sattvamahodadheḥ ।
sādhoriva vipatpāte mahattvaṃ nāvahīyate ।।

iti cintayati kṣipraṃ sahasrākṣe kṣitiprabhoḥ ।
nābheradhaḥśarīrārdhaṃ nikṛttamapatat kṣitau ।।

sa dvidhābhūtadehoapi harṣotsāhamayo abhavat ।
sarvabhūtaparitrāṇasattvena dhṛtajīvitaḥ ।।

tadājñayā śarīrārdhe śleṣṭe saṃpūrṇavigrahaḥ ।
svasthakṣatiḥ samutthāya brāḥmaṇastamabhāṣata ।।

aho virājase rājan pūnjaṃ virajasastava ।
nirvyājadehadānena viśeṣaṃ tu bnhavadyaśaḥ ।।

tvanmanomaṇivaimalyatulyaṃ kiṃcidakurvataḥ ।
upamānena dāridyramaho mugdhasya vedhasaḥ ।।

kṛttaḥ suvṛttaḥ saralaḥ parārthe madhurāśayaḥ ।
sahase duḥsahāṃ pīḍāmikṣukāṇḍa ivonnataḥ ।।

ityuktvā brāhmaṇākāraḥ śakrasta smṛtijanmabhiḥ ।
saṃjīvanaiṣadhijātaiḥ sudhāsyandairapūrayat ।।

tataḥ prakaṭitākāraḥ paritoṣātpuraṃdaraḥ ।
suśliṣṭanijadehārdhaṃ praśaśaṃsa mahīpatim ।।

athābmarānnipatitaḥ sitakusumasaṃcayaḥ ।
tatkālollāsitakṣoṇīharṣahāsa ivābabhau ।।

atrāntare munistasmau priyāṃ jāyāṃ jayaprabhām ।
ādāyābhyetya tadvṛttaṃ jātāścaryo nyavedayat ।।

pūtayā saṃgataḥ patnayā svakīrtyeva viśuddhayā ।
uvāca pṛṣṭaḥ śakreṇa nikāre nirvikāritah ।।

tataḥ siṃhāsane divyae viśvakarmavinirmite ।
ratnavarṣasamākīrṇe jambudvīpe sa bhūpatiḥ ।।

abhiṣiktaḥ surendreṇa prasādya dayitāsakhaḥ ।
dānapuṇyaprabhāvotthakuśalavyāpitaprajaḥ ।।

samāptasattvasaṃsārasaṃtāraṇakṛtavratah ।
samyaksaṃbodhisaṃbuddhamanāḥ pramudito abhavat ।।

maitraṃ cetastaruṇakaruṇaṃ sattvasiddhaṃ viśuddhaṃ āpannārtipraśamanaphalasphūītamātmapradānam ।
dṛṣṭvā rājñah pramudasalilakṣālitākṣo vilakṣaḥ
śakraḥ prāyādamaranagarīṃ pūritāṃ tadyaśobhiḥ ।।

iti sa vibudhavṛndaiḥ siddhayakṣoragendraiḥ pulakaruciravarcairarcyamānaprabhāvaḥ ।
avanimavanaśaktaḥ kalpayannākakalpāmabahvavibhavaśobhāmāptavān bodhisattvaḥ ।।

pūrvāvatārasaṃvāde dānotkarṣamudāharan ।
upadeśāya bhikṣūṇāmityāha bhagavān jinah ।।

iti kṣemendraviracitāyām bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ śrīsenāvadānaṃ nāma dvitīyaḥ pallavaḥ ।।

maṇicūḍāvadānam ।

asminnadbhutasarge makarākarajāyamānamaṇīvarte ।
ko api prakaṭitasugatiḥ puruṣamaṇirjāyate ।।

asti saubhiprabhāpūrakarpūraparipāṇḍuram ।
sāketaṃ nāma nagaraṃ saubhāgyatilakaṃ bhuvaḥ ।।

sevyaiḥ prabhāsattvamayairgaṅgāvimalamānasaiḥ ।
tīrthairiva sthitaṃ yatra pavitraḥ puṇyakartṛbhiḥ ।।

yaśaḥkusumite yatra puṇyasaurabhanirbhare ।
ramante sukṛtodyāne nandane puravāsinaḥ ।।

tatrābhūd bhūpatirbhuriguṇaratnamahodadhiḥ ।
bhīturyaśaḥśaśāṅasya mehacūḍa iti śrutaḥ ।।

sadā sadāśrayārheṇa kalikālāpahāriṇā ।
kṛtaḥ kṛtayugeneva yena dharmadharo janaḥ ।।

mahīpatiḥ kṣamāśaktaḥ śrīvṛtaḥ karuṇārataḥ ।
vallabho abhūt prajānāṃ yaḥ prakhyāto vijitendriyaḥ ।।

amarāsavasaṃpūrṇamahiṃsāsatradīkṣitaḥ ।
dadau yaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ puṇyāmabhayadakṣiṇam ।।

nirmado yaḥ prabhāve api vibhave api priyaṃvadaḥ ।
kṣamāśīlaḥ prabhutve api yauvane api jitendriyaḥ ।।

gambhīreṇonnatimatā śūreṇa śaśikāntinā ।
satpakṣeṇa kṣitibhṛtā yenātanyata vismayaḥ ।।

rājñastasyādvitīyasya babhūvābharaṇadvayam ।
tyāgapūrṇaṃ ca kāruṇyaṃ tārūṇyaṃ sukṛtaśriyaḥ ।।

padmākarasya tasyābhūddevī kāntimatī priyā ।
prabhātaśrīriva sadā nirdoṣābhyudayotsavā ।।

nītiḥ prabhuguṇevena tyāgena śrīrivojjvalā ।
rarāja rājacandreṇa sā śīleneva cārutā ।।

sadānandanavikhyātayaśaḥprasarayā tayā ।
merūstridivalakṣmyeva babhau bhūmibhṛtāṃ varaḥ ।।

kāle kalyāṇanilayaṃ bhartuḥ sā garbhamādadhe ।
bhūtyai bhuvanapadmasya divākaramivāditiḥ ।।

araṇiḥ pāvakeneva velevābdheḥ sudhāṃśunā ।
brahmābjeneva govindanābhirgarbheṇa sā babhau ।।

tasyā garbhānubhāvena dohadābhimataṃ nṛpaḥ ।
dadau sarvārthisārthebhyo vāñchitābhyadhikaṃ vasu ।।

punarbhūmibhujā pṛṣṭā dohadaṃ śubhagarbhiṇī ।
sarasvatīva sā cakre svayaṃ saddharmadeśanām ।।

pūrṇapuṇyamaṇirdharmanidhirvidhisamuddhṛtaḥ ।
vupadvipuladuḥkhebhyaḥ sadā rakṣati rakṣitaḥ ।।

kāntāradurgeṣu paricyutānāṃ tāpāturāṇāṃ paralokamārge ।
snigdhaḥ pravṛddhaḥ phalapūritāśaḥ chāyātarurdharmasamo asti nānyaḥ ।।

ālokastimire vipadviṣamaṇiḥ pāte karālambanaṃ
yācñākalpatarurjagajjayarathaḥ pātheyamanthe pathi ।
duḥkhavyādhimahauṣadhaṃ bhavabhayodbhāntāśayāśvāsanaṃ
tāpe candanakānanaṃ sthirasuhṛddharmaḥ satāṃ bāndhavaḥ ।।

ityādi dharmadhavalaṃ śrutvā nṛpavadhūvacaḥ ।
dharmaikaśaraṇaḥ śrīmān babhūva bhuvane janaḥ ।।

tataḥ kālena saṃpūrṇaṃ dyaurivāmṛtadīdhitim ।
asūta dārakaṃ devī jagattimiradārakam ।।

ajāyatāsya sahajaścūḍālaṃkaraṇaṃ maṇiḥ ।
prāgjanmāntarasaṃsakto viveka iva nirmalaḥ ।।

sa babhau subhagastasya mūrdhni puṇyamayo maṇiḥ ।
yasya prabhāprabhāveṇa yāminyo dinatām yayuḥ ।।

soṣṇīṣasya maṇestasya pīyūṣasyandibindivaḥ ।
nayanti hematām lohaṃ duritaṃ śamayanti ca ।।

śiśorjātismarasyātha vacasā tasya bhūpatiḥ ।
dadau hema sadārthibhyaḥ sarvaṃ maṇirasodbhavam ।।

puṣparatnadhvajacchatrapatākāvyajanāṃśukaiḥ ।
apūrayan puraṃ vyonmastasya janmani devatāḥ ।।

suprakāśoditāśeṣavidyāvidyotitātmanaḥ ।
maṇicūḍa iti khyātaṃ nāma tasyākaronnṛpaḥ ।।

sa cakārāśayaṃ harṣapīyūṣocchalitaṃ pituḥ ।
abhijātaḥ suto jātaḥ pārijāta ivodadheḥ ।।

paulomīva jayanteṇa jananī pūjyajanmanā ।
babhau tena kumāreṇa kumāreṇeva pārvatī ।।

tataḥ kālena sukṛtasopānaiḥ pṛthivīpatau ।
divyadhāmasamārūḍhe maṇicūḍo abhavannṛpaḥ ।।

arthicintāmaṇestasya dānena paripūrite ।
loke puṇyasukhāloke nārto abhūnna ca yācakaḥ ।।

tasya bhadragirirnāma babhūvaṃ gajapuṃgavaḥ ।
prabhorivānukāreṇa dānārdrakarapuṣkaraḥ ।।

taṃ kadācinmahāsthānasthitaṃ bhuvananāyakam ।
bhavabhūtiḥ samabhyāyādbhṛguvaṃśabhavo muniḥ ।।

divyakānyāṃ samādāya lāvaṇyalalitānanām ।
mūrtāmiva prabhālakṣmīmakṣīṇasya kṣapāpateḥ ।।

kucayoravivekena rāgeṇa caraṇābjayoḥ ।
netrayoścāpaleneva sā jagatyatilajjitā ।।

tapaḥśriyeva sahitaṃ taṃ kanyānugataṃ munim ।
aoūjayat prajānāthaḥ kṛtāsanaparigraham ।।

kanyāpi nṛpamālokya dhīraṃ gambhīrasundaram ।
parapīḍāsu kāruṇyānnyastacāpamiva smaram ।।

cūḍāratnasya kīraṇairduritakṣayakāribhiḥ ।
likhantaṃ kuṅkumeneva dikṣu rakṣākṣarāvalim ।।

vikṣepakṣiptamarutā cāmareṇa virājitam ।
socchāseneva sattvena jagatsaṃtāraṇaṃ vinā ।।

ratnodāreṇa hāreṇa hṛdayagrahakāriṇā ।
pātālavipadāṃ śāntyai śaiṣeṇeva niṣevitam ।।

vahantaṃ mahatā doṣṇā kṣamāṃ cittena ca kṣamām ।
prayayau sābhilāṣasya vismayasya vidheyatām ।।

gṛhītvā munirutsaṅge kuraṅgataralekṣaṇām ।
jīvanīṃ tāmanaṅgasya jagād jagatīpatim ।।

uditena jagannetraśatapatravikāśinā ।
bhavatā bhāti loko ayaṃ devena ca vivasvatā ।।

aho nu tava nāstyeva vibhūtisulabhodbhavaḥ ।
sādhoriva guṇadveṣaḥ saṃmohopacito madaḥ ।।

lokanāthasya te lokakāruṇyapūrṇacetasaḥ ।
rājan maitrījuṣā kīrtiḥ sthirā pāramitā param ।।

akhedasaralo dātā nirvyājasukṛto bhavān ।
ata eva viśeṣeṇa mānanīyo manīṣiṇām ।।

padmodarasamudbhūtā kanyā kamalalocanā ।
homāvaśeṣapayasā vardhiteyaṃ mayāśrame ।।

gṛhyatāmagramahiṣī patnītve bhavatā nṛpa ।
viṣṇoḥ śrīriva yogyeyaṃ tavaiva puruṣottama ।।

yajñapuṇyaphalaṃ pūrṇaṃ kālena mama dāsyasi ।
ityuktvā vidhinā rājñe kanyāṃ datvā yayau muniḥ ।।

priyāṃ padmāvatīṃ rājā ratiṃ prāpyeva manmathaḥ ।
araṃsta rucirodyāne sukṛte puṇyavāniva ।।

tataḥ kālena sā putraṃ vaṃśavalliva mauktikam ।
asūta padmacūḍākhyaṃ guṇānāṃ darpaṇaṃ pituḥ ।।

śakrādibhirlokapālairanullaṅghyamahodayaḥ ।
saṃstūyamānacaritaḥ svayaṃ kamalajanmanā ।।

yaśaḥsaurabhasaṃbhārasaṃpūritadigantaraḥ ।
sarvārthisārthakalyāṇakalanākalpapādapaḥ ।।

smṛtvā munervacaḥ kāle kartuṃ vipuladakṣiṇām ।
ahiṃsāvasusaṃpūrṇāmājahāra mahīpatiḥ ।।

tasmin yajñe samājagmuḥ sarvakāmairanargale ।
munayo bhārgavamukhā nṛpā duṣprasahādayaḥ ।।

vartamāne makhe tasmin niḥsaṃkhyavasuvarṣiṇi ।
rakṣorūpaḥ samuttasthau vahnimadhyāt sureśvaraḥ ।।

upasṛtya sa bhūpālaṃ kṛśo vikṛtavigrahaḥ ।
kṣuptipāsārdito asmīti yayāce pānabhojanam ।।

śāsanādatha bhūbhartustasmai vividhabhojanam ।
upaninyuḥ paricitāḥ pānaṃ ca paricārakāḥ ।।

tataḥ kiṃcidvihasyaiva kṣitipaṃ prāha rākṣasaḥ ।
nedamasmatpriyaṃ rājan vayaṃ hi piśitāśanāḥ ।।

sadyohatasya māṃsena rudhireṇa ca bhūyasā ।
tṛptirutpadyate asmākaṃ dīyatāṃ yadabhīpsitam ।।

sarvakāmaprado asīti tvamahaṃ samupāgataḥ ।
dadāmīti pratiśrutya na niṣedhastavocitaḥ ।।

iti rakṣavacaḥ śrutvā karuṇakulito nṛpaḥ ।
ahiṃsāniyamenābhūdarthivaimukhyaduḥkhitaḥ ।।

so acintayattadā daivājjāto ayaṃ dharmasaṃśayaḥ ।
na sahe duḥsahāṃ hiṃsāṃ naṃ naiṣphalyamarthinaḥ ।।

na ca māṃsaṃ śarīrebhyo labhyate vaiśasaṃ vinā ।
nāhaṃ pipīlakasyāpi kāyakleśalavaṃ sahe ।।

datvāhaṃ sarvabhūtebhyaḥ puṇyāmabhayadakṣiṇam ।
kathamasmai prayacchāmi māṃsaṃ prāṇivadhodbhavam ।।

iti saṃcitya nṝpatistamūce karuṇākulaḥ ।
svaśarīrasamutkṛttamasṛṅbhāṃsaṃ dadāmi te ।।

ityukte bhūmipatinā babhūvākulitaṃ jagat ।
na ca dehavyayotsāhaṃ sacivāstasaya sehire ।।

praṇayādvāryamāṇo api bhūpālairmunibhistathā ।
dadau svadehamutkṛtya tasmai māṃsamasṛgvasām ।।

ākaṇṭhaṃ pītaraktena rākṣasena kṣitiprabhoḥ ।
bhakṣyamāṇeṣu māṃseṣu kṣḥaṇaṃ khṣitirakampataḥ ।।

tataḥ padmāvatī devī patiṃ dṛṣṭvā tathāgatam ।
vilapantī nipatitā mohamūrcchākulābhavat ।।

manujendrasya devendrastaddṛṣṭvā sattvamūrjitam ।
rakṣorūpaṃ parityajya tamuvāca kṛtāñjaliḥ ।।

aho nu karmaṇā rājan duṣkareṇa tavāmunā ।
romāñcakañcukākīrṇaḥ kāyaḥ kasya na jāyate ।।

aho puṇyamasāmānyamaho sattvamanuttaram ।
aho dhariyamamaryādaṃ rājān virajasastava ।।

duḥkhitāḥ paraduḥkheṣu nirlobhā durlabheṣu ca ।
vipakṣeṣu kṣamāvantaḥ santaḥ sukṛtasetavaḥ ।।

samunmiṣati ko apyeṣa sattvotsāho mahātmanām ।
trailokyaṃ karuṇārdrāṇāṃ yena yātyanukampyatām ।।

uktveti divyauṣadhibhistaṃ kṛtvā svasthavigraham ।
prasādya lajjāvanataḥ śakraḥ svanilayaṃ yayau ।।

tataḥ samāpte vidhivadyajñe rājñāṃ mahīpatiḥ ।
cakre munivarāṇāṃ ca pūjāṃ tridaśapūjitaḥ ।।

sa ratnavarṣairyajñānte kanyāgrāmapurapradaḥ ।
sahitaṃ tridaśārheṇa hariṇā hemamālinā ।।

dadaru rājagajaṃ brahmarathākhyāya purodhase ।
yojanānāṃ śataṃ tūrṇaṃ ekenāhnā prayāti yaḥ ।।

tasmai samarpitaṃ dṛṣṭvā rājñā bnhadragiriṃ gajam ।
abhūdduṣprasaho rājā tatspṛhākṛṣṭamānasaḥ ।।

prayāteṣvatha bhūpeṣu vismiteṣu makhaśriyā ।
samarpite yajñaphale bhārgavāya mahībhujā ।।

tamuvāca samabhyetya svastivādapuraḥsaram ।
marīciśiṣyo vāhīkaḥ prāptapūjāsano munoḥ ।।

rājannadhyayanasyānte gururme gurudakṣiṇām ।
īhate paricaryārthī sāmānyajanadurlabhām ।।

ekastvameva vidhinā nirmito durlabhapradaḥ ।
bahavo jātu jāyante na loke kalpapādapāḥ ।।

devī padmāvatī putrasahitā gurave mama ।
tapaḥkṛśāya vṛddhāya dīyatām paricārikā ।।

ityukte muninā rājā dayitāviprayogajām ।
rujaṃ saṃstabhya manasa tamūce dhairyabhūdharaḥ ।।

prayacchāmi mune tubhyamīpsītām gurudakṣiṇām ।
sahitāṃ yuvajārena jīvitābhyadhikāṃ priyām ।।

ityuktvā sasutāṃ tasmai dadau padmāvatīṃ nṛpaḥ ।
svajīvite vinisnehastyāgaḥ sattvamayātmanām ।।

ādāya rājadayitāṃ virahakleśakātarām ।
saputrāmāśramaṃ gatvā pradadau gurave muniḥ ।।

atrāntare duṣprasahaḥ kururājaḥ kṣitīśvaram ।
dṛpto yayāce dūtena bhūtyai bhadragiriṃ gajam ।।

purohitārpitaṃ rājā na dadau d viradaṃ yadā ।
tadā vipulasaunyena svayaṃ yoddhuṃ samāyayau ।।

balinā kururājena ruddheṣu puravatmasu ।
babhūva bhūmipālasya sainyaṃ raṇarasodbhaṭam ।।

sa vīrakuñjarahariḥ śakto apyarividāraṇe ।
janakṣayabhayodvignaḥ kāruṇyāt samacintayat ।।

aho anukūlamitram me rājā duṣprasahaḥ param ।
mātaṅgalobhamohena sahasā śatrutāṃ gataḥ ।।

snehāntāḥ sujanaiḥ snehā niḥsnehāntāśca madhyamaiḥ ।
durjanairghoravairāntā bhavanti prāṇahāriṇaḥ ।।

aho bibhavalibhena kṣaṇakṣayiṇi jīvite ।
samudyamo ayamasmākaṃ paraprāṇanipātane ।।

hiṃsayāpapraśāntānām saktānāṃ kalikarmasu ।
raṇaraktābhiṣiktānāṃ bhaktārtho ayaṃ samudyamaḥ ।।

sevāvikrītajīvānāṃ caṇḍapiṇḍārthināmayam ।
kalaho duḥsahaḥ kruryapiśunānāṃ śunāmiva ।।

aho vibhavalubdhānām parasaṃtāpaśītalāḥ ।
svasukhāyaiva dhāvanti nṛśaṃsacaritā dhiyaḥ ।।

ye yudhi siddhisaṃnaddhā raktāntām bhuñjate śriyam ।
kutaḥ kruratare teṣāṃ hṛdaye karuṇākaṇaḥ ।।

eṣa duṣprahaso rājā lubdho vibahvamohitaḥ ।
na vadhyaḥ sāparādho api kāruṇyāyatanaṃ mama ।।

iti cintayatastasya kāruṇyāta kānanaiṣiṇaḥ ।
pratyekabuddhāścatvāraḥ svayaṃ vyomnā samāyayuḥ ।।

prātapūjāsanāḥ śrutvā sarvajñāstatsamīhitam ।
rājñaḥ praśamaśīlasya prasannāstattvamūcire ।।

saṃmohapaṭalāndheṣu saṃsāriṣu dayālutā ।
śobhate tava bhūpāla sattvalokavivekinaḥ ।।

kriyatāmīpsitaṃ rājan bodhau buddhirnidhīyatām ।
saṃprati pratirodhe asmin vanameva vigāhyatām ।।

svairanirjnarajnaṅkārakīrṇasaṃtoṣaśīkarāḥ ।
viviktakānanoddeśāḥ śamināmeva vallabhāḥ ।।

ityuktvānugrahadhiyā vidhāyāsya viyadgatim ।
prabhāprasādhitadiśaste tena sahitā yayuḥ ।।

yāteṣu svapadaṃ teṣu himavattaṭakānanam ।
saṃprāpya pṛthivīpālaḥ prayatapraśamo abhavat ।।

vivekavimalāstasya dhiyaḥ sattvavatāmiva ।
babhuḥ priyanivuḥ pūrṇanirvāṇyo vanabhūmayaḥ ।।

bhūdharāntarite tasmin sahasā bhūpabhāsvati ।
śuśucurmohatimiraprāptaśokaprajāḥ prajāḥ ।।

tatastatsacivā jagmurmarīcaṃ munimāśrame ।
śaktaṃ rājyasya rakṣāyai rājaputraiṃ yayācire ।।

muninā nirvikāreṇa dattamādāya mantriṇaḥ ।
rājasūnuṃ svanagare cakruḥ sainyasamudyamam ।।

muninā nirvikāreka dattamādāya mantriṇaḥ ।
subhaṭāgresarah prāpa kururājaṃ raṇājire ।।

sa tena hatavidhvastabhagnasyandnakuñjarah ।
palāyanaparitrāṇaḥ prayayauḥ hastināpuram ।।

balinā rājaputreṇa jite duṣprasahe yudhi ।
mantribhistadbhujanyastā bhūmiḥ śeṣadhṛtiṃ yayau ।।

rājño duṣprasahasyātha kālena kaluṣātmanah ।
babhūvāvṛṣṭidurbhikṣamarakopalpavaḥ pure ।।

sa vicintyānutāpārtastībrāṃ janapadāpadam ।
na viveda paritrāṇaṃ viphalasvastikakriyaḥ ।।

pṛṣṭhā vipatpratīkāraṃ tenāmātyāstamūcire ।
duḥsaho ayaṃ mahārāja prajānāṃ vyasanodbhavaḥ ।।

maṇicūḍasya bhūbharturyadi cūḍāmaṇiḥ prabho ।
labhyate sa sudhāsyandī teneyaṃ tīryate vipat ।।

cārebhyaḥ śrutamasmābhiḥ sa rājā himavattaṭe ।
sthitaḥ saṃsāravaimukhyavivekavimalāśayaḥ ।।

arthitaḥ sa dadātyeva viśvacintāmaṇirmaṇim ।
putradāraśarīrādi nādeyaṃ tasya kiṃcana ।।

iti mantrivacaḥ śrutvā tathetyādhārya cetasi ।
sa dvijān maṇiyācñāyau visasarja tadantikam ।।

asminnavasare rājā maṇicūṣaścaran vane ।
marīcerāśramopāntamavāpa vipulaṃ muneḥ ।।

devī padmāvatī tatra phalamūladhṛtavratā ।
vrajantī vijane bhītā vipune muniśāsanāt ।।

śabarairmṛgayāyātairdṛṣṭvā kaṣṭadaśāṃ śritā ।
jughṛkṣubhiḥ kampamān ācukrośa karuṇasvaram ।।

ākarṇya karuṇākrande kurarūīkūjitopamam ।
hā rājan maṇicūḍeti trāyasveti suduḥsaham ।।

sahasābhidrutaḥ kāntām dadarśa nṛpatirnijām ।
rāhusaṃtrāsitasyendordyutiṃ nipatitāmiva ।।

vītarāgāṅgavasanāṃ nirañjanaparigrahām ।
vadantīmiva saṃbhogasaṃyogānāmanityatām ।।

tāṃ rājahaṃsasugatām vihārastanamaṇḍalām ।
aśrukāṣāyanayanāṃ vilokya karuṇāvanīm ।।

saṃsāracaritāścaryavicāreṣvapi karkaśam ।
kṛpākṛpāṇīnirlūnamivāsīrbhūpatermanaḥ ।।

ekākīnaṃ vane devī vigatacchatracāmaram ।
dṛṣṭvā nāthamanāthaiva lokanāthaṃ tathāgatam ।।

tadviyogaviṣākrāntā taddarśanarasākulā ।
śokaharṣasamākīrṇā babhūva bhṛśavihvalā ।।

sā nītā śabarā rājñā śāpabhītāḥ pradurdruvuḥ ।
na nāmābhyudaye bhānordṛṣṭaṃ sapratibhaṃ tamah ।।

atrāntare śamadveṣī sar vabhūtāśayāśayaḥ ।
māraḥ puruṣarūpeṇa sametya nṝpamabravīt ।।

rājan rājīvanayanāṃ priyāṃ praṇayiṇīmimām ।
na tyakrumarhasyajane vane vanajalocana ।।

iyaṃ hi te manovṛttiriva niḥsukhatāṃ gatā ।
varjitā rājyabhogena rājarāja na rājate ।।

etadārkarṇya nṛpatistaṃ vijñāya manobhavam ।
antarāyaṃ vivekasya pratyabhāṣata sasmitaḥ ।।

jānāmi tvāmahaṃ kāmamakāmaṃ śamasaṃyame ।
saṃtoṣavatām ko nāma bhavatā na vimohitaḥ ।।

itivādini bhūpāle sahasāntarite smare ।
babhūva viklavā devī taptā virahavahninā ।।

duḥkhitāṃ tāmārtaduḥkhāṃ patibhogaviyoginīm ।
uvācāśvāsayan rājā jāyāṃ jitamanobhavaḥ ।।

devi dharmakriyāyuktā na śokaṃ kartumarhasi ।
duḥkhāvasānī virasaḥ sarvo ayaṃ bhogacibhramaḥ ।।

dehināṃ yaditāsaṅgāstaraṅgataralāyuṣām ।
lolapadmapalāśāgraskhalajjalalavākulāḥ ।।

imā muhūrtanartakyaḥ kālameghataḍillatāḥ ।
saṃsārasarparasanā vilāsacapalāḥ śriyāḥ ।।

bhogakṣaṇenaiva viyogarogo vibhūtayaḥ svapnavivāhatulyāḥ ।
vātāhatā dīpaśikhā sukhaśrīrunmattanṝtyaṃ bhavavṛttametat ।।

sarvopajīvyā karuṇā na lakṣmīḥ dharmaḥ prakāśaḥ satataṃ na dīpāḥ ।
yaśāṃsi ramyāṇi na yauvanāni sthirāṇi puṇyāni na jīvitāni ।।

satyavratastāmiti sāntvayitvā visṛjya jāyāṃ nilaye maharṣeḥ ।
cacāra saṃsāraparāṅbhukhānāṃ saṃtoṣapuṇyeṣu tapovaneṣu ।।

tadāgatāste tvarayā visṛṣṭāḥ pañca dvijā duṣprasahena rājñā ।
tamarthināmakamakālabandhuṃ viśuddhasattvaṃ dadṛśurvanānte ।।

te svastivādaṃ śanakaurvidhāya viśastadhairyā iva sādhvasena ।
tamūcire sūcitatīvratapāḥ dīrghoṣṇaniśvāsasamīraṇena ।।

rājan pure duṣprasahasya rājñaḥ krūropasargaurhataśāntavargaḥ ।
janaḥ kṛtaḥ kṛttasamastakāmaḥ prakāmamārtasvanamātraśeṣaḥ ।।

aśoṣadoṣapraśamaikahetuḥ trailokyarakṣāprathitaprabhāvaḥ ।
cūḍāmaṇirdeva bhavadvitīrṇaḥ karoti tasyopanipātaśāntim ।।

dayāyuṣaścandanapallavārdrāḥ svacchāśayāścandramaṇiprakāśāḥ ।
saṃtāpakāle śaraṇaṃ janānāṃ bhavadvidhā eva bhave bhavanti ।।

ityarthitastairaviluptasattvaḥ saṃpūryamāṇaḥ karuṇārasena ।
uvāca saṃcintya janopatātaṃ saṃkrāntamantaḥ śrutivartmaneva ।।

aho sa rājā sahate kathaṃ nu devopaghātena nipīḍitānām ।
vidāritāntaḥkaraṇaṃ prajānāṃ viyogaḥduḥkhodbhavamārtanādam ।।

ayaṃ maṇirmastakamūlajanmā niṣkṛttya tūrṇaṃ pratigṛhṛtāṃ me ।
dhanyo asmi yadyarthijanasya duḥkhakṣaye kṣaṇaṃ kāraṇatāṃ vrajāmi ।।

ityuktamātre vasudhādhipena dharādharāmbhodhimahīdharitrī ।
ciraṃ cakampe cakiteva tasya śirastaṭotpāṭanatīvraduḥkhāt ।।

tataḥ kṛpākomalacittavṛtteḥ sutīkṣṇaśastrairvacasā nṛpasya ।
sutīkṣṇaśastrādapi tīkṣṇacittaḥ svayaṃ śiraḥ pāṭayituṃ pravṛttaḥ ।।

tadduṣkaraṃ karma nareśvarasya vyomni vimānairnalināsanādyāḥ ।
surāḥ savidyādharasiddhasākhyāḥ samāyayudraṣṭumaluptasattvam ।।

vipāṭyamāne śirasi prasahya ratnaprabhāvibhramamādadhānaiḥ ।
sa raktapūrairabhikṣiktakāyaḥ sehe vyathāmarthisukhe pravṛttaḥ ।।

vilpkya taṃ sattva nibaddhadhairyaṃ tīvravyathāveganimīlitākṣam ।
yayurvirāmaṃ na nṛśaṃsavṛtterviprāḥ kṣaṇaṃ rākṣasatāmavāptāḥ ।।

vicārya rājā śvaśarīraduḥkhaṃ saṃsāriṇāṃ kleśamayaṃ śarīram ।
evaṃvidhairduḥkhasahasralakṣairākrāntamityārtataro babhūva ।।

so acintayaddehanibaddharatnadānena yatpuṇyphalaṃ mayāptam ।
tenograduḥkhaṃ kalayāmi mā bhūdapuṇyapāke narake narāṇam ।।

samuddhṛte rakravasavasikte tasminmaṇau niścalatālumūlāt ।
mūrcchākulo api prayayau saharṣaṃ saṃpūraṇenārthimanorathasya ।।

sa kampamānāṅgulipallavena datvā svahastena maṇiṃ dvijebhyaḥ ।
nimīlayan samtamasena lokaṃ papāta tigmāṃśurivātiraktaḥ ।।

aluptasattve patite pṛthivyāṃ tasmin surāṇāṃ saha puṣpavarṣaiḥ ।
maṇiṃ samādāya yayurdvijāste tūrṇaṃ puraṃ duṣprasahasya rājñaḥ ।।

sa ten asadyaḥ śamitopasargaḥ svargocitāsāditabhogavargaḥ ।
tadbodhisattvasya samastasattvasaṃtāraṇārhaṃ praśaśaṃsa sattvam ।।

atrāntare kiṃcidavāptasaṃjñaṃ nareśvaraṃ viśrutaratnadānam ।
samāyayurbhārgavagautamādyā marīcimukhyā munayo vanebhyaḥ ।।

marīcimevānugatā ca devī padmāvatī vīkṣya parikṣataṃ tam ।
saṃmohavegābhihatā papāta kṣaṇaṃ kṣitau bālalateva lūnā ।।

digantasaṃcāriṇī cāraṇānāṃ nabhaścarāṇāṃ nṛpasādhuvāde ।
sarājaputrāḥ saha mantrimukhyaiḥ prajāḥ prajānāthamathopajagmuḥ ।।

vīkṣyaḥ kṣitīśaṃ kṣatajokṣitāṅgamakṣīṇasattvaṃ patitaṃ pṛthivyām ।
pṛthavyathākleśajuṣaṃ janānāmabhūdabhūtārthavikalpajalpaḥ ।।

kuṭhārikaiḥ kaiścidaho dayārdraḥ sarvārthisevyaḥ saralaḥ suvṛttaḥ ।
durātmabhiḥ svārthalavābhiyuktaiḥ chāyātaruḥ kaṣṭamayaḥ nikṛttaḥ ।।

aho parārthojjhitajīvito ayaṃ parāṃ camatkāradaśāṃ prayātaḥ ।
sasaurabhacchinnatanurgatātmā bhavatyudāraḥ sahakāra eva ।।

lubdhasya na svaḥ svajano api jantoḥ na kāmakāmasya dhane anurodhaḥ ।
sarvātmanā sattvahitodyatasya deho api na snehapadaṃ dayāloḥ ।।

yeṣāṃ kṛte dainyamayaṃ prayāti sarvātmanā cārthijano arthibhāvam ।
ta eva dīnoddharaṇavratānāṃ prāṇāḥ paritrāṇapaṇe tṛṇāni ।।

iti pravāde vividhānubhāve vijṛmbhamāṇe munimaṇḍalasya ।
bhūpālamabhyetya sabāṣpacakṣurmunirmarīciḥ praṇayāduvāca ।।

aho nu niṣkāraṇabandhubhāvamālambya rājan dayayā janasya ।
prajāparitrāṇavidhānabhūmistanustaveyaṃ tṛṇavadvitīrṇā ।।

kṣayaḥ pravṛtto nirapekṣavṛttestavārthibandhornijajīvite api ।
yadeṣa kāmaṃ kamalānikāyaḥ kāyastvayāpāyapade niyuktaḥ ।।

apyasti rājan sukṛtavrate asmin phalaspṛhā prāṇapaṇe api kācit ।
asthārthihetostava pālubhedakhedādvikāraṃ bhajate na cetaḥ ।।

ityadbhutāviṣkṛtamānasena munīndramadhye muninā sa pṛṣṭaḥ ।
uvāca saṃstabhya rujaṃ prayatnādraktābhiṣiktaṃ vadanaṃ pramṛjya ।।

phalaspṛhā nāsti mune mamānyā kiṃ tveka eva pracuro abhilāṣaḥ ।
yaddhorasaṃsāranimagnajantusaṃtāraṇāyaiva bhave bhaveyam ।।

arthipriye dehavidāraṇe asmin naivāsti me ko api vikāraleśaḥ ।
yadyeṣa satyaḥ samayo mayoktastadastu me svasthamidaṃ śarīram ।।

ityuktamātre sahajānubhāve sattvocite sa tyadhanena rājñā ।
abhūdvapuḥ satyabalena tasya rūḍhavraṇaṃ tatkṣaṇajātaratnam ।।

tataḥ suraiḥ śakraviriñcimukhyairnātapraharṣairmunibhiśca sarvaiḥ ।
abhyarthito api kṣitipālanāya bhogābhilāṣī na babhūva bhūpaḥ ।।

avāptasaṃjñā muninā prayuktā padmāvatī rājasutena sārdham ।
patiṃ yayāve virahopaśāntyai siṃhāsanākrāntisukhaṃ prajānām ।।

tatastamabhyetya kṛpākulāste pratyekabuddhā jagato hitāya ।
dehaprabhāpūritadigvibhāgā babhāṣire harṣamivodgirantaḥ ।।

cirādavāpte virahāvasāne punaḥ parityāgadaśāmasahyām ।
na rājaputraḥ sahate na devī duḥkhānubandho hyasamṛnnipātaḥ ।।

svamarthine yaḥ radadāti dehamāpannaduḥkhapraśamaikahetuḥ ।
kathaṃ sa kuryāt svajane apyupekṣāṃ dharmo apyayaṃ yasya parārtha eva ।।

ityuktamākarṇya nareśvarastaistatheti niścitya dhiyā kathaṃcit ।
vyomnā vimānaiḥ svapurīmavāpya bheje nijaṃ rājyapadaṃ saputraḥ ।।

iti sa vipulasattvaḥ satyavān bodhisattvaḥ suciravihitarājyaḥ saugataṃ dhāma bheje ।
jinapuramaṇicaityacchatraratnapradīpaprakaṭitavividhaśrīrlakṣaṇābhyastabodhiḥ ।।

ityāha bhagavān buddhaḥ svavṝttāntanidarśane ।
dānopadeśe bhikṣūṇāṃ samyaksaṃbodhisiddhaye ।।

iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ maṇicūḍāvadānaṃ nāma tṛtīyaḥ pallavaḥ ।।

māndhātravadānam ।

śobhante bhuvaneṣu bhavyamanasāṃ yannākakāntākara- prauḍhodañcitacārucāmarasitacchatrasmitāḥ saṃpadaḥ ।
yaccotsarpati tarpitaśruti yaśaḥ karpūrapūrojjvalaṃ
svalpaṃ dānakaṇasya tat phalamaho dānaṃ nidānaṃ śriyaḥ ।।

abhūdupoṣadho nāma bhūbhṛdhyasya vibhāvataḥ ।
vibudhābhimatā kīrtiḥ sudhā dugdhodadheriva ।।

vasudhāmavato yasya vasudhāmavataḥ puraḥ ।
nanāma praṇatau kasya na nāma nṛpateḥ śiraḥ ।।

śuddhā dhīriva dharmeṇa dāneneva dayālutā ।
vibhūtirvinayeneva bhūṣitā yena bhūrabhūt ।।

guṇinaḥ prāṃśuvaṃśasya babhūvendudyuteḥ sthitiḥ ।
yasya sarvātapatrasya mūrdhni sarvamahībhṛtām ।।

yasyeśvaraśiraḥsthāyi śubhaṃ gaṅgājalojjvalam ।
bhramatyadabhraṃ lokeṣu bhuvanābharaṇaṃ yaśaḥ ।।

kartu kratusahasrāṇāṃ sahasrākṣādhikaśriyaḥ ।
yasya ṣaṣṭisahasrāṇi kalatraṃ sudṛśāmabhūt ।।

kadācinmunirakṣāyai rakṣaḥkṣayakṛtakṣaṇaḥ ।
vicacārāśvamāruhya sa taponanabhūmiṣu ।।

tatra rājarṣibhiḥ kaiścitputreṣṭikalaśaṃ dhṛtam ।
dūrādhvaśramasaṃtaptaḥ sa payaḥpūrṇamāpapau ।।

vijanāsāditaṃ pītvā sa mantrakalaśāt payaḥ ।
rājadhānīṃ samāsādya garbhaṃ lebhe vibhurbhuvaḥ ।।

svapnamāyendrajālādi yasyāḥ kautukavipraṣuḥ ।
jayatyadbhutasaṃbhārabhūmiḥ sā bhavitavyatā ।।

vidhervividhavaicitryacitrakarmavidhāyinaḥ ।
āścaryarekhāvinyāsaṃ kaḥ paricchettumīśvaraḥ ।।

kālena tasya mūrdhānaṃ bhittvā bāloṃ aśumāniva ।
rūḍhavraṇasya sahasā divyadyutirajāyata ।।

taṃ rājajāyā jagṛhurjagatsāmrājyalakṣaṇam ।
vātsalyaprasrutakṣīrāḥ puṇyaṃmūrtimivāśritam ।।

māṃ dhārayiṣyati śiśuḥ ślāghyo ayaṃ jananīpade ।
iti tāsāṃ mitho vākyairmāndhātābhūnnṛpātmajaḥ ।।

tasya pravardhamānasya bālakrīḍāvilāsinaḥ ।
ṣaḍindraḥ prayayau kālaḥ puṇyakrīḍakṣayāyuṣaḥ ।।

navayauvanamārūḍhaḥ sarvavidyāsu pāragaḥ ।
sa yāte pitari svargaṃ bheje rājyaṃ kramāgatam ।।

yakṣo divaukaso nāma sukṛterdāsatām gataḥ ।
abhiṣekopakaraṇaṃ divyaṃ tasyopanītavān ।।

sa svarṇairbaddhamukuṭaḥ kalpitoṣṇīṣaśekharaḥ ।
śradabhrāvataṃsasya meroḥ śobhāmavāptavān ।।

sapta ratnāni tasyātha prādurbhūtāni takṣaṇe ।
cakrāśvamaṇihastiśrīgṛhasenāgragāṇyapi ।।

babhuva cāsya putrāṇāṃ tulyarūpabalaujasām ।
sahasraṃ vijitārāterbhujānāmiva bhūbhujaḥ ।।

vasuṃdharāṃ samastābdhuivelākalitamekhalām ।
nikhilāṃ vidadhe doṣṇi śeṣaviśrāntirnirvṛtām ।।

bhuvanatrāṇasaṃsaddhah pratyagrakamalāśrayaḥ ।
cakravartī sa sukṛterviṣṇoḥ kara ivābabhau ।।

trijagajjāhnavī kīrtiḥ prabhāvābharaṇāḥ śriyaḥ ।
so ayaṃ sukṝtavallīnāṃ prathamaṃ kusumodgamaḥ ।।

sa kadāciddvanānteṣu vikāśikusumaśriyaḥ ।
ruciraṃ sacivaiḥ sārdhaṃ vicacāra vilokayan ।।

dadarśa tatra niṣpakṣān vihagān pādacāriṇaḥ ।
vyomamārgagatiṃ smṛtvā prayātān kṛśatāmiva ।।

pakṣahīnānagatikān vṛttikṣīṇānnirambarān ।
daridrāniva tān vīkṣya provāca kṛpayā nṛpaḥ ।।

aho varākaurvihagaiḥ kimetaiḥ kukṛtaṃ kṛtam ।
yadete pakṣavikalāḥ kṛcchracaraṇacāriṇaḥ ।।

ityukte bhūmipatinā karuṇākulitātmanā ।
puraḥsthito mahāmātyaḥ satyasenastamabravīt ।।

śrutametanmayā deva kathyamānaṃ vanecaraiḥ ।
kāraṇaṃ pakṣapatane yadabhūt pakṣiṇāmiha ।।

santi pañca śatānyatra puṇyadhāmni tapovane ।
tapaḥsvādhyāyasaktānāṃ munīnāṃ dīptatejasām ।।

teṣāmadyayanadhyānajapavighnavidhāyinaḥ ।
ete lokāhalaṃ cakruḥ khagāstarūvane sadā ।।

tasmai vihagasaṃghāya karṇāpāyakṛte param ।
atisaṃvardhamānāya cukopa munimaṇḍalam ।।

tadurbhūtamahāśāpatāpalpoṣeṇa sarvataḥ ।
kṣaṇena pakṣiṇāṃ pakṣā vyaśīryanta kṛtāgasām ।।

ta ete vihagāḥ pakṣarahitāḥ kṛcchravartinaḥ ।
tvadvipakṣā iva vane śrāntāśracaraṇacāriṇaḥ ।।

mahāmātyena kathitaṃ niśmaitanmahīpatiḥ ।
uvāca karuṇākrāntastaptaḥ śāpena pakṣiṇām ।।

aho tejaḥ pariṇataṃ śāntānāmapi kānane ।
aṅgārāṇāṃ munīnāṃ ca dahatyevānivāritam ।।

mithyātapasvibhiḥ kiṃ taiḥ svasukhāya na yaiḥ kṛtaḥ ।
manasaḥ kopataptasya pariṣekaḥ kṣamāmbubhiḥ ।।

prasannā dhīrmaṇo maitraṃ dayā dānaṃ damah kṣamā ।
yeṣāṃ teṣāṃ tapaḥ ślādhyaṃ śeṣāṇāṃ kāyaśoṣaṇam ।।

kiṃ tapobhiḥ sakopānāṃ vilputānāṃ vanena kim ।
vibhavaiḥ kiṃ salobhānāṃ durvṛttānāṃ śrutena kim ।।

evaṃ kaluṣacittāste tībramanyuparāyaṇāḥ ।
duḥsahā eva munayaḥ prayāntu viṣayānmama ।।

ityuktvā prāḥiṇottebhyaḥ saṃdeśaṃ puruṣairnṛpaḥ ।
yāvatī madvaśā bhūmistāvatī tyajyatāmiti ।।

vihaṃgapakṣapātena kupitasya mahīpateḥ ।
saṃdeśaṃ munayaḥ śrutvā vilakṣāḥ samacintayan ।।

catuḥsamudraparikhāmekhalāyāḥ kṣiteḥ patiḥ ।
narendro ayaṃ kkva gacchāmaḥ ko deśo asya vaśe na yaḥ ।।

iti saṃcintyaṃ munayaḥ pārśvaṃ kanakabhūbhṛtaḥ ।
surasiddhasamākīrṇaṃ jambūkhaṇḍāntikaṃ yayuḥ ।।

atha tasya mahībhartuḥ prabḥāveṇa mahīyasā ।
abhūdadṛṣṭaśasyā bhūdyāśca ratnāmbaraprasūḥ ।।

pākaśāsanavailakṣyakaraṇāstasya śāsanāt ।
saptāhaṃ hema vavṛṣurmeghāḥ saṃgḥātavarṣiṇaḥ ।।

sa prabhāveṇa mahatā saha sainyairnabhogatiḥ ।
cakre pūrvavidehākhyaṃ dvīpaṃ divyajanaṃ vaśe ।।

babhūvuragre saunyāni sphīṭaśauryabalaujasāṃ ।
bhaṭānāṃ vyomagamane tasyāṣṭādaśakoṭayaḥ ।।

godānīyaṃ tato dvīpamathottarakurūnapi ।
pārśvāni sa sumerośca śaśāsāsataśāsanaḥ ।।

sukhaṃ viharatastasya meroḥ kanakasānuṣu ।
bahuśakro yayau kālaścaturdvīpamahīpateḥ ।।

sa kadācit surān draṣṭuṃ vyāmnā gaccan suropamaḥ ।
cakāra nīlajaladairvyāptā iva gajairdiśaḥ ।।

atha teṣāṃ nirastānāṃ merupārśve tapasyatām ।
munīnāmapatan mūrdhni tadgajāśvaśakṛddivaḥ ।।

tataste krodhasaṃtaptadṛśā vyomāvalokinaḥ ।
cakruḥ piṅgaparbhāvallikalāpakapilā diśaḥ ।।

kopātkimetadityuktvā śāpāgnivisisṛkṣatā ।
abhyetya devadūtastān praharṣākulito avadat ।।

eṣā niḥśeṣabhūpālamauliviśrāntaśāsanaḥ ।
pākaśāsanatulyaśrīrmāndhātā pṛthivīpatiḥ ।।

nabhasā naradevi ayaṃ saha sainyaiḥ prasarpati ।
yasya kīrtanadhanyeyaṃ vāṇī puṇyābhimāninī ।।

na dṛṣṭo yasya nirdiṣṭasarvalokasukhaśriyaḥ ।
mohaḥ saṃbinmayasyeva vibhavaprabhavo madaḥ ।।

kauberaṃ dhanadavyaktyā kaumāraṃ śaktimattayā ।
aiśvaraṃ vṛṣasaṃyogādvaiṣṇavaṃ śrīsamāgamāt ।।

pratāpaprasarāt sauramaindavaṃ jananandanāt ।
aindraṃ dṛptabalacchadāddivyaṃ rūpaṃ bibhartyayam ।।

baliḥ prayātaḥ pātālaṃ dadhīco apyasthiśeṣatām ।
asya tyāgena jaladhiḥ kṣobhamadyāpi nojjhati ।।

śrutveti devadūtasya vacanaṃ munimadhyagaḥ ।
sasarja durmukho nāma muniḥ śāpajalaṃ divi ।।

prahasannatha taṃ prāha senānāṃ pariṇāyakaḥ ।
maharṣe saṃhara rūṣaṃ mā kṛthāstapasaḥ kṣayam ।।

vaiphalyalajjāṃ śāpo athaṃ yāsyatyagre mahīpateḥ ।
naite bata khagā yeṣāṃ yūyaṃ pakṣakṣayakṣamāḥ ।।

ityukte sauntyapatinā śāpastabdhāmanīkinīm ।
dṛṣṭvāgre vismayādūce kimetaditi bhūpatiḥ ।।

saṃrabdho atha samabhyetya senāpatiruvāca tam ।
teṣāṃ deva maharṣīṇāṃ śāpāt saimyaṃ na sarpati ।।

idaṃ ca cakraratnaṃ te vyomni śāpavighūrṇitam ।
dhatte jaladasaṃruddhatigmadīdhititulyatām ।।

etadākarṇya nṛpatirdṛṣṭā cāgre tathaiva tat ।
dṛśaiva divadhe śāpaṃ viphaloccaṇḍavilpavam ।।

dehakṣayaṃ maharṣīṇāṃ parirakṣan kṛpākulaḥ ।
jaṭā nyapātayad bhūmau sa līlālasaśāsanaḥ ।।

ajitakrodhamohānāṃ bhārabhūtā vṛthā vayam ।
itīva lajjayā teṣāṃ līnāḥ kṣititale jaṭāh ।।

atha meruśiraḥ prāpya nṛpaḥ suraniketanam ।
puraṃ sudarśanaṃ nāma dardarśa priyadarśanam ।।

nāgāstatra kṛtārakṣāḥ prakhyātodakaniḥsṛtāḥ ।
karoṭapāṇayo yakṣāḥ surā mālādharābhidhāḥ ।।

sadāmattāstathā devāḥ krodhottambhitasainikāḥ ।
mahārājakāyikākhyāstridaśā balavattarāḥ ।।

mahārājāśca catvāraḥ saṃnaddhakavacāyudhāḥ ।
jitvā rājñā prabhāveṇa nijasenāgragāh kṛtāḥ ।।

tataḥ kalpadrumodārakocidāramanoharam ।
dadarśa pārijātākhyaṃ saṃśrayaṃ tridivaukasām ।।

merormūrdhni tataḥ śubhraprabhāṃ mālāmivāmalām ।
sudharmākhyāṃ sabhāṃ prāpa svabhāsodbhāsitāmbarām ।।

hemavidramavaidūryastambhasaṃbḥārabhāsvaraḥ ।
prāsādo vaijayāntākhyaḥ prakhyāto yatra rājate ।।

yatrābjervadanairbhṛṅgairalakaistulyatāṃ gatāḥ ।
padminyaḥ suranārīṇāṃ padminīnāṃ surāṅganāḥ ।।

bimbataistridaśairyatra maṇibhūstambhabhittiṣu ।
suraloko bibhartyeko apyanekasuralokatām ।।

ratnatoraṇaharmyāṃnivahairyatra citritāḥ ।
vyāptā vibhānti kakubhaḥ śakrāyudhaśatairiva ।।

yatra bālānilālolakalpapādapapallavaiḥ ।
nṛtyaddhastā ivābhānti nandinyo nandanaśriyaḥ ।।

yatra caitrarathaṃ nāma devodyānaṃ manoramam ।
dhatte nityotsavaṃ premikāmaṃ kāmavasantayoḥ ।।

sarvakāmaṃ sarvasukhaṃ sarvartukusumojjvalam ।
sarvātiśayitaṃ dṛṣṭvā devānām sadanaṃ nṛpaḥ ।।

muhūrtavisamyāspandasānandasnigdhalocanaḥ ।
acnitayat sukṛtināmimāstāh phalabhūmayaḥ ।।

airāvaṇaṃ surapaterlolāliovalayākulam ।
dadarśa tatra sāmodaṃ sākāramiva nandanam ।।

puraṃdarastato jñātvā prāptaṃ bhūmipuraṃdaram ।
pratyudyayau pramuditaḥ saha sarvairmarudgaṇaiḥ ।।

pūjitaḥ surarājena ratnarājivirājitāṃ ।
rājarājah sabhābhūmiṃ bheje virajasāṃ varah ।।

tridaśeṣūpaviṣṭeṣu ratnaparyaṅkapaṅktiṣu ।
upāviśannṛpaḥ śrīmānāsanārdhe śatakratoḥ ।।

ekāsanajuṣostatra surendramanujendrayoḥ ।
rūpaṃ guṇagaṇodāram nirviśeṣamadṛśyata ।।

tatah sarvasurotsṛṣṭaspaṣṭalocanaṣaṭpadaiḥ ।
pīyamānamukhāmbhojaṃ vyājahāra harirnṛpam ।।

aho udayaḥ ślādhyaste tejasā tejasāṃ nidhe ।
bhavatā bhūṣitā bhūmirdyauśca devena bhāsvatā ।।

abhyunnataprabhāvo ayaṃ lasatsitayaśoṃśukaḥ ।
bhrājate te tribhuvane sāmrājyavijayadhvajaḥ ।।

tvatkathāmṛtapānasya tvaddarśanarasasya ca ।
preryate śrotranetreṇa sukhākhyāne sarasvatī ।।

sthirīkṛtastvayaivāyaṃ sukṛtāptavibhūtinā ।
karmaṇāṃ phalavādasya niścaraśchinnasaṃśayaḥ ।।

ata evendriyagrāme cakṣureva spṛhāspadam ।
puṇyaiḥ puṇyocitācārā dṛśyante yadbhavadvidhāḥ ।।

ityukte tridaśendreṇa māndhātā yaśasāṃ nidhiḥ ।
tvatprasādaprabhāvo ayamityuvāca natānanaḥ ।।

ityevaṃ pūjyamānasya tasya nityādaraiḥ suraiḥ ।
ṣaḍindraḥ praṇayau kālastridive vasataḥ sataḥ ।।

tatparākramavidhvastasamastāsuramaṇḍalaḥ ।
babhūva surarājasya nirapāyodayo jayaḥ ।।

dīptadānavasaṃgrāme tasya śauryamahātaroḥ ।
viśrāntiṃ bhejire devā bhujacchāyopajīvinaḥ ।।

tasya puṇyapaṇakrītaṃ bhiñjānasyākṣayaṃ sukham ।
kālapravāhe mahati prayayuḥ ṣaṭ puraṃdarāḥ ।।

satkarmaphalabhogasya lāñchanaṃ vimalaṃ manaḥ ।
kāluṣyājjāyate tasya pratyāsannaḥ parikṣayaḥ ।।

atha kālena kāluṣyakalitasya manorathaḥ ।
abhūllobhābhibhūtasya bhūtaperabhimāninaḥ ।।

tridaśānāmiyaṃ lakṣmīrmadbāhubalapālitā ।
tadimāṃ na sahe tāvadardhāsanaviḍambanām ।।

ahamekaḥ surapatiḥ prabhāvānna bhavāmi kim ।
ayaṃ mama bhujaḥ sarvajagadbhārabharakṣamaḥ ।।

cyāvayitvā surāśīśaṃ svargasāmrājyasaṃpadam ।
ekātapatratilakāṃ svayaṃgrāhocitāṃ bahje ।।

iti cintayatastasya śakradrohābhilāṣiṇaḥ ।
śubhraprabhā prabhāvaśrīrmāleva mlānatām yayau ।।

ghanodayasamutsiktā saujanyataṭapātinī ।
lolaṃ kaluṣayatyeva mānasaṃ śrītaraṅgiṇī ।।

pramādo vipadāṃ dūto duḥsaho mahatāmapi ।
kuśalonmūlanāyaiva kilbiṣākulitā matiḥ ।।

pāpasaṃkalpamātreṇa kṣitau kṣitipatiḥ kṣaṇāt ।
papāta visrastaphalaśchinnamūla iva drumaḥ ।।

hanti vidyāmanabhyāsaḥ śriyaṃ hanti madodayaḥ ।
vidveṣaḥ sādhutām hanti lobhaḥ samunnatim ।।

aho bata mahotkarṣaśṛṅgāroho mahodayaḥ ।
vibhavodbhavamattānāṃ sahasaiva patatyadhaḥ ।।

tena sarvavibhurnāma pūjitaḥ pūrvajanmani ।
tatphalādāptavān rājyaṃ spṛhaṇīyaṃ marūtpateḥ ।।

surādhipādhikaḥ ko api prabhāvo vismayāvahaḥ ।
analpapiṇḍastasyābhut pātradānāṃśasaṃbhavah ।।

dbandhumatyabhidhānāyāṃ nagaryāmuṣitaḥ śuciḥ ।
vaṇigutkariko nāma so abhavat pūrvajanmani ।।

vipaśyī nāma bhikṣāyai samyaksaṃbuddhāṃ gataḥ ।
viveśa ta dgṛhaṃ sarvasattvasaṃtāraṇodyataḥ ।।

pātre tasya ca cikṣepa mudgamuṣṭiṃ prasannadhīḥ ।
phalāni tatra catvāri petuḥ śeṣāṇī bhūtale ।।

tena dānaprabhāveṇa māndhātā pṛthivīpatiḥ ।
sarvadvīpapatirbhūtvā śakrārdhāsanamāptavān ।।

mudgaśeṣaścyuto yasmād bhūtau tasyānyacetasaḥ ।
tadasau phalaparyante patitastridaśālayāt ।।

luṭhati vikalakalpā yatra saṃkalpamālā
sphuranti na ca kadācit svapnamāyāntare yā ।
bhavati vibhavabhogābhoginī bhāgyabhājā-
matulaphalatatiḥ sā dānakalpadrumāṇām ।।

ityāha bhagavān buddhaḥ prītyā dānaphalaśriyam ।
nijajanmāntarākhyāne bhikṣūṇāmanuśāsane ।।

iti kṣemendraviracitāyām bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ māndhātravadānaṃ nāma caturthaḥ pallavaḥ ।।

candraprabhāvadānam ।

dugdhābdhirvibudhārthanātividhuraḥ kṣubdhaścakampe ciraṃ
kampante ca nisargataḥ kila phalotsargeṣu kalpadrumāḥ ।
ekaḥ ko api sa jāyate tanuśatairabhyastadānasthitir
niṣkampaḥ pulalotkaraṃ vahati yaḥ kāyaṃ pradāneṣvati ।।

asti kaulāsahāsinyāmuttarasyāmanuttarā ।
diśi bhadraśilā nāma bhuvanābharaṇaṃ purī ।।

yasyāṃ sitayaśaḥpuṣpāḥ saphalāḥ sarvasaṃpadaḥ ।
dānodyānalatāḥ prītyai babhūvuḥ puravāsinām ।।

yatra tripurajinnetraśikhitrasto manobhavaḥ ।
abalābhiścalakrīḍabhrūbhaṅgaireva rakṣyate ।।

muktājālojjvalā yatr abhāti hemagṛhāvalī ।
meroḥ śikharamāleva visphutatsphītatārakā ।।

tasyāṃ candraprabhaḥ śrīmānabhūd bhūmibhṛtāṃ varaḥ ।
kaulāsa iva yaḥ kāntyā cakāra dinacandrikām ।।

yasya dehaprabhāpūraiḥ pūrṇindudyutihāribhiḥ ।
niśāsu dīpakābhāsu nābhūtu snehaguṇakṣayaḥ ।।

smarajvaraṃ bhajante asya darśanenaiva tārakāḥ ।
iti cchatrachalādasya chāditaṃ khamivendunā ।।

pradiśatyeṣa satataṃ śriyaṃ satkośasaṃśrayām ।
iti taddarśanenaiva saṃkocaṃ prāpa padminī ।।

senāhaṃkāramutsṛjya tyāgaśubhraśriyā śriyaḥ ।
nirdiṣṭāśchatramukuṭaprakaṭāḥ puravṣinām ।।

śuśubhe vibhavastasya puṇyālaṃkāraṇonnateḥ ।
ārohati parām koṭīṃ namrasya dhanuṣo guṇaḥ ।।

catvāriṃśatsahasrāṇi vatsarāṇāṃ śatāṇi ca ।
babhūva dehināmāyustasya kāle kalidviṣaḥ ।।

tasya ṣaṣṭisahasrāṇi purīṇāṃ pūrṇasaṃpadām ।
babhūvurlokapālasya lokapālādhkāśriyaḥ ।।

yajvānaḥ kīrtitilakāstasya puṇyavibhūṣaṇāḥ ।
yajñadhūmalatābhaṅgairbabhurlolālakāḥ śriyaḥ ।।

tasya saṃpatkumudinīvikāsena sadoditaḥ ।
abhūnmantrī mahācandraścadraloka ivojjvalaḥ ।।

yena niścalalakṣyeṇa prabhoḥ prajñāpatākayā ।
rājyābdhikarṇadhāreṇa pāramuttaritaṃ yaśaḥ ।।

mahīdharābhidhaścāsau babhūvāmātyakuñjaraḥ ।
bhūmibhārasahastasya diṅgāga iva pañcamah ।।

mantraṇābhinnamantrasya yasya nītibṛhaspateḥ ।
tyājitāḥ pratisāmantāḥ śauryaṃ viṣamivāhayaḥ ।।

tenāmātyena sa nṛpaḥ sa ca rājñā vibhūṣitaḥ ।
guṇaḥ satpuruṣeṇeva guṇeneva ca sajjanaḥ ।।

kṛtajñaḥ saralaḥ svāmī sadbhṛtyo bhaktinirbharaḥ ।
sukṛtaprabhaveṇaiva bhāgyayogena labhyate ।।

iyameva cirabhrāntiviśrāntiḥ sarvasaṃpadām ।
yadguṇajñatayā vetti svāmisatpuruṣāntaram ।।

tau kadaciddadṛśatuḥ svapnamanye ca mantriṇah ।
kṣayo yasya phalaṃ dānavyasanena mahīpateḥ ।।

tau dṛṣṭvā durnimittāni prādurbhūtāni śaṅkitau ।
vyagrao babhūvaturnityaṃ śāntisvastikakarmasu ।।

nimittadarśanodvignāstapivanagatā api ।
viśvāmitraprabhṛtayaḥ svāmītyūcurmaharṣayaḥ ।।

atrāṇtare brahmabandhuḥ prāgjanmabrahmarākṣasaḥ ।
raudrākṣo nāma mātsaryakrauryadaurjanyaduḥsahaḥ ।।

śrutvā dānodbhavām kīrtiṃ rājñaḥ sarvaguṇojjvalām ।
nirguṇaḥ sa guṇadveṣi saṃtaptaḥ samacintayat ।।

aho batāsya nṛpatergīyate gagane yaśaḥ ।
aniśaṃ siddhagandharvagīrvāṇalalanāgaṇaiḥ ।।

sadā viśanti me karṇe tadguṇastutisūcayaḥ ।
kiṃ karomi prakṛtyaiva sahe nānyaguṇonnatim ।।

tadgatvā dānaśīlasya tasya dānārjitaṃ yaśaḥ ।
karomyeṣa śiroyācñāpratiṣedhena khaṇḍitam ।।

yaśastyājyate dānotthaṃ śiraścenna pradāsyati ।
atha dāsyati vidveṣapraśāntirme bhaviṣyati ।।

iti saṃcintya suciraṃ sa kauryakaṭhinaḥ śaṭhaḥ ।
gandhamādanapādāṇtavāsī bhadraśilāṃ yayau ।।

indrajālaprayogajñaḥ sa kṛtvā praśamocitam ।
veṣaṃ kaluṣasaṃkalpaḥ purīṃ prāpa mahīpateḥ ।।

asmin bhavavane nityaṃ guṇadoṣasamākule ।
kalpavṛkṣāḥ prajāyante jāyante ca viṣadrumāḥ ।।

aśeṣanāśapiśunairghorasaṃtrāsakāribhiḥ ।
durnimittairiva khalaiḥ khedaḥ kasya na dīyate ।।

guṇidveṣaḥ prakṛtyaiva prakāśaparipanthinaḥ ।
doṣaāśrayasya ko bhedaḥ khalasya timirasya ca ।।

svacchandaghātī sādhūnāṃ vidveṣaviṣaduḥsahaḥ ।
dīrghapakṣaḥ khalavyālakarālaḥ kena nirmitaḥ ।।

tasmin praviṣṭe nagaraṃ rūpiṇī puradevatā ।
uvācābhyetya bhūpālaṃ saṃtrāsataralekṣaṇā ।।

śiroyācaka eṣa tvāṃ brahmabandhurupāgataḥ ।
vadhyo asau jīvitocchedī jagato jīvitasya te ।।

niruddho nagaradvāri sa mayā malināśayaḥ ।
mama taddarśanatrastaṃ dhṛtiṃ na labhate manaḥ ।।

iti bruvāṇāṃ bhūpālaḥ provāca puradevatām ।
arthisaṃrodhasaṃjātalajjayā namitānanaḥ ।।

devi yācñābhiyāto asau praviśatvanivāritaḥ ।
dirghocchvāsaṃ sahe nāhamāśāvaiphalyamarthinaḥ ।।

yācñā praṇayināmarthe puṇyaprāptastanuvyayaḥ ।
yugasaṃkhyāmapi sthitvā vipadyante hi dehinaḥ ।।

etadeva sujātānāṃ pūjyaṃ jagati jīvitam ।
yadeṣāmagrato yāti nārthī bhagnamanorathah ।।

kriyatāmānukūlyaṃ me bhavatyā kuśalocitam ।
āśāvighāte saṃtāpastasya tūrṇaṃ nivāratām ।।

iti bhūmibhṛtaḥ śrutvā vaco niścalaniścayam ।
jagāmādarśanaṃ devī cintāsaṃtāpamānasā ।।

athāyayau sa kuṭilaḥ khalaḥ krakacaceṣṭitaḥ ।
dāruṇaḥ saralasyaiva cchedāya svayamudyataḥ ।।

tasminnṛpagṛhaṃ prāpte vivṛtadvāramarthinām ।
bhūrbhūpatikṣayabhayāccakampe sadharādharā ।।

narendracandramāsādya sa rāhurica durmukhaḥ ।
samabhyadhādvidhāya prāgaśivārthāmivāśiṣam ।।

svasti rājan dvijanmā hi vijane siddhisādhakaḥ ।
prātastvāmīpsitaprāptyai sarvārthisurapādapam ।।

dṛṣṭirvṛṣṭirivāmṛtasya mahatī saujanyamitraṃ manaḥ
kṣāntiḥ krodharajaḥpramārjanadī duḥkhārtamātā matiḥ ।
lakṣmīrdānajalābhiṣekavimalā satyopayujktaṃ vacaḥ
nityaṃ yasya sa eka eva hi bhavān jāto jagadbāndhavaḥ ।।

siddhaye kathitaṃ kaiściccakravartiśiro mama ।
dīyatāṃ ta tvadanyo vā dātuṃ śaknoti kaḥ parah ।।

santi spaṣṭārthadāścintāmaṇikalpadrumādayaḥ ।
durlabhārthapradātāro viralāstu bhavadvidhāḥ ।।

ityukte tena nṛpatirniṣkampavipulāśayaḥ ।
arthisaṃdarśanānandanirbharastamabhāṣata ।।

dhanyo ahaṃ yasya me brahmannarthināmarthasiddhaye ।
nirvikalpopakaraṇaṃ vyayaṃ yāti sujīvitam ।।

kadā prāṇāḥ parārthe me prayāntīti manorathaḥ ।
kimetāni na puṇyāni prārthyante te yadi tvayā ।।

āhopakaraṇasiddhyai ślāghyaṃ me gṛhyatāṃ śiraḥ ।
tattadeva sthiraṃ loke yadyadarthisamarpitam ।।

ityukte harṣayuktena bhūbhujā sattvaśālinā ।
tamūcaturmahāmātyau mahācandramahīdharau ।।

nijajīvitarakṣaiva dharmaste prathamaḥ prabho ।
tvayi jīvati jīvanti sarve jagati jantavaḥ ।।

na dātumarhasi śiraḥ sarvādhāraṃ hi te vapuḥ ।
dīyatāṃ brāhmaṇāyāsmai hemaratnamayaṃ śiraḥ ।।

sarvārthairarthisārthānāṃ pūryante yairmanorathāḥ ।
teṣāṃ saṃrakṣaṇenaiva sarvaṃ bhavati rakṣitam ।।

saṃkalpo ayaṃ dvijasyāsya krūraḥ kaluṣacetasaḥ ।
mūlacchedopajīvyo hi na kalpatarurarthinām ।।

hemaratnaśiraḥ prāpya yātveṣa śirasāsya kim ।
cintāmaṇirviniṣprekṣyo bhujyate na bubhukṣitaiḥ ।।

ityukte mantrimukhyābhyām hemaratnamayaṃ śiraḥ ।
siddho naivopayogyaṃ tanmameti brāhmaṇo abravīt ।।

athonmumoca nṛpatirmukuṭaṃ mauktikāṃṣubhiḥ ।
śrirovirahaduḥkhena sāśrudhāramivābhitaḥ ।।

mukuṭāni kṣaṇe tasminnipetuḥ puravāsinām ।
digdāhonmukhatulyābhirulkābhiḥ saha bhūtale ।।

rājñā pradāne śirasaḥ sarvathā parikalpite ।
tau cakratustanutyāgaṃ mantriṇau draṣṭumakṣamau ।।

ratnagarbhamathodyānaṃ praviśya pṛthivīpatiḥ ।
utphullacampakasyādhaḥ śiraśchettuṃ samudyayau ।।

udyānadevatā dṛṣṭvā taṃ śiraśchettumudyatam ।
mā kṛthāḥ sāhasaṃ rājannityuvāca śucākulā ।।

kampamānāḥ pralāpinyastaṃ mattālukulasvanaiḥ ।
nyavārayannavalatā lolapallavapāṇibhiḥ ।।

so api niścalasaṃkalpaḥ prasādyodyānadevatām ।
vimalāṃ bodhimālambya babhūva praṇidhānavān ।।

asmin ratnamayodyāne puṇyarāśisamunnatam ।
stūpamastu praśāstustu sattvasaṃtāraṇocitam ।।

yatkiṃcidarjitaṃ puṇyaṃ saṃkalpena mayāmunā ।
bhavantu tena saṃsāre niḥsaṃsārāḥ śarīriṇaḥ ।।

dhyātveti campakataroḥ śākhāyāṃ nṛpatiḥ śiraḥ ।
baddhvā kacakalāpena chittvā prādāddvijanmane ।।

atha narapate sattvotsāhasphuṭapraṇidhānataḥ
kimapi vimalaiḥ puṇyālokairdigantavisāribhiḥ ।
vigalitamahāmohaughāntaḥ śritaḥ parinirvṛtiṃ
praviratabhavābhyāsāyāsaḥ kṣaṇādabahvajjanah ।।

iti prāgjanmavṛttāntakathayā bhagavān jinaḥ ।
bhikṣūṇām vidadhe śuddhadānasaddharmadeśanām ।।

iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ candraprabhāvadānaṃ nāma pañcamaḥ pallavaḥ ।।

badaradvīpayātrāvadānam ।

dānodyatānām pṛthuvīryabhājāṃ śuddhātmanāṃ sattvamahodadhīnām ।
aho mahotsāhavatām parārthe bhavantyacintyāni samāhitāni ।।

harmyārohaṇahelayā yadacalāḥ svabhraiḥ sahābhraṃlihā
yadvā goṣpadalīlayā jalabharakṣobhoddhatāh sindhavaḥ ।
laṅghyante bhavanasthalīkalanayā ye cāṭavīnāṃ taṭās
tadvīryasya mahātmanām vilasataḥ sattvorjitaṃ sphūrjitam ।।

purā hi bhagavān buddhaḥ śrāvastyāṃ puravāsināṃ ।
upadeśaprakāśena jahārājñānajaṃ tamaḥ ।।

bhikṣusaṃghaiḥ parivṝtaḥ sa kadācidvaṇigjanaiḥ ।
kṛtānuyātro magadhāt svayaṃ cārikayā yayau ।।

mahārthasārthānugataṃ vrajantaṃ vanavartmanā ।
taṃ dṛṣṭvā taskaragaṇaḥ sālāṭavyāmacintayat ।।

eṣa prayātu bahgavān puraḥ sattvahite rataḥ ।
paścāt sārthaṃ grahīṣyāmaḥ pūrṇaṃ draviṇarāśibhiḥ ।।

bhagavānatha sarvajñasteṣāṃ jñātvā samīhitam ।
kimetaditi tānūce nirvikārasmitānanaḥ ।।

te tamūcuḥ parityajya krauryaṃ madhurayā girā ।
tatprasādasmitālokairvinaṣṭatimirā iva ।।

bhagavan jīvikāsmākaṃ nindyeyaṃ karmanirmitā ।
na bhṛtirna kṛṣirnānyarakṣaṇaṃ na pratigrahah ।।

sahajaṃ krauryamasmākaṃ nisargakaluṣātmanām ।
kriyate kiṃ svabhāvasya deva tīkṣṇā hi karṇikā ।।

tasmānna vṛttilopo naḥ kartumarhasi gamyatām ।
yāte tu tvayi sārthasya vayaṃ sarvārthahāriṇah ।।

iti teṣāṃ vacaḥ śrutvā karuṇāpūrṇamānasaḥ ।
dolālolāyitamatirbabhūva bahgavān kṣaṇam ।।

tataḥ sārthadhanaṃ sarvaṃ parisaṃkhyāya tatsamam ।
sa dadau cauracakrāya tatkṣaṇāptanidhānataḥ ।।

tadvidhena krameṇaiva punaḥ pathi gatāgataiḥ ।
ṣaṭkṛtvaḥ pradadau tebhyaḥ so arthaṃ sārthasya muktaye ।।

punaścopagate tasmin vartmanā tena sānuge ।
babhūva buddhiścaorāṇāṃ tadbhojananimantraṇe ।।

dṛśā diśanti vaimalyaṃ śubhaṃ saṃbhāṣaṇena ca ।
vrajanti saṃgamābhyāsaiḥ santaḥ sanmārgasetutām ।।

tatrātiryagdṛśā sarvaṃ sarvākuśalasaṃkṣayāt ।
teṣāṃ samāhitaṃ śuddhaṃ vidadhe bhagavān jinah ।।

yeṣāṃ saṃgrahavastūni vatvāri niyatātmanām ।
arthacaryā samānārthabḥāvastyāgaḥ priyaṃ vacaḥ ।।

yeṣāṃ brahmavihārāśca catvāraḥ sattvaśālinām ।
karuṇā muditopekṣā maitrī ceti parigrahaḥ ।।

yeṣāṃ kuśalamūlāni saktāni trīṇi cetasi ।
alobhaścāparidveṣo apyamohaśca mahātmanām ।।

dānaśīlakṣamāvīryadhyānaprajñājuṣāṃ sadā ।
upāyapraṇidhijñānabalairāśritacetasām ।।

paritrāṇaikavīrāṇāṃ sadaivādvayavādinām ।
vidyātrayapradīptānāṃ caturvaimalyaśālinām ।।

pañcaskandhavumiktānāṃ ṣaḍayatanabhedinām ।
saptabodhyaṅgayuktānāmaryāṣṭāṅgopadeśinām ।।

navasaṃyogahīnānām teṣāṃ daśabalātmanām ।
kiṃ vastvaviditaṃ loke jinānāṃ janaceṣṭitam ।।

tatasteṣvatikāruṇyāccaraṇālīnamūrdhasu ।
tathetyuvāca bhagavāṃstadbhojyopanimantraṇe ।।

taistatsaṃdarśanakṣīṇakilbiṣaiḥ samamarpitam ।
bhikṣusṃghairvṛto bhojyaṃ vidhivat sarvamādade ।।

tatastatpraṇidhānena jñānālokaśalākayā ।
te samunmīlitadṛśaḥ prakāśaṃ dadṛśuḥ padam ।।

te sadyastīvravairāgyaparipakkāḥ prasādinaḥ ।
pravrajyāyogamāsajya jagmurjagati pūjyatām ।।

tatteṣāṃ kuśalaṃ dṛṣṭvā sahasopanataṃ puraḥ ।
babhāṣe bhagavān pṛṣṭaḥ kimetaditi bhikṣubhiḥ ।।

etairyamāyaṃ saṃbandhaḥ sārtharakṣaṇaniṣkrayaiḥ ।
dvīpayātrāgatasyāsīdanyasminnapi janmani ।।

asti vistīrṇamārgasya svargavargāvadhirvidheḥ ।
purī vārāṇasī nāma kauśalotkarṣaharṣabhūḥ ।।

yasyāmamalakallolavāhinī suravāhinī ।
sadā dayeva hṛdayaṃ prasādayati dehinām ।।

ahiṃseva satām sevyā vidyeva viduṣāṃ matā ।
kṣameva sarvabhūtānāṃ yā viśrambhasukhasthitiḥ ।।

brahmakalpe nṛpe tasyā vikasatkamalāśraye ।
brahmadattābhidhe lokaṃ trailokyamiva rakṣati ।।

priyasenābhidhāno abhūt tatra vaiśravaṇopamaḥ ।
sārthavāho arthasārthānām sthānamabdhirivāmbhasāṃ ।।

tasyāsīt supriyo nāma saujanyanilayaḥ sutaḥ ।
prayayau yaṃ samāśritya guṇasārthaḥ kṛtārthatām ।।

dānaśīlakṣamāvīryadhyānaprajñāsamanvitah ।
dhātrā vilobhavāyaiva yaḥ kṛtaḥ sukṛtaśriyaḥ ।।

taṃ sarvavidyāḥ viśadāḥ kalāśca vipulāśayam ।
viviśuḥ sarasodārā mahodadhimivāpagāḥ ।।

guṇālaṃkṛtacāritraṃ lakṣaṇālaṃkṛtākṛtim ।
puruṣottamalubdheva yaṃ ślāghyaṃ śrīraśiśriyat ।।

kālena sukṛtakrītaṃ pitari tridivaṃ gate ।
cakre skandhataṭe tasya vyavahārabharaḥ sthitim ।।

so acintayadiyaṃ lakṣmīrvipulātmakramāgatā ।
tathāpi manye paryāptā na sarvārthimanorathe ।।

kiṃ tayā sumahatyāpi śriyā satpuruṣasthayā ।
pūrvāgatārthiubhukteva yā śeṣārthiṣu niṣphalā ।।

ratnākarasya vaipulyaṃ niṣphalaṃ vedhasā kṛtam ।
adyāpi pūrito yena naiko apyarthī sa vāḍavaḥ ।।

athavā pṛthusaṃkalpaḥ kenārthī paripūryate ।
jagāmābdhiragastyasya culukācamanīyatām ।।

kiṃ karomyatitāpo ayaṃ śrīrekā bahavi arthinaḥ ।
na tadāsādyate vittaṃ yat sarvārthibharakṣamam ।।

pañca ṣaṭ pūritā evaṃ nānye śrīkaustukādibhiḥ ।
itivādyāpi tapto antarjvaladaurvānalo ambudhiḥ ।।

tasmāt karomi yatnena niṃsaṃkhyadraviṇārjanam ।
na sahe duḥkhaniḥśvāsaṃ vimukhasya mukhe arthinaḥ ।।

iti saṃcintya sa ciraṃ sārthena mahatā vṛtaḥ ।
ratnadvīpapuraṃ gatvā vidadhe ratnasaṃgraham ।।

tataḥ pratīpamāyāntaṃ kṛtārthaṃ taṃ vanecarāḥ ।
sārthārtharaṇonmuktā dadṛśurdasyavaḥ pathi ।।

sārthārthaharaṇe dṛṣṭvā sa teṣāṃ sāhasodyamam ।
nijasaravsvadānena saṃrarakṣānuyānim ।।

punaḥ krameṇa tenaiva ratnadvīpagatāgatiḥ ।
sārthatrāṇāya caurāṇāṃ ṣaṭkṛtvaḥ pradadau dhanam ।।

tathaiva tvāṃ puṇyavipanvānisaṃprāptastathaiva tān ।
dadarśa caurān sārthārthaharaṇe adhikādarān ।।

so acintayadaho vittairmahadbhiḥ paripūritāḥ ।
mayaite na nivartante parārthaharaṇodyamāt ।।

jagat saṃpūrayāmyarthairiyuktvāpi mayāsakṛt ।
aho nu dasyavo naite varākāḥ paripūritāḥ ।।

acitotsāhahīnasya vyāhatottaravādinaḥ ।
vikatthanapratijñasya dhiṅme janma kujanmanaḥ ।।

iti cintayatastasya taptasyānuśayāgninā ।
vijane prayayau rātriḥ saṃvatsaraśatopamā ।।

taṃ śokapaṅkasaṃmagnaṃ gajendramiva niścalam ।
dīrghocchvāsaṃ maheśākhyā svapne provāca devatā ।।

sumate mā kṛthāḥ śokaṃ śarīrocchoṣaṇaṃ vṛthā ।
satsaṃkalpābhirūḍhasya bhaviṣyati tavepsitam ।।

na tadasti jagatyasmin svapnasaṃkalpadurlabham ।
yanna sidhyati yatnena dhīrāṇāṃ vyavasāyinām ।।

sā kāpyanupamā śaktirekasyāpi dvijanmanaḥ ।
yadājñāspanditenaiva vindhyaḥ kṣmāsamatām yayau ।।

viṣamaṃ samatāṃ yāti dūramāyāti cāntikam ।
salilaṃ sthalatāmeti kāryakāle mahātmanām ।।

parārtho ayaṃ tavārambhaḥ phalatyeva na saṃśayam ।
na bhavanti visaṃvādasaṃdigdhāḥ sattvavṛttayaḥ ।।

ratnāni badaradvīpe santi tridaśasevite ।
yeṣāmekaprabhāvo api trijagatpūraṇakṣamaḥ ।।

martyabhūmimatikramya sā hi bhūmirmahīyasī ।
āsādyate puṇyamayī nāsattvairnākṛtātmabhiḥ ।।

viṣādastyajyatām putra sthirā buddhirvidhīyatām ।
badaradvīpayātrāyāmutsāhaḥ parigṛhyatām ।।

śrūyatāmeṣa tatprāptyau diṅbhātrānukramakramaḥ ।
sphītasattvaprabhāvastvaṃ saṃsārottaraṇakṣamah ।।

asti paścimadigbhāge samullaṅghya mahīyasām ।
śatāni sapta dvīpānāṃ tathā sapta mahācalān ।।

saptāpatāścānulomapratilomābhidho ambudhiḥ ।
anukūlānilairyasmin pāramāpnoti puṇyavān ।।

tatastattulyanāmādrirvātaistimiramihakṛt ।
yatrākṣṇordiśati svāsthyamamoghākhyā mahauṣadhiḥ ।।

athāvartābhidho ambhodhirvairambhairyatra vāyubhiḥ ।
majjanonmajjanairjantuḥ saptāvarteṣu tāryate ।।

āvartākhyastataḥ śailaḥ śaṅkhanābho niśācarah ।
ghoraḥ prāṇaharo yatra tridaśatrāsakṛt sthitaḥ ।।

kṛṣṇasarpāvṛtā yatra śankhanābhirmahauṣadhiḥ ।
trāyate puṇyasaṃpannaṃ netre śirasi cārpitā ।।

atha nīlodanāmābdhī raktākṣo yatra rākṣasaḥ ।
makaryābhibhūtāṃ buddhavidyāvidvān vaśe ।।

atha nīlodanāmādrirnīlagrīvaḥ kṣapācaraḥ ।
pratīptanetro yatrāste rakṣasāṃ pañcabhiḥ śataiḥ ।।

tatraoṣadhimamoghākhyām rakṣatyāśīviṣaḥ sadā ।
dṛṣṭiniḥ śvāsasaṃsparśadaṃṣṭrotsṛjadviṣānalaḥ ।।

upoṣadhavratavatā maitreṇa karuṇātmanā ।
labhyate sā samutsārya kṛṣṇasarpaṃ mahauṣadhiḥ ।।

taṃ rakṣaḥśakaṭaṃ śailaṃ niṣphalaślakṣṇakandaram ।
tāmajjane śikhāyāṃ ca kṛtvā tarati puṇyavān ।।

atha vairambhanāmādriḥ pāre yasyottarā taṭe ।
ghorā tāmrāṭavī nāma mahāśālavanāntarā ।।

mahānajagarastatra tāmrākṣo nāma duḥsahaḥ ।
āsta yasyogragandhena vāyunaiva na jīvyate ।।

ṣaṇmāsān svapato yasya lālā vyāpnoti yojanam ।
kṣutsaṃtaptasya ṣaṇmāsānalpībhavati jāgrataḥ ।।

veṇugulmaśilābaddhāṃ guhāmutpāṭya medinīm ।
prāyauṣadhīṃ divārātraṃ jvalantīmañjanocitām ।।

tasmādajagarād ghorādanyato vā mahaujasaḥ ।
avairākhyāṃ buddhavidyāṃ japato na bhavedbhayam ।।

tataḥ sapta mahāśailā veṇukaṇṭakasaṃkaṭāḥ ।
tāmrapaṭāṅkapādena tīryante vīryaśālinā ।।

tataśca śālmalīvanaṃ sapta kṣārataraṅgiṇīḥ ।
uttīryāsādyate prāṅgustriśaṅkurnāma parvataḥ ।।

tatra triśaṅkavo nāma kaṇṭakā vajrabhedinaḥ ।
pādayorna viśantyeva tāmrapaṭṭāvanaddhayoḥ ।।

triśankurnāma taṭinī tatrāyaḥśaṅkuparvataḥ ।
upaskīlanadī tatra tato dvidhā dvidhā sarit ।।

athāṣṭādaśavakrākhyaḥ parvato niravagrahaḥ ।
tattulyasaṃjñātha nadī ślakṣṇi nāma giristataḥ ।।

athādridhūmanetrākhyo dhūmanirdigdhadiktaṭaḥ ।
dṛṣṭisparśaviṣairvyāptaḥ krūrāśīviṣamaṇḍalaiḥ ।।

tanmūrdhni palvalasyāntaḥ śilābaddhā mahāguhā ।
jyotīraso maṇiryasyāṃ jīvanī ca mahauṣadhiḥ ।।

bhittvā guhām tadabhyakraśiraḥpādakarodaraḥ ।
vajra-mantrabalopetaḥ krūrasarpairna bādhyate ।।

athograsattvasaṃkīrṇāḥ saptāśīviṣaparvatāḥ ।
nadyaśca tadvidhā yāsāmapāravārisaṃpadaḥ ।।

etaduttīrya nikhilaṃ puṇyaiḥ parahitodyataḥ ।
ārohati sudhāśailaṃ śṛṅgairāliṅgitāmbaram ।।

tatastasyāpare pārśve kalpavṛkṣopaśobhitam ।
puraṃ rohitakaṃ nāma dṛśyate svargasaṃnibham ।।

asti tatra magho nāma maghavāniva viśrutaḥ ।
sārthavāho mahāsattvaḥ sarvasattvahite rataḥ ।।

badaradvīpayātrāyāmudyatasyānavadyadhīḥ ।
mārgopadeśaṃ deśajñaḥ sa te sarvaṃ kariṣyati ।।

ityuktvotsāhya bahuśaḥ śubhadrairiva supriyam ।
vacobhiricitairdevī sahasāntaradhīyata ।।

prabuddhaḥ supriyaḥ sarvaṃ tattatheti vicintayan ।
pratasthe sattvamāruhya nijotsāhapuraḥsaraḥ ।।

sa vrajan vinitāyāsastena nirdiṣṭavartmanā ।
puṇyairdvādaśabhirvarṣaiḥ prāpa rphitakaṃ puram ।।

atrāntare karmayogāt tatra sārthapatirmaghaḥ ।
vyādhinā duścikitsyena babhūvāsvasthavigrahaḥ ।।

alabdhāntaḥpraveśo atha gṛhe rājagṛhopame ।
tasya vyalambata dvāraṃ supriyaḥ kāryasiddhaye ।।

tato vaidyāpadeśena sa praveśamavāptavān ।
upayogakathāprajñā na kasyādarabhūmayaḥ ।।

āyurvedavidhānajñaḥ sa tasyāriṣṭalakṣaṇaiḥ ।
ṣaṇmāsaśeṣamevāyurjñātvā cintāntaro abhavat ।।

tasya priyahitaprāyo bhaiṣajyaparicaryayā ।
atyalpenaiva kālena supriyaḥ priyatāṃ yayau ।।

bhaiṣajyayuktistatprītyā tasya vallabhatāṃ yayau ।
priyopanītaṃ yatkiṃ cit tatsarvaṃ manasaḥ priyam ।।

priyopacāraistasyātha vyādhirādrāvamāyayau ।
ādhiḥ śāmyati satsaṅgāt tao vyādhirviśīryate ।।

tataḥ saṃjātaviśrambhaḥ supriyaḥ praṇayānmagham ।
cakre viditavṛttāntaṃ paścānnijakathākṣaṇe ।।

badaradvīpayātrāyāṃ tasyotsāhaṃ mahātmanah ।
parārthe niścalaṃ jñātvā tamūce vismayānmaghaḥ ।।

aho batāsmin saṃsāre viḥsāre sārarūpiṇaḥ ।
jāyante maṇayaḥ kecit paracintāparāyaṇāḥ ।।

navaṃ vayaḥ priyā mūrtiḥ parārthapravaṇaṃ manaḥ ।
puṇyocitastathaivāyaṃ sthāne guṇasamāgamaḥ ।।

iyatīṃ bhūmimullaṅghya parārthe tvamupāgataḥ ।
karomi tava sāhāyyaṃ kiṃ tvahaṃ bhṛśamāturaḥ ।।

nibaddhāvadhayaḥ prāṇāḥ prayāntyeva śarīriṇām ।
te vrajantu mamānte api tvatsamāhitahetutām ।।

evameva vyayo yastu vyayaḥ sa parigaṇyate ।
parārthe jīvitasyāpi vyayo lābhaśataiḥ samaḥ ।।

na mayā badaradvīpaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ kiṃ tu śrutaṃ mayā ।
mahābdhau diskamuddeśaṃ taistairjānāmi lakṣaṇaiḥ ।।

ityuktvā bhūpatiṃ suhṛdbandhuvākye apyanādaraḥ ।
sa maṅgalapravahaṇaṃ supriyeṇa sahādadhe ।।

tataḥ pravahaṇārūḍhau tau yojanśatānyapi ।
pavanasyānulomyena jagmaturvipulāśayau ।।

sthāne sthāne jalaṃ dṛṣṭvā nānāvarṇaṃ mahodadheḥ ।
kimetaditi prapaccha supriyaḥ kautukānmagham ।।

jale lohācalāḥ pañca santyasya payasāṃ nidheḥ ।
tāmrarūpyamayāścānye hemaratnamayāḥ pare ।।

teṣāṃ chāyāviśeṣeṇa nānāvarṇaḥ pade pade ।
dṛśyate abdhirayaṃ dīptaḥ prāptāntarodgatauṣadhiḥ ।।

ityuktvā vyādhinākrāntaḥ prāptakālāvadhirmaghaḥ ।
prāṇānmumoca satkītivinyastasthirajīvitaḥ ।।

vajralepādapi dṛḍhaṃ yathā sattvaṃ mahātmanām ।
tathā yadi bhadedāyuḥ kimasādhyaṃ bhave bahvet ।।

kūlāvāptapravahaṇah supriyastadviyogajam ।
śucaṃ saṃstabhya vidadhe suhṝdastanusatkriyām ।।

etadevonnataṃ lakṣma sattvotsāhamahātmanām ।
vicchinnālambane kāle yatkartavyadṛḍhaṃ manaḥ ।।

punaḥ pravahaṇārūḍhaḥ sa samuttīrya vāridhim ।
ratnaparvatapārśvena viveśa vikaṭāṭavīm ।।

na viyogairna codvegairnābhiyogairdviṣāmapi ।
na rogaiḥ kleśabhogairvā hīyate mahatāṃ matiḥ ।।

sa tatrākrāntagaganaṃ niruddhāśeṣadiktaṭam ।
durārohaṃ dadarśāgre mūrtaṃ vighnamivācalam ।।

upāyahīnastaṃ dṛṣṭvā giriṃ mūrkhamivoddhatam ।
adhaḥ pallavaśayyāyām suptaḥ so acintayat kṣasṇam ।।

aho bata kiyān kālaḥ prayātaḥ prasthitasya me ।
badaradvīpanāmāpi na nāma śrūyate kkacit ।।

vyavasāyasahāyo me yo abhūtpuṇyapaṇaiḥ param ।
bhagnaplava ivākāle so api karmormiviplavaiḥ ।।

naṣṭopāye apyupāye asmin vyavasāyānmahīyasaḥ ।
na nāma vinivarte ahaṃ siddhirnidhanamastu vā ।।

tadekaṃ janmayātrāsu pūjyaṃ janma jagatrtraye ।
yasmin paropakrārāya jāyate jīvitavyayaḥ ।।

iti cintākulaṃ tatra taṃ jñātvā satyasāgaram ।
nīlo nāma samabhyetya yakṣaḥ prāhācalāśrayaḥ ।।

pūrveṇa yojanaṃ gatvā trīṇi śṛṅgāṇi bhūbhṛtaḥ ।
vetrasopānaniśreṇyā samāruhyātha gamyatām ।।

iti yakṣopadeśena sa vilaṅghya mahācalam ।
dadarśāgre samuttuṅgaśrṛṅgaṃ sphaṭīkabhūdharam ।।

tasminnekaśilāślakṣṇe durgame pakṣiṇāmapi ।
muhūrtamabhavattasya nirvyāpāro manorathaḥ ।।

abhyunnatam nirālambaṃ svasaṃkalpamivācalam ।
sa taṃ vicārya suciraṃ citranyasta ivābhavat ।।

atha candraprabho nāma yakṣaḥ śailaguhāśayaḥ ।
abhyetyaḥ sattvasaṃpannaṃ tamabhāṣaṭa vusmitaḥ ।।

krośamātramito gatvā pūrveṇāpūrvavibhramam ।
dṛśyate candanavanaṃ bālānilacalallatam ।।

tatrāste prasarā nāma guhālīnā mahauṣadhiḥ ।
labhyate deharakṣāyai samuttolya mahāśilām ।।

tatprabhāvakṛtālokaṃ sopānaiḥ sphaṭikācalam ।
sahasaiva samāruhya gamyatāmīpsitāptaye ।।

tatkṣaṇāt kṛtakārtheva sā prayāti mahāuṣadhiḥ ।
na khedastatkṛte kāryastaḍillolāḥ priyāptayaḥ ।।

iti yakṣopadiṣṭena vidhānena sa bhūdharam ।
samutkramya dadarśāgre nagaraṃ hemamandiram ।।

merūkūṭairivākīrṇaṃ prakāśairiva nirmitam ।
savāścaryairiva kṛtaṃ tad dṛṣṭvā vismito abhavat ।।

mahāhemakapāṭābhyāṃ ruddhaddhāram vilokya tat ।
nirjanaṃ vārasaṃcāraṃ vanānte niṣasāda saḥ ।।

atrāntare dinasyānte vyomānantapathādhvagaḥ ।
avāpāstācalopāntaṃ pariśrānta ivāṃśumān ।।

astaṃ gate sahasrāṃśau rajanīramaṇī śanaiḥ ।
tārāpatimivānveṣṭuṃ prasasārābhisārikā ।।

atha prakāśavibahvaiḥ sarvāśāpūraṇonmukhaḥ ।
bodhisattva iva svacchaḥ sudhādīdhitirudyayau ।।

sphīṭā tamaḥ samūhasya niḥśeṣapraśamocitā ।
mānasollāsinī jyotsnā sattvavṛttirivābabhau ।।

tamomohaṃ jahārendurdiśāṃ dinaviyogajam ।
paropakāre hi paro dūrāroho mahātmanām ।।

supriyaścandrakiraṇaiḥ pūryamāṇatanuḥ kṣaṇam ।
nidrāṃ kāryasamudrormikṣobhamudrāmavāptavān ।।

kṣapāyām kṣīyamāṇāyāṃ guṇadākṣiṇyasādarā ।
jagāda devatā svapne maheśākhyā sametya tam ।।

aho bata mahāsattva sattattvābhiniveśinā ।
parārthe vipulaḥ kleśaḥ kṛtaḥ sukṛtinā tvayā ।।

alpaśeṣe prayāse asmin nodvegaṃ kartumarhasi ।
aparyuṣitasattvānāṃ svādhīnāḥ sarvasiddhayaḥ ।।

haimaṃ yadetannagaraṃ trīṇi cānyānyataḥ param ।
santi ratnapurāṇyatra vicitrāṇyuttarottaram ।।

tebhyo niryānti kinnaryaścataśro aṣṭau ca ṣoḍaśa ।
dvātriṃśacca krameṇaiva tvayā dvāri vighaṭṭite ।।

jitendriyasya bhavatastatpramādamavedinaḥ ।
kimanyadacireṇaiv vāñchitāptirbhaviṣyati ।।

ityuktaḥ sādaraṃ devyā pratibuddho atha supriyaḥ ।
jaghāna nagaradvāraṃ triḥ samabhyetya pāṇinā ।।

tataścatasraḥ k innaryo niryayustaralekṣaṇāḥ ।
āścaryatarumañjarya iva līlānilākulāḥ ।।

mānasillāsakāriṇyo nayanāmṛtavṛṣṭayaḥ ।
vadanendusamudyotairdivāpi kṛtacandrikāḥ ।।

tāḥ saṃpūjya smarodāraṃ supriyaṃ priyadarśanāḥ ।
tasyābhilāṣapraṇayairātithyamiva cakrire ।।

candrakāntasamāsīnaṃ kṛtāsanaparigrahāḥ ।
jīvanauṣadhayo jātāḥ smarasyeva savigrahāḥ ।।

tāstamūcuḥ samunmīladvilāsahasitatviṣaḥ ।
dadatya iva karpūraṃ premopāyanatām puraḥ ।।

aho dhanyā vayaṃ yāsāṃ sadguṇālakṛtākṛtiḥ ।
svayaemvābhigamyo api bhavānadyāgato gṛham ।।

vidheṣaḥ kasya pīyūṣe candane kasya vāruciḥ ।
indau mandādaraḥ ko vā sādhuḥ kasya na saṃmataḥ ।।

strīṇāṃ yadyapi saubhāgyabhaṅgāya praṇayaḥ svayam ।
kramastvaddarśanenaiva tathāpi mukharīkṛtāḥ ।।

idaṃ ca kinnarapuraṃ vayaṃ ca praṇayārpitāḥ ।
ratnaṃ ca saubhāṣaṇikaṃ sādho svādhīnameva te ।।

iti tāsāṃ vacaḥ śrutvā supriyaḥ praṇayocitam ।
uvāca sattvadhavalāṃ diśan daśanacandrikām ।।

bahumānāspadaṃ kasya nedaṃ saṃbhāṣaṇāmṛtam ।
ātmano apyādarasthānam bahvatībhiḥ kṛtādaraḥ ।।

ślāghyaṃ darśanamevedaṃ tatrāpyayamanugrahaḥ ।
muktālatāstāpaharāḥ kiṃ punaścandanokṣitāḥ ।।

evaṃ vidhānām svacchānāmaindavīnāmiva tviṣām ।
ākṛtīnām samucitā rucirā lokavṛttayaḥ ।।

aucityacārucaritaṃ prasādaviśadaṃ manah ।
vātsalyapeśalā vāṇī na kasyādarabhūmayaḥ ।।

gṛhīto asmābhirācāraḥ pūjāparikarocitah ।
ātmārpaṇaṃ kulāntaṃ vaḥ parāyattā hi yoṣitaḥ ।।

kanyābhāvādapakrāntā yūyaṃ paraparigrahāḥ ।
viśrambheṇa bhagiṇyo me jananyaḥ snehagauravāt ।।

paravittaṃ viṣaṃ yeṣāṃ jananyaścānyayoṣitaḥ ।
parahiṃsātmahiṃsauva pakṣāsteṣāṃ niratyayāḥ ।।

pauśunyāsatyapāruṣyabhinnavādojjhitaṃ vacaḥ ।
sadaiva vadane yeṣām teṣām sarvāśiṣā diśaḥ ।।

abhidhyārahitaṃ ceto vyāpāraparivarjitam ।
mithyādṛṣṭivihīnaṃ ca yeṣāṃ te satpathaṃ śritāḥ ।।

daśākuśalamārgebhyo nirgatānāṃ nisargataḥ ।
ete kuśalavargasya mārgāḥ svarge nirargalāḥ ।।

dhīreva dhanyaṃ dhanamunnatānāṃ vidyaiva cakṣurvijitendriyāṇām ।
dayaiva puṇyaṃ puruṣottamānāṃ ātmaiva tīrthaṃ śucimānasānām ।।

evaṃvidho ayaṃ guṇasaṃniveśaḥ śīlena vaimalyamupaiti puṃsām ।
sadratnamuktānikarātiritaṃ śīlaṃ satāmābharaṇaṃ vadanti ।।

ityuktamākarṇya guṇānurūpaṃ sattvārthinā tena jitendriyeṇa ।
tuṣṭāstamūcurbhuvi candralokaṃ tāḥ kautukāyaivamukhaiḥ sṛjantyaḥ ।।

maṇerivānarghaguṇojjvalasya dṛṣṭaiva sādhorucitā ruciste ।
yayaiva maulau hṛdaye śrutau ca sadbhiḥ sadaivābharaṇīkṛto asi ।।

maṇirmahārhaḥ prathitaprabhāvaḥ pragṛhyatāmātmasamastvayāyam ।
dhvajārpito varṣati yojanānāṃ sahasramevārthisamīhitaṃ yaḥ ।।

uktveti ratnapravaraṃ taruṇyastasmei dadurmūrtamiva prasādam ।
ādāya taṃ ca praṇayopacāraṃ so api dvitīyaṃ puramāpa raupyam ।।

tatrādarāttaddviguṇābhireva sa pūjitah kinnarakāminībhiḥ ।
krameṇa tenaiva viśuddhabuddhirlebhe maṇiṃ taddviguṇaprabhāvam ।।

।
।।

prāptaśca taṃ ratnamayaṃ caturthaṃ puraṃ tataḥ sarvapurādhikaści ।
so abhyarthitastaddviguṇābhiragre guṇādhikaḥ kinnarasundarībhiḥ ।।

tathaiva saddharmakathāprasaṅgaistātoṣitāstena susaṃyatena ।
utphullanītpaladāmadīrghakaṭākṣavikṣiptakarāstamūcuḥ ।।

bhrātāsti naḥ kinnararājavaṃśaratnākarendurbadarābhidhānaḥ ।
tasyāspadaṃ dvīpamidaṃ mahārhaṃ svanāmacihnaṃ prathitaṃ samṛddhyā ।।
ratnaṃ cedam niyamavidhinā poṣadhākhyavratena nyastaṃ bhāsvatkiraṇanikaraṃ puṇyabhājāṃ prayatnāt varṣatyeva sthiraparahitavyāptaye gṛhyatām tat ।।
ityutpāṭyāmarataruphalaṃ sādaraṃ sundarībhiḥ
premoddāmapraṇayasubhagaṃ dattamāsādya ratnam ।
bālāhākhyaṃ vijitapavanaṃ taṃ prakṛṣṭaṃ turaṅgaṃ
so apyāruhya svanagaramagāllabdhamārgopadeśaḥ ।।

tasmin kāle vipulakuśalaiḥ svargamārgaṃ prayāte
vārāṇasyāṃ viśadayaśasi kṣmāpatau brahmadatte ।
śrīmān sarvapraṇayiphaladaḥ supriyaḥ pauramukhyair
lokatrāṇe vinihitamatirdharmarājye abhiṣiktaḥ ।।

tataḥ śiraḥsnānavidhikrameṇa tatpañcadaśyām dhvajamūrdhni ratnam ।
sa poṣadhopoṣita eva dhṛtvā cakāra viśvaṃ paripūrṇakāmam ।।

kṛtvā yātrām parahitaphalāṃ vatsarāṇām śatena
sthitvā rājye mahati nikhilaṃ pūrayitvā ca lokam ।
putraṃ dhṛtvā narapatipade prāpya sarvopaśāntiṃ
tattvajño asau kimapi paramaṃ brahmabhāvaṃ jagāma ।।

syurete dasyavaḥ sarve pūrvaṃ ye pūritā mayā ।
ratnadrīpābhigamane tasmin supriyajanmani ।।

iti śāstā svavṛttāntakathayā vidadhe vibhuḥ ।
dānavīryopadeśena bhikṣūṇāmanuśāsanam ।।

iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ badaradvīpayātrāvadānaṃ nāma ṣaṣṭhaḥ pallavaḥ ।।

muktālatāvadānam ।

kuślapraṇidhānaśuddhadhānmāṃ vimalālokavivekabodhakānām ।
parikīrtanamātrameva yeṣāṃ bhavamohāpahatesta eva dhanyāḥ ।।

purā parṣatsahasrāṇāṃ nyagrodhopavanasthitiḥ ।
kapilākhye pure cakre bhagavān dharmadeśanām ।।

amandānandasaṃdohasyandi candanaśītalam ।
tasya vāgamṛtaṃ dhanyāḥ kṛtāṅjalipuṭāḥ papuḥ ।।

rājā śuddhodanastatra dharmaśravaṇasaṃgame ।
puṇyopadeśasalilairlebhe vaimalyanirvṛtim ।।

atha tatra mahānāmā śākyarājakulodbhavaḥ ।
dharmopadeśamākarṇya prātaḥ svagṛhamabravīt ।।

aho nu bhagavān buddho dharmaḥ saṃghaśca siddhaye ।
buddhotpādo ayamasmākaṃ nirvāṇāya mahāphalaḥ ।।

upadeśaviśeṣāptānirvṛtestasya tadvacaḥ ।
śrutvā śaśiprabhā patnī praṇayāttamabhāṣataḥ ।।

anugrāhyā bhagavataḥ puruṣāḥ puṇyabhāginah ।
nindyāstadupadeśānāmanarhā yoṣito vayam ।।

iti jāyāvacaḥ śrutvā sa jagāda jagadguroḥ ।
bhadre bhagavato nāsti bhedaḥ kāruṇyadarśane ।।

samā sarvatra bhā bhānoḥ samā vṛṣṭiḥ payomucaḥ ।
samā bhagavato dṛṣṭiḥ sarvasattvānukampinaḥ ।।

mahāprajāpatervākyādaparāhṇakṣaṇaṃ tapaḥ ।
śuddhodanaḥ karotyeva rājā bahgavato antike ।।

iti patyuḥ priyagirā vṛtā śākyāṅganāgaṇaiḥ ।
yācane tadbhagavatah sā puṇyopavanaṃ yayau ।।

sā satvakusumaṃ tatra taṃ dadarśa mahāphalam ।
praśamāmṛtasaṃsiktaṃ karuṇākalpapādapam ।।

lateva pavanānamrā taṃ dūrāt praṇanāma sā ।
lobheneva parityakrā cyutakarṇotpalacchalāt ।।

vilokya kāñcanaruciṃ ratnabhūṣaṇabhūṣitām ।
ānandanāmā bhikṣustāmuvāca prahitodyataḥ ।।

veṣaḥ praśamaśūnyo ayaṃ mātarmunitapovane ।
darpotsikto na yuktaste viraktānāmidaṃ padam ।।

guṇasaṃyamasiktāni mukharābhraṇānyaho ।
nehāstadgrahaṇaṃ yuktamitīvopadiśanti te ।।

ityuktā tena sā tanvī vailajyavinatānanā ।
unmucyābharaṇaṃ sarvaṃ prāḥiṇonnijamadniram ।।

upaviṣṭeṣu sarveṣu nirdiṣṭakuśalastataḥ ।
anityataivaṃ bhagavānupadeśaṃ pravakrame ।।

mahāmohaprabhāvo ayaṃ yena nityamanityatām ।
nityatāmiva manyante mūḍhā jagati jantavaḥ ।।

asatye ramate lokaḥ satyapratyayamohitaḥ ।
na vetti sarvabhāvānāmabhāvānubhavāṃ sthitim ।।

kecid vyākaraṇaiḥ pare śrutipathaistarkapravādaiḥ pare kecittantraparigrahairbahuvidhairanyaiḥ kalākauśalaiḥ ।
saṃsaktāḥ punaruktajanmaśaraṇau yātā sahaiva kṣayaṃ
tatrāpyakṣyayalīlayā kṣaṇapadaṃ mugdhaurnibaddhā dhṛtiḥ ।।

viṣayaviṣamāpāyaḥ kāyaḥ prapañca yāśayā
kharataramarusphārākāro mohabhāvo bhavaḥ ।
hitabhūmi tathākāryaṃ kāryaṃ vivekināṃ tathā
niravadhirayaṃ dṛṣṭvā vyādhiryathā nivartate ।।

ityādyanityasaṃskārasaṃyuktaṃ yuktamudyate ।
dharmopadeśakuśalaṃ vaktuṃ bhagavati svayam ।।

ekā śākyavadhūstatra rūpasaubhāgyagarvitā ।
sthitā śauśavatāruṇyasaṃghau vayasi duḥsahe ।।

muktāhāraṃ stanataṭe lolāpāṅgairmuhurmuhuḥ ।
āliloke yaśaḥsphārasāraṃ ratipateriva ।।

hārāvalokinīṃ dṛṣṭvā tāmanekāgrahādasau ।
acintayādviraktena magatpatnī śaśiprabhā ।।

iyaṃ dharmopadeśe api capalā hāramīkṣate ।
bhāvānāṃ na śṛṇotyeva mūḍhā kṣaṇikatāmimām ।।

svaṃ hāraṃ darśayitvāsyā hārotsāhaṃ harāmyaham ।
adhikālokanenaiva darpaḥ śāmyati dehinām ।।

iti saṃcintya sā dāsīṃ rohikākhyāmabhāṣata ।
rohike gaccha me hāraṃ gṛhāt satvaramāhara ।।

ityuktā sā tayā tatra pravṛtte dharmasaṃśrave ।
akālagamanodvignā niḥśvasyācintayat kṣaṇam ।।

aho batāntarāyo ayaṃ saṃjātaḥ kuśale mama ।
nāsmin śrotuṃ labhe dharmaṃ yatparāyattajīvitā ।।
