puṇyasaurabhasaṃbhārāt kīrṇakāruṇyakesarāt ।
mukhapadmād bhagavato dhanyaḥ prāpnoti vāṅbhadhuḥ ।।

aho svācchandyavicchedastanubhaṅgaḥ sukhakṣayaḥ ।
sevā jagati jantūnāṃ duḥkhe duḥkhaparaṃparā ।।

sevāprayāsasaṃprāptaṃ dhanamānakaṇodayam ।
tatpamatyuṣṇaniḥśvāsairaho kṛcchreṇa pīyate ।।

mānaglānirguṇaglānirojaḥpunaśamaḥ śramah ।
prathamaṃ sevakasyaitat phalamīśvaradarśane ।।

lauhī bandhanaśṛṅkhalā caraṇayorhelāvamānāvanī
svavyāpāraniṣedhanityaniyatī nidrāsukhadrohiṇī ।
āśāsyasya viśālajālasaraṇiḥ satsaṅgabhogāśaniḥ
mugdhānāṃ mṛgatṛṣṭikāmarumahī sevā śarīrakṣayaḥ ।।

iti saṃcintya suciraṃ sā jagāma tadājñayā ।
sevāvikrītakāyānāṃ svecchāviharaṇaṃ kutaḥ ।।

vrajantīṃ tām parapreṣyāṃ kṛpaṇāṃ karuṇākulaḥ ।
nirīkṣya bahgavān divyacakṣuṣācintayat kṣasṇam ।।

asmin janmani śeṣo asyā saṃpūrṇo jīvitāvadhiḥ ।
iyaṃ varākī saṃsārāduddhartavyā svayaṃ mayā ।।

atha tām karmayogena vrahantīṃ sahasā pathi ।।
vatsavātsalyavivaśā śṛṅgābhyāmājaghāna gauḥ ।।
sā pradaghyau bhagavataḥ prasādāt tanmayasmṛtiḥ ।
janmāntarādhivāsena buddhālambanamānasā ।।

aho karmormibhiḥ śīrṇe saṃsāramakarākare ।
janmāvarteṣu jantūnāṃ majjanonmajjanakramaḥ ।।

puṃso lalāṭavipulopalapaṭṭikāsu niḥśarmakarmaghaṭitaprakaṭāṅkaṭaṅkaiḥ ।
nayastāni janmamaraṇaprasarākṣarāṇi naitāni pāṇiparimārjanayā calanti ।।

iyaṃ karmāyattā pracuracitravaicitraracanā
narāṇāṃ māyūracchadapaṭalatulyā pariṇatiḥ ।
yayā garbhārambhe kramanipatane vṛddhisamaye
kṣaye vā nānyat prābhajata tanulekhācchavirati ।।

saṃcintyātha puraḥ pravṛttasudaśāsannāvasannasthitiṃ prāptevāsamadāsabhāvakalanāvailakṣyaniḥ spandatām ।
ādhāya praṇidhānadhāmni dhavale saddharmaśuddhāṃ dhiyaṃ
saṃsāre vicikitsya eva malinaṃ tatyāja sā jīvitam ।।

tataḥ sā siṃhaladvīpe samīpe svargasaṃpadām ।
candralekheva dugdhābdhau divyadyutirajāyata ।।

ādhānajanmanastasya muktāvarṣeṃ divaścyute ।
sābhūnmuktālatā nāma siṃhalādhipateḥ sutā ।।

sā puṇyamiva lāvaṇyaṃ vahantī vṛddhimāgatā ।
lebhe vivekenāṅgānāṃ saṃtoṣamiva yaovanam ।।

tataḥ kadācidvaṇijaḥ śrāvastīpuravāsinaḥ ।
makarākaramuttīrya siṃhaladvīpamāyayuḥ ।।

te tatra rātriparyante viśrāntisukhamājaguḥ ।
dharmārthagāthāsaṃnaddhaprabuddhabuddhabhāṣitam ।।

tdantaḥpuraharmyasthā śrutvaiva śravaṇāmṛtam ।
kimetaditi papraccha tānānāyya nṛpātmajā ।।

te tāmūcuḥ pramuditāmidaṃ buddhasya bḥāṣitam ।
svabhāvārhaṃ bhagavataḥ sarvasattvānukampinah ।।

buddhāmidhānaṃ śrutviva pulakālaṃkṛtākṛtiḥ ।
sā babhūva samudbhūtasaṃvidbhavyānubhāvabhūḥ ।।

unmubhī sāmayūriva śabdaireva payomucaḥ ।
ka eṣa bhagavān buddha iti paparcchaḥ tān punaḥ ।।

tataste nikhilaṃ tasyai śraddhāsaṃvardhitādarāḥ ।
nyavedayan puṇyamayīṃ bhagavaccaritasthitim ।।

atha sā tatkathāvāptaprāgjanmakuśalodayā ।
vijñaptilekhaṃ pradadau teṣāṃ bhagavataḥ kṛte ।।

kālena sindhumuttīrya saṃrpāptāste nijāṃ pirīm ।
praṇamyāvedya tadvṛttaṃ dadurlekhaṃ mahātmane ।।

bhagavānapi sarvajñaḥ pūrvameva vibhāvya tat ।
muktālatāyāḥ kṛpayā svayaṃ lekhamavācayat ।।

aho smaraṇameva te kimapi puṇyapaṇyaṃ satāṃ
bhavātibahvabhaiṣajaṃ vyasanatāpatṛṣṇāpahat ।
bhavanmayakathākramopanatasaṃvidāsvādabhūḥ
sa eṣa bhagavan mahānamṛtasaṃvibhāgo mama ।।

iti saṃkṣiptalekhārthaṃ vibhāvya bhagavān svayam ।
īṣatsmitviṣā sattvaprakāśamadiśaddiśām ।।

tataścitrakarāśakyāṃ prabhāvairanupūritām ।
bhagavān prāhiṇot tasyai nyastāṃ svapratimāṃ paṭe ।।

punaḥ pravahaṇārūḍhā vaṇijaste tadājñayā ।
avāpya siṃhaladvīpaṃ tasyai paṭamadarśayan ।।

hemasiṃhāsananyaste paṭe dṛṣṭvā tathāgatam ।
janastanmayatādhyānādekībhāvamivāyayau ।।

adhastāllikhitaṃ tasmin puṇyaprāptamadṛśyata ।
tisraḥ śaraṇyā gatayaḥ pañca śikṣāpadāṇi ca ।।

sapratītyasamutpādaḥ sānulomaviparyayaḥ ।
āryāṣṭāṅgastathā mārgaḥ paramāmṛtanirbharaḥ ।।

svayaṃ bhagavatā vyastaṃ tasyopari subhāṣitam ।
śobhate bhāvanālīnaṃ bhrājiṣṇu kanakākṣaram ।।

viṣamaviṣayālolavyālāvalīvalayākulāt
taruṇatimirānniṣkramyāsmāt pramohamayādgṛhāt ।
jananamaraṇakleśāveśapravṛttapṛthivyathā
vrajata śaraṇaṃ bauddhaṃ dharmaṃ na cātra bhavādbhayam ।।

jinapratikṛtiṃ puṇyām paśyantī pārthivātmajā ।
anādikālopacitāṃ mumocājñānavāsanām ।।

prāṃśuṃ kavata kāñcanakāntakāyaṃ suskandhamājānubhujābhirāmam ।
dhyānāvadhānārthanimīlitākṣaṃ lāvaṇyadhārāyitatuṅganāsam ।।

svabhāvabhavyaṃ pravibhāsamānaṃ pralambanirbhūṣaṇakarṇapāśam ।
bālapravālāruṇavalkalāṅkaṃ saṃsaktasaṃdhyābhramivāmarādrim ।।

tviṣā diṣāṃ śīlamivādiśantaṃ ānandadānodyatavaktracandram ।
kṣamāguṇaṃ kṣāmiva śikṣayantaṃ puṇyocitā sā subhagaṃ vilokya ।।

praṇāmaparyantakapolacumbikarṇotpalānāṃ parivartanena ।
nirasya niḥsāraśarīratṛptiṃ satyānubhāvaṃ paramaṃ prapede ।।

srotaḥsamāpattiphalaprakāśaṃ sāsādya tatra kṣaṇalabdhabodhiḥ ।
vicintayantī sugataprabhāvaṃ samabhyadhādvismayaharṣabhūmiḥ ।।

aho mahāmohatamohareṇa dūrasthitenāmi tathāgatena ।
prasahya bḥāsvadvapuṣārpiteyaṃ vikāsalakṣmīḥ kuśalāmbujasya ।।

tīrṇo bahvaḥ satpraṇidhānamāptaṃ prasannamantaḥkaraṇaṃ kṣaṇena ।
aho nu tṛṣṇāparitāpaśāntyai samucchalantīva samāmṛtaughāḥ ।।

ityuktvā sā bahgavate muktāratnānyupāyanam ।
vitīrya saṃghapūjāyāṃ visasarja vaṇigjanam ।।

te mahodadhimuttīrya prāptā bahgavato antikam ।
tanmuktāratnanikaraṃ praṇamyāsmai nyavedayan ।।

vaṇigbhiḥ kathitāṃ śrutvā tatkathāṃ tatra bhikṣuṇā ।
ānandanāmnā pṛṣṭho atha babhāṣe bhagavān jinaḥ ।।

yāsau purā rohitākhyā dāsī śākyagṛhe abahvat ।
saiva muktālatā jātā satkarmapraṇidhānataḥ ।।

abhūnmahādhano nāma vārāṇasyāṃ vaṇik purā ।
tasya ratnavatī nāma patnī puṇyocitābhavat ।।

sā patyau pañcatāṃ yāte niḥputrā stūpaśekhare ।
pūjāṃ kṛtvā mahāhārāṃ bhaktiyuktā nyavedayat ।।

tena puṇyavipākena siṃhalādhipateḥ sutā ।
jātā muktālatā saiva prātā ca parinirvṛtim ।।

saiva janmani cānyasminnairvaryamadamohitā ।
pūjādhikṣepadakṣābhūddhāsī tenātivatsaram ।।

janmabhūmau janenātpaṃ yadyatkarma śubhāśubham ।
tasya tasya sa tadrūpaṃ bhuṅkte pariṇataṃ phalam ।।

nikhilakuśalamūlā kīrtipuṣpojjvalaśrīḥ
śubhaphalabharasūrirdharmavallī narāṇām ।
bhavati ca viṣavallī kilbiṣakleśamūla-
bhramanipatanamohānantasaṃtāpahetuḥ ।।

saṃtapte asmin kharataramaruṣphārasaṃsāramārge
pāpaṃ punyaṃ tyajata janatāḥ saktatīvrānutāpam ।
puṇyaṃ puṇyaṃ kuruta satataṃ puṇyapīyūṣasiktāḥ
puṇyacchāyātarutalabhuvaḥ śītalāḥ puṇyabhājām ।।

iti satpraṇidhānasya phalaṃ kathayatā svayam ।
bhikṣūṇāmupadeśo ayaṃ bhaktyai bhagavatā kṛtaḥ ।।

iti kṣemendraviracitāyām bodhisattvāvadānakalpatāyāṃ muktālatāvadānaṃ nāma saptamaḥ pallavaḥ ।।

śrīguptāvadānam ।

kṛtāpakāre api kṛpākulāni krūre apyalaṃ pallavakomalāni ।
dveṣoṣmatapte apyatiśītalāni bhavanti cittāni sadāśayānām ।।

purā surapurodāre pure rājagṛhābhidhe ।
śrīguptākhyo gṝhapatirbabhūva dhandopamaḥ ।।

dṛptaḥ sujanavidveṣī guṇeṣu viratādaraḥ ।
sadā dhanamadādhmātaḥ sā jahāsa matiṃ satām ।।

kaṭhine aṣvativakreṣu śūnyeṣu mukhareṣu ca ।
śankheṣviva khaleṣveva lakṣmīrdākṣiṇyamāśritā ।।

taṃ kadācit gururjñātiputraḥ kṣapaṇakaḥ khalah ।
mithaḥ svairakathāsaktaḥ puṇyadveṣādabhāṣata ।।

ya eṣa gṛdhrakūṭākhye girau bhikṣuśatairvṛtaḥ ।
sarvajñakīrtiḥ sugatāstrijagatpūjyatāṃ gataḥ ।।

naivāsya pratibhāṃ kāṃcid bhavyāmupalabḥāmahe ।
nītaḥ kiṃ tūnnatiṃ mūrkhairbahgavān bhagavāniti ।।

avicāyava satataṃ paroktamanubhāṣate ।
gatānugatikaḥ prāyaḥ prasiddhasaraṇau janaḥ ।।

vratādiniyamastasya dambha eva vibhāvyate ।
aśnāti maunakṛt matsyānekapādavrato bakaḥ ।।

tasmaāt tasyopahāsāya kriyatām kāpi vajṇcanā ।
māyāmohito dhūrtānām paro api parituṣyati ।।

iti tenoktamākarṇya śrīguptaḥ karkmamohitaḥ ।
patituṃ pāpaśvabhreṣu yuktyā tadupadiṣṭayā ।।

pradīptakhadirāṅgārapūrṇāṃ gūḍhāṃ khadāṃ gṛhe ।
kṛtvā saviṣamannaṃ ca yayau bhagavato antikam ।।

tena mithyāvihitayā bhaktyā bhoktuṃ nimantritaḥ ।
vijñāya sarvaṃ sarvajñastatheti prāha sasmitaḥ ।।

viṣagniyogakupitām patnīṃ saddharmavādinīm ।
gṛhe babandha śrīguptaḥ śaṅkito mantraviśravāt ।।

atha vijñātavṛtto api bhagavān svayamāyayau ।
vandyamāno jagadvandyaiścaturmukhamukhaiḥ suraiḥ ।।

śrīguptasya tamārambhaṃ vivedaṃ nagare janaḥ ।
dikṣu dhāvati pāpānāṃ suguptamapi pātamak ।।

tataḥ kaścit samabhyetya bhagavantamupāsakaḥ ।
uvāca caraṇālīnāścintayan dahanaṃ viṣam ।।

mithyānamrah priyālāpī guḍhavahniviṣānnadaḥ ।
parihāryaḥ prayatnena bhagavanneṣa durjanah ।।

kuryādanārye nāśvāsi kāryaṃ mādhuryamāśriye ।
antracchedī vigīrṇo hi madhudigdhamukhaḥ kṣuraḥ ।।

nānyastutiṃ guṇadveṣī sahate guṇinām khalaḥ ।
santastuṣyanti yenaiva tenakupyanti durjanāḥ ।।

tvayi lokatraye netraśatapatravikāśini ।
asya rāhoḥ padaṃ prāpte nāndhībhavati kiṃ jagat ।।

tacchrutvā bhagavānūce kiṃcit smitasitāṃśubhiḥ ।
tannikārogratimiraṃ dūrāt pariharanniva ।।

na mamāṅgaṃ spṛśatyagniḥ prabahvatyapi vā viṣam ।
paradveṣadaridrāṇāṃ doṣo api nirupadravaḥ ।।

aroṣaśītalaṃ cetaḥ siktaṃ yasya śamāmṛtaiḥ ।
kiṃ karotyanalastasya viṣaṃ vā viṣayadviṣaḥ ।।

viṣāyate tu pīyūṣaṃ kusumaṃ kuliśāyate ।
dveṣadoṣottarasyaiva candanaṃ dahanāyate ।।

tiryagyonigatasyāpi bodhisattvapadāsthiteḥ ।
kāruṇyamaitrīyuktasya nāgnirdahati vigraham ।।

purā kaliṅganṛpatiḥ khaṇḍadvīpābhidhāvanīm ।
dadāha mṛgasaṃghānām saṃkṣepe sa samudyataḥ ।।

kānane jvalite tasminnekastittiriśāvakaḥ ।
maitryā bodhiṃ samālambya dahanapraśamaṃ vyaghāt ।।

tasmādadrohamanasāṃ na bhayaṃ vidyate kkacit ।
śrūyatāṃ sattvasaṃpatteridamanyacca kautukam ।।

avṛṣṭiviṣame kāle muneḥ kasyacidāśrame ।
manuṣyasadṛśālāpaḥ śaśakaḥ suciraṃ sthitaḥ ।।

kṣutkṣāmaṃ munimālokya phalamūlaparikṣayāt ।
uvācācalasaṃkalpastadvyathāvyathitāśayaḥ ।।

bhagavan mam māṃsānāṃ saṃprati prāṇavartanam ।
kriyatāṃ rakṣaṇīyaṃ tat śarīraṃ dharmasādhanam ।।

ityuktvā dāvaśeṣāgnau vikṣepa śahskastanum ।
vāryamāṇo api yatnena praṇayānmuninā muhyuḥ ।।

tasya sattvaprabhāveṇa jvalajjvālākulo analaḥ ।
prayayau majṇjuśiñjānabhramarāmbhojakhaṇḍatām ।।

so api divyavapustatra kamale mahati sthitaḥ ।
praṇamyamāno munirbhirvidadhe dharmadeśanām ।।

iti bodhipravṛttānāṃ na vahnerna viṣādbhayam ।
bhagavān kathayitveti śrīguptabhavanaṃ yayau ।।

tatra tena praviśyaiva nikṣipte dakṣiṇe pade ।
babhūvāgnikhadā mañjuguñjadbhṛṅgasarojinī ।।

dṛṣṭvopaviṣṭaṃ śrīguptastaṃ sarorihavistare ।
taddṛṣṭinaṣṭakāluṣyaḥ provācaḥ caraṇānataḥ ।।

bhagavan mama pāpasya kṣantavyo ayaṃ vyatikramaḥ ।
mohāndhapatite rucyaṃ kāruṇyamadhikaṃ satām ।।

mamākalyāṇamitreṇa yo ayaṃ pāpapathe kṛtaḥ ।
upadeśaḥ pramoheṇa tatra trāṇaṃ bhavatsmṛtiḥ ।।

viṣadigdharasaṃ sarvaṃ bhojyaṃ te kalpitaṃ mayā ।
aho mamaiva saṃkrāntaṃ paścāttapamayaṃ viṣam ।।

iti bruvāṇaṃ śrīguptaṃ sāśrunetraṃ kṛpānidhiḥ ।
dṛṣṭvā babhāṣe bhagavān bhikṣusaṃghasya śṛṇyavataḥ ।।

viṣādaṃ mā kṛthāḥ sādho na vayaṃ vimukhāstvayi ।
ghoravairaviṣatyāgānnaivāsmāstapate viṣam ।।

vārāṇasyāṃ purā śrīmān brahmadatto abhavannṛpaḥ ।
abhūdanupamā nāṃ atasya prāṇasamāśrayā ।।

suvarṇabhāsasaṃjñasya tatpurāntavanasthiteḥ ।
ravaṃ mayūrarājasya sā kadācidathāśṛṇot ।।

sā tasya śadamākarṇya veṇuvīṇāsvanopamam ।
kimetaditi papraccha naranāthaṃ sakautukā ।।

rājovāca vanānte asminnasti ratnacchadaḥ śikhī ।
madhuraṃyojanavyāpi yasyaitat kaṇṭhakūjitam ।।

iti bruvāṇo nṛpatistatsaṃdarśanamarthitaḥ ।
premaprayatnaiḥ preyasyā prahasan punarabravīt ।।

darśanaṃ durlabhaṃ mugdhe tadvidhādbhutarūpiṇaḥ ।
tathāpi yadi nirbandhaḥ kriyate tatpariśramaḥ ।।

ityuktvā nṛpatistasya grahaṇe jālajīvinaḥ ।
vyasṛjat tasya saṃrpāptyaiḥ vidhāya vadhasaṃvidam ।।

vaśīkṛto na vettyeva mohādakṣiparīkṣayā ।
anurāgāhataḥ strībhirakarmāṇyapi kāryate ।।

prāptānām praṇayāt patnyāḥ prauḍhāyāḥ pādapīṭhatām ।
īrṣyayaiva vinaśyanti dhīdhṛtismṛtikīrtayaḥ ।।

tataḥ śākunikairnyastāḥ pāśabandhāḥ pade pade ।
prabhāvādbarhirājasy vyaśīryantaiva saṃtatam ।।

duḥkhitān yatnavaiphalyādbhītān nṛpatiśāsanāt ।
mayūrarājastān dṛṣṭvā karuṇākulatāṃ yayau ।।

so acintayadaho bhītāḥ kṣmāpateḥ śrūraśāsanāt ।
madbandhane visaṃvādādvarākā jālajīvinah ।।

saṃcintya kṛpayā spaṣṭagbhirvisṛjya tān ।
nṛpamānāyya tadveśma tenaiva sahito yayau ।।

sa tatrāntaḥpure nityaṃ sabhāryeṇa mahībhujā ।
pūjyamānaḥ paricayāduvāsa vihitādaraḥ ।।

snigdhaśyāmāmbudatviṣā sunīlamaṇiveśmasu ।
citrapatrarucā cakre saṃsaktendrāyudhabhamam ।।

atha digjayayātrāyām kadācidvasudhādhipaḥ ।
yayau tadupacārāya devīmādiśya sādaraḥ ।।

tataścānupamā devī patyau yāte pramādinī ।
rūpayauvanadarpāndhā nāluloke kulasthitim ।।

taruṇaṃ prekṣya rāgiṇyāstasyāḥ kandarpaviplave ।
bhūyaḥ pralambhabhīteva lajjā dūrataraṃ yayau ।।

malinaḥ kuṭilastīkṣṇaḥ karṇasaṃsparśanocitaḥ ।
capalaścapalākṣīṇāṃ sudṛśāṃ sadṛśaḥ kramaḥ ।।

vividhonmādakāriṇyaḥ saṃsāramakarākare ।
caranti prāṇahāriṇyaḥ kālakūṭacchadāḥ striyaḥ ।।

kusumāt sukumārasya krūrasya krakacādapi ।
ko jānāti paricchedaṃ strīṇāṃ citrasya cetasaḥ ।।

pracarantīṃ priyāṃ kaṇṭhe kṛtvā ye yānti nirvṛtim ।
śītalāṃ vimalāṃ snigdhāṃ khaṅgadhārāṃ pibanti te ।।

sācintayat sthitaḥ śalyamayamantaḥpure mama ।
mayūrarājaḥ śīlajñaḥ puruṣālāpaveṣṭitaḥ ।।

kathayiṣyatyavaśyaṃ me vṛttameṣa mahīpateḥ ।
nindyaṃ karma kṛtaṃ tāvadadhunā kiṃ karomyaham ।।

āstāṃ parijñātatattvo marmajño asau vidagdhadhīḥ ।
jātā me kṛtapāpāyāḥ śaṅkā niścetaneṣvapi ।।

iti saṃcintya sā t asya saviṣaṃ bhojanaṃ dadau ।
rāgamattāḥ khalāyattāḥ kiṃ kiṃ kurvanti na striyaḥ ।।

tayopācaryamāṇasya saviṣaiḥ pānabhojanaiḥ ।
vivṛddhā barhirājasya ruruce rucirā ruciḥ ।।

svasthamālokya taṃ devī rahasyodbhedaśaṅkitā ।
śanaiḥ śokāmayagrasyā trasyā tatyāja jīvitam ।।

evaṃ tasya viṣeṇāpi naiva glānirajāyata ।
mahatāṃ cittavaimalyaṃ nirviṣaṃ kurute viṣam ।।

rāgo viṣaṃ viṣaṃ moho dveṣaśca viṣamaṃ viṣam ।
buddho dharmastathā saṃghaḥ satyaṃ ca paramāmṛtam ।।

ghoraṃ viṣaṃ sṛjati mohamahāmburāśiḥ ghoraṃ viṣaṃ sṛjati rāgamahoragaśca ।
ghoraṃ viṣaṃ sṛjati vairavanāvaniśca janmakramo asti viṣamasya viṣasya nānyaḥ ।।

adharmakāmaḥ kṛtavānevamevānyajanmani ।
śrīgupto agnikhadāṃ sāpi tasyābhūtsahadharmiṇī ।।

ityuktvā bhagavān samyakkaruṇālokanāmbubhiḥ ।
cakāra vītarajasaṃ śrīguptaṃ śāsanonmukham ।।

kalitakuśalaḥ śrīgupto atha prakāśapadāptaye
śaraṇagamanānyeva trīṇi smaran vimalasmṛtiḥ ।
jinaparicayāt puṇyaṃ lebhe satām hi vilokanaṃ
bhavati mahate kalyāṇāya pramodasukhāya ca ।।

śrīguptasya nikārakilbiṣajuṣo apyajñānamohāpahaḥ
kṛtvāvaśyamanugraheṇa bhagavān kāruṇyapuṇyodyataḥ ।
bhikṣūṇāṃ bhavasaṃkṣayāya vidadhe nirvairatāśāsanaṃ
yenaite na bhavanti bandhabhavane bhūyo bhavagranthaye ।।

iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ śrīguptāvadānaṃ nāma aṣṭamaḥ pallavaḥ ।।

jyotiṣkāvadānam ।

dhanyānāmaśivaṃ bibharti śubhatāṃ bhavyasvabhāvodbhavaṃ
mūrkhāṇāṃ kuśalaṃ prayātyahitatāmityeṣa lakṣyaḥ kramaḥ ।
niśīthatimirāndhyamauṣadhivanasyātyantakāntipradaṃ
etaccaulukakūladṛṣṭahataye sarvatra maitraṃ mahaḥ ।।

purā rājagṛhābhikhye bimbisārasya bhūpateḥ ।
abhūt pauraḥ subhadrākhyaḥ paripūrṇagṛhasthiteḥ ।।

maurkhyānmohaprapannasya sarvadarśanavidviṣaḥ ।
tasya kṣapaṇakeṣveva babhūvābhyadhikādaraḥ ।।

tasya satyavatī nāma jāyābhijanaśālinī ।
garbhamādhatta pūrṇendubimbaṃ pauradarīva dik ।।

kalandakanivāsākhyo veṇukānanasaṃśrayaḥ ।
kadācit bhagavāt buddhaḥ prāptaḥ piṇḍāya targṛham ।।

pūjāṃ sabhāryaḥ kṛtvātmai taṃ sa papraccha sādaraḥ ।
garbhasthitamapatyaṃ yat kiṃrūpaṃ tadbhaviṣyati ।।

so avadat saṃpadaṃ bhuktvā putraste divyamānuṣīm ।
pravrajyayā śāsane me saṃyukto muktimeṣyati ।।

yāte bhagavati spaṣṭamityādiśya nijāśrayam ।
abhyāyayau gṛhapaterbhūrikaḥ kṣapaṇo gṛham ।।

bhagavadbhāṣitaṃ tattu subhadreṇa niveditam ।
śrutvā kṣapaṇakah kṣipramabhūddeṣaviṣākulaḥ ।।

gaṇayitvā sa suciraṃ grahajñānakṛtaśramaḥ ।
yadevoktaṃ bhagavatā praśne apaśyattathāvidham ।।

so acintayadayo satyamuktaṃ tena na saṃśayaḥ ।
tatprabhāvopamādāya kiṃ svasatyaṃ vadāmyaham ।।

tasya sarvajñatāṃ vetti subhadro yadi madgirā ।
tadeṣa kṣapaṇaśraddhāṃ tyakṣyati śramaṇādarāt ।।

iti saṃcintya sāmarṣaḥ sa subhadramabhāṣata ।
asatyemetat kathitaṃ tena sarvajñamāninā ।।

manuṣyaḥ kathamāpnoti devārhāṃ divyasaṃpadam ।
pravrajyā kiṃ tu satyeva kathaṃ tenāsya cintitā ।।

kṣīṇaḥ kṣudupasaṃtapto yasya nāstyanyato gatiḥ ।
tasya tasya subhikṣārhaṃ śaraṇaṃ śramaṇavratam ।।

paśyāmyahaṃ gṛhapate pramāṇaṃ yadi madvacaḥ ।
pratyutāyaṃ śiśurjātaḥ kulaṃ saṃtāpayiṣyati ।।

ityudīrya kṣapaṇake yāte gṛhapatiściram ।
vicārya vidadhe tāṃ tām yuktiṃ garbhanipātane ।।

yadā dravyaprayoge api naiva garbhah paricyutaḥ ।
tadāsya patnīmavadhīdekānte haṭhamardanaiḥ ।।

tataḥ śītavanaṃ tasyāṃ śmaśānaṃ tena pāpinā ।
prāpitāyām kṣapaṇakāstadvārtānanditā jaguḥ ।।

aho batāho sarvajñaḥ śiśoḥ satyaṃ taduktavān ।
seyaṃ sūnāvajāte asya jananī pañcatāṃ gatā ।।

iyaṃ sā śrīḥ śiśordivyā soktā divyamanuṣyatā ।
iyaṃ ca sāsya pravrajyā yat kukṣau nidhanaṃ gataḥ ।।

iti teṣāṃ pravādena sopahāsena sarvataḥ ।
śmaśānadarśanāyaiva babhūva janasaṃgamaḥ ।।

atrāntare divyadṛśā bhagavān bhūtabhāvanaḥ ।
sarvaṃ vijñāya tadbuddhaḥ pradadhyau sasmitaḥ kṣaṇam ।।

aho mohānubandhena dūrasthairapi dehinām ।
ālokaśchādyate mūrkhairmeghairiva vikāribhiḥ ।।

śubhaṃ kṣapayatā tena kṣapaṇena sa mugdhadhīḥ ।
aho gṛhapatiḥ pāpādakāryamapi kāritaḥ ।।

iti saṃcintya bahgavān svayaṃ bhikṣugaṇairvṛtaḥ ।
yayau śītavanaṃ kṣipraṃ śmaśānaṃ karuṇākulaḥ ।।

śmaśānacārikāṃ jñātvā rājā bhagavataḥ svayam ।
bimbisāraḥ sahāmātyaistāmeva bhivamāyayau ।।

tataḥ subhadrajāyāyāṃ prakṣiptāyāṃ citānale ।
kukṣiṃ bhittvāmbujāsīnaḥ śiśuḥ sūrya ivodyayau ।।

jvālitāṇalamadhyasthaṃ taṃ kaścinnāgrahīdyadā ।
tadā janasamūhasya hāhākāro mahānabhūt ।।

tatastaṃ saṃbhramāvṛddhagatiḥ sugataśāsanāt ।
kumārabhṛtyo jagrāha jīvakākhyaḥ kumārakam ।।

jināvalokanenaiva bālakagrahaṇakṣaṇe ।
abhūccitānalastasya haricandanaśītalaḥ ।।

jīvantaṃ jvalanānmuktaṃ ruciram vīkṣya dārakam ।
vailakṣyeṇa kṣapaṇakāḥ kṣaṇaṃ tasthurmṛtā iva ।।

tataḥ subhadraṃ bhagavān sarvabhūtahite rataḥ ।
babhāṣe vismayodbhāntaṃ putro ayaṃ gṛhyatāmiti ।।

sa tu dolākulamatiḥ kiṃ karomīti saṃśayāt ।
kṣapanānāṃ mukhānyeva śikṣāyai kṣaṇamaikṣata ।।

te tamūcurna bālo ayaṃ grāhyaḥ śmāśānavahnijaḥ ।
yatrāyaṃ tiṣṭhati vyaktaṃ na bhavatyeva tadgṛham ।।

iti teṣāṃ girā mūrkhaḥ sa jagrāha na taṃ yadā ।
tadā kṣitipatirbālamādade jinaśāsanāt ।।

jyotirmadhyādavāptasya jyotiṣkasadṛśatviṣaḥ ।
jyotiṣka iti nāmāsya cakāra bhagavān svayam ।।

tasya pravardhamānasya bhūpālabahvane śiśoḥ ।
deśāntaragataḥ kāle mātulaḥ samupāyayau ।।

sa viditvā svasurvṛttaṃ nidhanaṃ putrajanmani ।
kopāt subhadramabhyetya kampamānaḥ samabhyaghāt ।।

mūrkha kṣapaṇabhaktena tadgirā hatayoṣitā ।
tvayā tyaktasvaputreṇa kiṃ nāma sukṛtā kṛtam ।।

niścetanāḥ svabhāvena paramantrasamutthitāḥ ।
sahanto api vinighnanti vetālā iva durjanāḥ ।।

adhunaiva na gṛhṇāsi yadi rājagṝhāt sutam ।
tatte strīvadhamuddhuṣya kārayāmyarthanigraham ।।

ityuktastena tadbhītyā sa bhūpatigṛhāt sutam ।
ānināya cirānmuktamakāmena mahībhujā ।।

tataḥ subhadre kālena kālasya vaśamāgate ।
abhūnnirdirvibhūtīnāṃ jyotiṣko arka iva tviṣām ।।

arthikalpadrumaḥ prāya saṃpadaṃ divyamānuṣīm ।
sa buddhadharmasaṃgheṣu śaraṇyeṣvakaronmatim ।।

tadbhaktyupanataṃ divyaratnasaṃcayamadbhutam ।
pradadau bhikṣusaṃghebhyaḥ puṇyaratnārjanodyataḥ ।।

tasya devanikāyebhyaḥ sāścaryā vividharddhayaḥ ।
svayamevāyayurveśma mahodadhimivāpagāḥ ।।

tṛṇe ratne ca samadhīrbhavagānapi tadgṛhe ।
cakre tadanurodhena ratnapātraparigraham ।।

sa divyavastrayugalaṃ yaśasāmupamākṣamam ।
prāpa puṇyapaṇakrītaṃ nijaṃ gṛhamivāmalam ।।

kadācidatha tadvastraṃsnānārdraṃ nyastamātape ।
samīraṇenāpahṛtaṃ nyapatanmūrdhi bhūpateḥ ।।

vilokyāpūrvaruciram jyotiṣkasya tadaṃśukam ।
vidyaśrīvismito rājā tṛṇaṃ mene nijaśriyam ।।

bhoktuṃ nimantritaḥ prāpya tasya ratnamayaṃ gṛham ।
nṛpatiḥ svargamajñāsīt jyotiṣkabhavanasthitaḥ ।।

atha kālena bhūpālaḥ putreṇājātaśatruṇā ।
chadmanā rājyalubdhena dharmaśīlo nipātitaḥ ।।

atīte sadguṇe rājñi tasmin kṛtayugopame ।
adharma iva sa prāpa rājyaṃ rājavarātmajaḥ ।।

sa bhūbhṛddurlabhāṃ dṛṣṭvā jyotiṣkasya gṛhe śriyam ।
tamuvāca samabhyetya matpitrā tvaṃ vivardhitaḥ ।।

bhrātā tavāhaṃ dharmeṇa vibhavārdhaṃ prayaccha me ।
na cedbhāgadhandrohāt kalireva prajāyate ।।

ityuktastena kauṭilyāt jyotiṣkaḥ krūrakāriṇā ।
ratnapūrṇaṃ gṛhaṃ tasmai datvā prāyāt paraṃ gṛham ।।

sā divyaratnarucirasphītā lokopakāriṇī ।
hyotiṣkamevānuyayau śrīḥ prabheva divākaram ।।

punastyaktāpi sā saṃpat saptakṛtvaḥ prabhāvatī ।
jyotiṣkamaspṛṣṭanṛpā sādhvī parimivāyayau ।।

sarvasvāharaṇodyuktaṃ dasyucaurādiyuktibhiḥ ।
jyotiṣkaḥ kupitaṃ jñātvā nirviṇṇaḥ samacintayat ।।

apuṇyaparipākeṇa prajānāṃ janakopamaḥ ।
saṃyātaḥ smṛtiśeṣatvaṃ rājā vātsalyapeśalaḥ ।।

ko anyastatsadṛśo yasmin nirvyājasarale prajāḥ ।
pitarīva kṛtāśvāsāḥ sukhaṃ rātriṣu śerate ।।

dhaninastṛṇavatprāpyāḥ prāpyante ratnavadbudhāḥ ।
amṛtādapi duṣprāpyaḥ saujanyasaralo janah ।।

nirvyājavaidagdhyajuṣāmamugdhasaralātmanām ।
anuddhatonnatānāṃ ca viralaṃ janma tādṛśām ।।

adhunā dveṣadurvṛttaḥ pravṛttanikṛtirnṛpaḥ ।
pāpapākena lokānāmakāle kalirāgataḥ ।।

mitre jagati yāte astaṃ tasmin bhāsvati bhūpatau ।
doṣodayaḥ pravṛddho ayamandhakārāya tatsutaḥ ।।

nūnaṃ satāmatītānāṃ niṣkāraṇasuhṛt khalaḥ ।
yadvṛttaparabhāgeṇa yaśasteṣāṃ prakāśate ।।

tasmādiyaṃ parityājyā nṛpatyadhiṣṭhitā mahī ।
kāle k alau kṣitīśe ca janānāṃ jīvitaṃ kutaḥ ।।

varaparicayodārā dārāh satāṃ guṇinām guṇāḥ
kulamavikalaṃ bhavyā bhūtiryaśaḥ śaśisaṃnibham ।
sthitisamucitaṃ vṛttaṃ vittamanimittamanāpadaṃ
guṇavati nṛpe sarvaṃ bhavatyapāṃśulaṃ prajākulam ।।

dharmadrumasya dhanamūlasamudgatasya nirdoṣakāmakusumapravarojjvalasya ।
lokaḥ sukhāni kila puṇyaphalāni bhuṅkte hato na cet kunṛpatervinipātavātaiḥ ।।

kaliḥ kālaḥ patirbālastatpratāpaścitānalah ।
akālaviplavottālakhalavetālasaṃkulaḥ ।।

prītirviṣaṇṇā khinnā dhīḥ sukhaśrīrgatayauvanā ।
adhunā vibhavābhoge bhogayoge na me ruciḥ ।।

dhanaṃ bhūmirgṛhaḥ dārāḥ sutā bhṛtyāḥ paricchadāḥ ।
aho niravadhiḥ puṃsāmādhivyādhiparigrahaḥ ।।

yathā yathā vivardhante grīṣmoṣmaviṣamāḥ śriyaḥ ।
tathā tathā jvalatyeva tṛṣṇātāpaḥ śarīriṇām ।।

pravṛddhairapi vittaughe rājanyopārjitairnṛṇām ।
lavaṇābdheriva jalairvitṛṣṇā naiva jāyate ।।

nāsti nāstītyasaṃtoṣād ya eva dhanināṃ japaḥ ।
pubarbhave bhavet ko vā sa eva praśamo yadi ।।

kiṃ vittairdurnimittaiḥ kalikalahamohalobhānuvṛttaiḥ kiṃ bhogairviprayogairvyasanaśatapatanābhyāsasaṃsaktarogaiḥ ।
kiṃ vā mithyābhimānairnarapatisadanaprātasevāvamānaiḥ
asmin vairāgyameva kṣayasamayabhaye bhogyamārogyayogyam ।।

atikrānte kāle svajanasuhṛdālokavimale
samāpanne mohaprabala kāluṣyamaline ।
sukhāśvāsah puṃsāṃ praśamasalilasnātamanasāṃ
parityaktāyāse vijanavanavāse parivayaḥ ।।

iti saṃcintya sa ciraṃ paraṃ vairāgyamāyayau ।
duḥkhaṃ mohāya mūrkhāṇāṃ vivekāya ca dhīmatām ।।

sa datvā sarvamarthibhyaḥ prayayauḥ sugatāśramam ।
śrīśṛṅkhalākṛṣṭamatirna hi satyasukhonmukhaḥ ।।

yadaiva rājhaṃsena smaryate śuci mānasam ।
tadaivāsmai vasumatī sarasīva na rocate ।।

yāte duḥsahamohadhūmamaline bhogānurāgānale
saṃtoṣāmṛtanirjhareṇa manasi prāte śanaiḥ śītatām ।
naitāḥ pānamadottaraṅgavicaladvārāṅgarāṅganābhaṅgura-
bhrūbhaṅgakṣaṇasaṃgamāḥ śamavatāṃ kurvanti vighnaṃ śriyaḥ ।।

sarvajñaśāsanavinaṣṭabhavādhvakaṣṭaḥ pravrajyayā vimalameva padaṃ praviṣṭaḥ ।
saṃprāpya sarvasamatāmasamaprakāśaḥ nirlakṣyamokṣagamanāya munirbabhūva ।।

tām bodhisiddhimālokya jyotiṣkasya savismayaiḥ ।
bhikṣubhirbhagavān pṛṣṭaḥ prāgvṛttāntamabhāṣataḥ ।।

janmakṣetraśatoptānāṃ bījānāmiva karmaṇām ।
bhujyate phalasaṃpattiravisaṃvādinī janaiḥ ।।

rājño bandhumataḥ puryāṃ bandhumatyām mahāyaśāḥ ।
abhūdanaṅgano nāma śrīmān gṛhapatiḥ purā ।।

śāstātha samyaksaṃbyddho viaśvī nāma tā purīm ।
janacārikayā prātaḥ kadācit sukṛtaiḥ satām ।।

dvāṣaṣṭibhiḥ sa bhikṣūṇāṃ sahasaiḥ parivāritaḥ ।
śraddhayānaṅganenaitya praṇamyopanimantritaḥ ।।

sarvopakaraṇaistena traimāsaṃ paricāritaḥ ।
yathā tathaiva rājñāpi praṇipatya nimantritaḥ ।।

bhogaiḥ spardhānubandhena sa tābhyāmadhivāsitaḥ ।
anaṅganena paurārhairbhūpālārhaiśca bhūbhujā ।।

gajadhvajamaṇicchatracāmarodārayā śriyā ।
taṃ dṛṣṭvā pūjitaṃ rājña cintārto abhūdanaṅganaḥ ।।

tasya sattvāvadātasya pakṣapātī śatakratuḥ ।
cakāra divyayā lakṣmyā sāhāyyāṃ jinapūjane ।।

sa tayā divyayā bhūtyā bhagavantamapūjayat ।
yadagre cakravartidhrīrlajjābhājanatām yayau ।।

ratnairnyakṣatacandrasūryabhānarākaṃkīraṇairāvaṇabhair 
amlānāmbaragandhamālyaśabalaiḥ kampadrumāṇāṃ phalaiḥ ।
bhaktiprahvaścīvilāsacanāhelocchasaccāmaraṃ
tenābhyarcitamākalayya sugataṃ lajjānato abhūnnṛpaḥ ।।

iti bahutaraṃ bhaktyā śāstuḥ phalaṃ tadanaṅganaḥ
śubhapariṇateḥ puṇyodāraḥ purā samavāptavān ।
vimalamanasastasyaivāsau kṣaṇapraṇidhānataḥ para
iva ravijyotiṣko abhūt sa eva padāśritaḥ ।।

ityāha vimalajñānaprakāśitagatrtrayaḥ ।
praṇīdhānopadeśāya bhikṣūṇāṃ bhagavān jinaḥ ।।

iti kṣemendraviracitāyām bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ jyotiṣkāvadānaṃ nāma navamaḥ pallavaḥ ।।

sundarīnandāvadānam ।

te ke api sattvahitasaṃnihitānukampā bhavyā bahvanti bhuvane bahvabhītibhājām ।
vātsalyapeśaladhiyaḥ kuśalāya puṃsāṃ kurvanti ye varamanugrahamāgraheṇa ।।

nyagrodhārāmanirataṃ druṣṭuṃ kapilavastuni ।
bhagavantaṃ yayau nandaḥ śākyarājasutaḥ purā ।।

naiṣkamyadeśanāmantrakathāntesa puraḥsthitam ।
uvāca bhagavān prītyā pravrajyā gṛhyatāmiti ।।

prasādyābhinivedyāsya taṃ nandaḥ pratyabhāṣataḥ ।
bhagavan puṇyalābhāpi pravrajyābhimatā na me ।।

sarvopasthāyako bhūtvā bhikṣusaṃghaṃ yathepsitaiḥ ।
sarvopakaraṇaistāvat bhikṣyaṃ paricarāmyaham ।।

ityuktvā ratnamukuṭaiḥ spṛṣṭatatpādapaṅkajaḥ ।
rājaputraḥ svabhavanaṃ yayau jāyāsamutsukaḥ ।।

sa sundarī samāsādya dayitām ratisundarīm ।
vijahāra varodyānaṃ muhūrtavirahāsahaḥ ।।

tataḥ kadācid bhagavān prakṛtyaiva guṇipriyaḥ ।
svayaṃ nandasya bhavanaṃ bhikṣusaṃghaiḥ sahāyayau ।।

sānandavadanaḥ kṛtvā nandastatpādavandanāṃ ।
taṃ mahāharsanāsīnaṃ pūjayitvā vyajijñapat ।।

keṣāṃ puṇyaprarohāṇāṃ paripāko ayamīdṛśaḥ ।
kṛto ayaṃ yadbhagavatā darśanānugrahaḥ svayam ।।

smaraṇaṃ śravaṇaṃ vāpi darśanaṃ vā mahātmanām ।
seyaṃ kuśalavallīnāṃ mahatī phalasaṃtatiḥ ।।

asya maitrasya mahatastadālokasya darśanāt ।
hṛdayasya vikāsaśrīḥ kasya nāma na jāyate ।।

dānādapi priyataraṃ puṇyādapi mahāphalam ।
sadācārādapi śrlāghyaṃ mahatāṃ kilaṃ darśanam ।।

iti tasya bruvāṇasya bhaktipraṇayapeśalam ।
abhinandya puraḥ pūjāṃ bhagavān gantumudyayau ।।

anuvavrāja taṃ nandaḥ svacche kanakabhājane ।
varopacāramādāya madhuraṃ svamivāśayam ।।

pahcādvrajantamālokya bhaktyā bhagavataḥ pathi ।
niraikṣata kaṭākṣeṇa sundarī virahāsahā ।।

gurūṇāmagre sā saralataralāṃ locanagatiṃ
vihāyaiva trāsāñcitamukutitākṣī priyatamā ।
nirīkṣyālakṣyaṃ yat kṣaṇamavanatābhūttadadhikaṃ
na gantavyaṃ nāthetyavadadivaṃ maonādavacanam ।।

nandaḥ praṇayiṇīṃ dṛṣṭvā socchvāsaṃ calitānanām ।
ayamāgata evāhamacirādityabhāṣata ।।

tataḥ svamāśramaṃ prāptaṃ bhagavantaṃ kṛtāñjaliḥ ।
vrajāmi svagṛhaṃ tāvadityāha virahāsahaḥ ।।

tatastamāsanāsīnaḥ praṇataṃ bhagavān puraḥ ।
uvāca sasmitaṃ keyaṃ gamane saṃprati tvarā ।।

viṣayāsvādasauhārdasaṃmohārditavetasām ।
aho gṛhasukheṣveva nirvedavimukhā matiḥ ।।

guṇābharaṇamevāyurvivekābharaṇo guṇaḥ ।
praśamābahraṇaścāsau vairāgyābharaṇaḥ śamaḥ ।।

tajjāḍyaṃ tadasahyaśalyaśalakaṃ nyastaṃ suhṛccetasi
prājñistadgaṇitaṃ virācasamayairvaiphalyamevāyuṣaḥ ।
yadvairāgyavivekaśūnyamanasāmete paśūnāṃ yathā
yāntyāyānti ca cakranemicalanairnirlakṣaṇānāṃ kṣaṇāḥ ।।

puṇyaṃ sattvavatām śrutaṃ matimatām śīlaṃ ca vidyāvatām
sarvaṃ bhāgyavatām sukhaṃ śamavatāṃ naiva kkacit durlabham ।
duṣprāpastu samastavastuvasateḥ svalpāṃśako apyāyuṣaḥ
tadyasya kṣayameti niṣphalatayā śocyāya tasmai namaḥ ।।

vāmāvarte viṣayajaladhau pūrṇalāvaṇyasāre darpotsarpadviṣamamakarāṅkodbhavakṣobhyamāṇe ।
nityāsannaprabalavirajaprajjvaladvāḍavāgnau
puṃsāṃ setustaraṇaśaraṇe tīvravairāgyameva ।।

tasmādgṛhāṇa pravrajyāṃ rājaputra jitendriyaḥ ।
etāḥ striya iva kṣipraṃ samagamasukhāḥ śriyaḥ ।।

kriyatām kuśalāyaiva brahmacaryaparigrahaḥ ।
tyajyatāmeṣa niḥsāragṛhasaṃsāradurgrahaḥ ।।

iti śrutvā bhagavataḥ karuṇābahraṇaṃ vacaḥ ।
pratyabhāṣata taṃ nandaḥ pūrvapraṇayayantritaḥ ।।

sadā bhavadupāyaiva pravrajyā bhagavan mama ।
bhikṣusaṃghopakārārthe gṛha evādaraḥ param ।।

ityuktvā bhagavadvākyamatikrāntumanīśvaraḥ ।
kṛṣyamāṇaḥ priyāpremṇā so abhūddolākulāśayaḥ ।।

punaḥ punaścakārāsya bhagavān vratadeśanām ।
upakārodyatāḥ santaścintayanti na yogyatām ।।

yadā necchati nandastām pravrajyāmajitendriyaḥ ।
tadāsya bahgavadvākyamapatadvapuṣi svayam ।।

nandaḥ kāṣāyāvaraṇaḥ pātrapāṇiḥ sa tatkṣaṇam ।
babhau cābhīkararucirmahāpuruṣalakṣaṇaiḥ ।।

sa śāsanājjinasyābhūdāraṇyapiṇḍapātrikah ।
ākārādanagāratām prayātaḥ pāṃśukūlikaḥ ।।

priyāmuvāha satataṃ śyāmāṃ pravrajito api saḥ ।
śaśāṅka iva saṃvyaktāṃ hṛdaye lāñchanacchavim ।।

manasaḥ sphaṭikasyeva na vidmaḥ kena vartmanā ।
rāgaḥ ko api viśatyantarnāpaiti kṣālito api yaḥ ।।

virahāpāṇḍuraruciḥ saṃsaktāruṇacīvaraḥ ।
sa saṃdhyābhrakalaṅkasya jahāra śaśinaḥ śriyam ।।

vicaran virahākṣamaḥ sa vismṝtadhṛtirvane ।
janmavidyāmanaṅgasya na visasmāra sundarīm ।।

saṃpūrṇacandravadanāvadanadhyānaniścalaḥ ।
acintyacciraṃ tattadupaviṣya śilātale ।।

aho bhagavatāpyeṣa kṛto yatnādanugrahaḥ ।
nāyāti mama vaimalyaṃ rāgādhiṣṭhitacetasaḥ ।।

śrutaṃ saṃsāracaritaṃ niḥsaṅgavratamāsthitam ।
tathāpi mṛgasāvākṣīṃ na vismarati me manaḥ ।।

kāntākuṅkumalagnarāgasubhage gātre kṛtaṃ cīvaraṃ
tatpīnastanamaṇḍalapraṇayinā pātraṃ dhṛtaṃ pāṇinā ।
rāgo ayaṃ mama vardhate asya yadi vānyasyeva vṛddhiḥ paraṃ yadbodhivyavadhānabhūtamaniśaṃ dhyānaṃ tadālambanam ।।

kṣaṇena māṃ prāptamavehi mugdhe tāmevamuktvā gamane purastāt ।
aho mayā darśanavighnabhūtaṃ paścāt kṛtaghnavratametadāttam ।।

no gantavyamiti prakampataralā vākyaṃ yadūce na sā
saṃtyajya vyajanaṃ sthite gurujane jagrāha pāṇyañcalam ।
yatpādena likhantyapi kṣititalaṃ māmaukṣatālakṣitā
tenātyantaniṣedhamugdhavidhinā baddhaṃ tayā me manaḥ ।।

madviyuktā na sā nūnaṃ śete śokapralāpinī ।
puline cakravākīva harmye hariṇyalocanā ।।

hā priye taktasaktena kitaveneva kevalam ।
śritaṃ taccittacaureṇa mithyāvratamidaṃ mayā ।।

tyaktvā vratamidaṃ tāvad gacchām idayitāntikam ।
anurāgāgnitaptānāṃ tapastāpo hi duḥsahaḥ ।।

rājaputrī cirāyātaṃ nṛśaṃsamavalokya mām ।
manyunā navalagnena na jāne kiṃ kariṣyati ।।

na sarvatra vikārāya nikāraḥ premaduḥsahaḥ ।
durnivāro bhavatyeva snehalīno rajaḥkaṇaḥ ।।

yasmin kṣaṇe bhagavatā paśyāmi rahitaṃ vanam ।
mayā tadaiva gantavyaṃ gṝhamityeṣa niścayaḥ ।।

asminneva śilāpaṭṭe rucirairgiridhātubhiḥ ।
likhāmi tām śaśimukhīṃ saṃrpāpyālambanaṃ dhṛteḥ ।।

athavā kathamālekhyaviṣayaṃ yāti sā priyā ।
saundaryabidnako yasyāḥ sudhākuvalayendavaḥ ।।

dṛṣṭirmugdhakurangasaṃcaladalivyāptotpalodvātanī
lāvaṇyodadhikūlavidrumavanaṃ bimbādharāgratviṣaḥ ।
nirdoṣāmṛtaraśmisārthasaraṇiḥ sā kāpi vaktradyutiḥ
saundaryaṃ kathameti citrapadavīścaryasāraṃ vapuḥ ।।

iti saṃcintya sa śanairālilekha śilātale ।
sundarīṃ mukhamuktāśrusnātakampākulāṅguliḥ ।।

sa saṃkalpasamudgīrṇaṃ pratibimbamivāśritām ।
kṛtvā puraḥ priyatamāmūce adarbāṣpagadgadaḥ ।।

priyāmālikhyāhaṃ nikhilasukhavṛṣṭiṃ nayanayor
na paśyāmyudbāṣpaḥ kṣaṇamapi śaraccandravadanām ।
ayaṃ nūnaṃ tanvīvirahanirapekṣavratavataḥ
sphurattāpaḥ śāpaḥ kimapi mama pāpādupanataḥ ।।

phullāmbhojavanatviṣā spṛhāvaśāsaktāśrutoyaṃ vapus
tatkālopagatāntarāyajanitaḥ kopaḥ samutsṛjyatām ।
haṃho sundari dehi me prativacaḥ kiṃ maunamālambase
satyaṃ tvanmayarāgavīcaramidaṃ cittavrataṃ me vratam ।।

iti bruvāṇaṃ taṃ dṛṣṭvā dūrādālikhitaṃ ca tat ।
sāsūyā bhikṣavo abhyetya bhagavantaṃ babhāṣire ।।

bhagavan durvinītasya vātsalyādeva kevalam ।
śunaḥ kusumamāleva pravrajyeyaṃ tvayārpitā ।।

ākhilya sundarīmukhaṃ nandaḥ svairaṃ śilātale ।
tatpralāpajapāsakto dhyānālambanatāṃ gataḥ ।।

etadākarṇya bhagavān nandamāhvāyya kananāt ।
kimetaditi papraccha priyāvirahamohitam ।।

so abravīd bhagavan satyaṃ kāntāsaktasya me param ।
bhikṣūṇāṃ saṃmate apyasmin vane na ramate matiḥ ।।

iti dandavacaḥ śrutvā tamūce bhagavān jinah ।
mīlayanneva vaktrendukāntyā rāgasaroruham ।।

sādho tāvanna yuktā te saṃrāgānugatā matiḥ ।
vighnairnākṛṣyate cetaḥ kalyāṇābhiniveśinām ।।

kvāyaṃ yogastanutṛṇatulātyaktabhogābhiyogaḥ
kkāyaṃ nindyaḥ kṣaṇasukhalavāsvādasaṃvāda eṣaḥ ।
jātyaivāyaṃ harati kuśalaṃ dustaro māramārgaḥ
premāndhānām bhavati sahasā duḥsaho yoktrajātaḥ ।।

ityasya bhagavān kṛtvā ciraṃ vairāgyadeśanām ।
saṃsthātavyamihetyuktvā svakṛtyāya svayaṃ yayau ।।

tamevāvasaraṃ nandaḥ saṃcintya gamanocitam ।
pratasthe svagṛhaṃ hṛṣṭaḥ sundarīdarśanotsukaḥ ।।

vrajan dvāri pidhānāptairvihārairbahubhiścirāt ।
nagarābhimukhaṃ mārgaṃ sa kathaṃcidavāptavān ।।

atha vijñāya sarvajñastaṃ rāgād gantumudyatam ।
uvācābhyetya bhagavān nanda tūrṇaṃ kka gamyate ।।

sa jagāda vane tāvat bhagavan nāsti me ratiḥ ।
na hyaviśrāntacittānāṃ kriyā kācit prasīdati ।।

sā śrīścāmarahāsinī maṇimayī sā ramyaharmyāvalī
sā bālānilalolacārulatikā kāntā navodyānabhūḥ ।
sā tanvī kusumeṣukārmukalatā kṣāmodarī sundarī
no janmāntaravāsanā iva manaḥ saktaṃ vimuñcanti me ।।

sarāgeṇaiva manasā brahacaryaṃ carāmyaham ।
vratapañjarabandhena vihaṅga iva yantritaḥ ।।

tyaktvā vrajāmi pravrajyāmastu me narako akṣayaḥ ।
na vītarāgatāmeti mañjiṣṭhāraktamaṃśukam ।।

iti bruvāṇamasakṛt svapadaṃ gantumudyatam ।
nivāryānugrahadhiyā tamūce bhagavān jinaḥ ।।

mā kṛthā viplavaṃ nanda ninditaṃ hi śrutāśrutam ।
vidvajjanopadiṣṭena yathā yāti pṛthagjanaḥ ।।

vivekavyastadoṣāṇāṃ viduṣāṃ śīlaśālinām ।
niḥsārasukhalābhena nākārye dhīḥ pravartate ।।

gāḍharāgagṛhītasya jugupsāyatane param ।
jadhanyakarmaṇyāsaktiḥ kiṃ lajjājanane na te ।।

yonijayonisaṃsaktāḥ stanapastanamardinaḥ ।
aho bata na lajjante janmanyeva layaṃ gatāḥ ।।

sadāsajjanavarjitā jananījaghanāsaktiḥ ।
saṃmohāhatacittānāṃ paśūnāmeva dṛśyate ।।

rāmāramaṇamāno ayaṃ viramya tyajyatāṃ tvayā ।
bhogaiḥ saha bhujaṅgānāṃ dṛṣṭo bhavabile kṣayaḥ ।।

jaghanyā janayatyeva na kasya viratiṃ ratiḥ ।
yasyāṃ bhavati paryanteṣvapi naiva parāṅmukhaḥ ।।

gṛhajālavimuktastvaṃ kiṃ tatraivābhidhāvasi ।
na hi nirgasya sāraṅgaḥ punarviśati vāgurāṃ ।।

iti vākyād bhagavataḥ śāsanena niyantritaḥ ।
cintayan sundarīṃ nandaḥ praviveśāśramaṃ punaḥ ।।

tataḥ kadācidādiśya nanda māśramamārjane ।
āsanānugrahavyagraḥ prayayau bhagavān punah ।।

tacchāsanāt pravṛttasya nandasyāśramaśodhane ।
no bhūtalādapayayau rajo rāga ivāśayat ।।

tasyāhartuṃ gatasyātha salilaṃpārabhāgikam ।
muhuḥ pūrṇasamutkṣiptah śūnya evābhavaddhaṭaḥ ।।

tena vighnena gamane sutarām khinnamānasaḥ ।
tyaktvā tuprayayau nandaḥ sundarīdarśanotsukaḥ ।।

atha vijñāya sarvajñastaṃ yāntaṃ divyacakṣuṣā ।
babhāṣe sahasābhyetya stambhamānamanorathah ।।

pātrayogena taptasya śyāmaraktaruceḥ param ।
aho snehakalaṅkaste dīpasyeva na śāmyati ।।

alaṃ vāmābhilāṣeṇa nīlīrāga ivaiṣa te ।
saṃsaktaḥ ko api hṛdaye yannādyāpi virajyase ।।

andhīkaroti prārambhe ratistatkālakātaram ।
āliṅgati jugupseva vṛtte mukhyāṅgasaṃgame ।।

viṣayākhvādasaṅgena pāpamitrairivendriyaiḥ ।
duḥsahavyasanāvarte pātyate narake narah ।।

adhivāsayati sparśalekhenāpi kusaṃgamaḥ ।
praklinnamatsyakuṇapāt pūtigandha ivodgataḥ ।।

kalyāṇamitrasaṃparkaḥ sarvathā kuśalāvahaḥ ।
śubhāmeda iva vyāpto yaḥ karoti mahārhatām ।।

ityukte tasya bhagavān sākṣāts adasatoḥ pathi ।
ghrāṇasparśena saṃdarśya cakre tatsaṅgadeśanām ।।

atha nandaṃ samādāya bhagavān gandhamādane ।
yayau viriñciramarībālavyajanavījitaḥ ।।

tatra dāvānalapliṣṭāmaniṣṭakliṣṭavigrahām ।
kāṇāṃ karmaṭīkāmasmai darśayitvāvadajjinaḥ ।।

imāṃ paśyasi kiṃ nanda māndyanindyatarākṛtim ।
kasmaiciducitā ceyaṃ rocate priyadarśanā ।।

sattā sadasatornāsti rāgaḥ paśyati ramyatām ।
sa tasya lalito loke yo yasya dayito janaḥ ।।

pakṣapātaṃ samṛtsṛjya satyaṃ nanda tvayocyatām ।
asyāstasyāśca sundaryā lāvaṇyasya kimantaram ।।

anarthitvādvayaṃ naiva saundaryāntaravedinaḥ ।
arthipriyatvamāyāti prārthitaṃ tacca cārutām ।।

paśyāmyahaṃ viśeṣaṃ tu tasyā nāsyāśca kaṃcana ।
ramyatvaṃ māṃsavarmāsthiyantre samayamātrakam ।।

iti pṛṣṭo bahgavatā nandastaṃ pratyabhāsata ।
atyantānucitaḥ praśnaḥ ko api gauravayantritaḥ ।।

kimetad bhagavān vakti keyaṃ śoke biḍambanā ।
kkāpi vā viśvaguravo vineyāḥ prabhaviṣṇavah ।।

ratiḥ sādhikasundaryāḥ parabhāgeṇa rajyate ।
yāṃ dṛṣṭvā jagatāṃ jetā na ratiṃ smarati smaraḥ ।।

jyotsnayeva na tatkāntyā nodate kumudākaraḥ ।
guṇāntaraṃ na jānāti prasiddhiśaraṇo janaḥ ।।

baddhaṃ tayā vadanasaurabhasārahāramālokya puṣyanicayaṃ pṛthukeśapāśe ।
manye vilāsagatilovanakānticauraiḥ bhītyeva haṃsahariṇairvanamiva yātam ।।

analpaiḥ saṃkalpairbahuvidhavikalpairanupamā
na sā sāraṅgākṣīlikhitumapi śakyā paricitaiḥ ।
tulārohe ysyā vadanaparabhāge laghutaraḥ
sa nūnaṃ tārāṇāṃ gaganamadhirūḍhaḥ parivṛḍhaḥ ।।

puṇyaprahvaṃ lalitalalitabhrūlatālāsyalīlā
ramyaṃ tasyā yadi na vadanaṃ nandanaṃ labhyate tat ।
pravrajyeyaṃ sukṛtamadhikaṃ kiṃkarī kiṃkarī me
kasmādetaṃ vrataparikaraṃ bhārabhūtaṃ vahāmi ।।

iti nandavacaḥ śrutvā bhagavān rāganirbharam ।
upakṣipya prabhāveta ta nināya surālayam ।।

adarśayacca tatrāsya līlodyāne śatakratoḥ ।
sudhāmanthasamudbhūtāḥ kāntāstridaśayoṣitaḥ ।।

aruṇaiḥ kāntisaṃtānaiḥ pādapadmavanoditaiḥ ।
anuyātā ivāmbhodhikūlavidrumakānanaiḥ ।।

viśālalāsyasacivaiḥ pāṇibhirvijitāmbujaiḥ ।
saṃsaktaiḥ sahajasyeva pārijātasya pallavaiḥ ।।

kāntimādhuryalalitairmadanānandabāṇdhavaiḥ ।
helānimīlitāmbhojavadanaiścandrasundaraiḥ ।।

saṃmohanairjīvanaiśca kṛṣṇasārairvilokanaiḥ ।
kālakūṭacchadaspṛṣṭairamṛtoghairivāvṛtāḥ ।।

pūrṇayauvanalāvaṇyāḥ sahasaiva vilokya tāḥ ।
nandaḥ sānandavadanaḥ svedasnāta ivābhavat ।।

padmānanāsu vipulotpalalocanāsu kundastimātu nibiḍastabakastanīṣu ।
nandasya tāsu hṛdayaṃ yugapannipatya dolāvilāsataralālitumavāpa ।।

tataḥ provāca bahgavān nandaṃ tadgatamānasam ।
āsāṃ saṃdarśane nanda prītyā te ramate matiḥ ।।

āsāṃ tasyāśca sundaryā lāvaṇye kiyadantaram ।
utkarṣaḥ parabhāgeṇa sphuṭamevābhibhāvyate ।।

nirastasundarīrūpaṃ rūpamapsarasām yadi ।
tadetā eva kālena kariṣyāmi tvadāśrayāḥ ।।

ārogeṇaiva manasā brahmacaryaṃ prasannadhīḥ ।
cara tāvattataste ahaṃ dāsyāmyapsarasām gaṇam ।।

evaṃ bhagavato vākyānnandaḥ saṃjātaniścayaḥ ।
tathetyuktvā vrate cetaścakre svargāṅganāśayā ।।

mandādaraḥ svadāreṣu so abhūt tatsaṃgamecchayā ।
guṇapṇyatulāvṛtternāsti snehasya satyatā ।।

aho cismṛtasaṃvāsapravāsapariśoṣitā ।
puṃsāmābhyāsikī prītiḥ sahasānyatra dhāvati ।।

kṣaṇayauvanaramyāṇi premāṇi praṇayavyayaiḥ ।
na satyāni na nityāni na sukhāni śarīriṇām ।।

tato bhagavatā nandaḥ kṣaṇānītaḥ svamāśramam ।
tanniścayād brahmacaryaṃ cacāra niyatavrataḥ ।।

sa cisasmāra sundaryāḥ kāntisaṃpadamanyadhīḥ ।
kṣaṇapramuṣitā prītirmalaṃ yāti guṇeṣvapi ।।

tataḥ kadācidvicaran nandaḥ kkāpi vyalokayat ।
karālanarakāsaktāṃ dhīmān kumbhībhṛtāṃ bhuvam ।।

tām vilokyaiva sākampaḥ kimetaditi duḥkhitaḥ ।
sa papraccha tadāsaktān ghoranarakakāraṇam ।।

te tamūcuriyaṃ bhūmistaptakumbhīśatācitā ।
kalpitā rājaputrasya nandasyānandarāgiṇaḥ ।।

mithyāvrataḥ sa nādyāpi bhajate vītarāgatām ।
brahamcaryaṃ caratyeva svargastrūīsaṃgamāśayā ।।

mithyāvratānām lubdhānāṃ rāgadveṣakaṣāyiṇām ।
etāsu nityataptāsu kumbhīṣvevākṣayaḥ kṣayaḥ ।।

iti nanda samākarṇya jātaromāñcakañcukah ।
tatra cyutāmiva tanūṃ paścāttāpādamanyataḥ ।।

samamyetya tyaktarāgasaṃvāsavāsanah svayam ।
babhūvānuttarabrahmacaryaparyāptāṃyamaḥ ।।

ghanamohakṣayāttasya vimukte saṃśaye tataḥ ।
mahaḥ prasādamāpede śaradīvedadheḥ payaḥ ।।

niṣkāmaḥ praśamaṃ prāptaḥ parāṃ niṣṭhāmupāgataḥ ।
śuddhadhīḥ sa samabhyetya bhagavantamabhāṣata ।।

nāpsarobhirna sundaryā bhagavan kṛtyamasti me ।
etāḥ paryantavicchāyāḥ sapātā viṣayaśriyaḥ ।।

yathā yatheyaṃ bhāvānāṃ bhāvyate niḥsvabhāvatā ।
tathā tathā prqsīdanti nirāvaraṇavṛttayaḥ ।।

iti dandasya vadataḥ prāptasyārtapadaṃ śanaiḥ ।
bhagavān nirvāṇaśuddhāmasya siddhimamanyata ।।

keṣāṃ kuśalamūlānāṃ nandenāsāditaṃ phalam ।
iti bhikṣubhirabhyetya pṛṣṭhastānavadajjinaḥ ।।

janmāntarārjitaiḥ puṇyaiḥ sukṛtābhyāsakāriṇā ।
prāptāḥ kuśalamūlānāṃ nandena phalasaṃpadaḥ ।।

vipulavimala vaṃśe janma smarapratimā tanuḥ
surajanasakhī lakṣī vṛttiḥ priyāḥ satataṃ satām ।
praśamasalilasnātaṃ cetaḥ svabhāvagatirgatiḥ
kuśalakusumasyeyaṃ puṃsāṃ viśālaphalodgatiḥ ।।

stūpe vipaśyinaḥ samyaksaṃbuddhasyādaraḥ purā ।
nagaryāmaruṇāvatyāmaruṇena mahībhūhā ।।

kriyamāṇo maṇimaye maitro nāma dvijanmajaḥ ।
mahataḥ puṇyabhogasya bhāgī kārakatām yayau ।।

tatpuṇyapraṇidhānena jāto gṝhapateḥ kule ।
sa eva bhikṣusaṃghasya jantukāsnānasatrakṛt ।।

sa puṇyaśīlaḥ pratyekabuddhopasthāyakah purā ।
stūpaṃ cakre śobhamānaṃ mālabhivaraṇojjvalam ।।

tatpuṇyapraṇidhānena kṛkeḥ kāśīpateḥ sutaḥ ।
so abhvaddyutimān nāma divyalakṣaṇalakṣitaḥ ।।

kāśyapasyārhataḥ samyaksaṃbuddasyāntanirvṛtau ।
saptaratnamaye stūpe kṛte kāśīmahībhujā ।।

tatsūnurdhyutimān haumacchatramāropya bhāsvaram ।
jātastatpraṇidhānena nandaḥ śākyamuke adhunā ।।

iti sukṛtasamutthaiḥ pūrvajanvakramāptaiḥ kimapi vipulapuṇyaireva nandaḥ prapede ।
kulamamalamudāraṃ rūmamagryaṃ ca bhogaṃ śamaparicitamante satpadaṃ saugataṃ ca ।।

kathayotveti bhagavān nandakalyāṇakāraṇam ।
cakāra bhikṣusaṃghasya tāṃ tāṃ sukṛtadeśanām ।।

iti kṣemendraviracitāyām bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ sundarīnandāvadānaṃ nāma daśamaḥ pallavaḥ ।।

virūḍhakāvadānam ।

ārohati padamunnatamamalamatirvimalakuśalasopānaiḥ ।
narakakuhareṣu nipatati malinamatirghoratimireṣu ।।

śākyānāṃ nagare pūrvaṃ sphīte kapilavāstuni ।
mahataḥ śākyamukhyasya sumukhī dāsakanyākā ।।

śāstre kṛtaśramā sarvakalākauśalaśālinī ।
mālikā nāma kāmasya mālikeva guṇocitā ।।

prabhorgirā varodyāne kusumāvacayodyatā ।
bhramantaṃ taṃ samāyāntaṃ dadarśa sugataṃ puraḥ ।।

tasyānte asyāstamālokya prasannamabhavanmanaḥ ।
śaratkāla iva svacchaḥ prasādayati mānasam ।।

sācintayattadā lokaprītyā dṛḍhīkṛtāspadā ।
sukṛtaiḥ piṇḍapātaṃ me gṛhṇīyādbhagavānapi ।।

vijñāya tasyāh sarvajñaḥ saṃkalpaṃ karuṇākulaḥ ।
prasārya pātraṃ bhagavān bhadre dehītyuvāca tām ।।

datvā praṇamya sā tasmai paripūrṇamanorathā ।
praṇidhānaṃ pravidadhe dāsyaduḥkhanivṛttaye ।।

tataḥ kadācidāyātaḥ pituastasyāḥ sakhā dvijaḥ ।
naumittikastaṃ pradeśaṃ dṛṣṭvā tām vismito ava dat ।।

aho gṛhapatestasya putrī tvaṃ śrīmatah sutā ।
bandhuhīnā gatā dāsyaṃ dhanabhogavivarjitā ।।

aho mohaghanārambhakṣaṇoddyotanavidyutaḥ ।
saṃsārasarparasanāvilāsacapalāḥ śriyaḥ ।।

gamyānāṃ mā kṛthāścintāṃ jāne ahaṃ hastalakṣaṇaiḥ ।
acireṇaiva bhūbharturvallabhā tvaṃ bhaviṣyasi ।।

idaṃ paśyāmi te pāṇau lakṣmīkamalakomale ।
mālācakrāṅkuśākāramityuktvā prayayau dvijaḥ ।।

atha manmathasaṃbhogasuhṛnmadhupabāndhavaḥ ।
latāliṅganasaubhāgyabhavyo adṛśyata mādhavaḥ ।।

madhoḥ kesariṇastasya kāntāmānadvipadviṣaḥ ।
vibabhau jihmamānasya jihvevāśokamañjarī ।।

bālākapolalāvaṇyacauraścampakasaṃcayaḥ ।
sudṛśāṃ keśapāśeṣu yayau bandhanayogyatām ।।

sahakārairvirahiṇīnidhanaṃ vidadhe madhu ।
nirapekṣāparavadhe vidhurāḥ prabhaviṣṇavaḥ ।।

yayurmadhulihāṃ cūtalatā nirbharabhogyatām ।
sahasauva vidgadhānāmiva mugdhavibhūtayaḥ ।।

rūtāyudhaścūtalatācāpanyastaśilīmukhaḥ ।
jayatīti jagau bandī kandarpasyeva kokilaḥ ।।

asminnavasare śrīmān kosalendraḥ prasenajit ।
mṛgayānirgato aśvena hṛtastaṃ deśamāyayau ।।

dhanvīmanobhavākāraḥ so avatīrya turaṃgamāt ।
dadarśānanyalāvaṇyām kanyāṃ ratimivāparām ।।

tadvilokanavistīrṇaṃ manastasya mahātmanaḥ ।
vismayāddṛṣṭimārgeṇa praviveśa manobhavaḥ ।।

tāṃ lajjāvanatāṃ dṛṣṭvā sahasodbhūītasādhvasām ।
acintayannarapatiḥ kāntikallilinīhṛtaḥ ।।

keyaṃ navā śaśimukhī śyāmā taralatārakā ।
yatkāntiraniśaṃ netraśatapatravikāśinī ।।

bakulāmodavibhrāntabhramare pāṭalādhare ।
kāntaṃ vasantaṃ paśyāmi mukhe asyāḥ kumudāyudham ।।

aho lāvaṇyamamlānaṃ tāruṇyābharaṇaṃ tanoḥ ।
dhīrasyāpi dhṛtiryena śaṅkhe saṃgaliteva me ।।

aho nu madhumañjaryāḥ prārambhe apyadbhuto guṇaḥ ।
yena gantuṃ na śaknoti ṣaṭpado api padātpadam ।।

iti saṃcintya bhīpālastāṃ matvā vanadevatām ।
pṛṣṭvā viveda tadvṛttaṃ krameṇa kathitaṃ tayā ।।

tatastatra kṛtātithyastayā pallavavījanaiḥ ।
śuciśītaiśca salilaiḥ prāptavān nirvṛtiṃ nṛpaḥ ।।

śrāntaḥ saṃvāhane tasya tayā caraṇapadmayoḥ ।
kṛte karāptasaṃsparśe sa nidrām sahasā yayau ।।

kṣaṇena pratibyddho atha viśrāntamṛgayāśramaḥ ।
divyasparśena tām mene ratiṃ rūpāntarāgatām ।।

mahānapi tataḥ śākyaḥ saṃprāptaṃ kosaleśvaram ।
śrutvā taṃ deśamabhyetya pūjārhaṃ tamapūjayat ।।

sādareṇārthitāṃ tena svasutāmiva mālikām ।
ratnārhāya dadau tasmai smaramaṅgalamālikām ।।

tāmādāya manojanmavaijayantīṃ sitasmitām ।
nijaṃ jagāma nagaraṃ gajamāruhya bhūpatiḥ ।।

tasminnāganagotsaṅge sā lolālakaṣaṭpadā ।
babhau rājavasantena saṃgatā navamālikā ।।

rājadhānīṃ samāsādya sundaryā sahitastayā ।
ratnaharmyakarodāramandire vijahāra saḥ ।।

varṣākārābhidhā devī rājñaḥ prathamavallabhā ।
abhinnavṛttiṃ tām mene rājalakṣmīmiva kṣitiḥ ।।

divyasparśena sā tasyāḥ sā cāsyā rūpasaṃpadā ।
parasparaguṇotkarṣātparaṃ vismayamāpatuḥ ।।

divyarūpavatī jyeṣṭhā divyasparśavatī par ā ।
iti pravādaḥ sāścaryastayuorlokeṣu paprathe ।।

atrāntare tayordivyarūpasaṃsparśakāraṇam ।
āśrame bhikṣubhiḥ pṛṣṭaḥ provāca bhagavān jinaḥ ।।

purā śrutavarākhyasya dvijasya gṛhamedhinaḥ ।
kāntā śirīṣikā ceti priye bhārye babhūvatuḥ ।।

sa kadācidatho kāntābhrātā pravrajyayā śanaiḥ ।
pratyekabuddhatāṃ yātaḥ svasurbhavanamāyayau ।।

traimāsikopacāreṇa sa tayā patyurājñayā ।
bhaktyā nimantritastasthau tatsaptnyāvapūjitaḥ ।।

te cārumṛdubhirbhogaistamabhyarcyānyajanmani ।
jāte adhunā cārurūpadivyasaṃsparśasaṃyute ।।

kṛṣṭeṣu prathamaṃ prayuktavinayāmādāya gosaṃpadaṃ
satkṣetreṣu tapaḥ pratatptanuṣu prāptiṣvatisvādutām ।
yatkāle śubhabījamuptamucitaṃ satkarmaśakteḥ paraṃ
bhujyante phalasaṃpadaḥ sumatibhistasyaiva pākojjvalāḥ ।।

iti sarvajñavacanam tathyamākarṇya bhikṣavaḥ ।
tattatheti viniścitya babhūvuḥ śāntisaṃśrayāḥ ।।

atha kālena bhūbharturmālikāyāmabhūtsutaḥ ।
virūḍhaketimukhyākhyo vidyāsu ca kṛtaśramah ।।

priyastulyavayāstasya purohitasuto abhavat ।
māturduḥkhena jātatvādviśruto duḥkhamātṛkaḥ ।।

kadācit sahitastena hayārūḍho virūḍhakah ।
prāpa śākyavarodyānaṃ mṝgayāyām vinirgataḥ ।।

nyakkāraṃ cakrire tatra śākyāstasyodyatāyudhāḥ ।
ayaṃ dāsīsuto asmākamiti darpapravādinah ।।

gatvāsau svapuraṃ teṣāṃ vairaṃ darpyamacintayat ।
kuladarpāpavādo hi śalyatodaḥ śarīriṇām ।।

tasya nirdahyamānasya tatpratīkāracintayā ।
rājyāya jātā janake jīvatyapi parā spṛhā ।।

sa cārāyaṇamukhyānāṃ mantriṇāṃ śatapañcakam ।
svavaśaṃ piturākṛṣya vidadhe bhedayuktibhiḥ ।।

tataḥ kadācitsaṃjātavivekaḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ ।
dharmopadeśaśravaṇe vardhamānādaraḥ param ।।

cārātyaṇagṛhītāśvaṃ rathamāruhya saṃyataḥ ।
draṣṭuṃ jagāma sarvajñaṃ bhagavantam prasenajit ।।

prāyāśramaṃ bhagavataḥ kṛtvā pādābhivandanam ।
dharmānvayam sa śuśrāva tatprasādaprasannadhīḥ ।।

cārāyaṇo apyāśu gatvā rathena nagaraṃ javāt ।
akarodantare tasmin rājaputrābhiṣecanam ।।

bhagavantamathāmantrya nṛpatirgantumudyataḥ ।
dadarśa nānugānagre na rathaṃ na ca mantriṇam ।।

sa padbhyāmeva śanakaiḥ prasthitām pṛthivīpatiḥ ।
dūrādapaśyadāyāntīṃ varṣākārāṃ samālikām ।।

te pṛṣṭvā tadgirā jñātvā so abhiṣiktaṃ virūḍhakam ।
visasarja sutaiśvaryaparibhogāya mālokām ।।

varṣākārāṃ samādāya sa mitrasya mahīpateḥ ।
ajātaśatrornagaraṃ prāta rājagṛhābhidham ।।

sa tatptaśchatravirahāt kṣuptipāsāśramānvitaḥ ।
yayau vamanniva śvāsaṃ dīrgheśvāramamārutaiḥ ।।

sukhamaskhalitaṃ kena prāptaṃ kasyāyurāyatam ।
na kasyānupadaṃ dṛṣṭaḥ kṣayaḥ sapadi saṃpadaḥ ।।

sa jīrṇamūlakaṃ bhuktvā karmamūlamivāyatam ।
kṣaṇaṃ pītvā ca pānīyaṃ papātāptaviṣūcikaḥ ।।

anityatāmavijñāya mohāya patate janah ।
sa cāpāyanikāyasya kāyasyopāyatṛṣṇayā ।।

ajātaśatruḥ śrutvaiva kosaleśvaramāgatam ।
abhyetya pāṃśupūrṇāsyaṃ vigatāsuṃ dadarśa tam ।।

tasya jāyānuyātasya sa kṛtvā dehasatkriyām ।
bhagavantaṃ yayau druṣṭuṃ sugataṃ duḥkhaśāntaye ।।

sa taṃ praṇamya provāca bhagavan kosaleśvaraḥ ।
puraṃ me suhṝdaḥ prāya nirdhano nidhanaṃ gataḥ ।।

dhiṅbhāmasaṃpadaṃ pāpaṃ mihādayaśasaḥ padam ।
vibhavo yena naivāyaṃ mitropakaraṇīkṛtaḥ ।।

hṛdaye viniveśyāśāṃ prāptaḥ suhṝdamāpadi ।
suhṛnnaiṣphalyamāyāti yasya kiṃ tena jīvatā ।।

mitropakaraṇaṃ lakṣmīrdīnopakaraṇam dhanam ।
bhītopakaraṇaṃ prāṇā yeṣāṃ teṣāṃ sujīvitam ।।

kukarma kiṃ kṛtaṃ tena bhagavan ūrvajanmani ।
yasya pākena paryante prapede so atidurdaśām ।।

iti pṛṣṭaḥ kṣitīśena bhagavān sāśrucakṣuṣā ।
tamūce tāpaśamanīṃ diśan daśanacandrikām ।।

mā śucaḥ pṛthivīpāla svabhāvo ayaṃ bhavasthitaḥ ।
evaṃvidhaiva bhāvānāmasatyānāmanityatā ।।

visārisaṃsāravanāntare asmin nisargalolaḥ kila kāmabhṛṅgaḥ ।
svacchandajātajanapuṣkarajīvapuñjakiñjalkapuñjamaniśaṃ kavalīkaroti ।।

taraṅganto bhogāścakitahariṇīlocanacalāḥ kṣaṇe alakṣyā lakṣmīrjanajaladavidyotanataḍit ।
śarīrābje bālātapacapalarāgaṃ navavayaḥ kṣayaṃ yāti kṣipraṃ bhavamarūtaṭe jīvitakaṇaḥ ।।

mano maitrīpātraṃ parahitaratirdharmadhanatā
madodbhedacchedakṣamaśamavicāre paricayaḥ ।
ayaṃ tatvānveṣo viṣayasukhavaimukhyasukhinām
asāre saṃsāre parihṛtavikāraḥ paribhavaḥ ।।

janah śocati duḥkheṣu kṣipraṃ hata ivāśmanā ।
na karoti punastīvratadāpātapratikriyām ।।

paśyato apibhavāyāsaṃ nirvivekasya sarvathā ।
kriyate kiṃ janasyāsya mohādakuśalaspṛśaḥ ।।

purā vipraḥ suśarmākhyaḥ kutaścitprāpya mūlakam ।
nidhāya jananīhaste yayau snātuṃ nadītaṭam ।।

sāpi pratyekabuddhāya tām pāptāya tadantare ।
praṇatā pātrahastāya tadevābhimūkhī dadau ।।

atha snātvā samāyātastatsutastvaritaṃ kṣudhā ।
jananīṃ bhojanārambhe yayāce nijamūlakam ।।

puṇyaṃ putrānumodasva tanmayātithaye arpitam ।
iti māturvacaḥ śrutvāso abhūdviddha iveṣuṇā ।।

sadyo viṣūcikārtasya manmūlakamanalpakam ।
kukṣiṃ bhittvā viniryātu prāṇaiḥ saha ta vātitheḥ ।।

iti tasyāptapāpasya vākyāruṣyeṇa bhūyasā ।
visūcikaiva paryante babhūvaparajanmani ।।

prākpuṇyāntarapākena sa evādya prasenajit ।
vipulaṃ rājyamāsādya tayaivānte kṣayaṃ gataḥ ।।

saṃsārapathapānthānāmevaṃ karma śubhāśubham ।
pātheyamiva hastastham bhogāyaivopapadyate ।।

iti śrutvā bhagavatastathyaṃ pathyaṃ ca tadvacaḥ ।
evametaditi dhyātvā taṃ praṇamya yayau nṛpaḥ ।।

atrāntare prāptarājyaḥ śākyavairaṃ virūḍhakaḥ ।
purohitasutenaitya smāritastatkṣayodyataḥ ।।

prayayau śākyanagaraṃ gajāśvarathareṇunā ।
moheneva diśāṃ kurvan nirvivekaṃ dhiyāmiva ।।

sarvajño bhagavān jñātvā tasya tadduṣṭaceṣṭitam ।
gatvā śākyapuropānte tasthau śuṣkataroradhah ।।

dūrāttatra sthitaṃ dṛṣṭvā tamāgacchan virūḍhakaḥ ।
avatīrya rathādagramabhyetya praṇato avadat ।।

satsu snigdhapalāśeṣu ghanacchāyeṣu śākhiṣu ।
bhagavannatra viśrāntiḥ kimu śuṣkataroradhaḥ ।।

ityuktaḥ kṣitipālena taṃ prāha bhagavān jinaḥ ।
jñāticchāyā narapateḥ candanādapi śītalā ।।

nāsti jñātisamaṃ vittaṃ nāsti jñātisamā dhṛtiḥ ।
nāsti jñātisamā chāyā nāsti jñātisamah priyaḥ ।।

mamaite bhūpate śākyā jñātayasyatpurāntike ।
jātaḥ priyo ayaṃ tatprītyā śuṣkaśākho api pādapaḥ ।।

śrutvaitadviratāmarṣaḥ śākyānāṃ pakṣapātinam ।
bhagavantaṃ viditvaiva nyavartataḥ virūḍhakaḥ ।।

bhagavānapi śākyānāṃ jñātvāgāmi bhayaṃ tataḥ ।
śreyase śuddhasattvānām vidadhe dharmadeśanām ।।

śrotāpattiphalaṃ kaiścit sakṛdāgāmi cāparaiḥ ।
anāgāmiphalaṃ cānyaiḥ saṃprāptaṃ tasya śāsanāt ।।

śeṣāstu mūḍhamatayaḥ śākyāḥ prāpurna tatpadam ।
santi ke api khagā yeṣām vāsare timiro adbhavaḥ ।।

nivṛttasyātha nṛpateḥ purohitasutastataḥ ।
vairasarpasya suptasya vidadhe pratibodhanam ।।

sa tena preritaścakre matiṃ śākyakulakṣaye ।
vairānalaṃ pracalanaṃ karoti piśunānilaḥ ।।

ghoradurjanamantreṇa sahasotthāpitāḥ khalāḥ ।
vetālā kṣitipālāśca na kasya prāṇahāriṇah ।।

sainye gajarathodagre tatastasmin prasarpati ।
babhūva purasaṃkṣobhaḥ śākyānāṃ rūddhavartmanām ।।

tasmin bhagavān rakṣārthaṃ śākyānāṃ pakṣapātinam ।
samudyataṃ tatra mahāmaudgalyāyanamabravīt ।।

śākyānāṃ karmadoṣo ayaṃ sarvathā samupasthitaḥ ।
tatra rakṣavidhānaṃ te gagane setubandhanam ।।

puṃsamavintyavibhavāni śubhāśubhāni āyānti yānti ca muhurniravagrahāṇi ।
karmākṣarāṇi nijajanmapadasvahastanyastāni nāma na bhavanti nirarthakāni ।।

iti vākyādbhagavatastasmin yāte praṇamya tam ।
cakrire saṃvidaṃ śākyāh pratyāsanne virūḍhake ।।

hiṃsāsmābhirna kartavyā prāṇimātrasya kasyacit ।
śarāḥ śarīramasmākaṃ viśantvarisamīritāḥ ।।

iti saṃvidamādhāya te viyaṣṭikapāṇayaḥ ।
dhīrḥ parodyame tasthuravārayitakārmukāḥ ।।

atrāntare karmayogānnijadeśānavasthitaḥ ।
ajñātvā saṃvidaṃ śākyaḥ śaṃpākah samupāyayau ।।

sa dṛṣṭvā nagare baddhasaṃnāhaṃ vasudhādhipam ।
kopādekaścakārāsya raṇe subhaṭasaṃkṣayam ।।

yuddhe puruṣasiṃhena hatāste vīrakuñjarāḥ ।
prayayuḥ spṛhaṇīyatvaṃ yaśobhirmaktikairiva ।।

sa ko api tasya jajvāla kopitasya parairasiḥ ।
sa yayau yatpratāpena vipulāṃ ripuvāhinīm ।।

praveśaṃ na daduḥ śākyāḥ śaṃpākasya dviṣāṃ vadhāt ।
svajano api parityaktaḥ sa tairnistriṃśakarmaṇā ।।

nije api vimukhāḥ krūre sādhave dahrambandhavaḥ ।
dhānādapi vadānyatvaṃ sukṛtaṃ svajanādapi ।।

।
śatamaucityanityānāmāyuṣo api yaśaḥ priyam ।।

nirvāsitaḥ sa taiḥ prāptaḥ śanairbhagavato antikam ।
yayāce abhyudayāyāiva taṃ kiṃcinnijalāñchanam ।।

ṛddhaṃ bhagavatā dattaṃ nijakeśanakhāṃśakam ।
sa jagāma samādāya vākuḍaṃ nāma maṇḍalam ।।

tatra prajñāprabhāveṇa śauryotsāhaguṇena ca ।
sa prāpa rājyaṃ dhīrāṇāṃ sarvatra sulabhāḥ śriyaḥ ।।

dakṣāṇāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ lakṣmīḥ sahajaṃ viduṣāṃ yaśaḥ ।
vyavasāyasahāyānām kalatraṃ sarvasiddhayaḥ ।।

tatra sthito bhagavataḥ so atha keśanakhāṃśake ।
stūpapratiṣṭhāmakarodvarratnavirājitām ।।

virūḍhako api śākyānāṃ vairapāratitīrṣayā ।
punaryuktyā puradvhārabhedena sahasāviśat ।।

hatvā tatra sahasrāṇi śākyānāṃ saptasaptati ।
baddhvā kanyākumārāṇāṃ sa sahasramathāharat ।।

śatāni pañca śākyānām gajairlohaiśca mardanaiḥ ।
saṃpramṛjya purīṃ cakre kṛtāntanagarīmiva ।।

bhagavānapi śākyānām śatrūṇā bhedanaṃ kṛtam ।
karmānubaddhaṃ vijñāyaṃ babhūva vimanāḥ kṣaṇam ।।

papracchustaṃ samabhyetya bhikṣavaḥ karuṇākulāḥ ।
kiṃ karma vihitaṃ śākyairghoraṃ yasyedṛśaṃ phalam ।।

bhagavānaniti taiḥ pṛṣṭaḥ sarvajñastānabhāṣata ।
nijakarmavipākena śākyānāmeṣa saṃkṣayaḥ ।।

kṛṣṭau purā mahāmatsyau dhīvaraiḥ sarito antarāt ।
tadā nikṛttau śalyena bhūyo apyavyathayan dhṛtau ।।

kālena cārutām yātaistaireva parajanmani ।
hatau gṝhapatī dagdhvā tāveva dhanahāribhiḥ ।।

tau matsyau tau gṛhasthau ca virūḍhakapurohitau ।
dāsānāṃ taskarāṇām ca śākyānām mṛtyutām gatau ।।

iti śrutvā bhagavataḥ karmaṇāṃ phalasaṃtatim ।
avisaṃvādinīmeva menire sarvabhikṣavaḥ ।।

virūḍhako atha svapuraṃ prāpya vijayadurmadaḥ ।
jetānāmnā sutenoktaḥ praṇayādbālalīlayā ।।

deva kiṃ nihatāḥ śākyān na te asmākaṃ kṛtāgasaḥ ।
iti bruvāṇamavadhīnnijasūnuṃ virūḍhakaḥ ।।

nipātamatimṛdgati nihanti na karoti kim ।
madalabdhanadhāyāso mātaṃga iva darjanaḥ ।।

sa jagāda sabhāsīnaḥ svabhūjāvavalokayan ।
aho nu mama tāpāgnau dvisadbhiḥ śalabhāyitam ।।

kṛtāntatoraṇastambhau prājyau mama bhujāvimau ।
niṣḥśeṣavadhadīkṣāyāṃ śākyānāṃ gurutāṃ gatau ।।

taṃ tasya vikramaṃ ślāghyaṃ hṛtāstāḥ śākyakanyakāḥ ।
śrutvā babhāṣire tīvramudveganamitānanāḥ ।।

karmapāśanibaddhānāṃ khagānāmiva dehinām ।
nidhanollaṅghane śaktirnāsti pakṣavatāmapi ।।

yenāgniḥ śamameti tatkila jalaṃ prāpnotyalaṃ vāḍavaḥ
tigmāṃśugrahaṇaṃ karoti samaye helāvalehyaṃ tamah ।
paryālocanavartmanāmaviṣayaṃ sāścaryacaryāspadaṃ
sarvaṃ kārmikatantrayantimidaṃ kaḥ kasya kartuṃ kṣamaḥ ।।

etadākarṇya nṛpatiḥ padāntara iveragaḥ ।
karacchedaṃ dideśāsāṃ ghorāmarṣaviṣotkaṭaḥ ।।

tīre yasyāḥ kṛtaṃ tāsāṃ pāṇicchedanavaiśasam ।
sādyāpi hastagabhati khyātā puṣkariṇī bhuvi ।।

latāsvapi hkukūlāgniṃ krakacaṃ nalīnīṣvapi ।
mālāsvapi śilāvarṣaṃ pātayantyeva nirghṛṇāḥ ।।

tāśchinnapāṇikamalāstatra tīvravyathāturāḥ ।
bhagavantaṃ dhiyā dhyātvā śaraṇaṃ śaraṇaṃ yayuḥ ।।

tāsāṃ vijñāya sarvajñastīvrām marmāhativyathām ।
śacīmacintayaddevīṃ tatsamāśvāsanocitām ।।

tatsparśajātahastābjāstā divyavasanāvṛtāḥ ।
yayuścittaprasādena tāh svargaṃ tyaktavigrahā ।।

devakalpāstamāsādya divyapadmotpalāṅkitāḥ ।
dharmadeśanayā śāstustāh prāpurvipulaṃ padam ।।

bhikṣubhirbhagavān pṛṣṭastatkarmaphalamabhyadhāt ।
pāṇicāpalyametābhiḥ kṛtaṃ bhikṣuviḍambane ।।

karmaṇastasya pākena viśase patitāh param ।
mayi cittaprasādena prāptāścaitāh śubhāṃ gatim ।।

ityuktvā bhagavān karmaphalapākavicitratām ।
bhukṣīṇāṃ tatprasaṅgena vidadhe dharmadeśanām ।।

atrāntare gūḍhacārī rājñā praṇihitaścaraḥ ।
bhagavaccaritaṃ jñātvā virūḍhakamupāyayau ।।

so avadaddeva bhikṣūṇāṃ tenedaṃ kathitaṃ puraḥ ।
svakarmaphalamāsannaṃ tasya paśyāmi bhūpateh ।।

saptāhenāgninā dagdhaḥ sa pāpātmā purohitaḥ ।
avīcināmni narake duḥsahe nipatiṣyati ।।

iti tadvacanaṃ śrutvā nṛpatiḥ sapurohitaḥ ।
yatnāduvāsa saptāhaṃ jalānvitagṛhāntare ।।

kṣaṇāvaśeṣe saptāhe tasminnantaḥpuraṃ gate ।
sūryakāntārkasaṃtāpayogājjajvāla pāvakaḥ ।।

udbhūtena pralayasavanāvartinevāśu vegān
nirdagdho asau dhagiti śikhinā nārakaṃ prāpa vahnim ।
asmiṃllike jvalanajaṭilāḥ pāpināṃ pretya rāgāḥ
sarvatraiva sthirasukhabhuvaḥ śītalāḥ puṇyabhājām ।।

iti kṣemendraviracitāyām bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ virūḍhakāvadānaṃ nāma ekādaśaḥ pallavaḥ ।।

hārītikādamanāvadānam ।

duḥkhaṃ nudanti sukhasaṃpadamādiśanti saṃjīvayanti janatām timiraṃ haranti ।
sanmānasasya kalayanti vikāsahāsaṃ santaḥ sudhārdravadanāḥ śaśina karāśca ।।

bimbisāraḥ kṣiteḥ sāre pure rājagṛhābhidhe ।
sāraḥ samastabhūpānāmabhūdbhūmipuraṃdaraḥ ।।

kṣamādhāre bhuje yasya kṣamādhāre ca cetasi ।
bāhyaḥ samastacittānāmaśu nyastakaro janaḥ ।।

kurvatastyāgaśauryābhyāmāśāyāḥ paripūraṇam ।
pāṇau vimuktaratnaughe subaddho abhūdasigrahaḥ ।।

kadācidabhavattasya viplavo nagare guruḥ ।
navābhyudayasaṃjātadarpakāla ivākulaḥ ।।

tamāsthānasamāsīnaṃ janacintākṛtakṣaṇam ।
vyajijñipata saurājaṃ prajānāṃ janakopamam ।।

deva divyaprabhāvasya niyataḥ śāsanena te ।
janah sadā samudro ayaṃ maryādāṃ nātivartate ।।

yenāsya kṛtavṛttasya sanmārgeṇa prasarpataḥ ।
upasargodgamaḥ kasmādakasmādayamāgataḥ ।।

svadharmasaṃvṛttena hi karmaṇā śarmaṇā nṛṇām ।
sunṛpe na ca guhyānāmāpatanti vipattayaḥ ।।

hriyante naḥ prasūtīnāṃ gṛhiṇīnāṃgṛhe kayā ।
apatyāni phalānīva satkriyāṇāmasaṃyamāt ।।

kiṃtu bhūtānna vidmastān māyām cāpi mahīpate ।
yatprabhāveṇa nīyante kulāni nirapatyatām ।।

iti teṣāṃ girā bhūbhṛdabhūtsaṃkrāntatadvyathaḥ ।
paraṃ duḥkhaṃ viśatyantaḥ satāṃ kedāravārivat ।।

sarvāṅgavyāpinā tena janaduḥkhena bhūyasā ।
viṣeṇevāvṛtaḥ so abhūdudbhrāntahṛdayaḥ kṣaṇam ।।

so abravīt kiṃ karomyatrābhujādhīne vipaurūṣe ।
kathaṃ nāma pravartante durlakṣyeṣu pratikriyāḥ ।।

dinamekaṃ vrajantvadya bhavanto nijamāspadam ।
savrataścintayāmyeva rakṣāṃ vaḥ prasvakṣaye ।।

iti rājavacaḥ śrutvā hṛṣṭāḥ pauramahattamāḥ ।
jagadustaṃ samāvarjya pūjāvyañjanamajṇjalim ।।

deva tvadavadhānena praṇayākarṇanena ca ।
tvayi vinyastacintānāṃ nāsmākamadhunā śramaḥ ।।

anuddhatamudāraṃ c atvatprasādāvalokanam ।
idameva janasyāsya jīvitānīva varṣati ।।

kiṃ punaḥ priyametatte pīyūṣasadṛśaṃ vacaḥ ।
tāpāpahaṃ mṛhu svādu kiṃ kiṃ na vidadhāti naḥ ।।

kṛtī kṛtajñaḥ kāruṇyanidhiḥ sulabhadarśanaḥ ।
labhyate bhāgyabhogyena saujanyasaralaḥ prabhu ।।

pīyūṣādatipeśalaḥ paricayaḥ śrāvyaṃ vacaḥ pañcamam
ācāraḥ śaradinduvṛndamahaso asyānandasaṃdohadaḥ ।
saccitte vasatāṃ satām kimaparaṃ puṣpānmanah komalaṃ
saujanyaṃ haricandanādapi paraṃ saṃtāpanirvāpaṇam ।।

ityuktvā prayayuḥ paurāstaṃ praṇamya prasādinam ।
kirantastadguṇodārāmāśākusumamālikām ।।

rājāpi nagare kṛtvā bhūtapūjāvidhikramam ।
śāntisvastikasaṃbhāraṃ cakāra niyatavrataḥ ।।

yakṣī hārītikā nāma bālakān puravāsinī ।
haratīti sa śuśrāva puradevatayoditam ।।

tataḥ paurajanaiḥ sārdhaṃ sāmātyaḥ pṛthīvīpatiḥ ।
kalandakanivāsākhye sthitaṃ veṇuvanāśrame ।।

bhagavantaṃ yayau draṣṭuṃ sugataṃ doṣaśāntaye ।
sarvaduḥkhajvarāyāsajuṣāmakaṭukauṣadham ।।

taṃ dṛṣṭvā nṛpatirdūrātpraṇamya priyadarśanam ।
upaviśyāgratastasmai pauraduḥkhaṃ nyavedayat ।।

bhagavānapi vijñāya paurāṇāṃ saṃtatikṣayam ।
cintāniścañcalaḥ kṣipramuvāca karuṇānidhiḥ ।।

sa visṛjya jagadbandhuḥ sanṛpaṃ pauramaṇḍalam ।
pātracīvaramādāya yayau yakṣīniketanam ।।

tayā virahitaṃ prāpya tadgṛhaṃ bhagavān jinaḥ ।
priyaṃkarākhyaṃ tatputraṃ nināyaikamadarśanam ।।

yāte bhagavati kṣipraṃ yakṣī svagṛhamāgatā ।
prabhūtaputrā nāpaśyat priyaṃ putraṃ priyaṃkaram ।।

tamīkṣamāṇāṃ vivaśā hṛtavatseva dhenukā ।
babhrāma saṃbhramodbhrāntā sā janeṣu cā ।।

hā priyaṃkara hā putra kka nu paśyāmi te mukham ।
iti pralāpinī tāraṃ niḥśeṣāḥ sā yayau diśaḥ ।।

sā vicityāśu sarvāśā nirāśā putradarśane ।
krośantī parvatadvīpaṃ samudravalayam yayau ।।

martyabhūmimatikramya ghoreṣu nagareṣu sā ।
svargoddeśeṣva śeṣeṣu vimānodyānaśāliṣu ।।

śrāntā kkacinna viśrāntā yakṣiṇī praṇighātinī ।
putramanviṣya nāpaśyallokapālapureṣu ca ।।

kuberasyātha vacasā gatvā ca sugatāśramam ।
bhagavantaṃ viyogārtā śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇaṃ yayau ।।

tayā tadduḥkhavṛttāntaṃ sam niśamya niveditam ।
tāmavocata śocantīṃ kiṃcit smitasitādharaḥ ।।

hārīti tava putrāṇāṃ santi pañcaśatānyaho ।
iti tenoktamākarṇya yakṣī duḥkhakṣatāvadat ।।

putralakṣe api bhagavan sahyā naikasutakṣatiḥ ।
putrāt priyataraṃ nānyatkiṃ duḥkhaṃ tatkṣayātparam ।।

putravāneva jānāti putrasnehaviṣavyathām ।
sahajaiva sutaprītirakāraṇanibandhanā ।।

।
malino vikalaḥ kṣīṇaḥ kasya nendusamaḥ sutaḥ ।।

iti yakṣavadhūvākyaṃ śrutvā vātsalyavihvalam ।
bhūtānukampī bhagavān sasmitastāmabhāṣata ।।

śoko ayaṃ bahyputrāyā yadyekavirahe tava ।
hṛte tvayaikavatsānāṃ putraike kīdṛśī vyathā ।।

tvaṃ praviśya sadā gehaṃ strīṇāṃ putramalakṣitāṃ ।
aśnāsi putramātāpi vyāghrīva mṛgaśāvakān ।।

yena yena svadehasya duḥkhaṃ yātyupabhogatām ।
na tatparasya kurvīta samāno anubhavaḥ śucām ।।

tvaṃ buddhadharmasaṃghānāṃ trīṇi śikṣāpadāni cet ।
gṛhṇāsi hiṃsāvimukhī tatprāpnoṣi priyaṃ sutam ।।

ityuktā sā bhagavatā prāptaśikṣāpadā tataḥ ।
hiṃsāvirāmāt taṃ gatvā putraṃ prāpa priyaṃkaram ।।

tasyāḥ prāgjanmavṛttāntaṃ tasyāḥ karmaphalānvayam ।
bhikṣubhirbhagavān pṛṣṭastadvṛttāntamabhāṣataḥ ।।

purāsminneva nagare paurāh ke apyupabhoginaḥ ।
parvatodyānamālāyāṃ vijahrurnartanādinā ।।

atha tena pathā kāpi gopakāntā ghanastanī ।
mathitaṃ paṇyamādāya hariṇākṣī samāyayau ।।

garbhabhārālasagatiḥ pratyuptā gajagāminī ।
sā śanairupasarpantī saspṛhaṃ tān vyalokayat ।।

tasyā vanamṛgīmugdhairavadagdhā vilokanaiḥ ।
asaṃvṛttā vilāsārdraiste api sotkaṇṭhatāṃ yayuḥ ।।

sā tairnimantritā tatra madanakṣībatām gatā ।
hāritaṃ sahasā śīlaṃ na viveda pramādinī ।।

tatasteṣū prayāteṣu tadā tasyā ratiśramāt ।
papāta saha dhairyeṇa garbhaū kopādivāruṇaḥ ।।

atrāntare samāyātaṃ tatpuṇyaistena vartamanā ।
pratyekabuddhaṃ sādrākṣītkāyacittaprasādanam ।।

sāsmai mathitamūlyāptamāmrāṇāṃ śatapañcakam ।
dūrātpraṇāmavinatā manasaiva nyavedat ।।

tataḥ puṇyarddhimatyasmin jātā yakṣakule adhunā ।
jātamāmrārpaṇenāsyāḥ putrāṇāṃ śatapañcakam ।।

hiṃsāvatī pāpatyāgāt śīlavismaraṇātparam ।
pratyekabuddhapraṇateḥ prāptaśikṣāpadādya sā ।।

iti vividhavipākaṃ karmatantraṃ vicitraṃ kimapisa kathayitvā tatra yakṣāṅganāyāḥ ।
kalitakuśalasetuḥ saṃbhavābdhau janānāmakṛta sukṛtacittaṃ sarvalokasya śāstā ।।

iti kṣemendraviracitāyām bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ hārītikādamanāvadānaṃ nāma dvādaśaḥ pallavaḥ ।।

pratihāryāvadānam ।।

yaḥ saṃkalpapathā sadaiva carati projjṛmbhamāṇādbhutaṃ
svapnairyasya na saṃgatiḥ paricayo yasminnapūrvakramaḥ ।
vāṇī maunavatī ca yatra hi nṛṇāṃ yaḥ śrotranetrātithis
taṃ nirvyājajanaprabhāvavibhavaṃ manaurameyaṃ numaḥ ।।

pure rājagṛhābhikhye bimbirāseṇa bhūbhujā ।
pūjyamānaṃ jina dṛṣṭvā sthitaṃ veṇuvanāśrame ।।

mātsaryaviṣasaṃtaptā mūrkhāḥ sarvjñamāninaḥ ।
na sehire tadutkarṣaṃ prakāśamiva kauśikāḥ ।।

malinaiḥ svavināśāya parabhāgoditaiḥ sadā ।
kriyate vāsaraspardhā śārvaraistimirotkaraiḥ ।।

maskarī saṃjayī vairairajitaḥ kakudastathā ।
pūraṇajñātiputrādyā mūrkhāḥ kṣapaṇakāḥ pare ।।

ūcurnṛpatimabhyetya māramāyāvimohitāḥ ।
saṃgharṣadveṣadoṣeṇa dhūmenevāndhakāritāḥ ।।

eṣa sarvajñatāmānī vane yaḥ śramaṇaḥ sthitaḥ ।
ṛddhiprabhāvo bhavatā tasyāsmākaṃ ca dṛśyatām ।।

ṛddhiprabhāvādyatkiṃcit janavyāvarjanorjitam ।
drśyate mahadāścaryaṃ prātihāryaṃ taducyate ।।

śaktiḥ saṃsadi yasyāsti pratihāryasya darśane ।
asmākaṃ tasya vā rājan pūjāḥ santu jagatrtraye ।।

iti teṣām vacaḥ śrutvā taddarpavimukho nṛpaḥ ।
uvāca vāñchā keyaṃ vaḥ paṅgūnāṃ girilaṅghane ।।

asamañjasamevaitat kā spardhāgneḥ pataṅgakaiḥ ।
naitadvācyaṃ punarvādī mayā niṣkāsyate purāt ।।

iti rājñā guṇajñena pratyākhyātodyamāḥ khalāḥ ।
prayayuste nirālambe lambamānā ivāmbare ।।

bimbisāro narapatirmūrkhatāpakṣapātavān ।
anyaṃ vrajāmo bhūpālamiti te samacintayan ।।

atrāṇtare bhagavati śrāvastīmabhitaḥ purīm ।
prāpte tejavanārāmaṃ digantāneva te yayuḥ ।।

te prasenajitaṃ tatra prāpya kosalabhūpatim ।
prātihāryakṛtaspardhāṃ tāmevāsmai nyavedayan ।।

guṇāntarajño nṛpatisteṣām darpakṣayecchayā ।
ṛddhisaṃdarśanotsāhādyayau bhagavato antikam ।।

sa samabhyetya vinayāt praṇipatya tamabravīt ।
bhagavan darpabalanaṃ tīrthyānāṃ kartumarhasi ।।

ṛddhispardhānubandhena tvatprabhāvadidṛkṣayā ।
svaguṇaślāghayāsmākaṃ taiḥ karṇau badhirīkṛtau ।।

prakāśaya nijaṃ tejaḥ sajjanāvarjanam vibho ।
tīrthyābhidhānāmakhilaṃ prayātu pralayaṃ tamaḥ ।।

iti rājavacaḥ śrutvā nirvikāro mahāśayaḥ ।
bhagavān viratāmarṣaḥ saharṣastamabhāṣataḥ ।।

rājannānyopamardāya vivādāya madāya vā ।
vivekābharaṇārho ayaṃ kriyate guṇasaṃgrahaḥ ।।

mātsaryamalinaiḥ kiṃ tairvicāraviguṇairguṇaiḥ ।
ye haranti parotkarṣaṃ spardhābandhaprasāritāḥ ।।

guṇācchādanamanyasya svaguṇena karoti yaḥ ।
dharmastenāpraśastena svayameva nighātitaḥ ।।

sadguṇānāṃ parikṣaiva paravailakṣyakāriṇī ।
ucitā na hi śuddhānāṃ tulārohaviḍambanā ।।

guṇavānapi nāyāti yaḥ pareṣu prasannatām ।
sa dīpahastastatpātracchāyayā malinīkṛtaḥ ।।

loka ta eva sarvajñā vidmaḥ kimadhikaṃ vayam ।
parābhimānābhibhavaprāgalbhyaṃ svaparābhavaḥ ।।

iti śrutvā bhagavataḥ praśamābhimataṃ vacaḥ ।
bhṛśamabhyarthanāṃ rājā cakārāścaryadarśane ।।

tataḥ dṛcchrādbhagavatā kṛtābhyupagamo nṛpaḥ ।
rājadhānīṃ yayau hṛṣṭaḥ saptāhāvadhisaṃvidā ।।

asminnavasare bhrātā bhūmibharturasodaraḥ ।
cacārāntaḥpuropānte prāsādatalavartmanā ।।

salīlaṃ vrajatastasya karmavātairiveritā ।
kusumasrak papātāṃse rājapatnīkarāccyutā ।।

tasya vijñātadoṣasya doṣaṃ saṃbhāvya sākṣibhiḥ ।
piśunāḥ kiṃvadantīṃ tām cakrire rājagāminīm ।।

chidramalpamapi prāpya kṣudrāḥ sarvāpakāriṇaḥ ।
dvijihvāḥ praviśantyāśu prabhūnāṃ śūnyamāśayam ।।

piśunapretiro rājā bhrāturīrṣyāviṣolbaṇaḥ ।
chedamasyādideśāśu pāṇipādasya mūrcchitaḥ ।।

nikṛttapāṇicaraṇaḥ kumāraḥ karmaviplavāt ।
sa vadhyavasudhāśāyī viveśa viṣamāpadam ।।

tīvravyathāparivṛtaṃ śocadbhirmātṛbandhubhiḥ ।
dadṛśustaṃ kṣapaṇakāḥ kṣaṇaṃ nayanacālane ।।

tān samabhyetya śokārtāste rājasutabāndhavāḥ ।
jagadustatparitrāṇasaṃliptāḥ sarvaprāṇinah ।।

doṣaṃ nigṛhīto ayaṃ kālanāmā nṛpātmajam ।
sarvajñavādino yūyaṃ prasādo asya vidhīyatām ।।

iti tai prasaradbāṣpairarthyamānāh pralāpibhiḥ ।
te maunino niṣpratibhā vailakṣyādanyato yayuḥ ।।

atha tena yathāyāto bhikṣuḥ sugataśāsanāt ।
ānando vidadhe aṅgāni tasya satyopayācanāt ।।

rājaputrastu saṃjātapāṇipādaḥ prasannadhīḥ ।
jinaṃ śaraṇamabhyetya tadupasthāyako abhavat ।।

saptaratre vyatīte atha śrāntihāryaṃ gṛhaṃ mahat ।
ṛddhiṃ bhagavato draṣṭuṃ mahīpatirakārayat ।।

upaviṣṭe nṛpe tatra saha kṣapaṇakādibhiḥ ।
kalpavṛkṣīkṛtā bhūmirabhavat sugatecchayā ।।

tataḥ prāpteṣu deveṣu draṣṭuṃ bhagavataḥ prabhām ।
ratnapradīpaṃ bhagavān bheje siṃhāsanam mahat ।।

tejodhātuṃ prapannasya tasya gaṇḍasamudgataiḥ ।
vyāptaṃ pāvakasaṃghātairabhūdbhuvanamaṇḍalam ।।

śānte śanaiḥ kamalakānanasaṃnikāśe vahnau samastabhuvanasthitibhaṅgabhītyā ।
dehāttato bhagavataḥ karuṇāmburāśeḥ pūrṇāmṛtormivimalā rucayaḥ prasasruḥ ।।

lāvaṇyasāramaticandrasahasrakāntiṃ tejaḥ pratānaviphalīkṛtasūryacakram ।
taṃ nāganāyakanikāyavilocanāni prītyā papuḥ sukṛtalabdhamapūrvaharṣam ।।

vaidūryanālavipulāruṇaratnapātrakāntollasatkanakakesarakarṇikāni ।
abhyudyayuḥ kṣititalādatha tatsamīpe padmāni saurabhabharāhṛtaṣaṭpadāni ।।

teṣūpaviṣṭamatha kāñcanacārukāntiṃ snigdhekṣasṇaṃ sugatacakramadṛśyatārāt ।
pīyūṣapeśalaśaśidyutiśītalena yasyodayena sahasā sukhamāpa lokaḥ ।।

teṣāṃ prabhāvavibhavaṃ bahgavān babhāra madhye adhikaṃ kanakaśaila ivācalānām ।
suskandhabandhuraghanadyutisaṃniveśaḥ prāṃśuḥ surakṣitiruhāmiva pārijātaḥ ।।

svargāṅganākarakuśeśayakīryamāṇairamlānamālyavalayaiḥ kalitottamāṅgāḥ ।
tasyānanāmbujavilokananirnimeṣe martyā api kṣaṇamavāpuramartyabhāvam ।।

vyomāṅgaṇeṣu suradundubhiśaṅkhatūryaghoṣāvṛtaḥ kusumavarṣamahāṭṭahāsaḥ ।
gandharvakinnaramunīśvaracāraṇānāṃ sphīṭaścacāra bhagavatstutivādanādaḥ ।।

tatrāruṇādharadalāddaśanāṃśuśubhrād vyākīrṇakeśarakulāddaśanāravindāt ।
satsaurabhaṃ bhagavataḥ svarasaṃnivṛttaṃ dhanyāḥ papurmadhuravāṅbhadhu puṇyasūtam ।।

pāpaṃ vimuñcata niṣiñcata puṇyabījaṃ vairaṃ parityajata sāmyasukhaṃ bhajadhvam ।
jñānāmṛtaṃ pibataṃ mṛtyuviṣāpahāri neyaṃ tanuḥ kuśalakarmasakhī cirāya ।।

lakṣmīścalā taruṇatā ca jarānuyātā kāyo apyapāyanicayasya nivāsa eva ।
prāṇāḥ śarīrakakuṭiṣu muhūrtapānthā nityodaye kuruta dharmamaye prayatnam ।।

ityādibhirbhagavataḥ pravibhaktadīptajñānairvivekavimalaiḥ kuśalopadeśaiḥ ।
vajrairivāśu dalanaṃ prayayau janānāṃ satkāyadṛṣṭisamaviṃśatiśṛṅgaśailaḥ ।।

ṛddhiprabhāṃ bhagavataḥ pravibhāvya tīrthyā mantrahatā viṣadharā iva bhagnadarpāḥ ।
dīpā ivārkakiraṇapratibhābhibhūtāścitrārpitā iva yayuściraniścalatvam ।।

atrāntare bhagavataḥ satataṃ vipakṣaḥ sarvātmanā kṣapaṇako navadharmayakṣaḥ ।
kṣiptaśravān sa vṛtavarṣavaraiścakāra vidravya randhraśaraṇān bhuvi vajrapāṇiḥ ।।

addiśya tānatha kṛpārdrabhayāśaraṇyaḥ sarvopadeśaviṣayān bhagavān babhāṣe ।
bhūbhṛdvanābanimaṇirvivarādi sarvaṃ tene bhayeṣu śaraṇaṃ kila kātarāṇām ।।

buddhiṃ prabodha mama dhāmbi nidhāya buddhiṃ
dharmaṃ sasaṃghamapi ye śaraṇaṃ prapannāḥ ।
teṣā jagatkṣayabhayeṣvapi nirbhayāṇāṃ
naivānyataḥ śaraṇadainyaparigraho asti ।।

durvāre paralokatīvratimire dharmaḥ pravṛddho aśumān
dānaṃ duḥsahapāpatāpavipadāmabhyudgame vāridaḥ ।
prajñā mohamahāprapātaviṣamaśvabhre karālambanaṃ
dainyākrāntamahīnameva śaraṇaṃ sarvatra puṇyaṃ nṛṇām ।।

iti timiravṛtākṣṇāṃ cakṣurunmīlanārhaṃ daśanamaṇimarīcivyajyamānaprakāśam ।
sadasi sugatacandraḥ śuddhadharmopadeśaṃ sthirapadamiva kṛtvā kānanaṃ svaṃ jagāma ।।

iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ prātihāryāvadānaṃ nāma trayodaśaḥ pallavaḥ ।।

devāvatāravadānam ।

jayati mahatāṃ prabhāvaḥ paścādagre ca vartamāno yaḥ ।
janakuśalakarmasaraṇiḥ prakāśaratnadīpo vaḥ ।।

purā surapure pāṇḍukambalākhye śilātale ।
samīpe pārijātasya kovidārasya suprabhe ।।

kṛtvā tridaśasaṃghānāṃ bhagavān dharmadeśanām ।
anugrahāya martyānāṃ jambūdvīpamavātarat ।।

amarairanuyātasya tasyāvatarato bhuvam ।
vimānakānanākīrṇaṃ babhūva bhuvanāṅgaṇam ।।

tasya dantāṃśusaṃtānairupadeśamivācitam ।
jagrāha candraruciram cāmaraṃ caturānanaḥ ।।

chatraṃ śataśalākāṅkamanaṅkaṃ raṅkupāṇḍuram ।
prasādamiva sākāramādade asya puraṃdaraḥ ।।

saṃkāśyanagaropānte kānanodumbarāntike ।
avatīrṇaṃ sukṛtinaḥ sānandāstaṃ vavandire ।।

tasminnutpalavarṇākhyā bhikṣukī janasaṃgame ।
alabdhāvasarā draṣṭuṃ nṛparūpamupādade ।।

pradīptaratnamukuṭaṃ gaṇḍatāṇḍavikuṇḍalam ।
dṛṣṭvaivāsya navaṃ rūpaṃ jahāsoṣṇīṣapallavaḥ ।।

sā cintayantī ko vāyaṃ janairnirvivaraḥ puraḥ ।
antaraṃ nṛparūpaṃ me dṛṣṭvā dāsyati sādaraḥ ।।

atp anyathā tu bhagavatpraṇatirmama durlabhā ।
na guṇaṃ gauravasthānamaiśvaryapraṇayī janaḥ ।।

aho tṛṇatṛlālolairniḥsāravirasairdhanaiḥ ।
hriyate vāsanābhyāsānnirvicāratayā janaḥ ।।

dattāntarā sā sahasā janena nṛpagauravāt ।
lolahāraṃ bhagavataḥ praṇāmamakārot puraḥ ।।

asminnavasare bhikṣurudayī nāma saṃsadi ।
tāṃ vilokya tathārūpāmavadat sasmitānanaḥ ।।

iyamutpalavarṇākhyā bhikṣukī nṛparūpiṇī ।
ṛddhyā bhagavataḥ pādau vandate janavanditā ।।

utpalāmodavarṇābhuāṃ vijñāteyaṃ mayā purā ।
ityuktvā virate tasmin bhagavānapyabhāṣata ।।

ayuktameva bhikṣukyā darpadṛddhiprakāśanam ।
karoti praśamaglānimabhimānena ca jvaraḥ ।।

ityuktvā bhagavān kṛtvā tāṃ tāṃ śubhropadeśanām ।
visṛjya devān prayayau svapadaṃ saha bhikṣubhiḥ ।।

tatropaviṣṭaḥ pṛṣṭastaiḥ praṇatairbhikṣukīkathām ।
prāgjanmakarmasaṃbaddhāṃ sarvajñastānabhāṣata ।।

vārāṇasyāmabhūtpūrvaṃsārthavāho mahādhanaḥ ।
patnī dhanavatī nāma tasya prāṇasamābhavat ।।

pāṇipallavinī tanvīyaovanodyānamañjarī ।
phalapuṣpavatī kāle sā tasmādgarbhamādadhe ।।

atrāntare jalanidhidvīpānugamanodyatam ।
pratyāsannaviyogārtā sā vallabhamabhāṣata ।।

kiyatī dhanasaṃpattirvṛddhimadyāpi nīyate ।
yatkṛte ghpragambhīrastīryate makarākaraḥ ।।

bahvapāyaṃ dhanādānaṃ nirapāyā guṇārjanam ।
svadeśāt paradeśaṃ hi gacchanti draviṇārthinah ।।

kecidduḥkhānnivartante dūraṃ gatvāpi niṣphalāḥ ।
niścalā dhaninaścānye karmaṇāmeṣa niścayaḥ ।।

iti priyāvacaḥ śrutvā sārthavāhastato abhyadhāt ।
mugdhe saṃbhāvanāpātro bhavatyevaṃ dhanodyataḥ ।।

dhanārjanavihīnānāṃ puṅguvanmūlabhakṣaṇāt ।
adya śvo vā sukhasthānāṃ bhogaiḥ saha parikṣayaḥ ।।

svagṛhe api daridrāṇāṃ janah krakacaniṣṭhuraḥ ।
dhanināṃ paraloko api premasnigdhajanaṃ bhuvaḥ ।।

kṣīṇamapyudyataṃ vṛddhyai na veṇuṃ bandhate janaḥ ।
na tu sa pūrṇatāṃ yāti pratyāsannaparikṣayaḥ ।।

mūrkho api viduṣāṃ vandyaḥ strīṇāṃ vṛddho api vallabhaḥ ।
klibo api sevyaḥ śūrāṇāmāsannābhyudayo janaḥ ।।

kenānyakaraṇaṃ bhuktvā pītvā kāvyāmṛtāni vā ।
kṣaṇaṃ vicakṣaṇenāpi kṣuptipāse vivarjite ।।

yasyārthaḥ sa guṇonnataiḥ kṛtanutiḥ kaṃ vā na dhatte guṇaṃ
dāridyrodayadoṣadūṣitarucāṃ nirmālyatulyā guṇāḥ ।
vittenaiva guṇā guṇī na tu dhanī dhanyo dhanī no guṇī kāyādduṣkṛtasaṃnipātaśamanādāyurguṇānāṃ dhanam ।।

iti prāṇādhikārthasya patyurākarṇya sā vacaḥ ।
sāñjanāśrukaṇotkīrṇā latevābhṛtaṣaṭpadā ।।

atha pravahaṇaṃ bheje sārthanāthastayā saha ।
tīvratṛṣṇāgṛhītānāṃ hastapātraṃ mahodadhiḥ ।।

tasya jāyāsakhasyāsau karmavātānuvartinaḥ ।
abhajyata pravahaṇaṃ samanorathajīvitam ।।

tataḥ phalakamāsādya bhāgaśeṣācca karmaṇaḥ ।
kaśerudvīpamāsādya tatpatirvipadaṃ gataḥ ।।

anāthām tatra śocantīṃ vihaṅgaḥ puruṣākṛtiḥ ।
tāmāpa pādadīrṇāśāṃ suvarṇakulasaṃbhavaḥ ।।

sa kāntāṃ sumukho nāma tāmuvāca rucākṛtaḥ ।
samāśvasihi lolākṣi nirbhayo ayaṃ tavāśrayaḥ ।।

divyeyaṃ subhagā bhūmirvayaṃ tvatpraṇayaiṣaṇaḥ ।
puṇyāyātāsi kalyāṇi ghoro ayaṃ makarākaraḥ ।।

ityuktvā tena śanakairnītā ratnālayaṃ gṛham ।
saṃpūrṇagarbhā tanayaṃ cārurūpamasūta sā ।।

vardhamāne śiśau tasmin sā śanaiḥ priyavādinā ।
mugdhā tena vidagdhena saṃbhogābhimukhīkṛtā ।।

saralatvānmṛdutvācca samīpapraṇayī janaḥ ।
svayamāliṅgyate strībhirlatābhiriva pādapaḥ ।।

divyodyāneṣu sā tena ramamāṇāṃ ghanastanī ।
kumāraṃ rucirākāraṃ suṣuve sadṛśaṃ pituḥ ।।

tasmin padmamukhābhikhye yauvanālaṃkṛtākṛtau ।
sumukhaḥ pakṣiṇāṃ rājā kāle lokāntaraṃ yayau ।।

tataḥ padmamukhaḥ śrīmānāsasāda padaṃ pituḥ ।
guṇināmavivādena svādhīnāḥ kulasaṃpadaḥ ।।

prāptaiśvaryaṃ tamavadadvijane jananī sutam ।
tatprabhāvasya saṃbhāvya sarvatra prabhaviṣṇutām ।।

putra prāptā tvayā lakṣmīriyaṃ nijakulocitā ।
ayaṃ tu sārthavāhānme jātaḥ putro niraṃśakaḥ ।।

vārāṇasyāmayaṃ rājā śaśaktyā kriyatāṃ tvayā ।
prītīsaṃvādasāsvādaḥ svadeśe seva saṃpadaḥ ।।

iti māturgirā pakṣī pakṣapātena bhūyasā ।
skandhe bhrātaramāropya vyomnā vārāṇasīṃ yayau ।।

tatra siṃhāsanāsīnaṃ brahmadattaṃ mahīpatim ।
saṃjaghānaikadainaṃ sa vajragranakharaiḥ kharaiḥ ।।

abhiṣicyāgrajaṃ pūrṇaṃ tasminneva nṛpāsane ।
amātyān so avadadbhītān samagrānagravikramaḥ ।।

yasya rājño abhiṣiktasya mayā yaḥ pracalīkaraḥ ।
so apyatītaḥ prabho bhaktyā tamevānugamiṣyati ।।

ityuktvā pravarāmātyān svairaṃ vihagapuṇgavaḥ ।
yayau bhrātaramāmantrya punardeśanasaṃvidā ।।

sa eva brahmadatto ayamiti mantrita mantriṇām ।
sa nṛpaḥ khyātimāyātaḥ svajaneṣu pareṣu ca ।।

atrāntare samānītā sagarbhā hastinī vanāt ।
na mumocārdhaniryātagarbhaṃ ruddhamivāntare ।।

sādhvīkarāgrasaṃsparśādiyaṃ garbhaṃ vimuñcati ।
iti mauhūrtikādiṣṭaṃ rājñe mantrī nyavedayat ।।

śāsanādatha bhūbhartuḥ spṛṣṭvā hastena hastinīm ।
antaḥ purāṅganāścakrustatra satyopayāvanam ।।

tāsāṃ satyagirā garbhaṃ nātyajat kariṇī yadā ।
tadā vilakṣyaḥ sarvo abhūt bhūpasyāntaḥpure janaḥ ।।

atha gopāṅganābhyetya śīlasatyopayācanam ।
kṛtvā pasparśa kariṇīṃ yenāsau garbhamatyajat ।।

kṛtvā nijajāyānāṃ jñātvā śīladaridratām ।
mene gopāṃ manaḥsveva tāṃ jagatrtritaye satīm ।।

sa satījātilobhena sośumbāṃ nāma tatsutām ।
pariṇīyānināyāgre devīśabdasya pātratām ।।

tasyāḥ saṃcintya lāvaṇyaṃ capalatvaṃ ca yoṣitām ।
sa sarvagāmīnīṃ nidrāmapi tatyāja śaṅkitaḥ ।।

asminnavasare druṣṭuṃ bhrātaraṃ vihagādhiyaḥ ।
yayau padmamukhastatra snehādatiśayotsukhaḥ ।।

bhūpālo api tamāliṅgya prītyā vihitasatkṛtiḥ ।
vijane svakathāmasmai nivedya punarabravīt ।।

śīlasatyatulārohāt dṛṣṭadoṣeṇa yoṣitām ।
mamāntaḥpuravaimukhyāt vivāho abhinavaḥ kṛtaḥ ।।

rūpayauvanagāminmyām tasyāmapi na me dhṛtiḥ ।
ekatra dṛṣṭadoṣāṇāṃ sarvatrāśaṅkate manaḥ ।।

tasmāttava pure bhrātarvimānuṣye nidhīyatām ।
śīlaśankāṃ parityajya bhavāmi vigatajvaraḥ ।।

tasmāt pratiniśaṃ pakṣī śāsanāt tava madgṛham ।
prāpayiṣyati tāṃ svairamityayaṃ me manorathaḥ ।।

iti bhrāturvacaḥ śrutvā tamuvāca vihaṅgamaḥ ।
īrṣyāśaṅkākalaṅkena rājan mithyaiva mā kṛthāḥ ।।

na nāma ramate ramye nāsvādaṃ vetti bhojane ।
na paśyati na nidrāti nityamīrṣyāvaśāturaḥ ।।

klībaḥ kāmī sukhī vidvān dhanī namraḥ prabhuḥ kṣamī ।
arthī mānyaḥ khalaḥ snigdhaḥ strī satīti kathaiva kā ।।

saralatve api kuṭilāḥ sthāyinyo apyaticañcalāḥ ।
kulīnā apui pārśvasthamāliṅgantyabalā latāḥ ।।

dṛṣṭirlolādharo rāgī bhrūrvākrā kaṭhinau stanau ।
dṛśyate naiva nirdoṣaḥ strīṇāmavayaveṣvapi ।।

bhujyante kuśalaiḥ śyāmā bhramadbhramaravibhramaiḥ ।
mūlānveṣī sarojinyāḥ paṅkenaivāvalipyata ।।

naikasmin vismayabhuvāṃ sasmitānāṃ niyantrite ।
śuciśīlavirāmāṇāṃ rāmāṇāṃ ramaṇe matiḥ ।।
tathāpi matpurodyāne nirjane sā nidhīyatām ।।
ityuktaḥ pakṣiṇā bhrātā nṛpatirvisasarja tām ।
kāntāṃ kaśerukadvīpe taṃ ca satkṛtya sādaraḥ ।।

sāpi pratiniśaṃ vyomnaḥ khagārūḍhā samāyayau ।
divyagandhamayīṃ mālāmādāya dvīpasaṃbhavām ।।

pārijātānvayatarostāni puṣpāṇyavāpa sā ।
khyātāni timirāṇīva bhramadbhṛṅgāndhakārataḥ ।।

atha vārāṇasīvāsī kadācinmānavābhudhaḥ ।
prayayau samidhāhārī dvijanmā kānanaṃ yuvā ।।

tatra kinnarakāminyā sa dṛṣṭaḥ spaṣṭamanmathaḥ ।
yasya saṃdarśanenaiva sābhavadvismṛtasmṛtiḥ ।।

asau navābhilāṣeṇa janakeneva sārpitā ।
kāntā kāntimayī nāma vijahāra guhāgṛhe ।।

tatrābharaṇaratnāśuḥ pratītatimirotkare ।
ramamāṇā ciraṃ tena kāle putramavāpa sā ।।

balavān marududbhavaḥ sa bālye api yadā śiśuḥ ।
tadā mātā tasya saṃjñāṃ śīghraga ityasādhayat ।।

sāpi nivāghnasaṃbhogā sukhātṛptā guhāntare ।
priyaṃ dhṝtvā sadā yāti pidhāya śilayā gṛham ।।

kadācidatha vṛttāntaṃ nijapitrā niveditam ।
ākarṇya śīghragaścintāvismayākulito avadat ।।

śilānibaddhadvāre asminnandhasyaiva gṝhāntare ।
aho sneho apyayaṃ tāta tava bandhanatāṃ gataḥ ।।

ehi vārāṇasīmeva gacchāvaste nijāspadam ।
vioulāmapyayatnena śilāmutsārayāmyaham ।।

svadeśavirahakleśaṃ dyḥśaṃ sahase katham ।
tyaktuṃ na śakyate kauściddeśo deha iva svakaḥ ।।

bhāraṃ draviṇasaṃbhāraṃ vetti granthiguṇāguṇaḥ ।
bhogaṃ nirupabhogaṃ ca svadeśavirahī janaḥ ।।

ityuktvā sa guhāgohādutpāṭya vipulāṃ śilām ।
kṛtābhyupagamenāśu janakena yayau saha ।।

prayātayostatastūrṇaṃ samabhyetyātha kinnarī ।
śūnyaṃ dṛṣṭvā guhāgehaṃ nirvedādityavintayat ।।

aho me vismṛtasnehaḥ sa gataḥ kkāpi durjanaḥ ।
dvijihvānāṃ bhujaṃgānāṃ kauṭilyaṃ vā kimadbhutam ।।

na ramante palāyante paryante sukharāgiṇaḥ ।
cirasthā api niḥsnehāḥ śukā iva dvijātayaḥ ।।

iti saṃcintya sā patyurnikārātprītimatyajat ।
puṣpopamāni premāṇi na sahante kadarthanām ।।

vidyāguṇena kenāsau putro me bhuvi jāīvati ।
iti dhyātvā sakhīhaste tasmai vīṇāṃ dideśa sā ।।

saṃbhogasukhapaṇyaiva prītiḥ patiṣu yoṣitām ।
aparyuṣitavātsalyā putraprītistu niścalā ।।

javena vrajatostūrṇaṃ tayordaurjanyalajjayā ।
śīgragāya dadau vīṇāṃ tatsakhī vegagāminī ।।

ādyā tantririyaṃ nāsyāḥ spraṣṭavyā vighnakāriṇī ।
ityābhāṣya tayā dattāṃ vīṇāṃ prāpya jagāma saḥ ।।

tataḥ svadeśe janakaṃ svagṛhe viniveśya saḥ ।
vīṇāpravīṇaḥ sarvatra lābhapūjāmavāptavān ।।

tataḥ kadāvidvāṇijā ambudhidvīpagāminā ।
āropitaḥ pravahaṇaṃ divyavīṇānurāgiṇā ।।

vīṇāmūrcchanayā tasya śrotrapīyūṣadhārayā ।
kṣaṇe kṣaṇe samudro api nistaraṅga ivābhavat ।।

athādyatantrisaṃsparśādutpannopaplavoplute ।
bhagne pravahaṇe sarvavaṇijāmabhavat kṣayaḥ ।।

tato balāhakāvāptyā pavanapretitaḥ kṣaṇāt ।
kaśerudvīpamāsede karmaśeṣeṇa śīghragaḥ ।।

tatrābdhikūlasaṃlīnaṃ divyodyānaṃ praviśya saḥ ।
śyāmāṃ dadarśa sośumbāṃ mūrdhanyastabakastanām ।।

grandhantīṃ timirākhyānāṃ puṣpāṇāmujjvalasrajam ।
nibandhanaṃ tanuguṇaiḥ kurvāṇāmapyacetasām ।।

sāpi taṃ rucirākāraṃ dṛṣṭvā vismayamāyayau ।
dhīraṃ śaiśavatāruṇyasaṃdhimadhyasthatāṃ gatam ।।

māramārutasaṃcālasakampakarapallavā ।
sā śīrṇaśīlakusumā lateva praṇanāma tam ।।

cirārūḍheva sahasā prītiḥ prauḍhā tayorabhūt ।
prāgjanmasnehasaṃlīnaṃ na muñcati mano manaḥ ।।

ramamāṇāṃ divā tena niśāyāṃ ca mahībhujā ।
mene vāmācaritatāṃ tām priyo gūḍhakāmukaḥ ।।

tena vārāṇasīṃ gantuṃ jñātvā vṛttaṃ samarthitā ।
tannināya khagārūḍhā tadgirā mīlitekṣaṇam ।।

vārito api tadā vyomni nayanonmīlane tayā ।
so abahvatsahasaivāndhaścāpalādvivṛtekṣaṇaḥ ।।

sā tamantaḥpurodyāne nidhāya bhayakātarā ।
viveśa śokasaṃtaptā śayyāveśma mahīpateḥ ।।

dūyamānena manasā rajanīmativāhya tām ।
prātarna gantuṃ na sthātuṃ cintākrāntā śaśāka sā ।।

atrāntare samudbhūtaścyutasaurabhanirbharaḥ ।
madhumāso vilāsānāṃ yauvanaṃ puṣpadhanvanaḥ ।।

kokilālikulaiḥ kālaḥ kālaḥ kālo viyoginām ।
śīrṇaśokanavāśokaduḥsahaḥ pratidṛṣyate ।।

rājāpyaviratautsukyādudyānaṃ gantumudyataḥ ।
dinamekaṃ na tatyāja sośumbāṃ kāmamohitaḥ ।।

sa tayāsaha rāgasya madasya madanasya ca ।
saṃsāramiva viśrāntipadapuṣpavanaṃ yayau ।।

tatra bālānilālolalatāvailakṣyakāriṇīm ।
paśyan pramodamāsede yaditāmeva bhūpatiḥ ।।

anyarāgaviṣākrāntā sāpyabhūnmalinasmṛtiḥ ।
sukhamapyasukhaṃ vetti cintāśalyākulaṃ manaḥ ।।

antargatabhujaṃgābhiḥ strībhiratyantarāgiṇaḥ ।
kaṇṭhe kṛtābhirnṛtyanti mālābhiriva mohitāḥ ।।

tatraikāntalatākuñjanikuñjanihitasthitiḥ ।
andhaḥ saurabhamāghrāya sośumbātimirasrajaḥ ।।

sahasaiva vikāreṇa rāgādvismṛtasaṃvṛtiḥ ।
agāyanmadanakṣībā gaṇayanti bahyaṃ kutaḥ ।।

tanupavanavilāsaiḥ kīryamāṇaḥ priyāyāḥ
samadabadanapadmāmodasaṃbhārasāraḥ ।
