timirakusumagandhaḥ so ayamāyāti dūrāt
bhramarasaraṇivīṇāvibhramārāvaramyaḥ ।।

śrutvā hṛdayasaṃvādagītaṃ tattasya bhūpatiḥ ।
udyānavicayaṃ kṛtvā taṃ dadarśa latāntare ।।

gāḍharocamadakṣībaṃ sa taṃ papraccha śaṅkitaḥ ।
api jānasi sośumbāṃ tasya vā lakṣaṇaṃ tanoḥ ।।

so abravīt kiṃ na jānāmi sośumbāṃ bimbapāṭalām ।
upaviṣṭo adhare yasyā rāgarājye manobhavaḥ ।।

nyastaṃ smareṇeva tadūrūmūle lekhāmayaṃ svastikamasti kāntam ।
āvartaśobhā stanamaṇḍale vā lāvaṇyakallolanibhāsti tasyāḥ ।।

etadākarṇya nṛpatiḥ sadyaḥ saṃtāpaśoṣitam ।
mumoca rāgakusumaṃ nirmālyaminva cetasaḥ ।।

so abravīnnāsti nārīṇāṃ śīlarakṣā śatairati ।
khapuṣpamāleva satī sarvathā naiva jāyate ।।

ityuktvāndhena tāṃ rājā saha śmaśānakānanam ।
gardabhāropitāṃ tūrṇaṃ tatyāja nagarādbahiḥ ।।

sā tena saha nirlajjā vrajantī dinasaṃkṣaye ।
aṭavyāṃ caurapatinā prāptaiva saha saṃpadā ।।

janairabhidrute tasmin sahasā cauramaṇḍale ।
niraparāśa evāndhaścaurabhrāntyā nipātitaḥ ।।

cauro api niśāṃ bhuktvā sośumbāṃ kṣasṇasaṃgataḥ ।
gṛhītvābharaṇānyasyā jagāmottīrya nimnagām ।।

kāraṇḍavāyāh saritastasyāstīre nirambarā ।
śuśova sāñjanairaśrujālaiḥ sā malinastanī ।।

tasmin kṣaṇe mukhāsaktaṃ māṃsamutsṛjya jambuke ।
yāte jalotplutaṃ matsyaṃ tajjahāraṃ vihaṅgamaḥ ।।

matsye nimagne sahasā khagena piśite hṛte ।
sa babhūvobhayabhraṃśāccintāniścalalocanaḥ ।।

tasyāstaṃ vīkṣyaṃ duḥkhe api mukhe smitamadṝśyata ।
hāsaḥ parasya skhalite duḥsthasyāpyupajāyate ।।

sa tāṃ vailakṣyakupitaḥ provācānucitasmitām ।
aho hasasi māṃ loke hāsyāyatanatām gatām ।।

nṛpaṃ tyaktvāgatā hyandhamtyaktavāndhaṃ cauramāśritā ।
tavāhamubhayabhraṣṭaḥ tribhraṣṭāyāḥ smitāspadam ।।

āstām vaḥ parihāso ayaṃ taṃ yuktyāhaṃ karomi te ।
khalāste viṣamasthānām ye biḍambanapaṇḍitāḥ ।।

ityuktvā nagarīṃ gatvā sa nṛpāya nyavedayat ।
sośumbā te nadītīre tapoyukteti manmatiḥ ।।

atha nināya tām rājā vitīryābharaṇāmbaram ।
doṣamācchādayatyeva rāgadveṣaḥ śarīriṇām ।।

saivādyotpalavarṇeyamudāyī śīghrago apyasau ।
prāgjanmāntarapuṇyena bhikṣḥuvratamupāgatau ।।

abhavadatirasārdraṃ mānāsṃ rāgayoge
yadu madanavidheyaṃ rāgayuktaṃ yadasyāḥ ।
virataśamavirārā tena tasmin muhūtre
kṛtanarapatirūpānandinaṃ mām vavande ।।

iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ devāvatārāvadānaṃ nāma caturdaśaḥ pallavaḥ ।।

śilānikṣepāvadānam ।

balabhatuladhairyavīryaṃ sāścaryaṃ bhavati saprabhāvāṇām ।
mahadāśrayayogādyasmai sarvaṃ mahimatvamāyāti ।।

purā kuśīpurīṃ ramyāṃ mallānāṃ balaśālinām ।
svecchāvihārī bhagāvān pratasthe sugataḥ svayam ।।

te tadāgamanaṃ śrutvā kalyāṇaṃ kuśalaiṣiṇaḥ ।
vartmasaṃśodhanaṃ cakrurupacārapadodyatāḥ ।।

deśaṃ bhūṣayatāṃ teṣāṃ saṃsiktaṃ candanodakaiḥ ।
tṛṇakaṇṭakapāṣāṇasarkarāreṇuvarjitam ।।

madhye samāyayau bhūminimagnā mahatī śilā ।
avasannā visannā ca vadhūrvindhyagireriva ।।

tāmutpāṭayatāṃ teṣāṃ kuddālabhujarajjubhiḥ ।
māso jagāma na tvasyāḥ sahasrāṃśe apyabhūta kṣatiḥ ।।

atha samsārasaṃtāpapraśamāmṛtadīdhitiḥ ।
āyayau bhagavān sarvamānasollāsabāndhavaḥ ।।

ghanāndhakāravirativyaktasatphaladarśanaḥ ।
prasādasaṃvibhaktāśaḥ prakāśa iva śāradaḥ ।।

sa tān dṛṣṭvā pariśrāntān viphalakleśapiḍāītān ।
śrutvā ca tadvyavasitaṃ tānūce praṇatānanān ।।

aho kleśaphalārambhaḥ prayāsavyavasāyinām ।
saṃsārakarmaṇīvāsmin vyāpāre vaḥ samudyamaḥ ।।

prārambhe viṣamakleśaṃ kriyamāṇaṃ sasaṃśayam ।
siddhamapyanupādeyaṃ na prājñāḥ karma kurvate ।।

ityuktvā caraṇāṅguṣṭhaghaṭṭitām vāmapāṇinā ।
vinyasya dakṣiṇe pāṇau bhagavān vipulāṃ śilām ।।

visṛjya brahamlokāntamaparyantaparākramaḥ ।
cacārāścaryacaryāyāṃ dūtamiva jagattraye ।।

kṣiptāyāṃ sahasā tasyām tenātyadbhutakāriṇā ।
udabhūdganodbhūta iva vyāptajanaḥ svanaḥ ।।

anityaḥ sarvasaṃskāra ityabhrāntavidhāyinaḥ ।
sarvadharmā nirātmānaḥ śāntanirvāṇameva tat ।।

iti sphuṭodite śabde śilā bhagavataḥ kare ।
girīndraśīrṣakākārā sthitā punaradṛśyata ।।

kṣaṇena sā bhagavatā kṣiptā vadanamārutaiḥ ।
kṛtā visāriṇī dikṣu paramāṇuparaṃparā ।।

punarekīkṛtāmeva bhagavān paramāṇubhiḥ ।
śilāmanyatra nidadhe vismayaṃ ca jagattraye ।।

āścaryaniścaladṛśastato mallā balirjitam ।
vīryaṃ bhagavato vīkṣya praṇatāstaṃ babhāṣire ।।

aho mahāprabhāvo ayaṃ balavīryodayastava ।
niścayādhigame yasya na pragalbhāḥ surā api ।।

anugrahapravṛttena balena guruṇā tava ।
adhogatinimagneyaṃ janateva dhṛtā śilā ।।

vīryaprajñābalādīnām pramāṇāvadhiniścayam ।
api jānāti te kaścidāścaryatarakāriṇaḥ ।।

iti bruvāṇānāścaryaniścalānavalokya tān ।
tasyāṃ śilāyāmāsīnaḥ provāca bhagavān jinaḥ ।।

ekībhūtabalaṃ yaddhi bhūtānām bhuvanatraye ।
sugatasya tadekasya loke naiva samaṃ balam ।।

ambhāṃsi kumbhairambhodherjaganti paramāṇubhiḥ ।
śakyānyalaṃ laṅghayituṃ prabhāvo na tu saugataḥ ।।

saṃkhyāṃ sumeroryo vetti tulāmānena tattvataḥ ।
sugatānām na jānāti so api sudguṇagauravam ।।

kathayitveti bhagavān saṃprāpte suramaṇḍale ।
saśakrapadmanilaye cakre kuśaladeśanam ।।

mallāstadupadeśena tattadbodhisamāśrayāt ।
saśrāvakākhyāṃ pratyekasamyaksaṃbuddhatāṃ yayuḥ ।।

srotaḥprāptiphalaṃ kauścitsakṛdāgāmi cāparaiḥ ।
anāgāmiphalaṃ cāṇyaiḥ prāptamarhatpadaṃ paraiḥ ।।

ityāśyayānuśayadhātugatiṃ nirīkṣya jñātvā tathāprakṛtimapratimopadeśam ।
teṣāṃ cakāra bhagavāṃścaturāryasatyasamyakprakāśaviśadaṃ kuśalodayāya ।।

iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ śilānikṣepāvadānaṃpañcadaśaḥ pallavaḥ ।।

maitreyavyākaraṇāvadānam ।

asaṃgamo nāma viśuddhidhāmo śreyāṃsi sūte kuśalābhikāmaḥ ।
saṃsāravāmaḥ sukṛtābhirāmo manomalairvairarajovirāmaḥ ।।

purā gaṅgāṃ samuttīrya nāgānāṃ phaṇasetunā ।
bhagavān sugataḥ pāraṃprāpya bhikṣūnabhāṣata ।।

iha ratnamayaḥ pūrvaṃ yūpo abhūdadbhutadyutiḥ ।
darśayāṃi tamatraiva draṣṭuṃ vaḥ kautukaṃ yadi ।।

ityuktvā bhagavān bhūmau pāṇinā divyalakṣmaṇā ।
spṛṣṭvā nāgagaṇotkṣiptaṃ ratnayūpadarśayat ।।

taṃ dṛṣṭvā bhikṣavaḥ sarve nirnimeṣekṣaṇāściram ।
babhūvuścitralikhitām iva niścalavigrahāḥ ।।

tatkathāmatha taiḥ pṛṣṭaḥ provāca bhagavān punaḥ ।
atītānāgatajñānaṃ dantālokaiḥ kirannivaḥ ।।

devaputraḥ purā kaścit kāle svargaparicyutaḥ ।
mahāpraṇādanāmābhūnnṛpatiḥ śakraśāsanāt ।।

dharmavṛttānusaraṇasmaraṇāya mahītale ।
ucitaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ kiṃcit sa yayāce śatakratum ।।

tataḥ surapatervākyādviśvakarmā tadālaye ।
bhāsvaraṃ vidadhe ratnayūpaṃ puṇyamivonnatam ।।

tatastaddarśanāsakte jane kautukaniścale ।
kṛṣyādikarmaṇyucchinne rājñaḥ koṣakṣayo abhavat ।।

tatastena kṣitibhujā kṣipto ayaṃ jāhnavījale ।
tiṣṭhatyadyāpi pātāle ratnaiḥ sūryairivācitaḥ ।।

bhaviṣyatyasya kālena paricchinnaḥ parikṣayaḥ ।
na tajjagati nāmāste pariṇāme yadakṣayam ।।

āgāmisamaye puṃsāṃ varṣāśītisahasrake ।
śaṅkhaśubhrayaśāḥ śaṅkho nāma rājā bhaviṣyati ।।

puṇyalabdhamimaṃ yūpaṃ nṛpaḥ kalpadrumopamaḥ ।
sa purohitaputrāya maitreyāya pradāsyati ।।

maitreyo apyanmumādāya kṛtvā sapadi khaṇḍaśaḥ ।
arthicintāmaṇirlokamadaridraṃ kariṣyati ।।

yūpaṃ datvātha maitreyaḥ samyaksaṃbuddhatām gataḥ ।
anuttarajñānanidhirbhaviṣyati surārcitaḥ ।।

śaṅko rājā sahasrāṇāmaśītyā parivāritaḥ ।
sāntaḥpurāmātyagaṇo rājāpi pravrajiṣyati ।।

prāgjanmapraṇidhānena śaṅkhasya kuśalodayaḥ ।
kṛtasyāvaśyabhogyatvātpariṇāme phaliṣyati ।।

madhyadeśe purā rājā vāsavo vāsavopamaḥ ।
dhanasaṃmatanāmā ca nṛpo abhūduttarāpathe ।।

tayorvibhavasaṃgharṣo bhūto vairāgnitaptayoḥ ।
abhūd yuddhasamārambhasaṃbhārarabhasaṃ manah ।।

nagaraṃ ca praviśyātha sametya dhanasaṃmataḥ ।
cakre garajathānīkairgaṅgātīraṃ nīrantaram ।।

tatra ratnaśīkhī nāṃa samyaksaṃbuddhatām gataḥ ।
dṛṣṭastenārcyāmānāṅghrirbrahmaśakrādibhiḥ suraiḥ ।।

so acintayadaho rājā vāsavaḥ pṛthipuṇyavān ।
viṣayānte vasatyeṣ ayo hi tridaśavanditaḥ ।।

tatastasyānubhāvena tatra bhūpālayostayoḥ ।
yayau vairarajaḥ śāntyā mithyāmohaparikṣayam ।।

kṝtasaṃghiḥ pareṇātha vāsavaḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ ।
bhagavantaṃ samabhyetya sarvabhogaurapūjayat ।।

praṇidhānaṃ ca vidadhe pūjānte praṇamāmi tam ।
ahaṃ kuśalamūlena syāmetena mahāniti ।।

asminnavasare ghore śankhaśabde samudgate ।
provāca taṃ ratnaśikhī praṇataṃ purataḥ sthitam ।।

śankho nāma mahīpālaścakravartī bhaviṣyasi ।
paryante bodhiyuktaśca kuśalaṃ samāvāpsyasi ।।

evaṃ satpraṇidhānatah kṣitipatiḥ puṇyodayādvāsavaḥ
śaṅkho nāma nṛpa sa ratnaśikhinādiṣṭaḥ śriyaṃ prāpsyati ।
maitreyaḥ praṇayātkariṣyati tathā bodhau viśuddhāṃ dhiyaṃ
kalyāṇābhiniveśapuṇyataraṇirāḍya hi satsaṃgamaḥ ।।

iti kṣemendraviracitāyām bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ maitreyavyākaraṇāvadānaṃ nāma ṣoḍaśaḥ pallavaḥ ।।

ādarśamukhāvadānam ।

cittaprasādavimalapraṇayojjvalasya svalpasya dānakusumasya phalāṃśakena ।
hemādrirohaṇanagendrasudhābdhidānasaṃpatphalaṃ na hi tulākalanāmupaiti ।।

purā manojñe sarvajñaḥ śrāvastyāṃ jetakānane ।
anāthapiṇḍadārāme vijahāra mahāśayaḥ ।।

āryo mahākāśyapākhyastacchiṣyaḥ karuṇānidhiḥ ।
nagaropavanasyāntaṃ janacārikayā yayau ।।

tatra sudrugatiryoṣinnagarāśravalambikā ।
apaśyat kuṣṭharogārtā kāśyapaṃ taṃ yadṛcchayā ।।

sā taṃ dṛṣṭvā prasādinyā śraddhayā samacintayat ।
pātre asya piṇḍapātārhā kiṃ na jātāsmi puṇyataḥ ।।

vijñāya tasyā āścaryaśraddhāyuktaṃ manoratham ।
prasārya pātraṃ jagrāha piṇḍaṃ taṃ karuṇākulaḥ ।।

tīvracittaprasādena bhaktasārasamaraṇe ।
kuṣṭhinyā nipapātāsyāḥ pātre śīrṇakarāṅguliḥ ।।

tataḥ sā pātakamiva tyaktvānityakalevaram ।
devānāṃ tuṣitākhyānāṃ nilaye samajāyata ।।

śakrastadadbhutaṃ jñātvā dānapuṇypditādaraḥ ।
yatnātkāśyapasatpātraṃ sudhayā samapūrayat ।।

sudhārpaṇe apyasau bhikṣurnispṛhastṛṇalīlayā ।
praśamāmṛtasaṃpūrṇaścakre pātramadhomukham ।।

bhajante praṇayaprītiṃ kṛpaṇeṣu kṛpākulāḥ ।
santaḥ saṃpatsamādhmātavadane mīlitādarāḥ ।।

śrutvā tāṃ tuṣite devanikāye niratām nṛpaḥ ।
prasenajit bhagavataścakre bhojyādhivāsanām ।।

rājñastasya gṛhe dṛṣṭvā lakṣmīmāścaryakāriṇaḥ ।
āryānandena bhagavān pṛṣṭastatpuṇyamabhyadhāt ।।

purā gṛhapateḥ sūnurdāridyrāddāsatāṃ gataḥ ।
kṣetrakarmāṇi saṃsaktaḥ kṣutkṣāmaḥ klāntimāyayau ।।

svajananyā samānītāṃ niḥsnehalavaṇāṃ cirāt ।
kulmāṣapiṇḍimāsādya bhoktuṃ sādaramāyayau ।।

dhautahastaḥ kṣaṇe tasmin saṃprāptāya yadṛcchayā ।
dadau pratyekabuddhāya tām prasannena cetasā ।।

jātaḥ sa eva kālena bhūpālo ayaṃ prasenajit ।
tasya dānakaṇasyaivaṃ vibhūtiḥ prathamaṃ phalam ।।

śrutveti bhagavadvākyaṃ bhikṣūrvismayamāyayau ।
rājāpi vipulāṃ pūjāṃ cakre bhagavataḥ puraḥ ।।

rājārhairakhilairbhogaiḥ kṛtvā bhaktinivedanam ।
sa koṭīstailakumbhānāṃ dīpamālāmakalpayat ।।

dīpamekaṃ dadau tatra svalpakaṃ durgatāṅganā ।
snehakṣayātprayāteṣu sarveṣu na jagāma yaḥ ।।

vicintya praṇidhānena tayā vimalacetasā ।
bhāvinīm śākyamunitāṃ sarvajño asyāh samabhyadhāt ।।

ratnadīpāvaliṃ datvā rājā bhagavataḥ purah ।
upaviśya praṇamyāgre praṇayāttaṃ vajijñapat ।।

bhagavatpraṇidhānena tattatpuṇyānubhāvataḥ ।
na kasyānuttarā samyaksaṃbodhirbhavadarpitā ।।

bhavatprasādapraṇayāt prāptumicchāmi tāmaham ।
nirvikalpaphalāvāptyai sevyante kalpapādapāḥ ।।

iti rājavacaḥ śrutvā bhagavān samabhāṣata ।
durlabhānuttarā samyaksaṃbodhiḥ pṛthivīpate ।।

sūkṣmā mṛṇālatantubhyo giribhyo api garīyasī ।
samudrebhyo api gambhīrā sā sukhena na labhyate ।।

na dānairbahubhirlabdhaṃ mayaivānyeṣu janmasu ।
cittaprasādaviśadaṃ jñānaṃ tatkāraṇaṃ jaguḥ ।।

caturdvīpādhipatyena mayā māndhātṛjanmani ।
ciraṃ dānaphalaṃ bhuktaṃ bodhirnādhigatā tu sā ।।

dānena cakravartīśrīḥ sā sudarśanajanmani ।
bhuktā mayāmahīyasī bodhirnādhigatā tu sā ।।

purā datvā gajānaṣṭau velāmadvijajanmāni ।
mayā prāptaṃ mahatpuṇyaṃ bodhirnādhigatā tu sā ।।

kurūpaḥ kuśalātmāhaṃ rājaputraḥ purābhavam ।
yaḥ piśāco ayamityuktvā nijalatnyā vivarjitaḥ ।।

śriyai śrīskandho bhūtyāge prītiryasya sadā sthitā ।
sa duḥkhī rūpavaikalyāt kka vā sarvaguṇodayaḥ ।।

taṃ rūpavirahe dehatyāgārūḍhaṃ śacīpatiḥ ।
divyacūḍāmaṇiṃ datvā cakre pañcaśaropamam ।।

ṣaṣṭiḥ purasahasrāṇi tasya yajñeṣu yajvanaḥ ।
hemayūpābhirūpāṇi prāpurmerubalaśriyam ।।

tasmin mayātidānādrikṛte kuśalajanmani ।
tāni puṇyānyavāptāni bodhirnādhigatā tu sā ।।

mayā satyaprabhāveṇa triśaṅkunṛpajanmani ।
kṛtā vṛṣṭiḥ sudurbhikṣā bodhirnādhigatā tu sā ।।

mithilāyāṃ mahādevanṛpajanmani yajvanā ।
mayāptā puṇyasaṃpattirbodhirnādhigatā tu sā ।।

mithilāyāṃ purā puṇyaṃ nimibhūpālajanmani ।
prāptaṃ dānatapoyajñairbodhirnādhigatā tu sā ।।

purā nandasya nṛpateścatvāraḥ piśunāḥ sutāḥ ।
babhūvurādarśamukhaḥ pañcamaśca guṇādhikaḥ ।।

kālenāpannaparyantaḥ sa bhūpatiracintayat ।
ete madante catvāro rājyaṃ nārhanti karkaśāḥ ।।

putre mamādarśamukhe rājyaśrī pratibimbitā ।
suvṛtte labhate śobhāṃ prajñāvaimalyaśālini ।।

dhyātvetyamātyān so avādīt sa bhavadbhirnareśvaraḥ ।
kṛto antaḥpuravargeṇa yo abhyutthānena pūjyate ।।

maulirna kampate yasya sameva maṇipādukaiḥ ।
dvāradrumādrivāpīṣu nidhiṣaṭkaṃ sa paśyati ।।

ityuktvā tridivaṃ yāte nṛpatau mantriṇaḥ kramāt ।
taduktrairlakṣaṇaiścakrurādarśamukhamīśvaram ।।

dharmanirṇayakāryeṣu yaṃ vādiprativādinah ।
vilokyaiva svayaṃ tasthurnyāyairjayaparājaye ।।

purā nirabhiasṃghena prātavaiśasakilbiṣam ।
brāhmaṇaṃ daṇḍinaṃ nāma dayāluḥ prayayau puraḥ ।।

guyugārthe gṛhasthena mṛtena vaḍavāhateḥ ।
kuṭhārapātataḥ patnyā takṣavāsī vivāditaḥ ।।

śauṇḍikenātmajavadhāddīkṣitaṃ tulyanigraham ।
tadvipakṣabhayenoktvā tatsaṃtyaktaṃ vyamokṣayat ।।

amānuṣāṇāṃ sattvānāmadhyāśayaviśeṣataḥ ।
cakāra cittaśodhanaṃ tattatsaṃdehanirṇayam ।।

avṛṣṭimṛṣṭe durbhikṣe yena dvādaśavarsake ।
vihitaṃ sarvasattvānāmaśanaprāṇavartanam ।।

ityamūnmama puṇyāptirādarśamukhajnmani ।
na tu sā samyaksaṃbodhirvibodhitā mahodayā ।।

bahujanmaśatābhyāsaprasāsena mahīyasā ।
adya tu jñānavaimalyaṃ mayāptaṃ lutpasaṃvṛti ।।

jñānaprajñādhigamyā kimapi paratarānuttarā satyāsaṃvit
samyaksaṃbodhireṣā na ca khalu nṛpate labhyate dānapuṇyaiḥ ।
mohaśyāmāvirāme gataghanagaganavyaktavaimalyabhājāṃ
nirvyājānandabhūmirbhavati bhavatamaśchedinī sā dinaśrīḥ ।।

iti kṣemendraviracitāyām bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ ādarśamukhāvadānaṃ nāma saptadaśaḥ pallavaḥ ।।

śāriputrapravrajyāvadānam ।

nedaṃ bandhunoṃ suhṛt sodaro vā nedaṃ mātā na pitā vā karoti ।
yatsaṃsārāmbhodhesetuṃ vidhatte jñānācāryaḥ ko api kalyāṇahetuḥ ।।

kalandakanivāsākhye ramye veṇuvanāśrame ।
bhagavān viharan buddhaḥ pure rājagṛhe purā ।।

kilitaṃ copayiṣyaṃ ca dvau parivrājakau purā ।
prapannau bhikṣubhāvena cakāra śamasaṃvṛtau ।।

tataśca śāriputrasya bhikṣoḥ saṃdeśanāṃ vyaghāt ।
yayā sākṣātkṛtārhattvo so abhūnmokṣagatikṣamaḥ ।।

tasya tadadbhutaṃ dṛṣṭvā dhanārhaṃ sarvabhikṣubhiḥ ।
papracchuḥ pūrvavṛttāntaṃ sa ca tebhyo vyabhāṣata ।।

brāhmaṇasyāgnimitrasya bhāryā guṇavarābhavat ।
śūrpiketi kṛtaṃ pitrā krīḍānāma ca bibhratī ।।

bhrātā prathamaśīlākhyaḥ tasya śūrpasamābhidhaḥ ।
pratyekabuddhatāṃ yātaḥ kadācid gṛhamāyayau ।।

sa tayā bharturādeśād gṛhībhaktyādhivāsitaḥ ।
praṇatipraṇayācāraistoṣitaḥ paricaryayā ।।

kadāciccīvare tasya kurvāṇasya vipātraṇam ।
sūcīkarmavahād dṛṣṭvā praṇidhānaṃ samādadhe ।।

yatheyaṃ kartarīṃ tīkṣṇā yathā gambhīragāmiṇī ।
sūcī tathāparā prajñā mama syāditi sādarā ।।

pratyekabuddhavinayāt praṇidhānena tena ca ।
gatāsmin janmani saiva saprajñaśāriputratām ।।

sa eṣa śāriputro adya bhikṣuṣtīkṣṇatarāgradhīḥ ।
kalyāṇapātratām yātaḥ kalpavallī hi sanmateḥ ।।

vākyaṃ bhagavataḥ śrutvā papracchurbhikṣavaḥ punah ।
kasmānnāṭyakule jātaḥ śāriputro narādhame ।।

tatastān bhagavānūce pūrvasminneṣa janmani ।
abhūnmahāmatirnāma rājaputraḥ satāṃ mataḥ ।।

śrīmato api matistasya pravrajyāyāmajāyata ।
paripākaprasannānāṃ kāluṣyāya na saṃpadaḥ ।।

pravrajyā rājaputrāṇāṃ yūnāṃ naiva kulocitā ।
ityuktvā janakaḥ prītyā taṃ yatnena nyavārayat ।।

kadācit kuñjarārūḍhaḥ sa vrajan janavartmani ।
dṛṣṭvā daridraṃ sthaviraṃ kāruṇyādidamabravīt ।।

adhanyā dhanīno loke bandhubandhanayantritāḥ ।
pravrajyāṃ nāpnuvantyeva tvaṃ tu kena nivāritaḥ ।।

sa nyavedayanme daridrasya na pātraṃ na ca cīvaram ।
dhanopakaraṇānyeva śamopakaraṇānyapi ।।

rājasūnuriti śrutvā gatvā munitapovanam ।
pravrajyāṃ kārayitvāsya pradadau pātracīvaram ।।

so acireṇaiva kālena yātaḥ pratyekabuddhatām ।
rājaputraṃ samabhyetya divyāmṛddhimadarśayat ।।

tasya prabhāvamālokya sa pradadhyau nṛpātmajaḥ ।
aho mahodayatvānme pravrajyā durlabhābhavat ।।

dāridyrādavivekācc nīcānāmapi durlabhā ।
jāyeyamadhame kule tasmadasmi vivekavān ।।

sa eva śāriputro ayaṃ jñātastatpraṇidhānataḥ ।
pravrajito bhagavatā kāśyapenānyajanmani ।।

tenāyaṃ niyamapraṇayavinayī samyakprasādodayād
ādiṣṭaḥ kuśalāya satyanidhinā prajñāvatāmagraṇīḥ ।
kāle śākyamunerbhaviṣyati mataḥ śiṣyatvayogādvaraṃ
maudgalyāyana eṣa cātra kathitaḥ saṃvinmayānāṃ vadaḥ ।।

anyajanmani daridraḥ kārmikaḥ kenacidapi dayayā maharṣiṇā ।
dattapātracīvaro abhavaddarśitarddhirāsīdatulaprabhāvavān ।।

iti kṣemendraviracitāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ śāriputraprajajyāvadānam nāmāṣṭādaśaḥ pallavaḥ ।।

śroṇakoṭikarṇāvadānam ।

sa ko api puṇyātiśayodayasya varaḥ prabhāvaḥ paramākṣayo yaḥ ।
pratyakṣalakṣyaḥ śubhapakṣasākṣī janmāntare lakṣaṇatāmupaiti ।।

ramye purā bhagavati śrāvastyāṃ jetakānane ।
anāthapiṇḍadārāme vihāriṇi tathāgate ।।

babhūva vāsavagrāme balasenābhidho gṛhī ।
pūritāśaḥ phalabharaiśchāyātarurivārthinām ।।

jāyāyāṃ jayasenāyāṃ kāle kamalalocanaḥ ।
ajāyata sutastasya puṇyairmīrta ivotsavaḥ ।।

sajahā ratnadīpārcirabhūtkarṇasya karṇikā ।
nābhūnmūlyatulā yasya hemakoṭiśatairapi ।।

śravaṇānakṣatrajāto asau ratnakoṭyarhakarṇikāḥ ।
sa śroṇakoṭikarṇākhyaḥ kumāro abhūdguṇocitaḥ ।।

sa nirmalaruciḥ kāntaḥ kalābhiṃ paripūritaḥ ।
amandānandaniṣyandī na kasyendurivābhavat ।।

sa yuvā vāryamāṇo api pitrā dhanadasaṃpadā ।
jananī sāśrunayanā paraṃ puruṣayā girā ।।

priyaṃvado api nirbhartsyo viṣavarṣīva candramāḥ ।
mahāsārthena ratnārthī dūradvīpāntaraṃ yayau ।।

makarākaramuttīrya vrajatasyasya nirjane ।
karmormiviplavenābhūt svasārthavirahaḥ pathi ।।

sārtho api tamanāsādya vinivṛttaṃ śucā śanaiḥ ।
svadeśamarjitakleśaḥ praviveśa viśṛṅkhalāḥ ।।

so api taptamaruśreṇīlakṣaṇāṃ dakṣiṇāṃ diśam ।
śrāntaḥ praśāntaviśrāntirvāpigāhaṃ vyagāhata ।।

so acintayadaho vitte pratinittārjanodyamaḥ ।
mamāyamanayenaiva jātakleśaḥ phalodayaḥ ।।

aho dhanārjanāveśaḥ saṃtoṣavirahānnṛṇām ।
sarvāpavādasaṃvādo nindyānām vipadāṃ padam ।।

hemācale api saṃprāpte na paryāptirhanārjane ।
saṃsāre vāsanābhyāsadveṣamohaḥ śarīriṇām ।।

pṛthuprayāsavirasā dīpitā śrīrivāyatā ।
tṛṣṇāṃ tanoti nitarāmiyaṃmarumahītale ।।

aho bata kuraṅgāṇāṃ tṛṣṇāndhānāṃ pade pade ।
mamāpi janayantyeva mohaṃ marumarīcikāḥ ।।

iyaṃ tṛṣṇā śramaścāyamimā nirudakā bhuvaḥ ।
kiṃ karomi kka gacchāmi paśyāmi jvalitā diśaḥ ।।

iti saṃcintya sa śanaiḥ prasarpan salilāśayā ।
āyāsamiva sākāraṃ dadarśa puramāyasam ।।

ghoraṃ dvāri sthitaṃ tatra saṃtrāsasyeva sodaram ।
dadarśa puruṣaṃ kālakarālaṃ raktalocanam ।।

sa tena pṛṣṭaḥ pānīyaṃ yadā novāca kiṃcana ।
tadā svayaṃ praviṣṭena pretaloko vilokitah ।।

dagdhakaṣṭhopamān dhūlimalaliptānnirambarān ।
śuṣkāsthinsāyuśeṣāṅgān pretān dṛṣṭvā sa vivyathe ।।

tairyācitah sa pānīyaṃ pānīyavirahārditaḥ ।
parityajya nijāmārtimabhūttadduḥkhaduḥkhitaḥ ।।

tīvratṛṣṇāturānūce sa tānārtapralāpinah ।
mamāsmin marukāntāre niṣkṛpasya kutaḥ payaḥ ।।

kṛcchre asmin duḥsahe nyastāḥ ke yūyaṃ kena karmaṇā ।
yuṣmadaprakriyabandhaścātaḥ kṛcchraścarāmyaham ।।

nidrā niḥśalyakalpasya sukhasikteva tasya yā ।
nārtānnapaśyati dṛṣṭvā teṣāṃ kleśakṣaye kṣamā ।।

te tamūcurviruddhena karmaṇā mohasaṃcayāt ।
anivartya vayaṃ martyāḥ kṣiptā vyasanasaṃkaṭe ।।

adhikṣepāt kṣepakṣatipataradhairyairmadabharād anāryairmānavyasanerṣyābhiravāryavyatikaraiḥ ।
kṛtāsmābhirnityaṃ suhanahṛdaye nirdayatayā
vacobhirnārācairviṣaparicitaiḥ śalyakalanā ।।

dānaṃ nadattaṃ hṛtameva vittaṃ hiṃsānimittīkṛtameva cittam ।
asmārbhiraṅgairvihitā vikārāḥ parasya dārāpahṛtiprakārāḥ ।।

te vayaṃ kuhakāsaktā dakṣāḥ kṣudreṣu karmasu ।
prayātāḥ pretanagare ghore asmin kleśapātratām ।।

iti teṣāṃ vacaḥ śrutvā so anyatra ca tathāvidhān ।
pretān dṛṣṭvānabhipretān karuṇakulito abhavat ।।

nirgamya durgamāt tasmāt purātpuṇyabalena saḥ ।
vimalaṃ śītalacchāyamāsasāda vanāntaram ।।

atha dūradhvasaṃtaptaḥ pariśrāntaḥ śanaiḥ śanaiḥ ।
nipapātācalādandhastṛṣṭārta iva bhāṣkaraḥ ।।

dine puṇya iva kṣīṇe niḥśeṣāśāprakāśake ।
saṃmohamalinaṃ loke tamaḥ pāpamivodyayau ।।

kṣīṇabhṛṅgavihaṅgānāṃ nalinīnāṃ prasaṅginī ।
vikāsāsṃpasā mudrā nidreva samajāyata ।।

kāruṇyādiva śītāṃśurjyotsnāmṛtaśalākayā ।
sphāratāraṃ jagannitraṃ cakre vitimitaṃ tataḥ ।।

kṣayodayaparāvṛttirdrśitānekavibhramaḥ ।
saṃsāradinayāminyorjahāseva sudhākaraḥ ।।

netrānandasudhāvarṣe sukhasparśe niśākare ।
digvadhūvadanādarśe harṣe mūrta ivotite ।।

śroṇakoṭirdadarśāgre vimānamānanadyutim ।
kautukādanyarūpeṇa svargādbhuvamivāgatam ।।

tasminnapaśyatsamadāścatasrastridaśāṅganāḥ ।
diśaścandrodayānandavihārāyeva saṃgatāḥ ।।

tāsāṃ madhye varākāraṃ ramamāṇaṃ vyalokayat ।
taruṇapremasaṃbhāramiva sākāratām gataḥ ।।

ratnamaṇḍaleyūrakirīṭikacirāmśubhiḥ ।
ālikhantamivāścaryamamaryādaṃ diśāṃ mukhe ।।

tasya tāmadbhutām dṛṣṭvā saṃbhogasukhasaṃpadam ।
mene sa sukṛtākhyasya taroḥ sphītāṃ phalaśriyam ।।

prītyā tena kṛtātithyaḥ svādupānāśanādibhiḥ ।
tāṃ śroṇakoṭikarṇo atha nināya rajanīṃ sukham ।।

tārākusumavātāliprabhā prābhātikī tataḥ ।
anityateva śaśinaścakre lakṣmīparikṣayam ।।

kṣayaṃ kṣapāyāṃ yātāyām bhānau bhuvanacakṣuṣi ।
udite sarvabhūtānām sukhaduḥkhaikasākṣiṇi ।।

vimānaṃ suranāryaśca kṣasṇādadṛśyatāṃyayuḥ ।
vinaṣṭavadanacchāyaḥ puruṣaścāpatatkṣitau ।।

tatastasyāpatat pṛṣṭhe śunāṃ saṃgho atibhīṣaṇaḥ ।
trailokyaśāpapāpotthaḥ kleśarāśirivākhilaḥ ।।

sa taigrīvāmukhārabdhamāṃsagrāsāgrakarṣaṇaiḥ ।
ākrandirudhirakṣīrairbhakṣyamāṇaḥ kṣayaṃ yayau ।।

dinānte punarāyāntaṃ tadvimānamapaśyata ।
catasro apsarāsastāśca puruṣaḥ sa ca kāntimān ।।

taṃ śroṇakoṭikarṇo atha papracchātyantavismitaḥ ।
sakhe kimetadāścaryaṃ dṛśyate kathyatāmiti ।।

sa tena pṛṣṭaḥ provāca vayasya śrūyatāmidam ।
tvāṃ śroṇakoṭikarṇākhyaṃ jānāmi sukṛtocitam ।।

abhavaṃ vāsavagrāme duṣkṛtī paśupālakaḥ ।
paśūnāṃ māṃsamutkṛtya vikrītaṃ satata mayā ।।

piṇḍapātāya saṃprāpto māmāryaḥ karuṇānidhiḥ ।
kātyāyanākhyaḥ provācaḥ viramāsmāt kukarmaṇaḥ ।।

hiṃsāmayo hyayaṃ kleśo duḥsahaḥ sāhasaiṣiṇām ।
svaśarīre patatyeva chinnamūla iva drumaḥ ।।

ityahaṃ vāryamāṇo api tenānāryaḥ kṛpātmanā ।
yadā na virataḥ pāpāt tadā sa prāha māṃ punaḥ ।।

divā tvaṃ kuruṣe hiṃsāṃ sarvathā yadi nirdayaḥ ।
rātrau śīlasamādānaṃ gṛhāṇa samayānmama ।।

ityuktvā tena yatnena sarvasattvahitaiṣiṇā ।
dattā śīlasamādānamayī puṇyamatirmama ।।

kālena kālavaśagaḥ prāptaḥ so ahamimāṃ daśām ।
taptāṅgārasudhāvarṣairiva kīrṇo divāniśam ।।

rātrau śīlasamādānaphalaṃ hiṃsāphalaṃ dine ।
caryā matpuṇyapāpābhyām patitaḥ sukhaduḥkhayoḥ ।।

tasya me kuru kāruṇyaṃ sakhe kalusakāriṇaḥ ।
gatvā svadeśaṃmatputraṃ brūhi madvacasā rahaḥ ।।

asti me gṛhakoṭānte nikhātaṃ hemabhājanam ।
taduddhṛtya parityaktapāpavṛtti vidhīyatām ।।

āryakātyāyano nityaṃ piṇḍapātena pūjyatām ।
ityuktastena vinayāt tathetyuktvā jagāma saḥ ।।

sa dadarśa vrajan divyavimānamaparaṃ punaḥ ।
ratnapadmalatākāntaṃ dvitīyamiva nandanam ।।

tasmin sāṅgamivānaṅgaṃ saṃgataṃ divyayoṣitā ।
apaśyadvāsarārambhe puruṣaṃ ratnabhūṣitam ।।

tena prītyupacāreṇa kṛtātithyastathaiva saḥ ।
dinaṃ nināya dīrghaṃ ca kleśamadhye sudhāmayam ।।

atha vyomavimānāgrāt patite padminīpatau ।
apūryata jagad ghorairduḥkhairiva tamobharaiḥ ।।

tataḥ kṣapāpatirjyotsnāṃ vamanneva kṣapājaḍaḥ ।
śanakaiḥ pāṇḍurogīva gauradyutiradṛśyata ।।

sukumāre dināloke rātrau rākṣasayoṣitā ।
bhakṣite alakṣyata śaśī kapālabalasaṃnibhaḥ ।।

vyāpte candrikayā loke kālacandranacarcayā ।
vimānamagamat kkāpisā ca svargamṛgekṣaṇā ।।

vimānapatitaḥ so api puruṣaḥ sarvarūpayā ।
śanaiḥ saptabhirāvartaiḥ śatapadyā viveṣṭitaḥ ।।

sā tasya mūrdhni vivaraṃ kṛtvā mastiṣkaśoṇitam ।
āsvādayantī śanakaiścakāra śuṣiraṃ śiraḥ ।।

athāruṇakaracchanne socchvāsavadāne dine ।
bībhatsadarśanakleśādiva mīlitatārake ।।

prādurāsan punardivyavimānaṃ sā ca kāminī ।
yuvā sa cādbhutatanurdivyābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ ।।

pṛṣṭo ativismayāt tena svavṛttāntaṃ jagād saḥ ।
dvijo ahaṃ vāsavagrāmanivāsī manasābhidhaḥ ।।

taruṇī prātiveśyasya patnī malayamañjarī ।
abhūnmama bhujaṅgasya svairiṇī vallabhā bhṛśam ।।

paradāraratergrāme vyagrā me kṣamate matiḥ ।
minagnā viṣayagrāme samagrā me kṣayaṃ gatā ।।

āryakātyāyanaḥ pāpaṃ jñātvā mām cauryakāmukam ।
dayāvidheyaḥ kāruṇyāt provāca vijane śanaiḥ ।।

parāṅganāṅgasaṃsargaprītyā rūparateḥ kṣaibam ।
anaṅgāgnau patannāśaṃ pataṅgaṃ iva mā gamaḥ ।।

aho āsaktaraktānāṃ saṃpatanapramādinām ।
kāminām hiṃsakānāṃ ca paradārādaraḥ param ।।

pṛthu pravepathu svāpaśramavihvalānām gṛdhrāṅganāmukhanikhātanakhakṣatānām ।
saṃmohane paravadhūvihitaspṛhāṇāṃ romāñcakāriṇi paraṃ narake ca kāmaḥ ।।

tasmādasmānnivartasva vatsa kutsitakarmaṇaḥ ।
jāyate pātakaṃ sparśe śunāmevāśucau ratiḥ ।।

ityahaṃ kṛpayā tena niṣiddho apyaviśuddhadhīḥ ।
aniruddhena rāgeṇa baddhastāmeva nātyajam ।।

vijñāya māmavirataṃ tataḥ kātyāyano dadau ।
mahyaṃ śīlasamādānaṃ dinacaryāhitodyataḥ ।।

dinaśīlasamādānāt parastrīgamanānniśi ।
iyaṃ me puṇyapāpotthā sukhaduḥkhamayī sthitīḥ ।।

gatena vāsavagrāmaṃ vācyaḥ putro mama tvayā ।
suvarṇamagniśālāyāmasti gūḍhaṃ dhṛtaṃ mayā ।।

vṛttiḥ kāryā tadudbhṛtya pūjyaḥ kātyāyanaśca saḥ ।
praṇayāditi tenoktaḥ śroṇakoṭiryayau tataḥ ।।

so apaśyaddivyalalanāmagre maṇivimānagām ।
lakṣmīṃ lāvaṇyadugdhābdheranāyāsodgatāmiva ।।

tasya vimānapādeṣi caturṣu snāyusaṃyutam ।
sa dadarśātidurdaśaṃ baddhaṃ pretacatuṣṭayam ।।

sāpi taṃ pratyabhijñāya saṃbhāṣya snigdhayā girā ।
surocitaṃ dadau tasmai rasavat pānabhojanam ।।

bhuñjānasaṃjñayāṃ dūrāt pretairdainyena yācitaḥ ।
sa dadau kṛpayā tebhyaḥ kākebhya iva piṇḍikāḥ ।।

piṇḍo busatvamekasya prayāto anyasya lohatām ।
svamāṃsatvaṃ tṛtīyasya caturthasya prapūyatām ।।

vilokya tatkṛpāviṣṭaḥ sa teṣāṃ kaṣṭaceṣṭayā ।
papraccha tanmukhacchāyām vicchāyīkṛtapaṅkajām ।।

pṛṣṭā tadadbhutaṃ tena uvāca sā mṛgekṣaṇā ।
na śroṇakoṭirṇaiṣāṃ dattaṃ bhavati tṛptaye ।।

brāhmaṇasyāsya bhāryāhaṃ pūrvapādābalambinaḥ ।
nandanāmnaḥ sunandākhyā vāsavagrāmavāsinaḥ ।।

dvitīyapādasaṃsaktaḥ putro me niṣṭhurābhidhaḥ ।
paścātpādāvalambinyau dāsī ceyaṃ snuṣā ca me ।।

nakṣatrayogapūjāyām purā sajjīkṛate mayā ।
bhaikṣyopahāre me gehamāryakātyāyano aviśat ।।

mayā cittaprasādinyā piṇḍapātena so arcitaḥ ।
kurvanneva yayau kāntyā vaimalyānugrahaṃ diśām ।।

tataḥ snātvā samāyātastūrṇaṃ patirayaṃ mama ।
patpiṇḍapātamākarṇya pramidāya mayoditam ।।

kopāduvāca māṃ kasmād viśikhaḥ śramaṇaḥ śaṭhaḥ ।
apūjiteṣu pūjyeṣu busārhaḥ pūjitastvayā ।।

iti mohādanenokte putro apyeṣa jagād mām ।
pāke pūrvāśanāyogyaḥ sa kiṃ nāśnātyayoguḍān ।।

iyaṃ snuṣā me satataṃ pūrvabhakṣyāvabhoginā ।
mayokte śapathaṃ cakre svamāṃsādanavādinī ।।

iyaṃ dāsī ca bhaikṣyāṇā cairyāttadvyayakāriṇī ।
ākṣiptā cākarot satyaṃ pūyaśoṇitavādinī ।।

tatra te pretatām yātāḥ svavākyasadṛśāśanāḥ ।
ahaṃ tvāryaprasādena divyabhogopabhoginī ।।

tvayā tvāryaśamāptena vaktavyā duhitā mama ।
santi hemanidhānāni gṛhe catvāri te pituḥ ।।

tānyuddhṛtya yathāyogaṃ bhajasv asvajanisthitim ।
pūjanīyaḥ piturbhrātā nāmnā kātyāyana sadā ।।

sa ḥ śroṇakoṭikarṇastvaṃ gaccha deśaṃ tyaja śramam ।
varṣā dvādaśa saṃpūrṇāḥ svagṛhānnirgatasya te ।।

ityuktvā taṃ samādiśaya tasya pretacatuṣṭayam ।
suptasyaiva muhūrtena svadeśāptimakārayat ।।

utthitaḥ so api sahasā svadeśodyānakānanāt ।
viyogaśokātpitarau śuśrāvāndhyamupāgatau ।।

bhikṣudvijātithigaṇe pūjyamāne surālaye ।
svakaṃ pitṛgṛhaṃ dṛṣṭvā paraṃ vismayamāyayau ।।

niścitya sarvaṃ bhāvānāṃ kṣaṇikatvādanityatām ।
sneharāgaṃ samutsṛjya tatrasthaḥ samacintayat ।।

aho saṃmohanidreyaṃ nirantato divāniśam ।
svapnamāyāvilasitaiḥ karotyadbhutavibhramam ।।

janmavartmapradā mātā pitā bījavapatkhagaḥ ।
pānthapūjāsanaṃ kāyaḥ ko ayaṃ niyamasaṃgamaḥ ।।

śriyaḥ saṃsārābhrabhramaparicitāḥ kāñcanarucā
āśā dig nirbandhāstaḍita iva nirlepacapalāḥ ।
vapuḥ sarvāpāyaiḥ kṣayabhayanikāyaiḥ parigataṃ
jarārogodvegaistadapi na virāgastanubhṛtām ।।

śriye svastisamāptaye svajanasyāyamañjaliḥ ।
dākṣiṇyaiḥ kṣamataṃ śrīṣu pravrajyaiva priyā mama ।।

iti dhyātvā sa pitarau samāśvāsyāptalocanau ।
buddhau dharmapathe śuddhe śamadhāmni nyaveśayat ।।

sārthabhraṣṭaścirāyāt kṛśo api svajanasya ca ।
aluptasattvavibhavānnakṛpāspadatāṃ yayau ।।

anukampasva yadyetaṃ saṃsārakleśavihvalam ।
sataḥ kasyānukampyāste saṃpatsaṃparkanitspṛhāḥ ।।

paśupālakaviprastrīsaṃdeśādi yathoditam ।
nigadya tebhyaḥ kanakaprāptipratyayalakṣaṇam ।।

śāntaḥ kātyāyanaṃ prāpya pravrajyāṃ sa samādade ।
mugdhānām yadviṣādāya tatprasādāya dhīmatām ।।

sa samāsādya viśadaṃ sritaḥprāptiphalaṃ tataḥ ।
sakṛdāgāmyanāgāmiphalamarhatphalaṃ tathā ।।

traidhātuko vītarāgaḥ samaloṣṭāśmakāñcanaḥ ।
ākāśapāṇitulyo abhūdasicandanayoḥ samah ।।

śrāvastyām veṇugahane jinaṃ jetavane sthitam ।
bhagavantaṃ yayau draṣṭuṃ so atha kātyāyanājñayā ।।

praṇitātakṛtātithyaḥ prītyā bhagavatā svayam ।
sa śroṇakoṭīkarṇo atha babhāṣe harṣanirbharaḥ ।।

bhagavān dharmakāyena dṛṣṭo ayaṃ śrotravartmani ।
adhunā rūpakāyena puṇyairālokito mayā ।।

analpasukṛtaprāpyamidaṃ taddarśanāmṛtam ।
pītvā na tṛptimāyānti vañcitā eva te param ।।

aspṛhasyāpi te mūrtiḥ kurute kasya na spṛhām ।
nirlopasyāpi te dṛṣṭiraho harṣeṇa limpati ।।

tvatkathā tvadanudhyānaṃ tvatprāptistvanniṣevaṇam ।
etāḥ kuśalamūlānāṃ sphītāḥ phalasamṛddhayaḥ ।।

iti śrutvā bhagavatā prasādenābnhinanditaḥ ।
tadādiṣṭaṃ śamārāmaṃ sa vihāramavāptavān ।।

tasyāspadaṃ samabhyetya praṇayādbhagavānapu ।
śrutvāsya madhuraṃ dharmaṃ svādhyāyaṃ praśaśaṃsa saḥ ।।

tāṃ śroṇikoṭikarṇasya dṛṣṭvā praśamasaṃpadam ।
bhikṣubhirbhagavān pṛṣṭaḥ pūrvavṛttamabhāṣata ।।

vārāṇasyāṃ purā samyaksaṃbuddhe kāśyapābhidhe ।
nirvāṇadhātau niḥśeṣakāryatvāt parinirvṛte ।।

kṛkināmanṛpaścaityaṃ tasya ratnairakārayat ।
svayaṃ tatpuṇyasaṃbharaṃ svargaṃ vaktumivodgatam ।।

śīrṇasthāpitasaṃskāre tasmin saṃjñādhṛtaṃ dhanam ।
tatputraḥ prāptarājyo atha na dadau lobhamohitaḥ ।।

athottarāpathāyātaḥ sarthavāho arthadābhidhaḥ ।
pradadau pṛthivīmūlyaṃ tatkṛte karṇabhūṣaṇam ।।

kālāntaropagato api datvā cānyaddhanaṃ mahat ।
praṇidhānaṃ sa kṛtavān bhūyāsaṃ puṇyavāniti ।।

sa śroṇakoṭikarṇo ayaṃ puṇyaiḥ prātapadaṃ mahat ।
tadvidhenaiva saṃyātaḥ karṇabhūṣaṇalakṣaṇaḥ ।।

prasthānasamaye mātā śrāvitā paruṣaṃ vacaḥ ।
yasmādanena tenāsya babhūvāsya śramo mahān ।।

madhyeṣu mahataḥ śuklaguṇasatkarmavāsasaḥ ।
kṛṣṇakarmalavāṃśo api sphuṭa evāvadhāryate ।।

sukṛtasacivaḥ sattvetsāhaḥ pravāsasakhī dhṛtiḥ
viṣamataraṇe vīryaṃ seturvipadyadhikā kṛpā ।
śamaparicitā paryante ca prasādamayī matiḥ
pariṇatiriyaṃ puṇyaprāpteḥ sphuratphalaśālinī ।।

iti kṣemendraviracitāyām bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ śroṇakoṭikarṇāvadānaṃ nāmonaviṃśatitamaḥ pallavaḥ ।।

āmrapālyavadānam ।

dvijihvasaṅge kathamasti vṛttiranekamukhye kathamasti saukhyam ।
karmāntabandhe asti kathaṃ svaśaktiḥ prajñāprakarṣe kathamastyapāyaḥ ।।

mithilāyāṃ videheṣu jalasattvābhidho nṛpaḥ ।
abhūd bhujabhujaṅgasya viśrāntapṛthivībharaḥ ।।

khaṇḍo nāma mahāmātyastasyākhaṇḍalasaṃpadaḥ ।
babhūvāśeṣaṣāṅguṇyaparijñānabṛhaspatiḥ ।।

nītijñagauravāttasya nṛpe vyaktaṃ nalokini ।
sadābhavanmukhaprekṣī sarvaḥ kāryavaśājjanaḥ ।।

gatānugatikatvena pravāhapraṇayī bharaḥ ।
vardhate vāryamāṇasya svajanasya jalasya ca ।।

sarvaṃ tanmayamālokya janaṃ mātsaryamūrcchitāḥ ।
mantriṇaḥ saṃhatāstasya vinipātamacintayan ।।

te praviśyāśramam rājñastāṃ tasya prabahviṣṇūtām ।
muhuḥ śaṅkāspadaṃ kṛtvā śaśaṃsurbhedakovidāḥ ।।

tadgirā śaṅkito rājā tasya vaimukhyamāyayau ।
abalābālabhūpālā varṇapratyayāḥ param ।।

aśaṅkyādapi śaṅkante śaṅkādoṣe apyaśaṅkitāḥ ।
aviśeṣajñacapalā bhūpālāḥ kākaśaṅkinaḥ ।।

prabhorviraktiliṅgāni vilokyāmātyapuṃgavaḥ ।
svasutau gopasiṃhākhyau saśaṅkaḥ svairamabravīt ।।

dhūrtairme vītaviśvāsaḥ piśunairnṛpatiḥ kṛtaḥ ।
pratyayaṃ naiti hṛdaye vidāryāpi pradarśite ।।

viraktaḥ sthagitālāpadarśanaśravaṇaḥ prabhuḥ ।
śepha iva vṛddhasya yātaḥ śithilatāṃ mama ।।

piśunodbhūtabhedasya premṇaḥ saṃdhirna vidyate ।
na maṇiḥ śliṣyāti punaḥ pāṣāṇaśakalīkṛtaḥ ।।

dvijihṇakuṭilakrāntaḥ prabhuścandanapādapaḥ ।
na yātyarthakriyākārī guṇavānapi sevyatām ।।

kathaṃ nṛpanidhānārthī kuśalaṃ bhajate naraḥ ।
ghoradveṣaviṣāviṣṭadvijihvāghātavihvalaḥ ।।

tasmādvrajāmaḥ saṃtyajya dveṣadoṣeṇa bhūpateḥ ।
śaṅkāśalyamaye vṛtte me asmin deśe sthitena kim ।।

dakṣā rakṣākṣamāḥ śūrāḥ prabhutārthāḥ susaṃhatāḥ ।
santaḥ santi viśālāyāṃ vāsastatra mamepsitaḥ ।।

iti bruvāṇaḥ putrābhyāṃ tathetyuktaḥ sa sānugaḥ ।
udyānagatimānena prayayau saparicchadaḥ ।।

prayāṇaṃ nṛpatirjñātvā nivartanasamudyataḥ ।
yatnenāpi na taṃ prāpa notsṛṣṭaṃ labhyate punaḥ ।।

mūrkhāḥ satsu kṛtāvajñā vimuhyante kṣaṇena taiḥ ।
yāti teṣāṃ tu sarvatra ko api nārthī kṛtārthatām ।।

dhīmānamātyaḥ prāpto atha kṛṣṭo vaiśālikairguṇaiḥ ।
pūjitaḥ praṇayācāraiḥ saṃghamukhye pade sthitaḥ ।।

tadbuddhivibhavāptaśrīḥ so atha tatpramukho gaṇaḥ ।
kadācidanayāllekhe na parābahvapātratām ।।

atha kālena siṃhasya mantrisūnoḥ kanīyasaḥ ।
ajāyata sutā kāntā cailā nāma guṇocitā ।।

dvitīyā copacailākhyā sutā jātāsya sundarī ।
nanmanyeva tayoḥ prāha nimittajño vicakṣaṇaḥ ।।

cailāyāstanayo bhāvī pitṛhantā mahīpatiḥ । guṇavānupacailāyāḥ pūrṇalakṣahṇavāniti ।। 
jyeṣṭho mantrisutaḥ śauryādgopaḥ prauḍhamadoddhataḥ ।
udyānamardanakṣepairgaṇānāṃ dveṣyatām yayau ।।

tatpiturgauravāttasmai sānujāya vimanyavaḥ ।
viśālaśālatāmante jīrṇodyānadvayaṃ daduḥ ।।

sugatapratimāṃ cakre tatraikaḥ sukṛtocitām ।
vihāraṃ vaibhavodāraṃ bhuvanābharaṇaṃ paraḥ ।।

atha pitrā balotsiktaḥ sutaḥ pratyantamaṇḍale ।
gaṇakopabhayādgopaḥ karmāntopārjane dhṛtaḥ ।।

kālena tridivaṃ yāte tasmin mantrivare gaṇaiḥ ।
kanīyasastu sādhutvāt siṃhastasya pade dhṛtaḥ ।।

gopaḥ piturasaṃprāpya padaṃ gaṇavimānitaḥ ।
taddeśavāsavirasaḥ parihāramacintayat ।।

vāstavya kaṇṭakākīrṇe vyāghrāghrāte varaṃ vane ।
anekasvāmisaṃbhinnajane na tu viśṛṅkhale ।।

nānāmatakriyālāpaḥ kathamārādhyate gaṇaḥ ।
samīhitaṃ yadekasya datanyasmai na rocate ।।

itmānī sa saṃcintya gatvā rājagṛhaṃ puram ।
bimbisāraṃ narapatiṃ guṇaśriyamaśiśriyat ।।

sa tena mānitaḥ prītyā tasya viśrambhabhūrabhūt ।
cirarucyeva tatkālamābhāti guṇasaṃgatiḥ ।।

rājño atha bimbisārasya vallabhā pañcatāṃ yayau ।
tadviyogāgnisaṃtaptaṃ taṃ vicintya sa buddhimān ।।

upacailāṃ sutāṃ bhrātustadvivāhocitā vadhūm ।
gūḍhacārī tadādeśāt vaiśālakapurīṃ yaya ।।

kanyā gaṇopabhogyauva na kasmaicitpradīyate ।
iti vaiśālikaiḥ pūrvaṃ svadeśe niyamaḥ kṛtaḥ ।।

tatpure dvārarakṣāyai yakṣasthānāvalambinī ।
parapraveśe kurute śabdaṃ ghaṇṭī paṭīyasī ।।

sa praviśya tato bhrāturgūḍhamudyānacāriṇīm ।
upacailāṃ samāhatuṃ gataścailāmavāptavān ।।

yātastaṃ rathamāruhya ghaṇṭāśabdādabhidryutam ।
sa hatvā vīrapuruṣānavāpa nṛpateḥ puram ।।

tamūce devakanyeyaṃ prātā vimanasātmanā ।
pitṛhantā suto hyāsyā nimittajñena sūcitaḥ ।।

tasmādeṣā narapatermahiṣī na tavocitā ।
tvayi jīvati jīvanti prajānāṃ sarvasaṃpadaḥ ।।

ityuktastena tāṃ dṛṣṭvā tyuktaṃ naiva śaśāka saḥ ।
niruddhaḥ karmaṇā hyeva tanmukhālekhyalekhayā ।।

so avadat kka kadā dṛṣṭa putreṇa nihataḥ pitā ।
svayaṃ mayābhiṣektavyaḥ suto yady bhaviṣyati ।।

ityuktvā nṛpatiḥ kanyāṃ pariṇīyābhavatsukhī ।
kṛtakarmorminirmāṇe prabhavanti na buddhayaḥ ।।

bhoginastasya kālena tasyām sūnurajāyata ।
jyotiṣkacarite yasya vṛttamuktaṃ pitṛdruhaḥ ।।

tapovanamṛgādhānamṛgayāvyasane vane ।
evaṃvidho hyabhūttasya muniśāpaḥ sutākṛtiḥ ।।

atrāntare mahānnāma vaiśālikagaṇāgraṇīḥ ।
kanyāmāmravanātprāpa kadalīskandhanirgatām ।।

sā tasya bhavane kāntā vardhamānā śanaiḥ śanaiḥ ।
vidadhe vipulāṃ prītiṃ dānacintāṃ ac cetasi ।।

praṇayādāmrapālīti bandhubhiḥ sā kṛtābhidhāḥ ।
sūnuhīnamina tyaktvā bālyaṃ yauvanamādade ।।

tadvivāhodyatasyātha na sehe tatpiturgaṇaḥ ।
gaṇopabhogyā kanyeti samayasya vyatikramam ।।

pitaraṃ duḥkhasaṃtaptaṃ sametyātha jagād sā ।
bhavāmi gaṇabhogyaiva kiṃ tveṣa samayo yadi ।।

ekasyopari nānyasya praveśaḥ svapade sthitiḥ ।
paṇaḥ kārṣāpaṇaśataiḥ pañcabhiḥ pratyahaṃ mama ।।

saptāhenaiva vicayaḥ karyo veśmani nānyadā ।
ityasmin samaye va dhyaḥ sarvaścaiva vyatikramī ।।

iti tatsamayaṃ jñātvā tatpiturvacasā gaṇaḥ ।
akārod bāḍhamityuktvā dṛḍhaniścayamādarāt ।।

tataḥ saratnabhavane varābharaṇabhūṣite ।
hemaharmyasamārūḍhā dideśa dinacandrikām ।।

tataḥ paṇīkṛtaḥ kāmī yo yastāṃ samupāyayau ।
tasya tasyābhavat tasyāḥ prabhāveṇaujasaḥ kṣayaḥ ।।

draṣṭumeva na śekuste kiṃ punaḥ spraṣṭumākulāḥ ।
bhujaṅgabhogasaṃruddhāṃ tāṃ candanalatāmiva ।।

tataḥ sā sundarī bheje yauvanasyāpi yauvanam ।
guruṇā stanabhāreṇa madhyabhaṅgabhayapradam ।।

smarasaṃbhogarahitaṃ tattasyā rūpamadbhutam ।
śvabhrahemalatāpuṣpamiva niṣphalatāṃ yayau ।।

kautukāśāvinodāya nānādeśāntarāgataiḥ ।
akāri citrakārairbhūpālapratikṛtirgṛhe ।।

vidhāya citralikhitān sā krameṇa nareśvarān ।
dadarśa bimbirāsaya rūpaṃ ratipateciva ।।

tamālokyaiva sahasā samudbhūtamanobhavā ।
sa yena likhitastatra taṃ papraccha kutūhalāt ।।

ko ayaṃ sakhe prītilatāmādhavo vasudhāpatiḥ ।
prīṇāti locane yasya sudhāparicitā ruciḥ ।।

dhanyā kā nāma bhūbharturasya praṇayabhāgiṇī ।
lakṣyaṃ saubhagyajaṃ garvamurvaśyāḥ saṃhṛtaṃ yayā ।।

iti pṛṣṭatayā svairaṃ tāmūce citrakovidaḥ ।
bhūpatirbimbasāro ayaṃ sāraṃ sukṛtasaṃpadām ।।

śuaryarūpatulārohe devāḥ ke nākanāyakāḥ ।
śaṅke karoti naivāsya manmatho vā manoratham ।।

ityukte tena sā tasthau bhūpālanyastalocanā ।
sahasaivābhilāṣeṇa navīnābhimukhīkṛtā ।।

atrāntare bimbisāraḥ svairaveśmani nijane ।
kathānte gopamavadat kiṃcitsmitasitādharaḥ ।।

śrūyatāṃ yanmama sakhe kiṃcinmanasi vartate ।
niryantramitrasvacchandavādaḥ ko api sudhārasaḥ ।।

vaiśālikaurvarārohā gaṇaiḥ sādhāraṇikṛtā । rambhorūḥ śrūyate kāntā rambhāgarbhasamudbhavā ।। kavkatprabhāvavinaṣṭāśaistejasvipraṇayocitā । sā tairna dūṣitādyāpi mātaṅgairiva padminī ।।

śravaṇādeva sānandamaparyuṣitakautukam ।
na karoti manaḥ kasya tatstrīratnamayonijam ।।

abhilāṣi manastasyāṃ śrotāya jātaṃme saha cakṣuṣā ।
tadguṇaśrutidhanyāya śrotrāya spṛhayāmyaham ।।

ityukte bhūmipatinā gopastaṃ prayabhāṣata ।
bhujaṅgagaṇasaṃruddhaḥ sa rājan mānmatho nidhiḥ ।।

atyalpaskhalitaṃ prāpya duḥsahāpātadurgamaḥ ।
eṣa te viṣamaḥ panthā darśito viṣameṣuṇā ।।

labhate sā na nirgantuṃ na yuktaṃ gamanaṃ ca te ।
kimasmin viratopāye vadāmyubhayasaṃśaye ।।

ityuktastena nṛpatirnotkaṇṭhāgrāhamatyajat ।
vidvāṃso apyucitām nītiṃ na smaranti smarāturāḥ ।।

vaiśālikapurīṃ yāto gopena sahito atha saḥ ।
praviveśānyaveśena mandiraṃ hariṇīdṛśaḥ ।।

sā citradarśanenaiva dṛṣṭvā paricitaṃ dṛśoḥ ।
naranāthaṃ savailakṣyalakṣaṇaṃ kṣitimaikṣata ।।

lajjāniruttare tasyāḥ kampavyatikare param ।
raṇantī rasanā cakre svāgataṃ nṛpaterivaḥ ।।

vilokya dhanyatāmānī tatra citre nijaṃ vapuḥ ।
tāṃ lāvaṇyanadīṃ rājā nayanāñjalinā papau ।।

lajjāveśena sundaryāmābhijātyena bhūpatau ।
ābaddhamainayoḥ kṣipraṃ gopastāṃ sasmito avadat ।।

ayaṃ te citralikhitākāradhyānāvadhānataḥ ।
vyaktaṃ bhakṣiviśeṣena devaḥ pratyakṣatāṃ gataḥ ।।

tvayāyaṃ likhitaścitre tvamanena tu cetasi ।
na jāne yuvayoḥ ko nu prayātaḥ premadūtatām ।।

ityādibhiḥ kathābandhaiḥ parīpūrṇapramodayoḥ ।
yadyadeva smarādiṣṭam tattadāsvādatām gatam ।।

ghaṇṭāravākule loke rājā pracchannakāmukah ।
saptarātramanālokye tasthau tadbhavane rahaḥ ।।

lateva puṣpitā kāle tasmādgarbhamavāpya sā ।
cakre viditavṛttāntaṃ taṃ lajjāvanatā śanaiḥ ।।

āsanne viśmavicaye datvāsmai nṛpatiryayau ।
bhāviputraparijñānapratyayādaṅgulīyakam ।।

yāte bhāsvadvapiṣu nṛpatau saṃmate locanānāṃ sadyaḥ prodyadvirahatimirākrāntimīrākrāntimīlanmukhābjā ।
sābhūtsāyaṃtanatanutarāpāravātābhibhūtā
śokocchvāsavyatikaravatī hāsahīnā niśeva ।।

kapolaṃ pāṇipadmena saṃkalpena mahīpatim ।
navaṃ tānavamaṅgena vahantī nimimīla sā ।।

tataḥ kālena kalyāṇī pratibimbopamaṃ pituḥ ।
ajījanatsā natayaṃ vinayaṃ sādhudhīriva ।।

vardhamāne śanaistasmin kāle bimba ivaindave ।
bimbisārasya putro ayamiti lokeṣu paprathe ।।

apavādaparaistaistaistaṃ pratyanucittairyadā ।
bādhante śiśavaḥ krīḍāprasaṅge amarṣasaṃyatāḥ ।।

tataḥ sā preṣayāmāsa putraṃ vidyārjanocitam ।
vaṇiksārthena mahatā sāṅgulīyaṃ pituḥ padam ।।

bimbisāro api saṃprāpya sadṛśākāramātmajam ।
harṣadṛptaḥ pariṣvajya cakre tasya parigraham ।।

vṛttāṇte viśrute tasminnāmrapālyāh sakautukaiḥ ।
bhikṣubhirbhagavān pṛṣṭastatkathāmavadajjinaḥ ।।

pure rājagṛhe rājavallabhodyānakānane ।
babhūva mālatī nāma pūrvamudyānapālikā ।।

sā kadācit prasādārdraṃ puraḥ prāptaṃ yadṛcchayā ।
pratyekabuddhaṃ rājaṣiṃ cūtapuṇpaipūjayat ।।

ayonijā nṛpasyāhaṃ patnī syāmiti tatra sā ।
praṇidhānaṃ puraścakre tasya cittaprasādinī ।।

puṇyapuṣpaphalabhogaśālinī saiva divyatanurāmrapālikā ।
ityudāracaritā niśamya te bhikṣavaḥ sapadi vismayaṃ yayuḥ ।।

iti kṣemendraviracitāyām bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ āmrapālyavadānaṃ nāma viṃśatitamaḥ pallavaḥ ।।

jetavanapratigrahāvadānam ।

dṛṣṭaṃ muṣṭiniviṣṭapāradakaṇākāraṃ narāṇāṃ dhanaṃ
dhanyo asau yaśasā sahākṣayapadaṃ yadyasya vidyotate ।
dīnānāthagaṇārpaṇopakaraṇībhūtaprabhūtaśriyaḥ
puṇyārāmavihāracaityabhagavadbimbapratiṣṭhādibhiḥ ।।

śrīmān babhūva śrāvastyāṃ datto nāma gṛhābhipaḥ ।
sutastasya sudatto abhūdākaraḥ puṇyasaṃpadām ।।

sa bālya evālaṃkāraṃ yācakebhyaḥ sadā dadau ।
prāgjanmavāsanābhyāsaḥ kasya kena nirvāyate ।।

nityamābharaṇatyāgātparaṃ pitrā nivāritaḥ ।
nadīsamuddhṛtānyasmai sadaivānyānyadarśayat ।।

nidhidarśī sa sarvatra pitari tridivaṃ gate ।
dīnānāthapradānena babhūvānāthapiṇḍadaḥ ।।

kṛtadānah sa kālena putravān putravtsalaḥ ।
abhūt putravivāhārthī kanyānveṣaṇayatnavān ।।

kanyakāṃ yācituṃ kāṃcit puraṃ rājagṛhaṃ tataḥ ।
madhuskandhābhidhaṃ dakṣaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ visarsarja saḥ ।।

āsādya magadhān rājagṛhaṃ nagarametya saḥ ।
mahādhanaṃ gṝhapatiṃ yayāce kanyakām dvijaḥ ।।

anāthapiṇḍado nāma śrāvastyāmasti viśrutaḥ ।
tatputrāya sujātāya kanyāyām dehītyuvāca saḥ ।।

so abravīdeśa saṃbandhaḥ paramo asmatkulocitaḥ ।
vaṃśe asmākaṃ tu kanyānām śuklamādīyate mahat ।।

śataṃ śataṃ rathāgryāṇāṃ gajāśvāśvatarasya ca ।
dāśīnicayaniṣkānāṃ dīyatāṃ yadi śakyate ।।

ityukte tena taṃ vipraṃ sasmitaḥ pratyabhāṣata ।
anāthapiṇḍadagṛhe dāsye śulkaṃ tadalpakam ।।

brāhmaṇenākhile tasmin kanyāśulke pratiśrute ।
tamādarādgṛhapatirbhojanāya nyamantrayat ।।

sa bhuktvā vividhaṃ tatra bhakṣyabhojyamayantritaḥ ।
rātrau visūcikākrāntaścukrośa vipulavyathaḥ ।।

ye annamaśnanti laulyena niśi nidrāsukhāpaham ।
janmakarma kathaṃ kuryuḥ paralokasukhāya te ।।

tatyājāśucibhītyā taṃ gṛhātparijano bahiḥ ।
āspadaṃ nairapekṣyasya jātyā dāsajanaḥ śaṭhaḥ ।।

śubhena karmaṇā tasya saṃprāptastena vartmanā ।
samaudgalyāyanaḥ śāriputraḥ kāruṇyapeśalaḥ ।।

taṃ vaṃśasya dalāgreṇa nirlikhyāpi tathā mṛdā ।
prakṣālya dharmamādiśya tau tasya yayatuḥ śanaiḥ ।।

so api cittaṃ tayoragre prasādya tyaktavigrahaḥ ।
caturmahārājikeṣu deveṣu samājāyata ।।

tatra viśravaṇādeśānmartyaloke niketane ।
sa cakre śibiradvāre pūjādhiṣṣṭhānasaṃnidhim ।।

lekhavijñātasaṃbandhaviścayo atha yathoditam ।
anāthapiṇḍadaḥ śulkamādāya svayamāyayau ।।

sa saṃbandhigṛhaṃ prāpya dadarśāścaryakāriṇīm ।
śikharākārarājārhabhakṣyasaṃbhārasaṃpadam ।।

sa vismayādgṛhapatiṃ papraccha svacchamānasaḥ ।
bhūribhakṣyptsavaḥ ko ayamapi rājā nimantritaḥ ।।

sa taṃ babhāṣe bhagavān buddhaḥ saṃghaparigrahaḥ ।
mayā nimantritaḥ saṃghe so ayam mama mahotsavaḥ ।।

iti buddhābhidhānena jātaromāzncakaṇṭakaḥ ।
indusyandirivālkinnaḥ sahasaiva babhūva saḥ ।।

aviditaparamārthe kasyacinnāmamātre
sphurati sahajabhāvaḥ ko api janmānubandhaḥ ।
abhinavaghananāde vyaktaharṣabhilāṣaḥ
spṛśati lalitanṛtyodvṛttavṛttiṃ mayūraḥ ।।

so avadadvadanāmbhojasaṃjātābhinavadyutiḥ ।
ka eṣa bhagavān buddhaḥ kaśca saṃgho abhidhīyate ।।

iti pṛṣṭo gṛhapatistena provāca sasmitaḥ ।
aho bata na jānīṣe śāstāraṃ bhuvanatraye ।।

saṃsārapāśabhītānāṃ śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇaiṣiṇām ।
jina yastaṃ na jānāti sa loke vañcitaḥ param ।।

kiṃ tena mohalīnena viphalīkṛtajanmanā ।
ajñānataraṇopāyaṃ vayo yena vyayīkṛtam ।।

gotamo bhagavān buddhaḥ śākyarājakuladbhivaḥ ।
saṃbudhyānuttaraṃ samyaksaṃbodhimanagārikaḥ ।।

paścāt pravrajitānām ca tasyaivānugrahātparam ।
bhikṣūṇāṃ gatarāgāṇām samūhaḥ saṃgha ucyate ।।

sa eṣa buddhapramukhaḥ saṃghaḥ svakuśalaiṣiṇāḥ ।
mayā puṇyapaṇaṃ prāpyaṃ praṇayena nimantritaḥ ।।

iti tadvacanaṃ śrutvā tatsmṛtvānāthapiṇḍadaḥ ।
buddhālambanabhāvena niśi nidrāṃ samāyayau ।।

rajanyāṃ yāmaśeṣāyāṃ samākṛṣṭa ivetsukaḥ ।
prabhātamiti sa jñātvā puradvāreṇa niryayau ।।

śibikādvāramāsādya saṃprāpta iva devatām ।
madhuskandhena nirdiṣṭaṃ śreyaḥpanthānamāptavān ।।

bhagavāṃstaṃ tataḥ prāpya sa tṛṣṇārta ivāmṛtam ।
babhūvānupamāsvādaṃ pramodāmodanirvṛtaḥ ।।

taṃ dṛṣṭvā sādaraṃ dūrāt chāyātarumivādhvagaḥ ।
avāpa gatasaṃtāpaḥ śrāntiṃ viśrāntiśītalām ।।

tasya taddarśaneva vimalābhigataḥ manaḥ ।
śaratsamāgameneva ghanadhvāntojjhitaṃ nabhaḥ ।।

sa ko api puṇyaśīlānāmanubhāvaḥ prasādinām ।
bhavanti yatprasādena nirvighnāścittavṛttayaḥ ।।

so acintayadaho mohavihīnasya hi me tathā ।
anucchedavikāro ayaṃ jātaḥ praśamasaṃpadaḥ ।।

vañcito asmi na yatpūrvaṃ dṛṣto ayaṃ bhagavān mayā ।
nādhanyānāmiyaṃ yāti mūrtirlocanagocaram ।।

amṛtamadhirodārā dṛṣṭirdyutiḥ śaśipeśalā taruṇakaruṇāyattā vṛttiḥ prasādamayī matiḥ ।
ayamatiśayaṃ pratyāsannaḥ karoti virāgatāṃ vigatarajasāṃ niḥsaṃsāraḥ priyo api parigrahaḥ ।।

iti cittaprasādena cintayannupasṛtya saḥ ।
vidadhe tasya sānandaḥ pādapadmābhivandanam ।।

bhagavānapi tatprāptiprasādānandalakṣaṇam ।
uvāha vadanacchāyaṃ pūrṇakāruṇyapūritam ।।

dṛṣṭimāśvāsajananīṃ kāmaṃkāmapi tasya saḥ ।
visasarjojjvalāṃ janmarajaḥśuddhyai sudhānadīm ।।

athāsya bhagavān bhradrāṃ vidadhe dharmadeśanām ।
caturṇāmāryasatyānāṃ pratibhāvavidhāyinīm ।।

sa śāsanāddhi saṃvyastasamastakleśasaṃtatiḥ ।
nijaṃ janma nivedyāsmai praṇatastamabhāṣataḥ ।।

atikrānto asmi bhagavan bhavantaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ ।
vipannavāsanābhyāsaḥ saṃsāre na rame param ।।

karotyakuśalaṃ dūre śubhamāśu prayacchati ।
sūcayatyucitācāraṃ mahatamavalokanam ।।

sukhārhaṃ tvadvihārāya vihāraṃ paramādarāt ।
ratnasārapurodāraṃ svapuraṃ kārayāmyaham ।।

karotu tatra bhagavān satataṃ sthityanugraham ।
dhanairāsevito asmābhiḥ saparyāparicaryayā ।।

ityarthanāṃ tathetyasya bhagavān pratyapadyata ।
praṇayuprārthanābhaṅgapragalbhā na hi sādhavaḥ ।।

bhagavantamathāmantrya śrāvastīṃ sa purīṃ yayau ।
tadādiṣṭena sahitaḥ śāriputreṇa bhikṣuṇā ।।

tatra jetakumāreṇa hiraṇyārghoṇa bhūyasā ।
dattaṃ kāñcanamādāya vihāraṃ tamasūtrayat ।।

bhaktyutsāhādathārambhakṛtasāhāyyakah suraiḥ ।
vihāraṃ tridivākāraṃ cakārānāthapiṇḍadaḥ ।।

tatra jetakumāro api bhaktyā bhagavataḥ param ।
yaśaḥpuṇyapratiṣṭhāyai vidadhe dvārakoṣṭhakam ।।

ath atīrthyāstamālokya vihārārambhamadbhutam ।
sāpavādavivādena cakrurdveṣākulāḥ kalim ।।

raktākṣapramukhasteṣām mātsaryātkṣudrapraṇḍitaḥ ।
sapakṣa iva kṛṣṇāhiścakitaḥ purataḥ sadā ।।

ruddhe vihārasaṃbhāre tena vādajayāvadhi ।
anāthapiṇḍadagirā śāriputraḥ samāyayau ।।

raktākṣo atha tamāhūya prabhāvotkarṣadarśane ।
indrajālabalotphullaṃ sahakāramadarśayat ।।

śāriputraprabhāvotthairvipulaistanmukhānilaiḥ ।
unmūlitaḥ śakalatāṃ tīrthyotsāha ivāpa saḥ ।।

raktākṣavihitāṃ phullakamalāṃ padminīṃ tataḥ ।
paṅkaśeṣāṃ dvipaścakre śāriputravinirmitaḥ ।।

ratkākṣavakṣonikṣiptaḥ saptaśīrṣamahoragaḥ ।
śāriputreṇa nikṣiptastārkṣyapakṣāgramārutaiḥ ।।

tadāhūto atha vetālaḥ śāriputreṇa kīlitaḥ ।
prerito mantravirtyeṇa raktākṣaṃ hantumudyayau ।।

vetālābhihatastrāsānnaśyanmānamadajvaraḥ ।
śaraṇaṃ pādapatitaḥ śāriputraṃ jagāma saḥ ।।

raktākṣastena bhaṅgena śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ ।
pravrajyāyām vītarāgaḥ śuddhāṃ bodhismavāptavān ।।

tīrthyāstvanye paridveṣakrodhapāramitāṃśavaḥ ।
tatra karmakaravyājāttasthurbhikṣavadhodyatāḥ ।।

te atha dharmadruhaḥ kāle śāriputreṇa lakṣitāḥ ।
taddṛṣṭipātamātreṇa babhūvurmaitramānasāḥ ।।

āśayānuśayaṃ dhātuṃ prakṛtiṃ ca vicārya saḥ ।
dharmadeśanayā teṣāṃ dideśānuttarāṃ daśām ।।

atha tasya vihārasya nirvighnārambhakarmaṇi ।
anāthapiṇḍadaṃ prāha śāriputraḥ smitānanaḥ ।।

vihārasūtrapātasya tulya eva kṣaṇe mahān ।
haumo vihāraḥ saṃvṛttastuṣite devasadmani ।।

etadākarṇya saṃjātaprasādadviguṇāntaraḥ ।
hemaratnavarāgāraṃ vihāraṃ samakārayat ।।

vibhavairatha rājārhaiḥ pathi tenopakalpitaiḥ ।
vijñaptistridivaiḥ sārdhamāyayau bhagavān jinah ।।

tadāgamanaharṣeṇa prasanne bhavanatraye ।
anāthapiṇḍadastasmai vāridhārāmapātayat ।।

tasmin yadā na pradeśe vāridhārā papāta sā ।
tadā bhagavato vākyāt tvaritaṃ patitānyataḥ ।।

taṃ dṛṣṭvā kautukāt pṛṣṭo bhikṣubhirbhagavān punaḥ ।
uvāca śrūyatāmetad vāristambhasya kāraṇam ।।

anena pūrvabuddhebhye asminnevedamāspadam ।
pratipāditamityeṣā vāridhārānyataścyutā ।।

anenaiva purā samyaksaṃbuddhāya vipaśyine ।
ayameva varārāmapradeśaḥ pratipāditaḥ ।।

buddhāya śikhine prādāt puṣyajanmanyayaṃ punaḥ ।
tato dadau viśvabhuve jināya raghijanmani ।।

bhavadattābhidho bhūtvā kakucchandāya dattavān ।
dadau bṛhaspatirbhūṭvā kanakākhyāya tāyine ।।

kāśyapāya punaścāyaṃ prādādāṣāḍhajanmaniḥ ।
anenaivādhunā mahyaṃ deśo ayaṃ pratipāditaḥ ।।

kālena sudhanākhyo ayaṃ maitreyāya pradāsyati ।
sattvavān kṣāntiśīlatvānnidhānānyeṣa paśyati ।।

punaścāyaṃ gṝhapatirbhūtvā hemapradābhidhaḥ ।
cakre pratyekabuddhasya saṃskāraṃ parinirvṛtau ।।

ratnakumbhe tadasthīni dhṛtvā tatpraṇidhānataḥ ।
adhunā ratnakośārhaḥ saṃjāto ayaṃ suvarṇabhās ।।

śrutveti śāsturvacanābhidhānaṃ te bhikṣavaḥ sāramivāmṛtasya ।
kartuḥ pratiṣṭhārjitapūrṇapuṇyapuṣpādhivāsena bhṛśaṃ nananduḥ ।।

iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ jetavanapratigrahāvadānaṃ nāma ekaviṃśaṃ pallavaḥ ।।

pitāputrasamādānam ।

aho mahārhaṃ maṇivanmahattvaṃ bhavyā bhajante guṇagauraveṇa ।
vinā guṇaṃ yadvapuṣām gurutvaṃ sthūlopalānāmiva niṣphalaṃ tat ।।

śrīmān purā śākyapure narendraḥ śuddhodanaḥ śuddhisudhānidhānam ।
vairāgyayogātsugatatvamāptaṃ smṛtvā sutaṃ sutsukatāmavāpaṃ ।।

so acintayatpuṇyaguṇādhivāsaṃ sarasvatīvāsasaroruhaśri ।
manaḥ prasādasya vilāsasaudhaṃ drakṣāmi sūnorvadanaṃ kadāham ।।

ehīti taddarśanalālasena ye ye mayā jetavanaṃ visṛṣṭāḥ ।
te te tadālokananirnimeṣaṃ tatraiva tiṣṭhantyamṛtaṃ pibantaḥ ।।

saṃpreṣitastasya mayā sa nāyayau yo apyātmatulyaṃ praṇayādudāyī ।
sa lekhahastastridivābhirāme tatraiva lekhatvamirābhiyātaḥ ।।

saṃdeśavākyaṃ prahitaṃ mayā yat tadvismṛtaṃ tasya mukhena nūnam ।
sarvo hi nāma svahitābhilāṣī dhatte parārthe kila śītalatvam ।।

vilokanenaitya niṣiñca tūrṇaṃ pīyūṣapūreṇa mamāṅgasaṅgam ।
niḥsaṅgato viśramatāṃ muhūrtaṃ dayāvidheyaḥ kuru bandhukāryam ।।

ityetadākarṇya kathām sa kuryāt kṣaṇaṃ vilambaṃ mama darśane api ।
taccetasaḥ pallavapeśalasya na hi svabhāvaḥ praṇayāvabhaṅgaḥ ।।

manoratheneti puraḥ prayāte taddarśanāyeva dharādhināthe ।
pravrajyā vyañjitatatprasādaḥ samāyayau harṣarasādudāyī ।।

dṛṣṭvā tamānandavipūrṇamānasaṃ pravrajyayā tatsadṛśānubhāvam ।
utkaṇṭhitaḥ kuṇṭhitadhairyavṛttiḥ saṃmohamūrcchāṃ nṛpatiḥ prapede ।।

sa labdhasaṃjñaḥ śiśiraiḥ payobhiḥ papraccha taṃ kiṃ nu sameṣyatīti ।
so apyabravīddeva dinairbhavantamasaṃbhṛtaiḥ sādarameṣyatīti ।।

tataḥ prayāteṣu dineṣu keṣu vyomnā śanairbhikṣugaṇānuyātaḥ ।
sahāyayau nākasadām nikāyaiḥ sarvārthasiddhairbhagavān kumāraḥ ।।

dyusundarīpāṇisarojamuktamandāramālākalitaścakāśe ।
svargīyagaṅgāsphuṭaphenakūṭavilāsahāsāṅga ivāmarādriḥ ।।

saṃghaṭṭabhinnābhrasakhaiḥ skhalidbhiḥ saśabdajāmbūnadakiṅkiṇīkaiḥ ।
babhurvimānaiḥ kakubhāṃ mukhāni bhaktyeva śāsturvihitastavāni ।।

nirantarairantarivārkatāraiḥ suraiḥ savidyādharasiddhasaṃghaiḥ ।
paryāptasaṃsaktasitātapatrairvyāptaḥ samāptiṃ gaganaṃ jagāma ।।

taṃ sarvalokopakṛtiprapannaṃ sarvākṛtiṃ sarvamayāvabhāsam ।
samāpatantaṃ nabhaso atha digbhyaḥ kṣiteśca sarve dadṛśuḥ kṣaṇena ।।

praharṣarāśiṃ janalocanānāṃ puṇyapramāṇaṃ sukṛtotsavānām ।
lokastamālokanidhiṃ vilokya samullalannucchalitādbhutormiḥ ।।

āścaryabhūtaṃ ruciraprabhāvamudāyinā sūcitamākalayya ।
jagadguruṃ bhūmipatiḥ kumāraṃ kṛtāñjalistaṃ praṇanāma dūrāt ।।

athāvatīryāryajanānuyātaḥ saṃpūjyamānaḥ praṇayena rājñā ।
sphīṭaprabhābhāsitadigvibhāgāṃ nyagrodhinīṃ ratnabhuvam viveśa ।।

hemāsanaṃ śāsanasaṃniviṣṭalokatrayaḥ saṃgatapādapīṭham ।
sa tatra ratnāṅkuracitrapatraṃ bhāsvadvapurmerun ।।

tanmānasendornayanāmṝtaughaṃ manorathaprārthanayopayātam ।
vilokayannirvṛtinirnimeṣaḥ kṣaṇaṃ kṣitīśastridaśatvamāpa ।।

sa taṃ jagādāśruniruddhakaṇṭhaḥ sotkarṣaharṣākulitaṃ kumāram ।
hārāgraratnapratibimbasaktaṃ praveśayan prītirasādivāntaḥ ।।

saṃtoṣaśītācalavat svabhāvāt sarve ramante kuśalasthalīṣu ।
kṛtastvayāsmākamayaṃ tu kasmāt satsūpakārī virahopadeśaḥ ।।

snehātpramodādguṇagauravācca dhīrdhāvatīyaṃ tvayi me prasahya ।
āliṅganāya sthirasaṃgamāya pādapraṇāmāya ca tulyameva ।।

yadvastu kiṃcidgaditaṃ mayā tat śrotavyameva praṇayoparodhāt ।
guṇojjhitaṃ vā virasakramaṃ vā na snehamohasya bhavatyavācyam ।।

pratyarṇaratnapratibimbitārkaprauḍhaprabhāprāvaraṇānyamūni ।
tvaṃ hemaharmyāṇi vihāya kasmāt vigāhase śūnyavanāntarāṇi ।।

kāntākarāvarjitahemakumbhasatsaurabhāmbhaḥpravarābhiṣiktaḥ ।
ekaḥ kathaṃ snāsi vikāsipāṃśusaṃtaptatoyāsu marusthalīṣu ।।

gaṇḍasthalāt kuṇḍalaratnakānti kiṃ lambitaṃ maṇḍanameva vetsi ।
kasmādakasmāttava niḥsukhasya na candanaṃ nandanaminduśubhram ।।

mahāvitāne śayane nṛpārhe śeṣe na kiṃ śeṣaviśeṣaśubhre ।
lakṣmīnavāliṅganabhogayogyā kathaṃ tanuste sahate kuśayyām ।।

kāntāsmitormipratimāṃśukārhaṃ kiṃ cīvarasyocitametadaṅgam ।
pāṇau ca līlākamalāspade asmin pātraṃ kathaṃ te priyamadya jātam ।।

ayaṃ vihārastava kaṇṭhapīṭhaḥ sotkaṇṭhakāntābhujabandhanārhaḥ ।
saṃbhogalakṣmīkṣapitapramodaḥ karotyakasmāt praṇayāvabhaṅgam ।।

rūpaṃ vilakṣīkṛtapuṣpacāpaṃ mattebhakumbhoccakucā vibhūtiḥ ।
ratervilāsppavanaṃ vayaśca kenāsamaste kalito virāgaḥ ।।

śratveti taṃ śīlanidhirbadhāṣe śaśāṅkalekhālalitasmitena ।
saṃkrāntanānānṛparatnarāgāṃ kurvannalakṣāmiva rājalakṣmīm ।।

rājan jarārogahateva na syāttaraṅgalolā yadi jīvavṛttiḥ ।
tatkasya na syādaniśaṃ praharṣapīyūṣavarṣī viṣayābhilāṣaḥ ।।

śamāmṛtāsvādanasusthirāṇāmapātanaṃ śūnyavanāntabhūmeḥ ।
vibhūtilīlāmadavihvalānāṃ harmyāṇi paryantanipātanāni ।।

sakuṅkumaiḥ snāntiḥ nṛpāḥ payobhiḥ sarāgatāṃ yaiḥ satataṃ prayānti ।
saṃtoṣaśīlastu manaḥ prasādaśuddhāmbudhautā vimalībhavanti ।।

śrotraṃ śrutenaivana kuṇḍalena dānena pāṇirna tu kaṅkaṇena ।
vibhāti kāyaḥ karuṇākulānāṃ paropakāreṇa na candanena ।।

etāni mohāhatavallabhāni saṃsaktamuktāṃśusitasmitāni ।
satāṃ na bhogyāni bhavanti bhūbhṛducchiṣṭaśiṣṭāni vibhūṣaṇāni ।।

rāgāturāṇāṃ ritupāpitānāṃ nidrā dhanadhyānavatāṃ na nāma ।
śayyāsu susparśavatīṣu rājñā sarvatra śāntaḥ sukhameva śete ।।

nirmokakāntena varāmśukena bhujaṅgavṛttirna tu cīvareṇa ।
pātraṃ pavitrāṇi samāplitāni pīyūṣamaitrāṇyaśanāni sūte ।।

chatrāṇi vakrkraṃ bhṛśamaprakāśaṃ manivilolaṃ vyajanānilaughāḥ ।
saṃsaktajāṅyaṃ hṛdayaṃ nṛpāṇāṃ kurvanti hārā haricandanārdrāḥ ।।

viyogarogānugatā vibhūtiḥ kāntāh kṣaṇāntā viraso vilāsaḥ ।
yasminnapāyaḥ satatānuśāyī sa kasya bhogaḥ subhagopayogaḥ ।।

jāḍyaṃ sajṛmbhaṃ janayatyajasraṃ tanoti tṛṣṇābhramamohamūrcchāḥ karotyasahyaṃ sarasatvameva bhogopabhogaḥ prasabhaprayogaḥ ।।

yadā sukhaśrīrnavacandralekhā prabhātapuṣpāṇyapi yaivanāṇi ।
karmormimālāgrahaṇaṃ śarītaṃ tadā mamāyaṃ gamito anurāgaḥ ।।

sacāmarāh sadhvajapuñjapaṭṭāḥ savājivālā dvipakarṇatālāḥ ।
svabhāvalolāḥ kila rājalakṣmyaḥ sarve vilāsāh kṣaṇabhaṅgasaṅgāḥ ।।

uktveti tattatkuśalāya rājñaścittaprasādaṃ paramaṃ vidhāya ।
sa śāntikallolasudhāpravāhaṃ kiran dṛśā pārṣadamāluloke ।।

manīṣiṇāṃ śākyakulodgatānāṃ saptāyutāni pratipādya dharmam ।
cakre sahasrāṇi ca sapta tatra saṃprāptaparyāptaviśeṣabhāñji ।।

śaklodanādyaiḥ kuśalopapannaiḥ gaṇe atha tattulyasahasrasaṃkhyaiḥ ।
droṇodanādyairamṛtpdanādyaiścittaprasādaḥ sumahānavāptaḥ ।।

kecidyayuḥ śrāvakabodhiyuktapratyekabodhau niratāśca kecit ।
samyak tathānuttarabodhisaktāḥ pare babhūvurgaganaprasannāḥ ।।

srotaḥ pariprāptaphalaṃ tato anye sakṛttathāgāmiphalaṃ tathānye ।
anye apyanāgāṃiphalaṃ tadāpurarhatphalaṃ kleśavimuktimanye ।।

ekastu tatrārjitapāpaśāpastamaḥsamūhopahitapramohaḥ ।
māyeyamityāha hasan janānāṃ satyasthitiṃ saṃsadi devadattaḥ ।।

nṛpaṃ tu vātsalyanilīnameva putrodayātpratyupajātadarpam ।
maudgalyabhikṣurjinaśāsanena maharddhibhirvītamadaṃ cakāram ।।

dṛṣṭvāpi rājā bhagavatprabhāvaṃ nātyadbhutam pauruṣameva mene ।
abhyāsalīnāni janasya nūnaṃ sotkarṣakṛtyāni na vismayāya ।।

athāparedyurbhagavān surendrasaṃpādite hemamahāvimāne ।
sumeruśīrrṣṇīva samānakāntau siṃhāsane ratnamaye nyaṣīdat ।।

brahmendramukhyeṣu tataḥ sureṣu tatropaviṣṭeṣu pṛthuprabheṣu ।
babhustaduṣṇīṣaśikhāvilāsaiścandrāṃśumālājaṭīlā ivāśāḥ ।।

anyonyasaṃghaṭṭavilolahārairdhanāvahāraistridaśairviśadbhiḥ ।
nirantarām tām bhavametya rājā dvāreṣu mārgānna caturṣu lebhe ।।

sabhrūbhramaistatra kuveramukhyairnivāryamāṇābhimatapraveśah ।
vicchāyavakraḥ skhalitābhidhāyī bhūbhṛtparaṃ niṣpratibho babhūva ।।

praveśitastairjinaśāsanena kadācidāsādya tadagrabhūmim ।
śuddhodanast apraṇipatya mūrdhnā cittaprasādena puro asya tasthau ।।

śāstā tu tasmai caturāryasatyaprabodhikāṃ dharmakathām dideśa ।
jñānena yā viṃśatiśṛṅgamasya satkāyadṛgbhūdharamapyabḥāṅkṣīt ।।

tataḥ sa gatvā kṛtakṛtyajanmā śuklodanaṃ prāpta bhajasva rājyam ।
svasyāvratīttaṃ bhagavatpradiṣṭaṃ tacchāsanaṃ modayituṃ na rājyam ।।

droṇodane rājyaparāṅbhukhe api vairāgyayogādamṛtodane ca ।
jagrāha śuddhodanasaṃpradiṣṭāṃ tāṃ rājalakṣmīmatha bhadrakākhyaḥ ।।

rājārhabhogairatha pūjayitvā jinaḥ janeśaḥ śucisaṃpraṇitaiḥ ।
nyagrodhadhāma pratipādya cāsmai śuddhodanaṃ śuddhamanoratho abhūt ।।

droṇodanasyāpi sutau yuvānau rājājñayā preraṇayā ca mātuḥ ।
ekastu yaḥ pravrajito aniruddhaḥ paro mahānnāma gṛhī babhūva ।।

athābhavaccetasi bhadraksya rājño viraktasya vanābhilāṣaḥ ।
vivekabhājāṃ praśamapravṛttaṃ navāpi lakṣmīrna mano ruṇaddhi ।।

tataḥ samāhūya sa devadattaṃ rājyābhiṣekapratipannacittam ।
uvāca me pravrajanasya kālaḥ samāgataḥ kiṃ bhavatābhidheyam ।।

taṃ pratyuvācāttavivekadambhaḥ susaṃvṛtaṃ saṃsadi devadattaḥ ।
rājanna rājye asti mamābhilāṣaḥ pravrajyayā tvatsadṛśo bhavāmi ।।

śrutveti rājā kuṭilasya tasya mithyāvinītasya kadarthavākyam ।
udīritaṃ śākyagaṇastavāyaṃ saṃkalpasākṣīti hasannuvāca ।।

athārthatāpopahataḥ pradadhyau bhogānurāgāditi devadattaḥ ।
mayā kimetadavipātamuktaṃ bhajeta vā pravrajito api rājyam ।।

rājyaṃ samutsṛjya nijaṃ vrajantaḥ śākyaṃ kumārāḥ saha bhadrakādyāḥ ।
śuddhodanaṃ niryayurāyavṛttaprītiṃ puraskṛtya rathairdvipaiśca ।।

vrajatsu sarveṣvatha devadattaḥ kirīṭasaktaṃ pṛthipadmarāgam ।
jahāra raktāktamivāmiṣārthī śyenaḥ prabhāpallavitāmbarārkam ।।

naimittikairuktamathāsya lakṣmadṛṣṭvā tadugraṃ narakaprayāṇam ।
cittaṃ sadoṣaṃ kila durnimittaṃ nimittamanyat punaruktameva ।।

kokālikhaṇḍotkaṭamorakāṇāṃ tithyādināmnām madadurmadānāṃ ।
saṃsūcitānyatyadhikāni tatra tathāvidhānairbahulakṣaṇāni ।।

bhūpapramodādatha bhadrako api tairdevadatapramukhaiḥ sahaiva ।
pravrajyayā cīvarapātrayogāt cakāra vairāgyamayīmiva kṣmām ।।

rājñastathā rājakumārakāṇāmutsṛṣṭahārāṅgadakuṇḍalānām ।
sāsro virāgādavatārya teṣāṃ keśānupālī kila kalpako abhūt ।।

mūrkhaḥ sa nīco api jinājñayaiva pravrajyayā pūjyataro babhūva ।
cittaprasādasya parasya manye na kāraṇaṃ paṇḍitatā najātiḥ ।।

sāmīcikāyāmatha bhadrako api jñātvā nṛpaḥ pārṣadikaṃ tamenam ।
nīcasya pādau kathamasya vande mahīpati sanniti niścalo abhūt ।।

tamabravīdaskhalitābhimānaṃ vikalpabhinnaṃ bhagavān vihasya ।
pravrajyayā mohamahānuvandhī saṃtyajyate jātimayo abhimānaḥ ।।

śrutveti rājñā saha rājaputraiḥ kṛte praṇāme pṛthivī cakampe ।
na devadattaḥ paruṣābhidhāyī padau vavande bhagavadgirāsya ।।

kampāt kṣitervismitamānasena pṛṣṭastato bhikṣugaṇena śāstā ।
uvaca rājā kila kalpasya janmāntare apyasya kṛtaḥ praṇāmaḥ ।।

purā yuvā kāśipure vilokya bhadrābhidhānām gaṇīkāṃ daridraḥ ।
sevām vyaghāt sundarakastadāsyai rāgo hi sarvavysanopadeṣṭā ।।

tayā visṛṣṭaḥ kusumoccayāya punahpunarbhṛṅga ivādhikārthī ।
tatsaṅgamānaṅgamanorathena śrāntaḥ sa babhrāma vanāntareṣu ।।

atrāntara śrāntataraḥ kṣitīśaḥ prāpto vanāntaṃ mṝgayārasena ।
taṃ brahmadattaḥ prasamīkṣya gītaṃ tasyāśṛṇocchannatanurlatābhiḥ ।।

navanavakusumāśayā kimevaṃ madhukaraṃ tāpahato asi gaccha tūrṇam ।
vikasitakamalānanābjinī sā bhavati hi saṃkucitā dināvasāne ।।

tasyā hi gītaṃ nṝpatirniśamya smitaprabhāghaṭṭitahārakāntiḥ ।
uvāca taṃ tīvrakarārkatāpaḥ ko ayaṃ sakhe gītarasābhioyogah ।।

so apyabravīdbhūmipate na nāma tapto ravistaptatarastu kāmaḥ ।
svakarmaduḥkhāni vihanti loke na grīṣmadagdhāni marusthalāni ।।

ityarthavadvākyaguṇārpaṇena sa bhūpatervallabhatāmavāpa ।
saṃvādasaṃsparśasubhāṣitaṃ hi keṣām c asatkārapadaṃ na yāti ।।

tenātha rājā vijane śramāturaḥ śītopacārairapanītatāpaḥ ।
prītyā tamādāya tataḥ sahaiva svarājadhānīmagamat kṛtajñah ।।

tatrāsya jīvaprada ityudantasaṃtoṣa saṃpūritacittavṛttiḥ ।
rājyārdhadānābhimukhaḥ sa tasthau cittānuvṛttasya kimasya deyam ।।

rājyārdhadānaprasṛte atha tasmin nācintayat sundarakaḥ kṛpāyām bhadrāṃ vinā rājyasukhena kiṃ me dhanyo hi tatprītisudhābhiṣiktaḥ ।।

mahmaṃ na rājyādyapi rocate ardhamakhaṇḍitālpāpi hi śobhate śrīḥ ।
ekārthayoge hi sadā vivādaḥ dvayorhi bhogaiḥ kalireva mūrtaḥ ।।

tasmānnṛpaṃ kuṇṭhamahaṃ nipātya samastarājyena bhavāmi pūrṇaḥ ।
kṣaṇaṃ vicintyetyanutāpataptaḥ tīvraṃ manaḥ svasya punaḥ pradadhyau ।।

kiṃ cintitaṃ nindyaparaṃ mayaitat ko ayaṃ prakāraḥ khalu tīkṣṇatāyāḥ ।
kṛtaghnasaṃkalpakalaṅkalepādaho nu lajjā nijacetaso api ।।

svastyastu rājyāya namaḥ sukhebhyaḥ saṃmohamātā kṣamatāṃ ca lakṣmīḥ ।
yeṣāmanāsvāditacintitānāmevaṃvidhā dhīḥ prathamaḥ svabhāvaḥ ।।

bhramaṃ vidhatte vidadhāti mūrcchāṃ nipātayatyeva tamastanoti ।
āghrātamātraiva karoti puṃsāmaho vināśaṃ viṣavallarī śrīḥ ।।

ciraṃ vicintyeti sa jātacittaḥ pratyekabodhirvimalaḥ prabhāte ।
abhyarthamāno api nareśvareṇa rājyaṃ n ajagrāha nivṛttatṛṣṇaḥ ।।

pratyekabuddhatvamavāptamenaṃ kālena dṛṣṭvā nṛpatirmaharddhiḥ ।
tatpādapadmacyutamaulimālyaścittaprasādocitamityavecat ।।

sa ko api satkarmavipākajanmā vandyo vivekaḥ praśamābhiṣekaḥ ।
yasya prabhāvādvirataspṛhāṇāṃ tyājyeva ratnākaramekhalā bhūḥ ।।

śrutveti rājñā kathitaṃ tadarthajātaṃ tadabhyarthanayā vidhāya ।
tatkalpakaḥ śāntipadaṃ prapede sevāntaraṅgaḥ kila gaṅgapālaḥ ।।

prāptaṃ tamayuttamakarmayogāt pravrajyayā sajjanapūjyabhāvam ।
rājā vavande praṇataḥ pṛthivyāḥ kampastadābhūdapi ṣaḍvikāraḥ ।।

so ayaṃ rājā vihitavinatirbhadrako brahmadatto
paśyopālī sa kila kuśalī kalpako gaṅgapālaḥ ।
ityāścaryaṃ bhagavaduditaṃ bhikṣavaste niśamya
svacchaṃ cittaṃ sukṝtaśaraṇe menire hetumeva ।।

iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ pitāputrasamādānam nāma dvāviṃśatitamaḥ pallavaḥ ।।

viśvaṃtarāvadānam ।

cintārantādadhkarucayaḥ sarvalokeṣvanindyā
vandyāste anyaiḥ puruṣamaṇayaḥ ke apyapūrvaprabhāvāḥ ।
yeṣāṃ naiva priyamapi paraṃ putradārādi datvā
sattvārthānām bhavati vadanamlānatā dainyadūtī ।।

bhagavān bhikṣubhiḥ pṛṣṭaḥ purā śākyapure jinaḥ ।
jagāda pūrvavṛttāntaṃ devadattakathāntare ।।

purī babhūva viśvākhyā viśvāsavasatiḥ śriyaḥ ।
viśvopakārasaktasyasukṝtasyeva janmabhūḥ ।।

saṃjayākhyo abhavat tasyāmamitratimirāṃśumān ।
netrānandasudhāsūtirvicitracarito nṛpaḥ ।।

tasya viśvaṃtaro nāma vadānyastanayo abhavat ।
apūrvatyāginā yena hṛtaṃ kalpatayoryaśaḥ ।।

īrṣyāvirahitāstulyaṃ vidagdhena prsādhitāḥ ।
satyena bhāratī yena dānena śrīḥ śrutena dhīḥ ।।

adyāpi yasya dikkāntākarṇābharaṇatām gatam ।
vibhāti ketakīgarbhapalāśaviśadaṃ yaśah ।।

sa kadāciddadau divyaratnālakāramarthine ।
athaṃ vijayasāmrājyamanorathaharaṃ tviṣā ।।

datte rathavare tasmin vismayenākhilo janaḥ ।
babhūvākrāṇtahṛdayaścintayā ca nareśvaraḥ ।।

mahāmātyānathāhūya harṣahīno mahīpatiḥ ।
uvācopacitodvegacintākrāntamanorathah ।।

datto rathaḥ kumāreṇa sa jaitraḥ śatrumardanaḥ ।
yatprabhāvārjitā seyaṃ mahārathavarūthinī ।।

lakṣmī sukhaniṣaṇṇā me yātā niścalatām tayā ।
rathe sauryapathe tasmin jayakuznje ca kuñjare ।।

iti rājavacaḥ śrutvā tamabhāṣanta mantriṇaḥ ।
rājan doṣastavaivāyaṃ vātsalyena pramādyataḥ ।।

dharmaḥ kasya na harṣāya dānaṃ kasya na saṃmatam ।
kiṃ tu mūlahatādvṛkṣānnivartante palārthinaḥ ।।

vikrītaḥ paradeśe ca rathastena dvijanmanā ।
ityuktvā mantriṇaḥ sarve śalyaviddhā ivābhavan ।।

atha kālena saṃprāpte vasante madanotsave ।
vipāke sukṛtasyeva hṛdayānandadāyini ।।

svayaṃgrahopajīvyasya madhormadhukarārthinaḥ ।
lokaḥ puṣpavanairyāto yaśobhiriva śubhratām ।।

aśokaṃ lokasacchāyamupakārodyataṃ drumam ।
madhu vidhūtaṃ saṃnaddhe kalikālaṃ kṛtaṃ jagat ।।

rājaputraḥ samāruhya kuñjaraṃ rājavardhanam ।
yayau phullān vane druṣṭumarthikalpatarustarūn ।।

vrajantaṃ prati sāmantaprayuktātaṃ dvijāḥ pathiḥ ।
babhāṣire samabhyetya svastivādapuraḥsarāḥ ।।

cintāmaṇirgīyase tvaṃ ślāghyo jagati jaṅgamaḥ ।
yasya saṃdarśanenārthī gāḍhamāliṅgyate śriyā ।।

dvāveva viśrutotkarṣavideṣau bhadrajanmani ।
dānārdrahastastvaṃ loke gajaścāyaṃ sthironnatiḥ ।।

asmabhyaṃ sukṛtpdāra kuñjaro ayaṃ pradīyatām ।
tvadanyena vadānyena dātumeṣa na śakyate ।।

ityarthitastaiḥ sotsāhaḥ sa tebhyastu dadau dvipam ।
sajīvamiva sāmrājyaṃ saśaṅkhadhvajacāmaram ।।

datvā bodhipradhānena praṇidhānena śuddhadhīḥ ।
ratharatnaṃ dvipendraṃ ca so abhūdānandanirbharaḥ ।।

śrutvaiva nṛpatirdattaṃ viśrutaṃ jayakuznjaram ।
rakṣāprakārarahitāṃ rājalakṣmīmamanyata ।।

sa rājyabhraṃśabhītena kupitena mahībhujā ।
niṣkāsitaḥ kumāro atha pratasthe praṇipatya tam ।।

mādrīdayitayā sārdhaṃ jālinaṃ nāma dārakam ।
kṛṣṇābhidhāṃ tathā kanyāmādāya sa yayau vanam ।।

vane api śeṣa ṃ sa dadau vāhanādikamarthine ।
samaṃ hi mahatāṃ sattvaṃ saṃpatsu ca vipatsu ca ।।

mādyrāṃ kadācidyātāyāṃ puṣpamūlaphalāptaye ।
brāhmaṇaḥkaścidabhyetya rājaputramabhāṣata ।।

paricārakāhīnāya caturau bālakāvimau ।
dehi mahyaṃ mahāsattvaṃ sarvado hyasi viśrutaḥ ।।

śrutvaitadavicāryaiva dārakau dayitau param ।
datvā sa tasmai sahasā sehe tadvirahavyathām ।।

dhanaputrakalatrādi loke kasya navallabham ।
dānādanyadvadānyānāṃ na dayāvatām ।।

atha mādrī samabhyetya bālakau bālavatsalā ।
apaśyantī puraḥ patyuḥ patitāpannamūrcchitā ।।

sā labdhasaṃjñā dīptena vyāptā śokakṛśānunā ।
śiśupradānavṛttāntaṃ śrutvaivābhūtpalāpinī ।।

tasyāścetasi duḥkhāgnirapatyasnehaduḥsahaḥ ।
priyapremānusṛtyaiva prayayau puṭapākatām ।।

atrāṇtare samabhyetya viprarūpaḥ sureśvaraḥ ।
bhṛtyārthī dayitām patnīṃ rājaputramayācata ।।

yācitastena sahasā śucaṃ jāyāviyogajām ।
dhiyā saṃstabhya sattvābdhiḥ sa tasmai vitatāra tām ।।

sadyaḥ pradānataralāṃ saṃtrastāṃ hariṇīmiva ।
so avadaddayitāmantaḥ kalayan bodhivāsanām ।।

samāśvāsihi kalyāṇi na śokaṃ kartukarhasi ।
svapnapraṇayakalpo ayamasatyaḥ priyasaṃgamaḥ ।।

śuśrūṣayā dvijasyāsya dharme te ramatām matiḥ ।
vilolalokayātrāyāṃ dharmaḥ sthirasuhṛt satām ।।

dṛṣṭvā sarve svajanasujanā bāndhavāścānubhūtāḥ
nyastā kaṇṭhe kṣaṇaparimalamlāyinī mitrālā ।
dāre putre kṣapitamaniśaṃ yauvanaṃ jīvitaṃ ca
prāpto nāptaśtiraparicayaḥ ko api dharmādṛte anyaḥ ।।

ityuktvā vallabhāṃ lobhaparityāgāduvāha saḥ ।
dyutiṃ vadanapadmena dhairyavṛttiṃ ca cetasā ।।

viyogaśokavikalāṃ mādrīṃ dṛṣṭvā kṛpākulaḥ ।
nijarūpaṃ samādhāya śacīpatiruvāc atām ।।

viṣādaṃ mā kṛthāh putri devo ahaṃ tridaśeśvaraḥ ।
arthibhyastvā dadātyeṣa tasmādasi mayarthitā ।।

adhunā saiva patyustvaṃ nyāsībhūtā mayārpitā ।
taṃ dadātyeṣa nānyasmau dīyate katham ।।

kariṣyāmi tavāvaśyaṃ dārakābhyāṃ samāgamam ।
ityudīrya sahasrākṣaḥ sahasāṇtaradhīyataḥ ।।

atha tau dārakau vipraḥ samādāyārthalipsayā ।
viśvāmitrapuraṃ gatvā lobhādvokretumudyatah ।।

viśyāmitraḥ parijñāya rājaputrasya dārakau ।
jagrāha mahatārthena bāṣpasaṃruddhalocanaḥ ।।

kālena tridivaṃ yāte viśvāmitramahīpatau ।
bheje viśvaṃtaro rājyaṃ paurāmātyagaṇārthitaḥ ।।

rājye viraktasya tasya dānavyasaninaḥ param ।
sattvena vardhamānarddhirna kaścid yācako abhavat ।।

tadvittapūrṇavibhavo brāhmaṇaḥ so api jambukah ।
kṛtaghnaḥ svaprabhāvānme saṃpadityabhyadhājjanam ।।

viśvaṃtaraḥ sa evāham devadattaḥ sa ca dvijaḥ ।
uktveti cakre bhagavān bhikṣūṇāṃ dānadeśanām ।।

ālambanaṃ śvabhraśatāvapāte ghorāndhakāre suciraprakāśaḥ ।
āśvāsanaṃ duḥsahaduḥkhakāle dānam narāṇāṃ paralokabandhuḥ ।।

iti kṣemendraviracitāyām bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ viśvaṃtarāvadānam nām atrayoviṃśaḥ pallavaḥ ।।

abhiniṣkramaṇāvadānam ।

hasati sakalalolālokasargāya bhānuḥ paramamamṛtavṛṣṭayai pūrṇatāmeti candraḥ ।
iyati jagati pūjyaṃ janma gṛhṇāti kaścit vipulakuśalasetuḥ sattvasaṃtāraṇāya ।।

purā śuddhodanaḥ śrīmān rājā śākyapure abhavat ।
yaśaḥśaśāṅkajanakaḥ sudhāsindhurivāparaḥ ।।

khalāsaktā svabhāvena lakṣmīrguṇigaṇārpitā ।
āścaryakāriṇā yena kṛtā satpakṣapātinī ।।

adyāpyakhiladiktīryavanāsaktairvivekibhiḥ ।
yaśobhiḥ śucibhiryasya munivratamivohyate ।।

syāmahaṃ śuddhamāteti purā praṇidhitaḥ kila ।
viśvakarmasuto martyamājagāmāmaladyutiḥ ।।

kīrtiḥ satpuruṣasyeva tasyābhūdvallabhā param ।
mahāmāyābhidhā devī candrasyeva kumudvatī ।।

sāpaśyaddantinaṃ śvetaṃ svapne kukṣau vihāyasā ।
gatamārohaṇaṃ śaile praṇatiṃ ca mahājanāt ।।

atrāntare bodhisattvastuṣitāt tridaśālayāt ।
garbhaṃ tasyāḥ samāpede svayaṃ lokānukalpayā ।।

vahantī bodhisattvaṃ sā garbhe bhuvananandanam ।
induṃ dugdhābdhiveleva babhūva pāṇḍuradyutiḥ ।।

ikṣvākurājavaṃśyena tena garbhasthitena sā ।
bhūrnidhānavatīvābhūd bhavyalakṣaṇalakṣitā ।।

babhūva dohadastasyā dānapuṇyamayodayaḥ ।
aṅkure apyavisaṃvādi sahakārasya saurabham ।।

atgha kālena saṃpūrṇaṃ sā lumbinīvane sthitā ।
asūta tanayaṃ devī divākaramivāditiḥ ।।

māturgarbhamalāspṛṣṭaṃ kukṣiṃ bhittvā sa nirgataḥ ।
tāṃ cakre atha svabhāvena svasthāṅgī vigatavyathām ।।

nirgacchanneva ruddho asau balajijñāsayā kṣaṇam ।
śakreṇa vajrasārāṅgastasyāśakyatvamāyayau ।।

jātamātaḥ śuiśurgatvā svayaṃ sapta padāni saḥ ।
diśo vilokayannūce suvyaktākṣarayā girā ।।

iyaṃ nirvṛtiḥ pūrvā ca gatirlokeṣu dakṣiṇā ।
paścimā jātirapyeṣā saṃsārādiyamuttarā ।।

iti tasya bruvāṇasya pṛthivī samakampata ।
tamakṣayabalaṃ dhartumaśakteva jagadgurum ।।

chatraṃ tasya yaśaḥ śubhraṃ sattvasmeraṃ sacāmaram ।
vyomāmbudhārādhautasya jagṛhustasya devatā ।।

asminnavasare pṛṣṭaḥ s vastrīyeṇāsitābhidhaḥ ।
nāradena prabhāṃ dṛṣṭvā kiṣkindhādristhito muniḥ ।।

kasmādarkaśatāloka ivālokaḥ pradṛśyate ।
tamodaridrāṃ yeneti girayaḥ saguhāgṛhāḥ ।।

vismayāditi tenoktaḥ so avadaddivyalocanaḥ ।
jātaḥ puṇyaprabhāso ayaṃ bodhisattvasya janmani ।।

acireṇaiva taṃ vatsa drakṣāvaḥ kuśalāptaye ।
ityuktvā munirānandād viśrāntisukhito abhavat ।।

putrajanmani sarvārthasiddhiṃ śuddhodanaḥ param ।
dṛṣṭvā sarvārthasiddho ayamiti nāmāsya nirmame ।।

śākyavardhananāmābhūd yakṣaḥ śākyapurāśrayaḥ ।
yatpraṇāmeṇa śākyānāṃ śiśavo nirupadravāḥ ।।

tatsthityā preṣitaḥ pitrā praṇāmāya saguhyakaḥ ।
taṃ bodhisattvamālokya nipapātāsya pādayoḥ ।।

athotsaṅge samādāya hṛṣṭastaṃ pṛthivīpatiḥ ।
lakṣaṇāni nimittajñaistasya dehe vyalokayat ।।

lakṣaṇajñāstataḥ sarve nṛpamūcuḥ savismayāḥ ।
deva divyakumāro ayaṃ lakṣaṇairupalakṣyate ।।

jāyate lakṣaṇairetairviśvaviśrāntaśāsanaḥ ।
śakrādhipaścakravartī bhagavān sa tathāgataḥ ।।

dīrghāṅgulidalau cakralāñchanau supratiṣṭhitau ।
aruṇau caraṇāvasya kāntau kamalakomalau ।।

rājahaṃsa iva prāṃśuḥ sajālāṅgulipallavaḥ ।
eṣa jānuyugaḥ śrīmānājānubhujabhūṣitaḥ ।।

sakośabastiguhyaśca nyagrodhaparimaṇḍalaḥ ।
dakṣiṇāvartaromāṅkaḥ pariṇāhasamonnatiḥ ।।

rajomalalavāspṛṣṭastajāmbūnadadyutiḥ ।
hastapādāṃsakaṇṭhāgraspaṣṭasaptacchadākṛtiḥ ।।

siṃhapūrvārdhakāyaśca bṛhatspaṣṭāṅgavigrahaḥ ।
catvāriṃśatsamāprotaśukladantaḥ sunāsikaḥ ।।

dīrghapratanujihvaśca meghadundubhiniśvanaḥ ।
abhinīlākṣagokṣmaḥ sahajoṣṇīṣamastakaḥ ।।

sitorṇāṅko bhruvorbhāgaḥ svastikoraḥsthalojjvalaḥ ।
lekhāśṛṅgābjahasto ayaṃ chatrākāraśirāḥ śiśuḥ ।।

rājannayam te tanayaścakravartī bhaviṣyati ।
samyaksaṃbodhisaṃbuddhaḥ sarvajño vā bhaviṣyati ।।

ityuktvā teṣu jāteṣu lebhe harṣaṃ mahīpatiḥ ।
saptabhidivasaiḥ śāsturjananī tridivaṃ yayau ।।

tasya janmani śākyānāṃ munīnāmiva śāntatā ।
dṛṣṭvā yadā śākyamunirnāmābhūtsa tadā śiśuḥ ।।

devānāmapi devo ayamiti niścitya tejasā ।
devātideva ityasya nāma cakre mahīpatiḥ ।।

nāradenātha sahitastattvadarśī tapovanāt ।
taṃ samabhyāyayau draṣṭumādarādasito muniḥ ।।

sa bodhisattvaṃ bālārkamiva kalpaprakāśanam ।
dṛṣṭvā vikāsivakrkraśrīrlebhe kamalatulyatām ।।

so abrāvīdvihitātithyaṃ nṛpatiṃ praṇataṃ muniḥ ।
rājan guṇagaṇeneva spṛhaṇīyo asi sūnunā ।।

etāni lakṣaṇānyasya mokṣalakṣmīsamāgamam ।
vadanti cakravartiśrīḥphalaṃ naiṣāṃ vinaśvaram ।।

asya bodhiprabhāveṇa saṃbuddhasy mukhāmbujam ।
dhanya padmākarasyeva netrapātraṃ kariṣyati ।।

vibudhāḥ śuddhasattvasya bodhidugdhamahodadheḥ ।
dhanyā vāgamṛtairasya bhaviṣyantyupajīvinaḥ ।।

puṇyabhāji jagatyasminneka evāsmi vañcitaḥ ।
etatsaṃdarśanaṃ yasya pūrṇakālasya durlabham ।।

ityuktvā nṛpamāmantrya gatvā vyomnā tapovanam ।
suprasannaṃ manaḥ kṛtvā dehatyāgamacintayat ।।

sa paryantopadeśāya nāradenābhicoditaḥ ।
tamuvācāmṛtaṃ vatsaṃ kumāraḥ kathayiṣyati ।।

adhigamyāmṛtaṃ tasmānnṛpasūnoranāmayam ।
tariṣyasi bhavāmbodhimityuktvā tanumatyajat ।।

śrīrasatkriyāṃ tasya kṛtvā sapadi nāradaḥ ।
yayau vārāṇasīṃ siddhyai lebhe kātyāyanābhidhām ।।

vardhamānaḥ kumāro atha sarvavidyāsu pāragaḥ ।
lipipravīṇo abhinavām lipiṃ brāhmīṃ vinirmame ।।

nāgāyutasamaprāṇe tasmin jagati viśrute ।
vaiśālikaiḥ priyāyāsmai preṣito mattakuñjaraḥ ।।

bhaviṣyati cakravartītyasya prātamupāyanam ।
devadattaḥ paridveṣāt taṃ jaghāna mahāgajam ।।

cyutaṃ cakarṣaṃ dvidataṃ nandaḥ sapta padāni tam ।
kumārastu tadutkṣipya prākārād bahirakṣipat ।।

ekanārāvanirbhinnasaptatālamahītalaḥ ।
chedyabhedyāstraśastreṣu sa evātiśayaṃ yayau ।।

tatatulyaguṇāṃ patnīṃ rājasūnuryaśodharām ।
avāpa viśrutāṃ loke śuddhaśīla ivonnatim ।।

atrāntare mahāvātavicyutaḥ saptayojanaḥ ।
saritpravāhasaṃrodhaṃ vidadhe vipuladrumaḥ ।।

sāṃ sphāratarusaṃruddhā rohikā nāma nimnagā ।
śīlabhraṣṭeva vanitā prayayau pratilomatām ।।

rājaputrastamutkṣipya bhaṅktvā vikṣupya taṃ drumam ।
nyavārayat prajāmatsyajalakallolaviplavam ।।

tataḥ kadācidudyāne haṃsaṃ niśitayantriṇā ।
devadattena nihataṃ kumāraḥ samajīvayat ।।

saṃtāpaṃ tadvivādena devadatto adhikaṃ yayau ।
na sahante hi kuṭilāstulyakulagoṇonnatim ।।

kadācid gopikā nāma kumāraṃ rājakanyakā ।
kandarparūpamālokya kimapyautsukyamāyayau ।।

śuddhodanaḥ sutasthaitāṃ jñātvā cittocitāṃ vadhūm ।
apūrayadvivāhena manmathasya manoratham ।।

naimittikāstato abhyetya nṛpamūcuḥ suniścayāḥ ।
putraste cakravartī vā munirvā saptame ahani ।।

tacchrutvā nṛpatiḥ sūnoścakrāvrtipadāptaye ।
pravrajyācakitaścintāṃ dinasaṃkhyāmayīṃ yayau ।।

lolāṃ sarvaḥ srhiyaṃ vetti śāntasthirasukhāmapi ।
atthāpi bhogaraktānāṃ saṃpatsvevādaraḥ param ।।

tataḥ kadācidudyānavihārāya nṛpātmajaḥ ।
prayayau rathamāruhya valgutuṅgaturaṅgamam ।।

sa vivarṇaṃ jarājīrṇam kīrṇaśīrṇaśiroruham ।
suśuṣkaparuṣākāraṃ dadarśa puruṣaṃ pathi ।।

sa taṃ dṛṣṭvā nijaṃ kāyamālokyācintayacciram ।
aho paryāptapāko ayaṃ kāyasyāsya jugupsitaḥ ।।

vayaḥ paryāptamāpto api paryāptaṃ nāśrayatyayam ।
atīva palitavyājājjarā vṛddhaṃ hasatyasau ।।

śarīre saṃtatasnāyupāśaprotāsthipañjare ।
vṛddhaḥ puṣṇāti manye ahamaho mohavihaṅgamam ।।

sārathe kiṃ karotyeṣa kiṃ na yāti tapovanam ।
asṃkocameti vṛddhasya dehena saha sā matiḥ ।।

vṛddho avalambate yaṣṭiṃ na tu dharmamayīṃ dhiyam ।
jarākuṭilakāyasya svabhāvo nirvivekatā ।।

jugupsāṃ janayatyeṣa vṛddhaḥ praskhalitākṣaraiḥ ।
vacobhiścyutadantābhairgalallālālavākulaiḥ ।।

naṣṭā dṛṣṭiḥ kṛśaḥ kāyaḥ śaktirluptā hatā śrutiḥ ।
tathāpi mohād dṛṣṭaiva vṛddhasya taruṇīpriyā ।।

dhatte dhavalatāṃ vṛddhaḥ kimetāmatigarhitām ।
lolā paraṃ viraktāpi yadyasyātipriyā tanuḥ ।।

iti cintayatastasya nirvedaḥ samajāyata ।
manyamānasya sāpāyaṃ kāyaṃ nicayamāpadām ।।

punaśca samaye anyasminnapaśyad vyādhitaṃ naram ।
vipakkakūṇapaprāyaṃ sapūyamiva pāṇḍaram ।।

sa pradadhyau tamālokya samuddiśya nijāṃ tanum ।
aho nu sahajaivāsmin kāye rogagaṇodgatiḥ ।।

idameva mahaccitramiyaṃ māṃsamayī tanuḥ ।
na yāti kledavaiklavyaṃ kṣaṇaṃ paryuṣīte api yat ।।

iti dhyātvā sa sodvegaḥ śarīravicikitsayā ।
babhūva rājyasaṃbhopgarāge vigatitādaraḥ ।।

athānyasmin kṣaṇe mālyavastrācchāditavigraham ।
dadarśa dehasatkāravyagrabandhujanaṃ śavam ।।

taṃ dṛṣṭvā sahasodvegadayāduḥkhaghṛṇākulaḥ ।
ciraṃ niḥsārasaṃsāraparihāramacintayat ।।
eṣa pretavanaṃ yāti saṃsaktāṃ hṛdaye vahan ।।
aho nu viṣayābhyāsavilāsādhyavasāyinām ।
nṛṇāmantyakṣaṇe kaṣṭā kāṣṭhapāṣāṇatulyatā ।।

udvegavāribhavasāgarabudbude asmin kālānilākulitakarmalatāgrapuṣpe ।
māyāvadhūnayanavibhramasaṃvibhāge puṃsāṃ ka eṣa vapuṣi sthiratābhimānaḥ ।।

noktaṃ kiṃcit parahitayutaṃ na śrutaṃ dharmayuktaṃ
naiva ghrātaṃ kuśalakusumaṃ satyarūpaṃ na dṛṣṭam ।
naiva spṛṣṭaṃ śamapadamiti vyaktamāsaktacintā-
viśrānto ayaṃ vahati sahasā niścalatvaṃ gatāyuḥ ।।

rājasūnurvicintyeti śarīraṃ vipadāplutam ।
aśeṣaviṣayāsaṅge parām naḥ snehatām yayau ।।

athāgre nirmitaṃ devaiḥ sa śuddhāvāsakāyikaiḥ ।
vyalokayat pravrajitaṃ pātrakāṣāyadhāriṇam ।।

taṃ dṛṣṭvaiva babhūvāsya pravrajyābhimukhī matiḥ ।
īpsitālokanaprītyā svabhāvo hi vibhāvyate ।।

virāgyakāraṇam tatra nṛpasūnoḥ pade pade ।
vilokya sārathiḥ sarvaṃ kṣitipāya vyanedayat ।।

kumāro atha piturvākyāt grāmālokanakautukī ।
vrajan pathi nidhānāni vivṛtāni vyalokayat ।।

tatpūrvapuruṣanyastaiḥ strīkarairutthitānyapi ।
yadā sa nāgrahīttāni tadā viviśurambudhim ।।

tataḥ sa karṣakān pāṃśuvyāptapāṇḍuśiroruhān ।
vidīrṇapāṇicaraṇān kṣutpipāsāśramāturān ।।

halakaddālaviṣamollekhapakṣavraṇāditān ।
vilokya kleśavivaśān babhūva karuṇākulaḥ ।।

vidhāya dayayā teṣāṃ draviṇauradaridratām ।
sa vṛṣāṇāṃ vṛṣarataḥ kleśamuktimakārayat ।।

tataḥ pratinivṛtto atha sānujaḥ pārthivātmajaḥ ।
madhyāhnapṛthusaṃtāpe taralastaraṇitviṣaḥ ।।

rathaghoṣonmukhaśikhiśyāmīkṛtadigantaraḥ ।
svedavārikaṇākīrṇaḥ prabhāsnigdhavanasthalīm ।।

so avaruhya rathāttatra gaṇḍaskhalitakuṇḍalah ।
viśrāṇtyai viśrutayaśā jambucchāyāmaśiśriyat ।।

sa babhārorasi vyaktāṃ svedāmbukaṇasaṃtatim ।
vapurāśleṣalalitāṃ hārasyeva kuṭumbinīm ।।

chāyāsu parivṛttāsu śanakaiḥ sarvaśākhinām ।
tasya jambūtarucchāyā na cacāla tanustanoḥ ।।

sā tasya śītalacchāyā tāpaklāntimavārayat ।
saṃsāraviratasyeva tīvravairāgyavāsanā ।।

putradarśanasotkaṇṭhastaṃ deśamatha bhūpatiḥ ।
ājagāma gajotsarpatrastabhramaracāmaraḥ ।।

chāyāṃ sa niścalāṃ dṛṣṭvā kumārasya prabhāvataḥ ।
gauravādbhutasaṃprāptaḥ praṇataṃ praṇanāma tam ।।

tataḥ sa sahitaḥ pitrā nagaraṃ gantumudyataḥ ।
apaśyat puraparyante śmaśānaṃ śavasaṃkulam ।।

sa dṛṣṭvā kuṇapākīrṇamaśivaṃ śivakānanam ।
sodvegaṃ sārathiṃ prāha sthagitasyandanaḥ kṣaṇam ।।

sārathe paśya jantūnāṃ kāyāpāyamatīṃ daśām ।
dṛṣṭvedamapi rāgārdraṃ mano mohapramādinām ।।

parastrīdarśanāttṛptaṃ netramāsvādya sādaram ।
asyāsatyavatī jihvā paśya kākena kṛsyate ।।

asyāḥ stanamukhanyastanakhollekhasukhasthitiḥ ।
khṇḍayatyadharaṃ gṝdhraḥ kāmīva madanirbharah ।।

ete dṛṣṭaniṣakṭavāyasaśakṛnniṣṭhivinaḥ pādapā
mūrcchantīva vipākapūyakuṇapāghrāṇena niṣkūṇitāḥ ।
dṛṣṭvā gṛdhravidāryamāṇamasakṛt kīrṇārdratantra śavaṃ
bhūyo vātavilolapallavakarairācchādayantīva ca ।।

kṣībasyevācalasya drutahṛtahṛdayā jambukī kaṇṭhasaktā
raktābhivyaktakāmā kamapi nakhamukhollekhamāsutrayantī ।
āsvādyāsvādya yūnaḥ kṣaṇamadharadalaṃ dattadantavraṇāṅkaṃ lagnānaṅgakriyāyāmiyamatirabhasotkarṣamāviṣkaroti ।।

ityuktvā jātaviratirbhavabībhatsakutsayā ।
kalayan kleśanirvāṇaṃ praviveśa purāntaram ।।

tatra harmyagatāpaśyat taṃ kanyābhijanojjvalā ।
mṛgajā nāma mṛgajānodinī mṛgalocanā ।।

sarāgataralā dṛṣṭḥ śrotrasaṃcāriṇī param ।
abhūttaddarśane tasyāḥ sahasaiva virekiṇī ।।

sā tadālokanenaiva bālā lajjāsahiṣṇūnā ।
smareṇeva samākṛṣṭā sakhīṃ prāha puraḥsthitām ।।

kā dhanyā lalanā loke sparśenāsya śaśitviṣaḥ ।
yasyā madanasaṃtaptā tanurnirvāṇameṣyati ।।

nirvāṇaśabdaṃ śrutvaiva rājaputraḥ samīhitam ।
tāṃ dadarśonmukhaḥ padmavanānīva diśan dṛśā ।।

sa tasyāstena vacasā vapuṣā va prasāditaḥ ।
hāraṃ suvṛttaṃ cittaṃ ca vikṣepāsyai guṇojjcalam ।।

ālokanānukūlyena bhāvaṃ vijñāya bhūpatiḥ ।
putrasyāntaḥpurapade tāmādāya nyaveśayat ।।

ṣaṇṇāṃ kāṇtāsahasrāṇāṃ vṛtamantaḥpuraṃ tataḥ ।
viveśa rājatanayaḥ priyāṃ śāntiṃ vicintayan ।।

atrāṇtare narapatiṃ prāhurnaimittikāḥ sphuṭam ।
munirvā cakravartī vā prātaste bahvitā sutaḥ ।।

tataḥ saṃcintya nṛpatiḥ pravrajyām cakitaḥ param ।
akārayat puradvāraguptiṃ ruddhagamāgamām ।।

droṇodanamukhān bhrātṝn dvāreṣu viniveśya saḥ ।
nagarasya svayaṃ makhye tathā sāmātyasainikaḥ ।।

rājaputrādatha prāptagarbhā devī yaśodharā ।
vabhāṣe śāradīva dyauḥ pratyāsannendupāṇḍurā ।।

ekarātrāvaśeṣe atha nagaradvārarakṣaṇe ।
śamapravṛttārkamabhūt pravrajyābhimukhaṃ dinam ।।

ciraṃ vicarya saṃsāraṃ śāntiṃ yāte divaspatau ।
kāṣāyāmbaramālambya yayau saṃdhyāvadṛśyatām ।।

aśeṣāśātamomohavirāmavimalāṃ śanaiḥ ।
indurgāmuditaścakre pūrṇālokavilokinīm ।।

sarāgatāpe vabhasaścetasīva gate ravau ।
śuddhenduhṛdayasyābhūt prasādaḥ ko apyaviplavaḥ ।।

athāsminnantare kāntāsaṃtatāntaḥpurodare ।
ratnaharmyapraviṣṭendudyutisaṃdohahāsini ।।

niḥsāravirasaṃ sarvaṃ rājasūnurvilokayan ।
jagāa gaganasvacchasvacchandocchalitasmṛtiḥ ।।

gaṇo ayaṃ nārīṇāṃ madanadahanolkāparikaraḥ
parityājyastīvravyasanaśatasaṃtāpasacivaḥ ।
idānīṃ yuktā me tarutalalatāśītalare
parityaktāgārapraśamasukhasāre pariṇatiḥ ।।

etāścandradyutimadamayā yāmi nāryo vane asmin
nidrāmudrāniyamitadṛśaḥ saṃstarasrastavatrāḥ ।
svapnotpannānucitavacanāḥ keśasaṃchāditāṃsāḥ
kṣipraṃ mandānilavicalitān lajjayantīva dīpān ।।

saralasrastagātrāṇāṃ nirlajjānāṃ vivāsasām ।
suptānāṃ ca mṛtānāṃ ca bhedaḥ ko nāma dehinām ।।

iti tasya bruvāṇasya saṃjāte gamanodyame ।
mithaḥ kathā samabhavannagaradvārarakṣiṇām ।।

bho bhoḥ kaḥ ko atra jāgarti jāgrato nāsti viplavaḥ ।
prabhucittagrahavyagrāḥ samagrā eva jāgrati ।।

jāgarti saṃsāragṛhe manīṣī mohāṇdhakāre svapiti pramattaḥ ।
jjīvitameva loke mṛtasya suptasya ca ko viśeṣaḥ ।।

iti marhyasthitaḥ śrutvā rātrau rājasutaḥ kathāḥ ।
prasthitaṃ satpatheneva nijaṃ mene manoratham ।।
nivṝtterlakṣaṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā sa svapnaṃ kṣaṇanidrayā ।।
tataḥ prabuddhā sahasā trastā devī yaśodharā ।
tatkālopanataṃ svapnaṃ dayitāya nyavedayat ।।

paryaṅkābharaṇāngāni svapne bhagnāni me vibho ।
śrīrvrajantī mayā dṛṣṭvā candrārkau ca torihitau ।।
