ityākarṇya sa tāmūce mugdhe satyavivarjitaḥ ।
saṃsāra eva svapno ayaṃ svapne svapno api kīdṛśaḥ ।।

svapne adya nābhisaṃjātā latā vyāptā vihārasā ।
merūpadhānaśirasā pūrvapaścimavāridhau ।।

bhujābhyāṃ caraṇābhyām ca dakṣiṇābdhirmayā dhṛtaḥ ।
bhadre svapnaḥ śubho ayaṃ te strīṇāṃ bhartuśubhaṃ śubham ।।

ityukte bodhisattvena noce kiṃcid yaśodharā ।
punaśca nidrābhimukhī babhūva mīlitekṣaṇā ।।

śakrabrahmamukhāḥ sarve sametyātha sudhābhujaḥ ।
cakrire bodhisattvasya sattvotsāhaprapūraṇam ।।

tairdevaputrāścatvāraḥ samādiṣṭā mahājavāḥ ।
sahāyā gamane tasya bhūśailābdhidhṛtikṣamāḥ ।।

śakrādiṣṭena yakṣeṇa pāñcikākhyena nirmitaiḥ ।
saharmyāsaktasopānairavatīrya viniryayau ।।

suptaṃ sārathimādāya chandakākhyaṃ prabodhya saḥ ।
utsādamiva jagrāha kaṇṭhakākhyaṃ turaṅgamam ।।

taṃ tīkṣṇaruciraṃ lakṣmīkaṭākṣataralaṃ harim ।
sa cakre saṃyamālīnaṃ mūrdhi saṃspṛśya pāṇinā ।।

śamodyame sumanasā s ako apyantarbahiḥ samah ।
śiśavo api vimuñcanti yatprabhāveṇa cāpalam ।।

balajijñāsayā nyastaṃ tenātha caraṇaṃ kṣitau ।
na te kampayituṃ śekurdevaputrāḥ savismayāḥ ।।

chandakena sahāruhya nistaraṅgaṃ turaṅgamam ।
sa jagāhe mahadvyoma vimalaṃ svamivāśayam ।।

prayayau taralāvartinartitoṣṇīṣapallavaḥ ।
saṃsarpipavanollasaiḥ śokocchvāsa iva śriyaḥ ।।

tasyābharaṇaratnāṃśulekhābhiḥ śabalaṃ nabhaḥ ।
jagrāha sūtrapatrālīvicitramjiva cīvaram ।।

kīrṇāśrubindukalitā vilolanayanotpalāḥ ।
vrajantaṃ dadṛśurdṛśyāstamantaḥpuradevatāḥ ।।

saṃsāramiva vistīrṇaṃ puraṃ sanṛpabāndhavam ।
dūrāt pradakṣiṇīkṛtya kṣamyatāmityabhāṣata ।।

kṣapāyāṃ kṣaṇaśeṣāyām jane nidrābhimudrite ।
taṃ dadarśa mahānnāma prabuddho rājabāndhavaḥ ।।

divi dṛṣṭvā vrajantaṃ taṃ śaśāṅkaśaṅkayā hṛtaḥ ।
ūce ciraṃ vicāryoccairbāṣyāzncitavilocanah ।।

citrametad viraktavtaṃ bandhujīvopamasya te ।
kumāra rucirākāra na yuktaṃ yuktakāraṇam ।।

vaṃśotkarṣaviśeṣārthū nibaddhāśaḥ pitā tvayi ।
kasmānnirāśa kriyate sarvāśābharaṇa tvayā ।।

iti śākyasya mahataḥ śrutvā vākyaṃ nṛpātmajaḥ ।
tamūce bāndhavaprītirbandho vandhanaśṛṅkhalā ।।

ayaṃ kāyaḥ kṣayaṃ yāti mithyāgṛhasukhapriyaḥ ।
viṣayograviṣrtānāmamṛtāyatanaṃ vanam ।।

hastākṛṣṭastriphaṇiphaṇabhṛnmastakanyastamṛtyu
kaṇṭhābaddhitkaṭaviṣalatāpallavālolamālaḥ ।
dīptāṅgāraprkaragahanaṃ gāhate durgamārgaṃ
saṃsāre asmin viṣayanicaye sapramodaḥ pramādī ।।

ityudīrya vrajan vyomnā vilaṅghya nagaraṃ kṣaṇāt ।
bahirbhūtalamabhyetya sa yayau vājinā javāt ।।

mahatā śākyamukhyena bodhitasyātha bhūpateḥ ।
antaḥpure ca kāntānāmudbhūtaḥ karuṇaḥ svaraḥ ।।

atha brahmendradhanadapramukhastridaśairvṛtaḥ ।
rājasūnurvanaṃ prāpa gatvā dvādaśayojanam ।।

avaruhyātha turagātg vimucyābharaṇāni saḥ ।
uvāca sūcitānandaśchandakaṃ vadanatviṣā ।।

gṛhītvābahraṇāni tvaṃ hayaṃ ca vraja mandiram ।
medānīmasti me kṛtyametairmāyānibandhanaiḥ ।।

vane asminnahamekākī śamasaṃtoṣabāndhavaḥ ।
ekaḥ saṃjāyate jantureka eva vipadyate ।।

viṣamaviṣayayogaṃ bhogamutsṛjya re kaḥ sarasarati viśeṣakleśaśoṣapravṛttaḥ ।
paribhavabhuvane asminneṣa naḥ saṃniveśaḥ śamitamadanakāntiḥ śāntimeva śrayāmi ।।

ityuktvābharaṇānyasya dīptānyaṅke mumoca saḥ ।
tyaktaśokānvitānīva muktāpakkaṇasaṃcaye ।।

cūḍāṃ niskṛṣya khaṅgena sa cikṣepa nabhaḥsthale ।
śakraśca tam samādāya nināya divamādarāt ।।

keśaḥ kleśa ivotkṛtto yatra tena mahātmanā ।
keśapratigrahaṃ caityaṃ sadbhistatra niveśitam ।।

chandako apyaśvamādāyaṃ prayātaḥ saptabhirdinaiḥ ।
śanaiḥ prāpa puropāntaṃ śokārtaḥ samacintayat ।।

śūnyaṃ turagamādāya parityajya nṛpātmajam ।
draṣṭuṃ śaknomi nṛpatiṃ kathaṃ putrapralāpinam ।।

vicintyeti hayaṃ tyaktvā sa tatraiva vyalambata ।
śūnyāsanaḥ paraṃ vājī mūrtaḥ śoka ivāviśat ।।

taṃ dṛṣṭvāntaḥ purajanaḥ sāmātyaśca mahīpatiḥ ।
pratipralāpamukharāścakrire nikhilā diśaḥ ।।

udbhūtārtasvaraiḥ kaṇṭhaiḥ sotkaṇṭhaiḥ sa viṣādavān ।
sarvairgṛhītakīrṇāśrurvājī jīvitamatyajat ।।

sa bodhisattvasaṃsparśapuṇyaprāptipavitritaḥ ।
jagrāha brāhmaṇakule janma saṃsāramuktaye ।।

śakradattaṃ kumārastu yatra kāṣāyamagrahīt ।
kāṣāyagrahaṇam tatra caityaṃ cakre mahājanaḥ ।।

vibhavamabhavavṛttyai janma janmapramuktyai
vijanamapi janānāṃ mohagartānnivṛttyai ।
iti sa kuśalakāmaḥ kāmamutsṛjya bheje
guṇakṛtajanarāgaḥ ślāghyatāṃ tyaktarāgaḥ ।।

iti kṣemendraviracitāyām bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāmabhiniṣkramaṇāvadānaṃ caturviśaḥ pallavaḥ ।।

māravidrāvaṇāvadānam ।

jayanti te janmabhayapramuktā bhavaprabhāvābhibhavābhiyuktāḥ ।
yaiḥ sundarīlocanacakravartī māraḥ kṛtaḥ śāsanadeśavartī ।।

tatastapovane cāsmin bodhisattve tapojuṣi ।
tadupasthāpakāḥ pañca vārāṇasyāṃ pravavrajuḥ ।।

spṛhaṇīyo munīndrāṇāmatha śākyamuniḥ śanaiḥ ।
svayaṃ senāyanīgrāmaṃ janacārikayā yayau ।।

tatra senābhidhānasya kanye gṛhapateḥ sute ।
nandā nandabalākhyā ca cāruvṛtte babhūvatuḥ ।।

śuddhodanasya bhūbhartuste śrutvā viśrutaṃ sutam ।
cakrāte tadvivāhārthaṃ vrataṃ dvādaśavārṣikam ।।

āmodinīnāṃ hṛdaye sadā sūtravadāsthitaḥ ।
mālānāmiva bālānāmabhilāṣaḥ svabhāvajaḥ ।।

dhenūnāṃ pītadugdhānāṃ dugdhaṃ tābhyāṃ punaḥ punaḥ ।
gṛhīṭvā sphaṭikasthālyā vratānte pāyasaṃ śubham ।।

vidhivatpāyase siddhe viprarūpaḥ sureśvaraḥ ।
taṃ samabhyāyayau deśaṃ devaśca kamalāsanaḥ ।।

harṣādatithibhāge atha kanyakābhyām samuddhṛte ।
śakro avadatsarvaguṇodayāyāgre pradīyatām ।।

matto ayamadhikastāvadbrahmaṇaḥ prathamo api ca ।
ityukte surarājena provāca caturānanaḥ ।।

matto adhiko deva āste śuddhāvāsanikāyikaḥ ।
ityukte brahmaṇā te api jagadurgaganasthitāḥ ।।

sarvaprativiśiṣṭo asau bodhisattvastapaḥkṛśaḥ ।
nadyāṃ nirājanākhyāyāṃ vigāhya salile sthitaḥ ।।

etadākarṇya kanyābhyāmāhūya maṇibhājane ।
avatīryārpitaṃ bhaktyā tadasmai madhupāyasam ।।

bodhisattvastadādāya ratnapātrīṃ dadau tayoḥ ।
datteyaṃ na punargrāhyetyuktvā jagṛhaturna te ।।

sā tena nadyāṃ nikṣiptā nāgairnītā prabhāvatī ।
vikṣobhyāpyāhṛtā tebhyastārkṣyarūpeṇa vajriṇā ।।

prasādī bodhisattvo atha kanyāyugalamabhyadhāt ।
dānasya praṇidhānena bhavatyoḥ kiṃ samīhitam ।।

te tamūcaturānandanidhiḥ śuddhodanātmajaḥ ।
sarvārthasiddho abhimataḥ kumāraḥ patirāvayoḥ ।।

udyamaṃ māralīlāyāḥ sarasaṃ tadvacastayoḥ ।
na lilimpa manastasya pādmaṃ dalamivodake ।।

sa jagāda kumāro asau na kiṃ pravrajitaḥ śrutaḥ ।
na tasya lolanayanāḥ priyāh śriya iva striyaḥ ।।

ityanīpsitamākarṇya dīrghaṃ niśvasya kanyake ।
ūcaturdānadharmo ayaṃ siddhau tasyaiva jāyatām ।।

adṛṣṭasnehasaṃśliṣṭaḥ praviṣṭo antaḥ parāṅbhukhaḥ ।
na nāma sucirābhyastaḥ pakṣapāto nivartate ।।

iti tadvacanaṃ śrutvā bodhisattvaḥ prasannadhīḥ ।
prayātaste samāmantrya viśrāntyai kānanāntaram ।।

pāyasāmṛtabhāgena labdhadivyabalodayaḥ ।
pracchāyatarusucchāyamāruroha mahīdharam ।।

paryaṅkabandhamādhāya tatra tasmin sukhaṃ sthite ।
ahaṃkāra ivātyuccaśirāh so adrirvyagīryata ।।

viśīrṇabhūdhare tasmin sa pradadhyau viṣaṇṇadhīḥ ।
sapakṣālāni karmāṇi mayā kāni kṛtānyaho ।।

iti cintāśatocchvāsaṃ tamūcurvyomadevatāḥ ।
na tvayā vihitaṃ sādho karma kiṃcidasāṃpratam ।।

acchinnottaptakuśalaṃ dhartuṃ na kṣamate kṣitiḥ ।
sa tvamuttaptakuśalaḥ proccaśailaśatāgdguruḥ ।।

nirañjanīṃ samuttīrya saritaṃ vraja niścalam ।
siddhidaṃ bodhisattvānām deśaṃ vajrāasnābhidham ।।

devatādiṣṭamārgeṇa prasthitasyāsya bhūtale ।
pādanyāsairabhūttasya hemapadmaparaṃparā ।।

pṛthivī vrajatastasya prollasatsalilākulā ।
raṇantī kāṃsyapātrīva pronnanāma nanāma ca ।।

tāni tāni nimittāni pravṛttāni dadarśa saḥ ।
yeṣāmanuttarajñānanidhānasādhanaṃ phalam ।।

nirañjanāya bhuvane nāgo andhaḥ kālikābhidhaḥ ।
buddhotpāditadṛrabhūmeḥ śabdamākarṇya niryayau ।।

sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpannaṃ dīptajāmbūnadadyutim ।
sa bodhisattvamālokya provāca racitāznjaliḥ ।।

nalinanayana kāntastvaṃ vane yauvane asmin
viharasi virahārtiṃ saṃpadāmarpayitvā ।
aśamaśamaviśeṣonmeṣasaṃtoṣahetur
bhavasi bhavasamudre dehināṃ satyasetuḥ ।।

athāmuñcantyete bhayataralatāmatra hariṇāḥ
yathā līlācakraṃ viharati samīpe khagagaṇaḥ ।
sasattvāsattvānā kimapi hṛdayāśvāsasadanaṃ
tathā manye bauddhaṃ vapuridamanāyāsasukhadam ।।

karikalabhakah padmaprītyā karoti hareḥ karaṃ
sukhayati śikhī snigdhālāpaṃ kalāpaśikhānilai ।
bhavati hariṇī lolāpāṅgā puraḥ praṇayonmukhī
praśamasamayasyeyaṃ puṇyaprasādamayī sthitiḥ ।।

adyaiva buddhatvamavāpya śuddhaṃ tvaṃ bodhimeṣyatya khilāṃ trilokīm ।
sadyaḥprasādapramadāvadātāṃ kumudvatī pūrṇa ivāmṛtāṃśuḥ ।।

anyonyaṃ dinanāthadīptamahasaḥ sadyastavālokanāl
lokānāṃ kanalaprabodhakalayā divyaprakāśaspṛśām ।
niryātī hṝdayānnibaddhamadhupaśreṇiva saṃbandhana-
trastāntarna punaḥ kariṣyati padaṃ mohāndakārāvaliḥ ।।

iti bruvāṇāṃ vinayānnāgarājaḥ prasannadhīḥ ।
bodhisattvaṃ samābhāsya samuttīrya nadīṃ yayau ।।

vajrāsanapadaṃ prāpya bodhimūlamanākulam ।
dakṣiṇāgraiḥ kuśaiścakre śaktadattaiḥ sa saṃstaram ।।

tatropaviśya paryaṅkabaddho niścalaniścayaḥ ।
manthāvasānaviśrāntaḥ sa dugdhābdhirivābabhau ।।

asādhāraḥ kṣamādhāraḥ sa dhīrasaralākṛtiḥ ।
ruruce kāñcanaruciḥ paro merurivācalaḥ ।।

asāvakṣayaparyantaḥ paryaṅko ayaṃ mama sthiraḥ ।
babandheti sa saṃkalpaṃ kṛtvā pratimukhīṃ smṛtim ।।

atrāṇtare samabhyetya māraḥ saṃyamamatsaraḥ ।
lekhahārastatra tūrṇaṃ bodhisattvamabhāṣataḥ ।।

akāmakāmatā keyaṃ loke bandhanadā matā ।
akālakalikākārā matiste kāsya kāmanā ।।

gṛhītaṃ hataśaṅkena devadattena te puram ।
niruddhantaḥpuraśreṇīrbaddhaḥ śuddhodano nṛpaḥ ।।

iti śrutvaiva vacanaṃ śokāmarṣaviṣojjhitaḥ ।
aśikṣitavikāreṇa cetasā sa vyacintayat ।।

aho batāntarāyaṃ me māraḥ kartuṃ samudyataḥ ।
nartayatyeṣa durvṛttaḥ śisvaṇḍikrīḍayājagat ।।

māra māra virāmaste daurjanyasya na jāyate ।
ekena hiṃsāyajñena prāpteyaṃ kamratā tvayā ।।

yajñadāṇatapaḥślāghāṃ nātmanaḥ kartumutsahe ।
svaguṇodīraṇamlānaṃ puṇyapuṣpaṃ hi śīryati ।।

iti nirbhatsitastena cittastenaḥ śarīriṇām ।
sāmarṣaḥ prayayau māraḥ samārambhād hatodyamaḥ ।।

athādṛśyanta lalitā lālityāñcitalocanāḥ ।
bhramadbhṛṅgaraṅgiṇyaḥ kāntāścūtalatā iva ।।

cārutaccaritātṛptāstisrastāḥ kāmakanyakāḥ ।
sarāgaṃ pādanalinīnyāsaiścakrustapovanam ।।

vilocanena hariṇī kariṇī gativibhramaiḥ ।
tatra tābhirmukhāmbhojairnalinī malinīkṛtā ।।

yauvanābharaṇairaṅgauranurāgāvilepanaiḥ ।
lāvaṇyavasanaistāsāṃ kāmo abhūdapyacetasām ।।

vajrāsanasamādhānadhyānaniścalalocanam ।
taṃ vilokyābhavat tāsāṃ vismayadhyānadhāraṇā ।।

tā bodhisattvasaṃkalpān madarāgamayaṃ vayaḥ ।
parityajyaiva sahasā salajjā bhejire jarām ।।

pratīpagamanāttāsāmatha bhagnamanorathaḥ ।
manmathaḥ prathitārambhaḥ sainyasaṃbḥāramādade ।।

sarvapraharaṇairvyāptaṃ nānāprāṇimukhairbhayaiḥ ।
ṣaṭtriṃśatkoṭīvipulaṃ balaṃ tasya samudyayau ।।

svayamākarṇaniṣkṛṣṭakopakrūraśarāsanaḥ ।
māraḥ sphāravikāreṇa bodhisattvaṃ samādravat ।।

śastravṛṣṭistadutsṛṣṭā saha pāṃśuviṣāśmabhiḥ ।
prayayau bodhisattvasya mandārāmbujatulyatām ।।

punarmārabalotsṛṣṭā śastravṛṣṭirghṛtakṣame ।
cakrire devatāstasya vajrapratisamāśrayam ।।

smaro api naṣṭasaṃkalpaḥ samādheḥ śrotrakaṇṭakam ।
ghaṇṭāpaṭuraṭatpatraṃ nirmame sphaṭīkadrumam ।।

taṃ tāramukharaṃ vṛkṣaṃ māraṃ ca sabalāyudham ।
cakravāṭe samutkṣipya cikṣipurvyomadevatāḥ ।।

bhagavānatha saṃprāptaprasannajñānanirmalaḥ ।
sarvavitsarvagaḥ saravjātismṛtiparo abhavat ।।

sa tatrānuttarajñānasamyaksaṃbodhimāpitaḥ ।
dadarśa sarvabhutāṇi gatiṃ karmorminirmitām ।।

atha śākyapure māraḥ pravādamasṛjaddivaḥ ।
bodhisattvaḥ prayāto astaṃ tapaḥkleśavaśāditi ।।

tatra śuddhodano rājā putrasnehaviṣāturaḥ ।
nipapāta tamākarṇya vajrāhata iva kṣitau ।।

antaḥpure sahanṛpe prāṇatyāgakṛtakṣaṇe ।
suvṛttapakṣapātinyastamūcurvyomadevatāḥ ।।

putrastavāmṛtaṃ pītvā samyaksaṃbuddhatām gataḥ ।
tenāvalokitasyāpi nāste bhṛtyubhayaṃ kutaḥ ।।

iti sāntaḥpurāmātyaḥ śrutvā narapatirvacaḥ ।
abhūtpratyāgataprāṇaḥ sudhāsikta iva kṣaṇāt ।।

tasmin mahotsavānande bodhisattvavadhūḥ sutam ।
kāntaṃ yaśodhaāsūta rāhugraste niśākare ।।

rāhulākhyaḥ sa bālo api nṛpaterjanmaśaṅkinaḥ ।
jananyā saśilaḥ śuddhyai nikṣipto ambhasi pupluve ।।

bhagavānapi saptāhaṃ sthito niścalavigrahaḥ ।
vajraparyaṅkabandhena devānām vismayaṃ vyadhāt ।।

sa brahmakāyikākhyābhyām devatābhyāṃ virodhitaḥ ।
avadatparamānandasudhāsaṃdohasundaraḥ ।।

aho tava mayā jñātā pūrvameṣā sukhasthitiḥ ।
yayā surāsuraiśvaryasukhaṃ duḥkhagaṇāyate ।।

lāvaṇyāmbhaḥplāvitāṅgāstaruṇyaḥ pīyūṣārdraḥ svargasaṃbhogavargaḥ ।
asyāśeṣatyāgahelāsukhasya spardhābandhe pāṃśuniḥsāra eva ।।

saṃtapto ahaṃ viṣayaviṣamakleśasaṃsārapānthaḥ
klāntaḥ śāntyāśritimupagataścandanacchāyayeva ।
saṃjāteyaṃ sakalakaraṇavyāpinī nirvṛtime
viśrāntānām śamahimavane kiṃ sukhasyopamānam ।।

asminnavasare puṇyaparipākeṇa tadvanam ।
vaṇijau pṛthusārthena prāptau trapusabhallikau ।।

devatāpretitau bhaktyā bhagavantamupetya tau ।
praṇatau piṇḍapāto ayaṃ gṛhyatāmityabhāṣatām ।।

dayāvidheyaḥ sarvajñastadākarṇya vyacintayat ।
pūrvaiḥ pātre gṛhīto ayaṃ na pāṇī pātravarjite ।।

iti cintayatastasya mahārājābhidhāḥ surāḥ ।
datvā sphaṭikapātrāṇi catvāri tridivaṃ yayuḥ ।।

kṛtvātha bhagavān pātre piṇḍapātapratigraham ।
anugrahaṃ tayoścakre śaraṇyatrayaśāsanāt ।।

vitatasukṛtasākṣī puṇyanikṣepadakṣaḥ kṣayitavipadaśeṣaḥ prārthanākalpavṛkṣaḥ ।
bhavati kuśalamūlaiḥ kasyacidbhāgyabhājaḥ śubhapariṇatidīkṣādakṣiṇaḥ sādhusaṅgaḥ ।।

iti kṣemendraviracitāyām bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ māracidrāvaṇāvadānam nāma pañcaviṃśaḥ pallavaḥ ।।

śākyotpattiḥ ।

vaṃśaḥ sa ko api vipulaḥ kuśalānubandhī yaścāruvṛttamucitaṃ guṇasaṃgrahasya ।
ratnaṃ viśuddharucisūcitasatprakāśaṃ muktāmayaṃ jagadalaṃkaraṇaṃ prasūte ।।

nyagrodhārāmanirataṃ purā kapulavāstuni ।
śākyāḥ svavaṃśaṃ papracchurbhagavantaṃ tathāgatam ।।

taiḥ pṛṣṭaḥ svakulotpattiṃ sa maudgalyāyanaṃ puraḥ ।
vaktuṃ nyayuṅkta kṛtvāsya vimalajñānadarśanam ।।

sa vilokya yathātattvamatītaṃ jñānacakṣuṣā ।
tānavocata saṃsmṛtya śrūyatāṃ śākyasaṃbhavaḥ ।।

aśeṣe asmin jalamaye jagatyekārṇave purā ।
sthite pavanasaṃsparśātpayaḥ paya ivābhavat ।।

jale tasmin ghanatayā yāte kaṭhinatām śanaiḥ ।
abhūdvarṇarasasparśaśabdagandhamayī mahī ।।

tasyāmābhāsvarā devāścyutāḥ karmaparikṣayāt ।
tattulyavarṇasaṃbhūtāḥ sattvāḥ sattvabalādhikāḥ ।।

aṅgulyā rasamāsvādya tattṛṣṇātīvramohitāḥ ।
āhāradoṣātsaṃprāpourgururūkṣavivarṇatām ।।

annaprasavinī teṣāṃ krameṇābhūdvasuṃdharā ।
tamobhiśca viluptānām kṣetrāga ।।

tatasteṣāṃ kṣatatrāṇāt kṣatriyaḥ kṣitipālane ।
mahāsaṃmatanāmābhūjjanasya mahato mataḥ ।।

tasyānvaye mahatyāsīnṛpaḥ śrīmānupoṣadhaḥ ।
amlānakīrtikusumaḥ pārijāta ivodadhau ।।

cakravartī sutastasya māndhātābhūdayonijaḥ ।
jagatyekātapatrasya yasya vaṃśo mahānabhūt ।।

vaṃśe sahasravaṃśasya kṛkistasyābhavannṛpaḥ ।
cittaprasādamakarod bhagavān yasya kāśyapaḥ ।।

ikṣvākuranvaye tasya tasya cābhūd virūḍhakaḥ ।
prītyā kanīyasaḥ sūnorjyeṣṭhāstena vivāsitāḥ ।।

ekībhūya tataḥ sarve svadeśavigataspṛhāḥ ।
kumārāḥ kapilākhyāsya maharṣerāśramaṃ yayuḥ ।।

dhyānakālāṇtarāyāṇāṃ bālyāduccaiḥ pralāpinām ।
so anyatra nirmame teṣāṃ puraṃ kapulavāstviti ।।

kālena putravātsalyādanutāpena bhūpatiḥ ।
ānīyantāṃ kumārāste sacivānityabhāṣata ।।

tamūrcurmantriṇaḥ sarve rājan prāptapurottamāḥ ।
pratyānetumaśakyāste jātāpatyapṛthuśriyaḥ ।।

iti teṣāṃ pitustatra śakyāśakyavicintane ।
babhūvuḥ śākyasaṃjñāste nṝpurasteṣu vaṃśakṛt ।।

tadvaṃśeṣu pañcapañcasahasreṣu mahībhujām ।
atīteṣu kṣitipatiḥ śrīmān daśaratho abahvat ।।

tasyānvaye siṃhahanurbabhūva pṛthivīpatiḥ ।
na raṇe siṃhamiva yaṃ sehire rājakuñjarāḥ ।।

jyeṣṭhaḥ śuddhodanastasya sutaḥ śuklodanaḥ paraḥ ।
droṇodanastadanujaḥ kanīyānamṛtodanaḥ ।।

kanyāścatasraḥ śuddhākhyā śuklā droṇāmṛtā tathā ।
śuddhodanasya bhagavān sūnurnandastathāparaḥ ।।

śuklodanasya tanayau dvau tiṣyākhyo atha bhadrikaḥ ।
droṇodanasya dvau putrāvaniruddho mahāṃstathā ।।

ānandadevadattākhyāvamṛtodanasaṃbahvau ।
śuddhāsutaḥ supraśuddhaḥ śuklāsūnuśva mālikaḥ ।।

droṇāputraśca bhadrāṇirvaiśālyakhyo amṛtāsutaḥ ।
rāhulo bhagavatsūnuryasmin vaṃśaḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ ।।

ityujjvalajñānamayena tena vaṃśaṃ yathāvatkathitaṃ niśamya ।
śākyā babhūvarbhagavatprabhāvaiḥ
saṃbhāvitotkarṣaviśeṣaśuddhāḥ ।।

iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ śākyotpattīrnāma ṣaḍviṃśaḥ pallavaḥ ।।

śroṇākoṭīviṃśāvadānam ।
sa ko api sattvasya vivekabandhoḥ puṇyopasannasya mahān prabhāvaḥ ।
nāpaiti yaḥ kāyaśateṣu puṃsaḥ kastūrikāmoda ivāṃśukasya ।।

jine sarvajagajjantusaṃtāpakaruṇāhrade ।
pure rājagṛhe veṇuvanāntaravihāriṇi ।।

śrīmānabhūdbhūmipatiścampāyāṃ potalābhidhaḥ ।
jahāra dhanadarpāndhyaṃ dhanena dhanadasya yaḥ ।।

ajāyata sutastasya manorathaśatānvitaḥ ।
dhanānāmīpsitāvāptya sukhasakhyo vibhūtayaḥ ।।

śravaṇarkṣeṇa jātasya sa sūnostasya janmani ।
prītyā dadau daridrasya koṭīnāṃ viṃśatiṃ tadā ।।

sa śroṇakoṭiviṃśākhyaḥ śiśuḥ khyātastadābhavat ।
vibhavaḥ sukṛtenaiva yena vaṃśo vibhūṣitaḥ ।।

prāptavidyaḥ sa sarvārthaiḥ saha vṛddhimupāgataḥ ।
cakāra sukhaviśrāntiṃ vyavahāradharaḥ pituḥ ।।

sa kadācitprabhāpuñjamiav sūryasya maṇḍalāt ।
avatīrṇaṃ puraprātaṃ maudgalyāyanamabravīt ।।

ko bhavānarkasaṃkāśaḥ prakāśitadigantaraḥ ।
tridaśeśaḥ śaśāṅko vā devo vā draviṇeśvaraḥ ।।

sa taṃ babhāṣe na suraḥ śiṣyo bhagavatastvaham ।
buddhasya vibudhādhīśavandyamānaguṇaśriyaḥ ।।

svacchaṃ tasya prayacchantaṃ piṇḍapātaṃ mahāmuneḥ ।
sattvaśuddhodayāvāptaṃ bhogyaṃ bhagavataḥ priyam ।।

iti śroṇasya bhagavannāmnā śravaṇagāminā ।
ravibhakrasya jātyāpi romāñcaḥ samajāyataḥ ।।

prāgjanmavāsanāyuktaḥ svabhāvo yasya yaḥ sthitaḥ ।
sa tasyodīraṇenāpi sphuṭa eva vibhāvyate ।।

sa tasmai viṃśatisthālībhāgaṃ nākajanocitam ।
prahiṇodbhaktisaṃsaktaśraddhāyuktena cetasā ।।

tatastaṃ preṣitaṃ tena bhagavān bhaktisaṃsadā ।
anugrahāgrahavyagraḥ samagraṃ svayamagrahīt ।।

asminnavasare bhaktyā sthālībhāgaṃ nṛpocitam ।
samādāya svayaṃ rājā bimbisāraḥ samāyayau ।।

śroṇaprahītabhogānāmāmodaṃ tatra pārthivaḥ ।
āghrāya śakraprahitaṃ sarvaṃ divyamamanyata ।।

pātraśeṣaṃ bhagavatā dattamāsvādya bhūpatiḥ ।
śroṇena preṣitaṃ śrutvā tadanu vismayaṃ yayau ।।

bhagavantaṃ praṇamyātha rājadhānīṃ nareśvaraḥ ।
praviśyācintayatsphītāṃ divyāṃ śroṇasya saṃpadam ।।

gacchāmi taṃ svayaṃ gatvā draṣṭavyo asau amhāyaśāḥ ।
iti niścitya sacivaiḥ sa yātrārambhamādiśat ।।

potalaḥ kṣitipaṃ jñātvā svayamāgamanodyatam ।
nītijñaṃ putramekāṇte śroṇakoṭimabhāṣata ।।

putra tvām draṣṭumāyāti varṇāśramagururnṛpaḥ ।
ityeṣa bhṛśamutkarṣaḥ sadoṣaḥ pratibhāti me ।।

kṣitīśā lakṣatāṃ yātaṃpakṣapātodyatā iva ।
avilambitamāghnanti śarā iva guṇacyutāḥ ।।

bhṛtyānāmapi vidveṣyo bhavatyatiśayonnatiḥ ।
abhimānaikasārāṇāṃ kiṃ punaḥ pṛthivībhūjām ।।

rūpe vayasi saubhāgye prabhāve vibhave śrute ।
svasutasyāpi saṃgharṣānnotkarṣaṃ sahate janaḥ ।।

jane dveṣamaye putra guṇamācchādya jīvyate ।
ācchāditaguṇaḥ padmaḥ priyastīkṣṇarucerapi ।।

uddhataḥ kasya na dveṣyaḥ praṇataḥ kasya na priyaḥ ।
drumaṃ pātayati stabdhaṃ namtraṃ rakṣati mārutaḥ ।।

sa cābhigamyo bhūpālastvāṃ yadi svayameṣyati ।
tadeṣaṃ darpamohaste śreyase na bahviṣyati ।।

tasmāditaḥ svayaṃ gatvā praṇamyaṃ praṇama prabhum ।
nakṣatrarāśisadṛśaṃ datvā hāramupāyanam ।।

pituḥ śrutveti vacanaṃ śroṇakoṭirhahīpatim ।
prayayau nāvamāruhya draṣṭuṃ ratnavibhūṣitaḥ ।।

sa rājadhānīmāsādya prāpya dṛṣṭvā ca bhūpatim ।
dadau hāraṃ parṇamyāsmai harṣahāsamiva śriyaḥ ।।

taṃ dṛṣṭvā svayamāyātaṃ nṛpatiḥ snigdhayā dṛśā ।
hemaromāṅkacaraṇaṃ vismayādityabhāṣata ।।

aho puṇyamaheśākhyaḥ ko api tvaṃ sattvabāmdhavaḥ ।
yasya saṃdarśanenaiva manovṛttiḥ prasīdati ।।

guṇebhyaḥ paramaiśvaryamaiśvaryātsukhamuttamam ।
sukhebhyaḥ paramārogyamārogyātsādhusaṃgamaḥ ।।

api dṛṣṭastvayā sādho bhagavān veṇukānane ।
tatpādapadmayugalaṃ draṣṭumarhasi me mataḥ ।।

ityukte kṣitināthena saujanyātpakṣapātinā ।
taṃ śroṇakoṭīviṃśo api praṇayātpratyabhāṣata ।।

asmādatulyakalyāṇātprasādāddevadeva te ।
adhunā yogyatāyātā bhagavaddarśane mama ।।

ityukte tena sahitaḥ pratasthau sthitikovidaḥ ।
bhaktyā tathāgataṃ draṣṭuṃ padbhyāmeva mahīpatiḥ ।।

aspṛṣṭapādasya bhuvā śruṇasyājanmavāsarāt ।
mahārhavastraiḥ prasthāne bhṛtyairācchāditā mahī ।।

bhagavadbhaktivinayādgauravācca sa bhūpateḥ ।
vastrāṇyavārayadbhṛtyairavācca iva kṣitau ।।

vāriteṣvatha vastreṣu divyavastrairvṛtā mahī ।
aprayatnopakaraṇāḥ saṃpadaḥ puṇyaśālinām ।।

nivārya dinyavastrāṇi bhūmau tenārpite pade ।
vicacālācalā pṛthvī saśailavanasāgarā ।।

tataḥ sa bhūmipatinā saha prāpya jināśramam ।
bhagavantaṃ vilokyāsya vidadhe pādavandanam ।।

upaviṣṭasya tasyāgre hṛṣṭasyālokanāmṛtaiḥ ।
cakre śamavivekasya bhagavānabhiṣecanam ।।

āśayānuśayaṃ dhātuṃ prakṛtiṃ ca vicārya saḥ ।
satyasaṃdarśanāyāsya vidaśe dharmadeśanām ।।

satkāyadṛṣṭiśailo asya tayā viṃśatiśṛṅgavān ।
jñānavajreṇa nirbhinnaḥ srotaḥprāptipadaspṛśaḥ ।।

pravrajyāyāṃ tatastasya jātāyāṃ sahasā svayam ।
bhagavantaṃ praṇamyātha vismitaḥ prayayau nṛpaḥ ।।

tīvravrate api śroṇasya kadācitsamajāyata ।
vāsanāśeṣasaṃskārādbandhabhogasukhasmṛtiḥ ।।

sa tamāhūya bhagavān vilakṣaṃ prāha sasmitaḥ ।
ko ayaṃ parivitarkaste pratisaṃlīnacetasaḥ ।।

viśliṣṭātyantakṛṣṭā vā tantrī bahvati visvarā ।
samā mādhuryamāyāti tasmātsāmyaṃ samāśrayet ।।

ityādeśādbhagavataḥ sarvasāmyamupāgataḥ ।
sa prāpa vimalajñānaṃ paścāttāpavivarjitaḥ ।।

tasya tāmadbhutāṃ siddhiṃ vilokya pṛthuvismayāḥ ।
papracchurbhikṣavaḥ sarve bhagavantaṃsa cābhyadhāt ।।

śroṇasya śrūyatām śreyaḥkarma janmāntarārhitam ।
na hyapuṇyānubhāvānāṃ bhavantyadbhutasaṃpadaḥ ।।

vipaśvī bhagavān samyaksaṃbuddhaḥ sugataḥ purā ।
purīṃ bandhumatīṃ nāma janacārikayā yayau ।।

tatra bhaktyā sukṛtibhirbhaktāyopanimantritaḥ ।
vāreṇa pratyahaṃ gehaṃ yayau teṣāṃ sahānugaḥ ।।

tato daridraḥsaṃprāptavāro brāhmaṇadārakaḥ ।
indrasomābhidhaścakre yatnāt yadyogyabhojanam ।।

sa prayatnena mahatā bhojyaṃ bhaktipavitritam ।
āchādya vastrairvasudhāṃ prahvastasmai nyavedayat ।।

tadbhogapraṇidhānena jātaḥ so ayaṃ mahādhanaḥ ।
sauvarṇaromacaraṇaḥ śroṇakoṭī suropamaḥ ।।

na vastrarahitā bhūmiḥ spṛṣṭānena kadācana ।
kampastaccaraṇasparśādata evābhavadbhuvaḥ ।।

iti sugatavacaḥ sudhāvadātaṃ daśanamayūkhamivonmiṣatsvabhāvam ।
praṇihitahṛdayaḥ paraṃ nipīya sthirakuśalāya babhūva bhikṣusaṃghaḥ ।।

iti kṣemendraviracitāyām bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ śroṇakoṭīviṃśāvadānaṃ saptaviṃśaḥ pallavaḥ ।।

dhanapālāvadānam ।

daurjanyaduḥsahaviśālakhalāpakārairnaivāśaye vikṛtirasti mahāśayānām ।
vyālolvaṇakṣitibhṛdākulito api sindhurnaivotsasarja hṛdayādamṛtasvabhāvam ।।

pure purā rājagṛhe bahgavān veṇukānane ।
kalandakanivāsākhye vijahāra manohare ।।

tatra vitrāsitānekaśatrinistriṃśabāndhavaḥ ।
ajātaśatrunāmābhūd bimbisārasuto nṛpaḥ ।।

śākyavaṃśyaḥ suhṛttasya devadattābhidho abhavat ।
kṣudramantreṇa yasyāsīt sa vetāla ivotkaṭaḥ ।।

sa kadācitsukhāsīnaṃ rahaḥ prāha mahīpatim ।
na rājan phalito adyāpi mamāpi tvatsamāśrayaḥ ।।

nithopacārarahitaḥ sukhaniryantratantrayoḥ ।
mitho manorathatrāṇānmitraśabdaḥ pravartate ।।

ya eṣa śākyaśramaṇaḥ sukhe veṇuvane sthitaḥ ।
taṃ hatvā prāptumicchāmi tatpadaṃ devavanditam ।।

kṣīyate na yayā śatrurlabhyate na yayā yaśaḥ ।
vardhate na yayā mānaḥ kiṃ tayā mitrasaṃpadā ।।

mahādhanābhidhānena tatpaureṇa nimantritaḥ ।
sa puraṃ prātarāgantā dāmbhikaḥ saha bhikṣubhiḥ ।।

rājamārgaṃ praviśataḥ sa tasya vyālakuñjaraḥ ।
utsṛjyatāmabhimukhaḥ krodhāndho dhanapālakaḥ ।।

ityukte devadattena nṛpatirmitravatsalaḥ ।
buddhaprabhāvaṃ saṃcintya nāha kiṃcidavāṅbhukhaḥ ।।

devadatto api nirgatya rājasauhārdadurmadaḥ ।
prāha hastimahāmātraṃ hāraṃ datvāsya toṣaṇam ।।

śramaṇaḥ prātarāgantā puraṃ bhikṣuśatairvṛtaḥ ।
preraṇīyastvayā tasmai gaja ityāha bhūpatiḥ ।।

devadattavacaḥ śrutvā tathetyuce dvipādhipaḥ ।
śreṇī hi meṣamūrkhāṇāmekayātānupātinī ।।

jñātvāpi tamabhiprāyaṃ sarvajñaḥ pāpacetasām ।
prātaḥ samāyayau sārdhaṃ bhikṣūṇāṃ pañcabhi śataiḥ ।।

atha hastipakotsṛṣṭaḥ kṛṣṭaprāsādapādapaḥ ।
tamabhyadhāvadāviddhaḥ krodhāndhaḥ krūrakuñjaraḥ ।।

anāyattaḥ paricayādaṅkuśasya gurorapi ।
khalaviddhāniva dveṣī madena malinīkṛtaḥ ।।

sevavyasanasaktānāmasakṛtkarṇacāpalāt ।
prāṇāpahārī bhṛṅgāṇāṃ bhṛtyānāmiva duṣpatiḥ ।।

mandaropadrave tasmin drumadrohiṇyabhidrute ।
vidrute sahasā loke hāhākāro mahānabhūt ।।

tasyāñcatkarṇatālānilatulitasaratsāndrasindūrapūraiḥ
saṃpūrṇe rājamārge cyutacakitavadhūraktavastrāsamānaiḥ ।
uddaṇḍoccaṇḍaśuṇḍabhramaṇaravalasatsādhvasāyāsitāśā
vyālolālakābhabhramaramiladvibhramaḥ saṃbhramo abhūt ।।

purapramāthavyathite jane kolāhalākule ।
āruroha mahāharmyaṃ devadattaḥ pramattadhīḥ ।।

bhagavadgrahaṇaṃ draṣṭuṃ so abhavadbhṛśamutsukaḥ ।
unmūlanena guṇināṃ mātaṅgaḥ parituṣyati ।।

vidruteṣu gajatrāsāt teṣu sarveṣu bhikṣuṣu ।
ānanda eka evābhūd bhikṣurbhagavato antike ।।

tatra pañcānanāh pañca niryayurbhagavatkarāt ।
karālakesarasaṭāstannakhāṃśucitā iva ।।

dvipastadgandhamāgrāya pardāpasmāravāraṇam ।
abhūt srutaśakṛnmūtraḥ sahasaiva parāṅmukhaḥ ।।

javena vidrutastatra dantī darpadaridratām ।
prāptaḥ pradīpadahanāḥ sa dadarśa diśo daśa ।।

sa vilokya jālavahnijvalajjvālākulaṃ jagat ।
pādapadmāntikaṃ śāstuḥ śītalaṃ samupāyayau ।।

saṃkocābhiruceḥ sacintamanasaḥ pradhvastavaktradyuter dainyāpannavihīnadānamadhupaprārabdhakolāhalaḥ ।
lobhāndhasya mahāvyayotsava iva kleśoṣmaniśvāsinas tasyābhūtparitāpaniślathagaterbhārāyamāṇaḥ karaḥ ।।

taṃ pādamūlamāyāntaṃ bhītaṃ kāruṇyasāgaraḥ ।
śāstā kareṇa pasparśa cakrasvastikalakṣmaṇā ।।

kumbhavinyastahastastaṃ provāca bhagavān jinaḥ ।
putra svakarmaṇainemāṃ prāpto asi tvamimāṃ daśām ।।

vivekālokahaladaḥ kāyo ayaṃ māṃsabhūdharaḥ ।
bhāraste mohasaṃbhāraḥ pāpādupanataḥ paraḥ ।।

ityukte karuṇardreṇa bhito bhagavatā gajaḥ ।
sa labdhaścāsamālānalīno niścalatām yayau ।।

devadattasya saṃkalpe kuñjare ca mahotkaṭe ।
bhagne nirvighnaharṣo abhūtsamudgatādbhuto janaḥ ।।

tataḥ kṛtvā gṛhapatergṛhe bhojyapratigraham ।
bhagavān bhikṣubhiḥ sārdhaṃ kānanaṃ gantumudyayau ।।

abhisṛtya gajendro api jinasya caraṇābjayoḥ ।
kṛtvā kareṇa saṃsparśaṃ vapustatyāja kauñjaram ।।

cāturmahārājikeṣu deveṣu viśadadyutiḥ ।
upapannaḥ sa sahasā sugataṃ draṣṭumāyayau ।।

svamāśramapadaṃ prāptaṃ bhagavantamupetya saḥ ।
praṇanāmārkasaṃkāśaṃ pradīptamaṇikuṇḍalaḥ ।।

tasya keyūramukuṭaprabhāpallavapūritāḥ ।
śakracāpairiva vyāptā virejurghanarājayaḥ ।।

vinayādupaviśyāgre sa śāstuḥ srastakalmaṣaḥ ।
taṃ divyapuṣpairākīrya sattva śubhrairabhāṣataḥ ।।

bhagavan bhavataḥ pādapadmasaṃsparśanena me ।
durdaśāduḥkhasaṃtāpaḥ śāntaḥ saṃtoṣaśālinaḥ ।।

śamaślāghyā kāpi vyasanaviṣadoṣoṣmaśamanī
sudhāvṛṣṭirdṛṣṭirbata bhagavataḥ snigdhamadhurā ।
yayā spṛṣṭaspṛṣṭaṃ kharataravikāravyatikaraṃ
vimutyāntaḥśāntiṃ śrayati hatamoha paśurapi ।।

iti tasya bruvāṇasya bhagavān bhavaśāntaye ।
satyadarśanasaṃśuddhāṃ vidadhe dharmadeśanām ।।

maulimuktāṃśuśubhreṇa śirasā caraṇadvayam ।
sa śāstuḥ prayayau natvā hasanniva bhavabhramam ।।

gate tasmin mukhaśaśiprakāśitanabhastale ।
bhagavān bhikṣubhiḥ pṛṣṭastadvṛttāntamabhāṣata ।।

pūrvakalpāntare śāstuḥ kāśyapākhyasya śāsane ।
abhūtpravrajito apyeṣa śikṣāpadanirādaraḥ ।।

anādarātkuñjaratābhogaḥ saṃghopasevanāt ।
satyadṛṣṭibalenānte saṃprāptaḥ śāsanagrahaḥ ।।

prāgjanmavihitaṃ karma kasyacinna nivartate ।
karmopadiṣṭasaṃbandhabhaktibhogaiḥ sacetasaḥ ।।

tasmin vyatikare ghore sarvaistyakro asmi bhikṣibhiḥ ।
na tvānandena tatrāpi śrūyatām pūrvasaṃgatiḥ ।।

śaśāṅkaśītasarasi bhrātarau rucirau purā ।
pūrṇamukhaḥ śukhaśceti rājahaṃsau babhūvatuḥ ।।

kadācidbrahmadattasya vārāṇasyāṃ mahīpateḥ ।
brahamamatīṃ puṣkariṇīṃ ramyāṃ pūrṇamukho yayau ।।

sa tasyāṃ lolakamalakiñjalkaparipiñjaraḥ ।
vijahāra sarojinyāṃ haṃsānāṃ pañcabhiḥ śataiḥ ।।

pūrvapuṇyānubhāvena taṃ rūpātiśayojjvalam ।
dadarśaṃ kāryāṇyutsṛjya jano niścalalocanah ।।

taṃ śrutvā bhūpatistatra sthitaṃ taddarśanotsukaḥ ।
kuśalān grahaṇe tasya vyasṛjajjālajīvinaḥ ।।

tasmin gṛhīte nalīnīlīlāsmitasitatviṣi ।
śatāni pañca haṃsānāṃ tyaktvā taṃ prayayurjavāt ।।

ekastu tasya saujanyādabaddho api subaddhavat ।
tadarthaṃ vyathitastasthau premapāśavaśīkṛtaḥ ।।

tatastaiḥ prāpitaṃ rājā rājahaṃsaṃ vilokya tam ।
snehabaddhaṃ dvitīyaṃ ca vismitastāvavalokayat ।।

haṃsaḥ pūrṇamukhaḥ so ahamānandastasya cānugaḥ ।
gatāstadadya ca tyaktvā māṃ gaṃsā eva bhikṣavaḥ ।।

pūrvasminnabahvatkāle vārāṇasyāṃ mahīpatiḥ ।
tutturnāma manaḥpaṭṭe likhitaṃ yadyaśaḥ paraiḥ ।।

sahasrayodhastasyābhūd dākṣiṇātyo niratyayaḥ ।
karadaṇḍīti vikhyātaḥ saṃgrāmāgresaraḥ priyaḥ ।।

kadācid ghorasamare pañcāmātyaśatāni tam ।
nṛpaṃ tyaktvā yayurbhītyā karadaṇḍī tu nātyajat ।।

ahameva sa bhūpālaḥ sacivāste ca bhikṣavaḥ ।
karadaṇḍī sa evāyamānando na jahāti mām ।।

janmāntare api siṃho ahaṃ māsaṃ kūpe nipātitaḥ ।
upekṣitaḥ kṣaṇādbhṛtyaiḥ śṛgālairye adya bhikṣavaḥ ।।

ekena ca nakhaiḥ khātaṃ dīrghaṃ kṛtvāsmi mokṣitaḥ ।
jambukena sa evāyamānando adya mamānugaḥ ।।

kūṭapāśanibaddhasya mṛgayūthapateḥ purā ।
lubdhakāgamane eva jagmustadanugā mṛgāḥ ।।

anuraktā na tatyāja taṃ mṛgī sāśrulocanā ।
prītiśṛṅkhalayā baddhā yātā nispandatāmiva ।।

atha lubdhakamāyāntaṃ dṛṣṭvā mṛgavadhodyatam ।
sāvadanmama bāṇena prathamaṃ hara jīvitam ।।

iti spaṣṭagirā tasyāḥ snehena ca sa vismitaḥ ।
mumoca lubdhakaḥ prītyā hariṇaṃ hariṇīsakham ।।

mṝgayūthapatiḥ so ahamānandaḥ sā kuraṅgikā ।
ityeṣa prītisaṃbandhaḥ prāgvṛttamanuvartate ।।

śrutveti vākyaṃ sugatasya sarve lajjānilīnā iva bhikṣavaste ।
sānandamānandamukhāravindaṃ prabhābhirāmaṃ dadṛśuḥ spṛhārdrāḥ ।।

iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ dhanapālāvadānaṃ aṣṭaviṃśaḥ pallavaḥ ।।

kāśīsundarāvadānam ।

jayati sa sattvaviśeṣaḥ sattvavatām sarvasattvasukhahetuḥ ।
dehadalane api śamayati kopāgniṃ śāntimuccairyaḥ ।।

dharmopadeśe bhagavān kauṇḍinyasyāgravartinaḥ ।
bhikṣoḥ kathāprasaṅgena pṛṣṭp bhikṣubhirabhyadhāt ।।

brahmadattasya tanayo vārāṇasyāṃ mahīpateḥ ।
kāśisundaranāmā va kālabhūśca babhuvatuḥ ।।

yauvarājyabharaikarhaḥ kumāraḥ kāśisundaraḥ ।
dharmādharmamayaṃ rājyaṃ vicāryācintayacciram ।।

kṣaṇakṣayiṇi tāruṇye jīvite vīcicañcale ।
rājye svapnavivāhe asmin mohamūle na me matiḥ ।।

rāgapralāpabahule māyāmphamahe muhuḥ ।
veśyārodananiḥsāre saṃsāre nāsti satyatā ।।

pravrajyāmanaghastasmādagārādanagārikam ।
nistriṃśavṛttisaṃsaktābhirāgaḥ kiṃ vibhūtibhiḥ ।।

rājasūnurvicintyeti vivekavimalāśayaḥ ।
uvācābhyetya bhūpālamaraṇyagamanotsukaḥ ।।

mama saṃbhogavargo ayaṃ rājannaivopayujyate ।
yauvarājyābhiṣekārhaḥ samārambho nivāryatām ।।

krodhāgnitaptāḥ sutarāmetāstāta na me matāḥ ।
baddhabandhabhayāyāsajananyo rājasaṃpadaḥ ।।

vyāptāḥ krūratarācārairjvalitāḥ pārthivaśriyaḥ ।
kurvanti kasya nodvegaṃ śmaśānāgniśikhā iva ।।

chatrasaṃchāditā lokāścāmarānilalolitāḥ ।
patanti pātakaśvabhre madakṣībāḥ kṣitīśvarāḥ ।।

mṛdubhogāṃśukābhyāsasukumāre mahībhujām ।
kāye patati paryante kleśaḥ kuliśadāruṇaḥ ।।

cintāsaṃtatasaṃtāpatīvratṛṣṇāpralāpinām ।
rājyajvarajuṣāṃ naiṣāṃ mohamūrcchā nivartate ।।

vakrāṇāṃ ratnadīptānāṃ dvijihānāṃ pade pade ।
chidrasaṃdarśināṃ rājñāṃ vyāpāraḥ paramāraṇam ।।

nṛpavaṃśaśatocchiṣṭāṃ manyate māmananyagām ।
itīva śrīḥ kṣītīśānāṃ hāracāmarahāsinī ।।

vyañjitavyajanocchvasā lakṣmīrmuktāśrusaṃtatiḥ ।
rājñāṃ mohābhṛtātītabhūpatismaraṇādiva ।।

tasmādvrajāmi pravrajyāvivarjitajanasthitiḥ ।
saṃtoṣaśītalacchāyaṃ saṃtāpaśamanaṃ vanam ।।

aviśrāntasya saṃsārapathapānthasya durvahaḥ ।
kāyo asya yatsadāpāyaḥ kiṃ punaḥ pṛthivībharaḥ ।।

iti putravacaḥ śrutvā bhūptirbhṛśamapriyam ।
pravrajyāśabdacakitaḥ sodvegastamabhāṣataḥ ।।

asya vaṃśasya mahataḥ sāmrājyasya vṛddhaye ।
āśānibaddhavṛddhena tvayi putra mayā param ।।

vatsa saṃkalpabhangaṃ me na kāle krtumarhasi ।
idaṃ tava mahacchāyaṃ yauvanaṃ na vanocitam ।।

samantrābhyāsayuktānām śaktānāṃ sādhudarśane ।
jitendriyāṇāṃ saravtra nṛpāṇāmavanaṃ tapaḥ ।।

svapade api sarojasya niḥsaṅgasalilasthitiḥ ।
dṛṣṭvā vane apyaśokasya lalanācaraṇāhatiḥ ।।

svagehasulabhairbhogairyāvaddṛṣṭivisūcikā ।
tāvadete parityuktaṃ śakyante viṣayāḥ kṣaṇam ।।

sukhamantaḥ parityajya svajanaṃ gṛhanirgataḥ ।
abhyastabhogacirahakleśaṃ na sahate janaḥ ।।

śrūyate smaryate dharmaḥ kriyate ca sukhād gṛhe ।
vane śuṣyanti śuṣkāṇāṃ śravaṇāsmaraṇakriyāḥ ।।

kṣaratkṣatajapādasya darbhasaṃdarbhasūcibhiḥ ।
tataḥ kiṃ duḥkhamaparaṃ paralole bhaviṣyati ।।

bhuñjānaṃ janamīkṣante yātāścarmāsthiśeṣatām ।
paradataṃ sadāśnanti pretā iva tapasvinaḥ ।।

vane nivasanaṃ putra pāṃśuprāvaraṇaṃ samam ।
pālanaṃ brahmacaryasya makarākaraśoṣaṇam ।।

dāvāgnidhūmavikaṭabhrukuṭimukheṣu gonāsavāsaghanaghūkaguhāgṛheṣu ।
siṃhāhatadviradalohitalohiteṣu tyaktvā gṛhaṃ bhavati kasya dhṛtirvaneṣu ।।

kāmī saṃyamamicchati smarati ca śyāmārateḥ saṃyamī
tṛptastīvrataravrateṣu ramate bhakṣyaṃ kṣudhā kāṅkṣḥati ।
ekākī janamīhate janavanodvegī vanaṃ vāñchati
tyaktvānveṣaṇatatparāḥ punarapi prāpyāvamānaṃ janāḥ ।।

na māṃ putra parityajya gahanaṃ gantumarhasi ।
bhavantu tava śatrūṇāṃ vanavāsamanorathāḥ ।।

vyaktamauktikahāsinyaḥ karavālalatā iva ।
tyaktā na punarāyānti māninyo nṛpasaṃpadaḥ ।।

ityukro apyasakṛt pitrā niścayānna cacāla saḥ ।
vajraratnaśikhākalpaḥ saṃkalpo hi mahātmanām ।।

jananībhiramātyaiśca bandhupauramahattamaiḥ ।
sa prārthito apyabhūnmaunī nirāhāro dinatrayam ।।

rājabhogī tapasvī vā jīvatveṣa nijecchayā ।
kāmānuvartī lolo ayamityūciḥ sacivā nṛpam ।।

sa kathaṃcidanujñātaḥ sāśrunetreṇa bhūbhujā ।
yayau paurajanākrandamaunī munitapovanam ।।

vairāgyaparipākeṇa tatra maitrīpavitritām ।
bheje sa sarvasattveṣu vivekadayitāṃ dayām ।।

babhūvustatprabhāveṇa tatra sarvavanaukasāṃ ।
jātivairājalatyāgaśītalāścittavṛttayaḥ ।।

tyakte prāṇavadhe prasaktahariṇīvṛndaiḥ pulindaiḥ paraṃ
siṃhairvāraṇadāraṇanyuparame sarvāṅgasaṅgīkṛte ।
māyūrāvaraṇairdaridrajaghanā muktākalāpojjhitās
tatrocchvāsavirāgaśuṣyadadharā jātāḥ kirātāṅganāḥ ।।

kṣamāṃ tyaktvābdhivasanāṃ saravbhūtakṣamāśritaḥ ।
so abhavat kṣāntivādīti viśutaḥ kāśisundaraḥ ।।

atrāntare mahīharṣe brahmadatte divaṃ gate ।
udvega iva bhūtānāṃ bhūpālaḥ kalibhūrabhūt ।।

athadabhrabhramadbhṛṅgabhrūbhaṅgamalinānanaḥ ।
munisaṃyamavidveṣī vasantaḥ pratyadṛśyata ।।

madanonmādabhutasya prodbhūtasya mṛgīdṛśām ।
mānavidhvaṃsadūtasya cutasya ruruce ruciḥ ।।

raktāśokasya pārśvasthalatāliṅganaśaṅkitaḥ ।
īrṣyāluriva puṣpāṇi jahāra malayānilaḥ ।।

udyānayauvane tasmin kāle kokilasaṃkule ।
sāntaḥpuro nṛpaḥ prāyād vanālokanakautukī ।।

nānāvarṇapatatpuṣpaprakārapracitāni saḥ ।
paśyan vanāni ramyāṇi śanaiḥ prāpa tapovanam ।।

vanasthalīṣu kāntāsu tatra kanyāsakhaściram ।
vihṛtya rativiśrāntaḥ kṣasṇaṃ nidrāmavāptavān ।।

apūrvakusumasmerāścinvānāstatra mañjarī ।
antaḥpurāṅganāśceruḥ saṃcāriṇyo latā iva ।।

atrāntare kṣāntivādī viviktoddeśanirvṛtaḥ ।
ekānte niścalastasthau śāntimantarvicintayan ।।

amandānandaciṣyandī vandanīyo manīṣiṇām ।
kṛśo apyakṛśasaundaryaḥ śaśīva prathamoditaḥ ।।

pariṇāmamanojñena rekhāsaṃsthānaśobhinā ।
purāṇacitrarūpeṇa naiva śūnyā tadākṛtiḥ ।।

taṃ dṛṣṭvā rājalalanāścittadarpaṇamārjanam ।
tatraiva niścalāstasthustāścitralikhitā iva ।।

prabuddho atha nṛpaḥ kṣipraṃ nāpaśyaddayitāḥ puraḥ ।
dadarśa vanamanviṣya parivārya sthitā munim ।।

bhujaṅgastā vilokyaiva śvasannīrṣyāviṣākulaḥ ।
visasarja varocūpahalāhalamivotkaṭam ।।

kastvaṃ munivyañjanayā citrakṛtrimamātrayā ।
muṣṇāsi mugdhagṛdayā nūnaṃ nārīpratārakaḥ ।।

parastrīharaṇe dhyāna japastadvighnavāraṇe ।
dhūrtānāṃ paramopāyaḥ saralāśvāsanaṃ tapaḥ ।।

mukhamādhuryadhūrtasya vṛttirvalkalinastava ।
aho nu mohajananī vane viṣataroriva ।।

munikalpasamākalpaścaritaṃ punarīdṛśam ।
siddhiṃ saṃbhāvitāṃ vāpi vetti kastattvamāntaram ।।

ityukte bhūbhujā krodhādakrodhamadhurāśayaḥ ।
nirvikāreṇa manasā kṣāntivādī jagād tam ।।

kṣāntivādī munirahaṃ na māṃ śankitumarhasi ।
etāsu nirviśeṣo me kāntāsu ca talāsu ca ।।

iti tenoktamākarṇya kṣāntaṃ paśyāmi te adhunā ।
iti bruvāṇaściccheda hastau tasyāsinā nṛpaḥ ।।

viśase api kṣamāśīlaṃ nivikāraṃ vilokya tam ।
cakarta caraṇau tasya praśamāya samatsaraḥ ।।

pradiśantyaśivaṃ mārge jihvayā dūṣayanti ca ।
lumpantyaṅgāni paryante khalāḥ kauleyakā iva ।।

tāḍane api kṣamāsaktāḥ skandhacchede api mauninaḥ ।
śītalāstīvratāpe api saralāḥ saralā iva ।।

nikṛttapāṇicaraṇaḥ sa saṃstabhya pṛthuvyathām ।
rakṣan manyumanaḥkṣobhaṃ kṣamayā samacintayat ।।

tyaktānyakarmaṇānena cchinnānyaṅgāṇi me yathā ।
saṃsāraviṣamakleśacchedaṃ kuryāmahaṃ tathā ।।

kopamohādavajñāya nṛpatau bhrātaraṃ munim ।
purīṃ prayāte rajasā śokamlāneva bhūrabhūt ।।

tatastadduḥkhakupitā rājñe tatkṣāntidevatā ।
cakre nagaryāṃ durbhokṣamarakāvṛṣṭiviplavam ।।

naimittikebhyo vijñāya rājāmuniparābhavāt ।
devatākoapajaṃ doṣaṃ taṃ prasādayituṃ yayau ।।

nipatya pādayostasya kṣamasvetyabhidhāya saḥ ।
paścāttāpaviṣādena niścetana ivābhavat ।।

tamabravītkṣāntivādī rājan manyurna me aṇvapi ।
karmarekhāparicchedādīdṛśī bhavitavyatā ।।

sarvāṇi na gaṇayati svacchandā bhavitavyatā ।
na dhairyaṃ na guṇaṃ nārthaṃ na tapo nāpi gauravam ।।

antrasthitaprasavabījaparaṃparāṇi bhinnāni kālaparipākavicitritāni ।
janmasthale vipulamūlabalasya janturbhuṅkte phalāni nijakarmamahīruhasya ।।

tvayi tasmānna me kaścid vikāro asti mahīpate ।
satyenānename paśya rudhiraṃ kṣīratāṃ gatam ।।

aṅgacchede apyakaluṣi babhūva yadi me manaḥ ।
satyenaitena ściṣṭāni tānyevāṅgāni santu me ।।

iti śuddhadhiyastasya tībrasayopayācanāt ।
śliṣṭānyaṅgāni tānyeva sahasā sv āsthyamāyayuḥ ।।

mukuṭaspṛṣṭacaraṇastamuvāca nṛpastataḥ ।
mune mahāprabhāvo asi tapasā tatkimicchasi ।।

puṇyahastāvalambena mphāndhaṃ karuṇānidhe ।
pāpāvasāne patitaṃ māṃ tvamuddhartumarhasi ।।

ityarthitaḥ kṣitīśena pratyabhāṣata taṃ muniḥ ।
saṃtāraṇāya magnānāṃ baddhānāmapi muktaye ।।
āśvāśanāya bhītānāṃ nirvāṇāya vimuhyatām ।।
yadā tu samyaksaṃbodhiṃ tāmavāpnoṣyanuttarām ।
mohacchedaṃ kariṣyāmi tadā jñānāsinā tava ।।

prayayau munirityuktvā tamāmantrya svamāśramam ।
tameva manasā dhyāyan rājadhānīṃ nṛpo apyagāt ।।

kṣāntivādī sa evāhaṃ kauṇḍinyaḥ kālabhūrayam ।
āsādya samyaksaṃbodhimṛddhṛto ayaṃ mayādhunā ।।

iti sugatamukhāravindanirmitamadhuramadhupratimaṃ vacaḥ prasannam ।
bhramarabhava ivoditapramodaḥ kimapi babhūva nipīya bhikṣusaṃghaḥ ।।

iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ kāśīsundarāvadānaṃ nāma ūnatriṃśaḥ pallavaḥ ।।

suvarṇapārśvāvadānam ।

ślāṣyaḥ ko api sa sattvasārasaralaḥ saujanyapuṇyasthitir
nindya ko api sa dharmamārgagamane vighnaḥ kṛtaghnaḥ param ।
citraṃ yaccaritaṃ vicārya suciraṃ romāñcacarcācitas
tulyaṃ yāti janaḥ sabāṣpanayanastadvarpane mūkatām ।।

devadattaprasaṅgena bhikṣubhirbhagavān purā ।
pṛṣṭaḥ kathāmakathayat pūrvavṛttāntasaṃśrayām ।।

mahendrasenanāmābhūd vārāṇasyāṃ nareśvaraḥ ।
yayuḥ kṣitīśvarāḥ sarve yasya lakṣmyā vilakṣatām ।।

candraprabhābhavattasya divyakīrtiriva priyā ।
yasyāḥ patyuḥ prabhāveṇa svapnāḥ satyatvamāyayuḥ ।।

babhūva samaye tasmin mṛtayūthapatirvane ।
suvarṇapārśva ityāptanāmā hemamayacchaviḥ ।।

nīlaratnodarāspharamuktāhāranibhaprabhā ।
abhūddṛṣṭicchaṭā yasya bhūṣaṇaṃ kānanaśriyaḥ ।।

pravālavalliśṛṅgasya citraratnacitatvacaḥ ।
tasyāścaryasudhāmbhodhilaharī ruruce ruciḥ ।।

bodhisattvāvatārasya tasya kāntamabhūdvapuḥ ।
pūrvaṃ sukṛtacitrasya lakṣaṇaṃ hi surūpatā ।।

dīrghadṛṣṭirbabhūvāsya vayasyo vṛddhavāyasaḥ ।
labdhakānveṣaṇatrāse digvilokanatatparaḥ ।।

tau kathābhirmithaḥ prītyā vivikteṣu vijasratuḥ ।
prākpuṇyairjāyate vāṇī tiraścāmapi māṇuṣī ।।

sa kadācijjalānveṣī yathūnāthaḥ sahānugaiḥ ।
taṭinyā veṇumālinyāḥ pulinaṃ samupāyayau ।।

tasya tārataraṃ śrutvā dīrghamākrandaniśvanam ।
hariṇā dudruvuḥ sarve grīvāvalanavibhramaiḥ ।।

suvarṇapārśvastu tadā kṛpāpāśavaśīkṛtaḥ ।
tatraiva niścalastasthau marmaviddha iveṣuṇā ।।

taduddharaṇasaṃnaddhaṃ dīrghadṛṣṭiṃ vilokya tam ।
kākaḥ provāca na sakhe yukto ataṃ te samudyamaḥ ।।

puṣpopamā vipatkāle kṛtārthāḥ kuliśopamāḥ ।
kṛtamete na manyante svakāyasuhṛdaḥ khalāḥ ।।

ityasau vāryamāṇo api kākena karuṇākulaḥ ।
avatīryāśu saritaṃ saralastamatārata ।।

vimucya bandhanānyasya sa śṛṅgābhyāmaśaṅkitaḥ ।
taṃ pādapatitaṃ dīnamavadadgantumudyatam ।।

na tvayā kathanīyo ahamatrasthaḥ kasyacitsakhe ।
prārthayante suvarṇaṃ māṃ carmalubdhā hi lubdhakāḥ ।।

ityuktastena vinayāt tattathetyabhidhāya saḥ ।
yayau kuṭilakākhyastaṃ praṇamya prastutastutiḥ ।।

atrāntare narapateḥ patnī candraprabhā niśi ।
svapne dadarśāsanasthaṃ mṛgaṃ saddharmavādinam ।।

satysvapnātha sā devī prabuddhā nṛpamabravīt ।
suvarṇahariṇaḥ svapne deva dṛṣṭo mayādbhutaḥ ।।

tamahaṃ draṣṭumicchāmi sākṣādupagataṃ mṛgam ।
aṅkādiva mṛgāṅkasya nirgataṃ rāhuśaṅkayā ।।

ityuktaḥ praṇayātprīto devyā ca pṛthivīpatiḥ ।
mṛgagrahāya vyasṛjat lubdhakān draviṇapradaḥ ।।

tataḥ pratinivṛttāste vanamanviṣya lubdhakāḥ ।
niṣphalāgamanakruddhaṃ sakampā jagadurnṛpam ।।

iyatīṃ jagatī deva vicitā nicitācalaiḥ ।
bhrāntā vayamaviśrāntā na labhyastadvidho mṛgaḥ ।।

āścaryaracanākṛṣṭalocanaś cārulocanaḥ ।
svapnasaṃpannarūpo asau hiraṇyahariṇaḥ kutaḥ ।।

mano vinodane tasmin yadi deva prasīdati ।
kurvantu kāñcanamṛgaṃ kuśalāḥ ke api śilpinaḥ ।।

iti śrutvā sa nṛpatirdadadbahutaraṃ dhanam ।
mṛgānveṣaṇasaṃkalpe babhūvābhiniveśavān ।।

tataḥ kuṭilako abhyetya nṛpaṃ śrutvā bahupradam ।
uvāca draviṇādāne lubdhakebhyo api lubdhadhīḥ ।।

prasādaḥ kriyatāṃ deva mṛgaṃ saṃdarśayāmyamah ।
dṛṣṭaḥ kanakasārāṅga sāraṅgaḥ samayā vane ।।

ityākarṇya kṣitipatiḥ praharṣitphullalocanaḥ ।
bhadra saṃdarśaya kkāsau kkāsāvityavadanmuhuḥ ।।

tamevāgresaraṃ kṛtvā mṛgamārgapradarśakam ।
sasainyaḥ sa yayau svacchacchatracandrodayācalaḥ ।।

dīrghadṛṣṭirdadarśātha kākastaruśiraḥsthitaḥ ।
gajavājivrajodīrṇareṇupravāraṇaṃ vanam ।।

suvarṇapārśvamabhyetya jagāda mṛyayūthapam ।
hitamuktaṃ mayā pūrvaṃ na śrutaṃ na kṛtaṃ tvayā ।।

sa eṣa puruṣaḥ prāptaḥ saṃnaddhaiḥ saha dhanvibhiḥ ।
mayā nivāritenāpi saṃhāreṇa na tṛpyate ।।

adhunā kka nu gantavyaṃ kiṃ kartavyaṃ bhayodbhave ।
hitaṃ kimanuvartavyaṃ tulyaṃ martavyameva vā ।।

kṛtaghnaḥ krūracaritaḥ kṣudro ayaṃ saṃghapātakah ।
tvayaivātmavināśāya rakṣito viṣapādapaḥ ।।

svaśarīrapradasyāpi saṃhāreṇa na tṛpyate ।
sasattvasāgaragrāsī kṛtaghno vāḍavānalaḥ ।।

upakāraḥ kṛtaghneṣu viśvāsaḥ kuṭulātmasu ।
upadeśaśca mūrkheṣu karturdoṣāya kevalam ।।

iti kākena kathite pratyāsanne ca pārthive ।
acintayat prāptakālaṃ hitaṃ yūthasya yūthapah ।।

subhaṭānāmiyaṃ senā vigāhedgahanaṃ mahat ।
karoti matprasaṅgena muhūrtenaiva nirmṛgam ।।

tasmātsainyapradhānasya gacchāmi svayamantikam ।
ekasyaiva vadho me astu sarve jīvantvamī mṛgāḥ ।।

iti niścitya sa yayau samīpaṃ bhūpatermṛgaḥ ।
paraprāṇaparitrāṇe tṛṇaṃ prāṇāṃ mahātmanām ।।

tamāyāntaṃ drutaṃ dṛṣṭvā hṛṣṭaḥ kuṭulakah puraḥ ।
so ayamityāśu pāṇibhyām rājñe dūre vyadarśayat ।।

tatkṣaṇe droṇaśāpena vajreṇeva nipātinā ।
karu paricyutau tasya pāpapādapapallavau ।।

tadvṛttaṃ vismitaḥ śrutvā mṛgeṇa kathitaṃ nṛpaḥ ।
abhūtkṛtaghnacarite dhikkāramukharānanaḥ ।।

tataḥ kṣitipatiḥ prītyā parayā mṛgam ।
tam nināya svanagarīṃ gauraveṇa garīyasā ।।

rājadhānīmathāsādya tasmai ratnāsanaṃ nṛpaḥ ।
datvā sāntaḥpurāmātyastasyāgre samupāviśat ।।

sa bodhisattvo hariṇastasyāṃ parṣadi divyadhīḥ ।
dharmaṃ dideśa yenābhūjjanaḥ śikṣāpadānvitaḥ ।।

suvarṇapārśvaḥ sāraṅgaḥ so ayamevābhavaṃ purā ।
yo abhavat kuṭilaḥ krūro devadattaḥ sa cādhunā ।।

iti sukṛtacitaṃ bhagavatā bhavabhītibhidā
kathitamudārasattvarucirasya tataścaritam ।
praśamamayaṃ niśamya kuśalāya sa bhikṣugaṇaḥ
kimapi babhūva puṇyaparipākavivekaruciraḥ ।।

iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ suvarṇapārśvāvadānaṃ triṃśaḥ pallavaḥ ।।

kalyāṇakāryavadānam ।

pratyakṣalakṣaṇaparīkṣita eṣa loke saṃlakṣyate sujanadurjanayorviśeṣaḥ ।
arkaḥ prakāśaviśadaṃ vidadhāti viśvamandhīkaroti nikhilaṃ jagadandhakāraḥ ।।

sarvajñaḥ pūrvavṛttāntamaśeṣamavalokayan ।
asminneva kathārambhe bhagavān punarabravīt ।।

nṛpaḥ pātaliputrākhye pure bhūmipuraṃdaraḥ ।
abhūtpuraṃdaro nāma mandiraṃ puṇyasaṃpadaḥ ।।

kalyāṇakārī tasyābhūt sūnurguṇagaṇonnataḥ ।
akalyāṇābhidhānaścadvitīyo nirguṇaḥ sutaḥ ।।

kalyāṇakārī sarvārthikaruṇākalpapādapaḥ ।
chatrāvaśeṣāmakarod dāṇaśīlaḥ śriyaṃ pituḥ ।।

tasmai manoramāṃ nāma puṇyaseno mahīpatiḥ ।
dūtaṃ visṛjya lekhena svasutām v acasā dadau ।।

pratyāsannavivāho atha nṛpaṃ rājasuto abhyadhāt ।
prāptaḥ pariṇayastāta saṃpratyeṣa na me mataḥ ।।

vātsalyapeśalatayā madāttāḥ prakṛtiśriyaḥ ।
mayā dānavyasaninā koṣaste śuṣirīkṛtaḥ ।।

tasmātpravahaṇenāhaṃ samuttīrya mahodadhim ।
ratnadvīpaṃ vrahāmyeva divyaratnārjanodyataḥ ।।

divyasaṃpadamāsādya kariṣye dārasaṃgraham ।
kalatramakṛtārthasya trāsanaṃ sukhasaṃpadām ।।

iyuktvā sa pituḥ prāpya śāsanaṃ caraṇānataḥ ।
jagāhe jaladhiṃ lolakallolāliṅgitāmbaram ।।

bhrātā tamanuvajrāja saujanyavyañjano anujaḥ ।
nirguṇaḥ saguṇadveṣadrohamantarvicintayan ।।

jyeṣṭhastamabravīdvatsa samudre karmaviplavāt ।
ahaṃ grāhyastvayā skandhe jāte pravahaṇakṣaye ।।

iti bhrātrā kṛtāśvāsastathetyūve sa taṃ śaṭhaḥ ।
doṣodyataḥ praṇayitāṃ khalaḥ samavalambate ।।

tataḥ pravāhaṇārūḍhaḥ pavanairanukūlatām ।
yātaiḥ puṇyairiva prāpya ratnadvīpaṃ nṛpātmajaḥ ।।

dovyaratnāni saṃprāpya pratyāvṛtte tataḥ śanaiḥ ।
rājaputre pravahaṇaṃ drāgabhañjat prabhañjanaḥ ।।

bhagne pravahaṇe tasmin bhrātaraṃ pūrvasaṃvidā ।
sa jagrāha śaṭhaḥ kaṇṭhe taṃ bhujaṅga ivānujaḥ ।।

karmavāteritastūrṇaṃ kūlaṃ prāpya nṛpātmajaḥ ।
avāpa sahasā nidrāmāndhyaprathamadūtikām ।।

tasya suptasya ratnāni dṛṣṭvā baddhānyathānujaḥ ।
prahartuṃ vyasanacchidre krūraḥ samupacakrame ।।

utpāṭya gāḍhabaddhasya sa tasya nayanāmbujam ।
taṃ tārakaṃ bhayāmbhodhau cakāra gatatārakam ।।

āttaratne gate tasmin vājasūnurgatadyutiḥ ।
mātaṅgonmūlitāmbhoja ivābhūtkamalākaraḥ ।।

sa babhūva nirālokaḥ śokatīvratamovṛtaḥ ।
kṛṣṇapakṣakṣapārambha iva sūryenduvarjitaḥ ।।

atrāntare samāyātastaṃ deśaṃ gokuśādhipaḥ ।
rājaputraṃ vilokyāndhamabhūt saṃkrāntatadvyathah ।।

sa taṃ nītvā svanilayaṃ paricaryāparaḥ pārḥ ।
tasyāsīdguṇasaujanyasnehāveśavaśīkṛtaḥ ।।

tatra śokasujāṃ śāntyai sadā cetovinodinīm ।
vīṇāṃ svarapravīṇo asau pūrvābhyastamavādayat ।।

satsaṃgamaḥ pṛthuvivekakathābhoyogaḥ
kāvyāsavaḥ priyasuhṛtpraṇayo vihāraḥ ।
vīṇāsvanah kusumakāntavanāntavāsaḥ
śokāgnitaptamanasāmamṛtāvagāhaḥ ।।

tasya gopapateḥ patnī tīgavīṇāvicakṣaṇā ।
paśyantī rājatanayaṃ prayayau sābhilāṣatām ।।

kṛtopadeśā satataṃ kuṭilā vīṇayeva sā ।
mūrcchantī navarāgeṇa sotkaṇṭhā samacintayat ।।

subhago ayaṃ mamātīva dṛśi citte ca cartate ।
nivartate na me tāpaḥ premṇi cenna pravartate ।।

dhanyeyaṃ nakhasaṃpātaiḥ kkaṇantī rāgiṇīmuhuḥ ।
yātāsya vallakī puṇyairaṅkārohaṇayogyatām ।।

iti saṃcintya sā svairaṃ tamuvāca savibhamam ।
spṛśantī tatkarāmbhojaṃ sakampakarapallavā ।।

lalanāsulabhāṃ lajjāṃ mamedaṃ tvadgataṃ manaḥ ।
akṛtajña iva prītiṃ na saṃsmarati mānada ।।

na śīlaṃ na kulācāraṃ nābhimānaṃ na saṃśayam ।
apekṣante smarakṣiptā vailakṣyarahitāḥ striyaḥ ।।

praṇayānmama saṅkalpaṃ saphalaṃ kartumarhasi ।
bhavanti mānitāḥ prītyai devatā iva yoṣitaḥ ।।

iti tasya vacaḥ śrutvā bhinnasvaraviśṛṅkhalam ।
capalāṃ rājaputrastāṃ trastāntaḥkarṇo avadat ।।

neyaṃ mātaḥ samucitā sataḥ śīlaparicyutiḥ ।
dhikkilbiṣaviṣaspṛṣṭaḥ naṣṭaśīlasya jīvitam ।।

parāṅganāpariṣvaṅgamaṅgairaṅgīkaroti yaḥ ।
āliṅgati pataṅgo ayaṃ narakāgniśikhāṃ punah ।।

paropakāraniratāh paradāranirādarāḥ ।
ye apyahiṃsāvyasaninaste jīvanti mṛtāḥ pare ।।

iti tenoktamākarṇya sābhūdbhagnamanorathā ।
nidhanābhyadhikaḥ prītipratiṣedho hi yoṣitām ।।

tataḥ svapatimabhyetya bhujaṅgī bhaṅgamāgate ।
manorathe manyuviṣaṃ vamantīva jagāda sā ।।

paravatsalatā sādho doṣāya saralasya te ।
ko hyavijñātaśīlānāṃ svādhīnīkurute gṛham ।।

pareṣu bhṛśamāśvāsaṃ spṛśataste na śobhanam ।
guptaṃ cittaṃ ca vittaṃ ca jano jānāti kasya kaḥ ।।

paradārasahasrākṣastvayāndhaḥ sa gṛhe dhṛtaḥ ।
dīnāndhajanavātsalyāt paśya tasyocitaṃ phalam ।।

adyāhaṃ tena vijane saṃgame bhṛśamarthitā ।
yadyasya nayane syātāṃ syāt kathaṃ me palāyanam ।।

ityuktaḥ sa tayā kopāttapto gopapatirbhṛśam ।
dvare niṣkāsya taṃ cakre gehaṃ cittaṃ ca śītalam ।।

pitā tyajati yatputraṃ suhṛnmitraṃ nihanti yat ।
bandhucchedāsidhārāṇāṃ taddārāṇāṃ vijṛmbhitam ।।

bhruvordṛśoryatkauṭilyaṃ yattaikṣṇyaṃ yacca cāpalam ।
kucayoryacca kāṭhinyaṃ tatsarvaṃ hṛdi yoṣitām ।।

kalyāṇakārisārthena pathaḥ saṃtāritaṃ śanaiḥ ।
pitari tridivaṃ yāte śuśrāva bhrātaraṃ nṛpam ।।

sa puraṃ puṇyasenasya śvaśurasya mahīpateḥ ।
kālena prāppa dūrādhvakleśapraśamabāndhavam ।।

atrāntare sutā tatra mahībharturmanoramā ।
vācā dattā purā yasmai tasminnabdhicyute śrute ।।

āhūteṣu narendreṣu niviṣṭeṣu yathākramam ।
āruhya ratnaśibikāṃ svayaṃvarabhuvaṃ yayau ।।

vilokayantī bhūpālān sā śanaiścalalocanā ।
yadṛcchayāgataṃ tatra rājaputraṃ dadarśa tam ।।

andho api tasyāḥ sahas āsa yayau priyatāṃ dṛśoḥ ।
grahamadhye kumudvatyā meghāndho api priyaḥ śaśī ।।

nṛpeṣu pratiyāteṣu vilakṣeṣvaphalāgamāt ।
mahīpatisutāntastaṃ vavre guṇavinirgatam ।।

sāpu hāraṃ parikṣipya kaṇṭhe tasyāyatekṣaṇā ।
śanakaurmadhurālāpā tvadvaśāsmītyuvāca tam ।।

strīvṛttacakitaḥ so api vijane tāmabhāṣata ।
prajñādaridrayā nedaṃ striyā yuktaṃ kṛtaṃ tvayā ।।

smarasauhārdamitreṣu padmanetreṣu rājasu ।
sthiteṣu vandhyajanmāndhaḥ kasmādasmi vṛtastvayā ।।

anyavakrkrāvalokinyo jāyāścakṣuṣmatāmapi ।
vadhūḥ kiṃ punarandhasya dine apyanyābhisārikā ।।

lalanābhirna me kṛtyaṃ pratyayastāsu nāsti me ।
kulakūlanipātinyo nimnagāḥ kuṭilāḥ stiyaḥ ।।

ityuktā tena paruṣaṃ lajjālolā nṛpātmajā ।
tamūce nātha sar vatra na śaṅkāṃ kartumarhasi ।।

dṛṣṭadoṣaḥ kkacinnāryām yadi tvamatiśaṅkitaḥ ।
aduṣṭāpi tvayā nāma tadvyāptā kriyate katham ।।

tvayyeva yadi me prītirananyaśaraṇam manaḥ ।
tena satyena te netramekaṃ bhavatu nirmalam ।।

ityuktamātre sudṛśā dakṣiṇaṃ tasya lecanam ।
satyānubhāvenābhūttatpraphullakamalopamam ।।

rājaputraḥ prahṛṣṭo atha tām prasādya silocanām ।
uvāca tanmukhāmbhojalāvaṇyaguṇacismitḥ ।।

kalyāṇakārī subhagaḥ sa evāhaṃ nṛpātmajaḥ ।
yasmau purā tvaṃ guruṇā vacasā pratipāditā ।।

sa evāhaṃ yadi paraṃ nirvairaḥ pāṭane dṛśaḥ ।
tena satyena nayanaṃ svasthaṃ bhavatu me aparam ।।

satyopayācaneneti sahasaivāsya locanam ।
dvitīyamapi vaimalyamavāpa saha cetasā ।।

tato viditavṛttena puṇyasenena bhūbhujā ।
kṛtasāhāyyakaḥ prāpa svarājya sa priyāsakhaḥ ।।

kalyāṇkārī yaḥ so ahaṃ devadattaḥ sa cānujaḥ ।
tena pūrvānubhāvena tadvidho adyāpi vartate ।।

ityudāramupakāranirmalaṃ bodhisattvacaritaṃ niśamya te ।
bhikṣavaḥ khalviceṣṭitaṃ ca tattulyamapratimavismayaṃ yayuḥ ।।

iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ kalyāṇākāryavadānamekatriṃśaḥ pallavaḥ ।।

viśākhāvadānam ।

vāmāḥ sajjanavāmāḥ prāyeṇa bhavanti nīrogiṇyaḥ ।
timironmukhī sarāgā kṣipati raviṃ bhūdharātsaṃdhyā ।।

devadattasya carite bahujanmāntarāśraye ।
kathite api punaḥ prāha bhagavān jñānasāgaraḥ ।।

purā kaliṅgaviṣaye nṛpatiḥ śatrubhaṅgakṛt ।
śrīmānabhūdaśokākhyaḥ prakhyātāsaṃkhyavikramaḥ ।।

tasya śākhaḥ praśākhaśca catvāraḥ sadṛśāḥ sutāḥ ।
anuśākho viśākhaścetyabhavan bhuvi viśrutāḥ ।।

tāruṇyamattāste pitrā sapatnīkāḥ pravāsitāh ।
savikāranikāreṇa putrasneho api naśyati ।।

te śanaiḥ kṣīṇapātheyā durdaśāmiva duḥsahām ।
vikaṭāmaṭavīṃ prāpyaṃ kṣutkṣāmāḥ samacintayan ।।

etāḥ striyo vipatkāle gulphabandhanaśṛṅkhalāḥ ।
kṛcchralabdhe ca bhāginyaḥ sthitāḥ parṇāśane api naḥ ।।

iti cintayatāmāsīt teṣāṃ strībadhaniścayah ।
durdaśādagdhabhāgyānāṃ ghorā saṃjāyate matiḥ ।।

teṣāṃ madhyādviśākhastu pāpasaṃkalpaśaṅkitaḥ ।
bhāryāmādāya kṛpayā palāyya prayayau pṛthak ।।

sā kalaṅkavatī nāma bhṛśaṃ vaiklavyamāgatā ।
dūrādhvadhāvanaśrāntā mūrcchitā nyapatadbhuvi ।।

tataḥ sā karuṇārdreṇa bhartrā prāṇakṣayakṣaṇe ।
śarāvedhasamudbhūtaṃ pāyitā nijaśoṇitam ।।

tām raktapānasaṃprāptajīvitām sattvasāgaraḥ ।
svāṅgaṃ niṣkṛtya māṃsena prāṇavṛttimakārayat ।।

nirjalaṃ ghorakāntāraṃ samuttīrya krameṇa tau ।
pracchāyapādapaśyāmaṃ prāptau girinadītaṭam ।।

viśrāntayostayostatra kṛttapādakaro naraḥ ।
tīvrākrandī nadīvegenohyamānaḥ samāyayau ।।

dṛṣṭvaiva karuṇāśliṣṭaḥ kaṣṭāṃ vipadamāśritaḥ ।
vigāhya saritaṃ dorbhyāṃ viśākhastamatārayat ।।

tataḥ pratyāgataprāṇāṃ toyamūlaphalādibhiḥ ।
sa taṃ cakre dinaireva saṃrūḍhacchedanirvyatham ।।

svastho api gativaikalyānnaiva gantuṃ kkacit kṣamaḥ ।
sa tasthaui tatra tatpatnyā kāle kalitabhojanah ।।

rājaputrastu jāyāyāmabhūdviralasaṃgamaḥ ।
siṃhālparatayaḥ śūrāḥ prāyeṇa vijigīṣavaḥ ।।

divyauṣadhirasāhāraparipūrṇatanuḥ śanaiḥ ।
tatpatnī vikalāyāsmau cakāra surataspṛhām ।।

snehena nopalipyante na badhyante guṇena ca ।
gurave na ca sajjanti svecchasparśasukhāḥ striyaḥ ।।

sā tena niśi niḥśabdaṃ ramamāṇā ghanastanī ।
niḥśaṅkasuratātṛptā patiṃ vighnamamanyata ।।

sā patyuḥ svairiṇī tena vidadhe vadhasaṃvidam ।
pāpeṣu śikṣākuśalāḥ kaluṣāḥ kila yoṣitaḥ ।।

sā śiraḥśūlamatulaṃ vadantī svasya chadmanā ।
cakre likhitapāpāsyā lalāṭe paṭṭabandhanam ।।

tasyāḥ śirorujāṃ tīvrāṃ vyatītaḥ pārthivātmajaḥ ।
kāruṇyāttatpratīkāre tāṃ tāṃ yuktimacintayat ।।

viṣādacintāstimitaṃ śvasantaṃ sā jagād tam ।
śītārtakūjadbhramarā himamlāneva padminī ।।

evaṃvidhaṃ me kanyāyāh śiraḥśūlaṃ purābhavat ।
pāṣāṇabhedalepena bhiṣagbhiśca nivāritam ।।

pāṣāṇabhedavyāpto ayaṃ prāgbhāgo asy mahībhṛtaḥ ।
rājjvāvatīrya bhavatā gṛhyatāṃ yadi śakyate ।।

dhārayiṣyāmi pāṇibhyāmahamālambanaṃ tava ।
ityuktaḥ praṇayātpatnayā tathetyāha nṛpātmajaḥ ।।

tatpāṇidhṛtarajjvātha vihitālambanaḥ śanaiḥ ।
so avatīrṇaḥ śilāsphālagarjadgirinadītaṭam ।।

bheṣajādānasaṃsaktaḥ saṃtyaktālambanastayā ।
sa papāta mahāśvabhre strīcittacapalāmbhasi ।।

śubhasya karmaṇaḥ śeṣādabhagnatanureva saḥ ।
uhyamānaḥ pravāheṇa dhīraścitamacintayat ।।

nārīcittābhamāvartaṃ darśayantyā nijāśayam ।
mama strīniyame nūnamupadeśaḥ kṛto anayā ।।

durvijñeyāḥ pratatamatibhiḥ svapnasaṃkalpakalpā
rāgadveṣavyasanaviṣamāyāsavinyāsasaktāḥ ।
kāmātkāmī sakalajanatāmohane saṃpravṛttāḥ
pātāyaiva kṣasṇaparicitasyāpi māyāḥ striyaśca ।।

iti saṃcintayanneva nadīvegena bhūyasā ।
prāpitaḥ sukṛteneva sa purīṃ puṣkarāvatīm ।।

tasminnavasare tatra niṣputre nṛpatau mṛte ।
nimittajñairmahāmātyairgṛhītaḥ sa sulakṣaṇaḥ ।।

abhiṣiktaḥ sa taistatra vidhivanmaṅgalodakaiḥ ।
abhūdvivāhavidveṣī dṛṣṭastrīcaritādbhutaḥ ।।

kalaṅkavatyapi girau bodhisattvavivarjite ।
mandvīryauṣadhiḥ kāle vṛtticchedākulābhavat ।।

skandhe bhagnāṅgamāropya sā grāmapuravartmasu ।
janaṃ pativratāsmīti girā bhikṣāmayācata ।।

parivratāgauraveṇa sarvastasyau dadau bahu ।
mithyāśīlapravādo api sūte vipadi saṃpadam ।।

aṭantī sā śanaiḥ prāptā nagarīṃ puṣkarāvatīm ।
satīti vanditā sarvairvṛpadvārāntike yayau ।।

rājā strīvṛttavidveṣī vandate tu pativratām ।
iti saṃcintya tadbhaktyā nṛpaṃ prāha puhohitaḥ ।।

dūredeśāntarāddeva prāptā kāpi pativratā ।
yayeyaṃ caraṇanyāsairbhūtadhātrī pavitritā ।।

he deva paśya tāṃ śādhvīṃ skandhāropitabhartṛkām ।
pativratāpraṇāmena puṃsāmāyurvivardhate ।।

nṛpaḥ purohiteneti tatsaṃdarśanamarthitaḥ ।
tamuvāca na jānīṣe brāhmaṇaḥ sarale bhavān ।।

snigdhā strīti pravādo ayaṃ nirvyājeti matibhramaḥ ।
satīti vyomapuṣpāptiḥ pāpā strīti na saṃśayaḥ ।।

niṣphalāścagnurohiṇyaḥ saralā janasaṃgame ।
nāryo vetasavallarya iva nirmūlabandhanāḥ ।।

bhedadrohaikaśīlābhyo duḥśīlābhyaḥ svabhāvataḥ ।
namaḥ strībhyo namaḥ strībhyo namaḥ strībhyo namo namah ।।

dṛṣṭastrīvṛttadoṣāya taccintāvyathitānmane ।
apyeṣā pṛthivī mahyaṃ ratnapūrṇā na rocate ।।

nagamṛgavadhūmugdhāstīkṣṇāḥ paraṃ paravañcane
tanuvitaraṇe saktāḥ puṃsāṃ haranti ca jīvitam ।
dadhati ca bhayaṃ puṣpāyāte pibanti ca pāvakaṃ
saralakuṭilā naiva jñātā vicāraśataiḥ striyaḥ ।।

tathāpi yadi nirbandhastava paśyāmi tāṃ striyam ।
ityuktvā harmyamāruhya tām dadarśa nareśvaraḥ ।।

tāmeva sa parijñāya pāpāṃ kṛttāṅgasaṅginīm ।
sacivebhyaḥ kṣitipatistadvṛttāntaṃ nyavedayat ।।

nṛpaṃ sāpi parijñāya pāpā kṣaṇamadhomukhī ।
nirastā prayayau tūrṇaṃ pihitaśravaṇairjanaiḥ ।।

viśākhanāmā naranāthasūnuḥ so ahaṃ vadhūḥ sāsya ca devadattaḥ ।
śrutvetivṛttaṃ kathitaṃ jinena bhikṣuvrajastaccaritaṃ nininda ।।

iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ viśākhāvadānaṃ dvātriṃśaḥ pallavaḥ ।।

nandīpanandāvadānam ।

sa ko api puṇyapraśamānubhāvaḥ śuddhātmanāmastyamṛtasvabhāvaḥ ।
yasya prabhāveṇa bhavanti sadyaḥ krūrā api krodhaviṣapramuktāḥ ।।

purā tathāgate jetavanārāmavihāriṇi ।
tadājñayā bhikṣugaṇe girikānanacāriṇi ।।

sumerupariṣaṇḍāyāṃ sthitvā dhyānaparāyaṇāḥ ।
āyayurbhikṣavaḥ pāṇḍuvicchāyavadanāḥ kṛśāḥ ।।

te atha kṛtvā bhagavataḥ pādapadmābhivandanām ।
ūcire bhikṣubhiḥ pṛṣṭā dehadaurbalyakāraṇam ।।

sumeruṃ triguṇāvṛttyā veṣṭayitvā vyavasthitau ।
adṛṣṭau vainateyasya nāgau nandopanandakau ।।

tau sadā trividhocchvāsaṃ sṛjataḥ kīrṇapāvakam ।
bhavanti bhasma sparśena sahasaiva śilā api ।।

vayaṃ tadviṣaniśvāsairnidagdhā dhyānayoginaḥ ।
vivarṇavadanacchāyāh kevalaṃ kṛśatāṃ gatāḥ ।।

iti taiḥ kathite śāstā bhikṣusaṃghārthitaḥ puraḥ ।
nāgayordamane yogyaṃ maudgalyāyanamādiśat ।।

sa sumeruṃ samāsādya śṛṅgairāliṅgitāmbaram ।
suptau dadarśa nāgendrau yogenāntarhitākṛtiḥ ।।

yodhyamānau śanaistena bubudhāte yadā na tau ।
tadā mahānāgavapurbhūtvā sa samaveṣṭayat ।।

prabuddhau pīḍitau tena dṛṣṭvā taṃ bhīṣaṇākṛtim ।
viṃdrutau nararūpeṇa tasthaturbhayavihvalau ।।

nāgarūpaṃ parityajya kṛtvā rūpaṃ svakaṃ tataḥ ।
palāyamānāvanyonyaṃ t au maudgalyāyano avadat ।।

nāgau kka gamyate tūrṇa bhayaṃ saṃtyajyatāmidam ।
na sa nāgaḥ sthitastatra yena vidrāvitau yuvām ।।

sarvathā yadi nastyea tadbhayād yivayordhṛtiḥ ।
kriyate kiṃ śaraṇyasya na buddhasyābhivandanam ।।

iti tenoktamākarṇya vinayāttau tamūcatuḥ ।
prasādaḥ kriyatāmārya bhagavaddarśanena nau ।।

iti bravāṇau nāgendrau nītvā bhagavato antikam ।
sa ta dvṛttāntamāvedya praṇamya samupāviśat ।।

bhagavānatha nāgendrau babhāṣe śaraṇāgatau ।
praṇāmaṃ cakratū ratnaprabhābhūṣītabhūtalau ।।

śikṣāpadāni saṃprāpya sarvabhūtābhayapradau ।
śaraṇaprāptisamayādadhunā nirbhayau yuvām ।।

ityālokanamātreṇa doṣadveṣavivarjitau ।
kṛtau bhagavatā samyak jagmatustaṃ praṇamya tau ।।

saṃdarśanenaiva mahāśayānāṃ prabhāpadeśena śarīralagnaiḥ ।
sīṃsrā api dveṣaviṣoṣmataptāḥ śamāmṛtaiḥ śītalatāṃ vrajanti ।।

tatpūrvajanmavṛttāṇtaṃ bhikṣubhirbhagavān jinaḥ ।
prabhāvavismayātpṛṣṭaḥ sarvadarśī jagādā tān ।।

kṛkirnāma purā śrīmān vārāṇasyāṃ nareśvaraḥ ।
kāśyapākhyād bhagavataḥ prāptavān dharmaśāsanam ।।

amātyayoḥ sa vinyasya rājyaṃ nandopanandayoḥ ।
babhūva bodhisaṃsaktaḥ satyadarśananirvṛtaḥ ।।

dharmadahrmamayaṃ rājyaṃ kṛtvā tau tasya mantriṇau ।
sarvopakaraṇairyuktaṃ vihāraṃ kāśyapāya ca ।।

kālena jātau nāgendrāvetau nandopanandakau ।
vihārārpaṇapuṇyena padaṃ merurabhūttayoḥ ।।

iti jinanigaditaphaṇivaracaritaṃ paratanupariṇatiparicitasukṛtam ।
śrutavati śamanayamuniparinivahe viṣadharaniyamanaguṇanutirudabhūt ।।

iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ nandopanandāvadānaṃ trayastriṃśaḥ pallavaḥ ।।

gṛhapatisudattāvadānam ।

dattaḥ parahitabhāvanayā yadu tanudhanakaṇaśeṣaḥ ।
aparikṣayaguṇakalpanayā bhavati supuṇyaviśeṣaḥ ।।

atha vyatīte kasmiṃścit kāle bhagavato antike ।
nandopanandayordharmadeśanāṃ śrotumāyayau ।।

rājā prasenajiddraṣṭuṃ bhagavantamupāgataḥ ।
tābhyāmakṛtasatkārapraṇāmaḥ komapāyayau ।।

sa praṇamya jinaṃ gatvā pradadhyau nigrahaṃ tayoḥ ।
śastravṛṣṭiṃ saṃsṛjantau tau ca vyomnā samāgatau ।।

sarvajñapreṣitastūraṇaṃ maudgalyāyana etya tām ।
śastravṛṣṭiṃ narapateścakre padmotpalāvalim ।।

punargatvā bhagavataḥ samīpaṃ pṛthivīpatiḥ ।
saṃprāptau kṣamayāmāsa tasyādeśāt phaṇīśvarau ।।

athārthitaḥ pārthivena bhagavān rājamandiram ।
bhaktipūtaṃ yayau bhoktuṃ bhaktaṃ bhikṣugaṇaiḥ saha ।।

bhakṣyeṣu pacyamāneṣu rātrau tatrāgnivilpavaḥ ।
jāto jinaprabhāveṇa sahasā śāntimāyayau ।।

bhuktvā gate bhagavati kṣitipaḥ svapure abhyadhāt ।
jvalanajvālanaṃ rātrau vārayan daṇḍasaṃvidā ।।

atrāṇtare gṛhapatiḥ sudattasyātmaji yuvā ।
mithyādoṣadṛddhibalo nāma rājñābhighātitaḥ ।।

pūrvaṃ bhagavataḥ śāstuḥ śāsanānugraheṇa saḥ ।
labdhajñānadhṛtiḥ putraduḥkhe apyāsīdaduḥkhitaḥ ।।

aputraḥ svadhanaṃ bhūri dīnebhyaḥ pratipādya saḥ ।
cakārātirasādekapaṇaśeṣaṃ śanaiḥ śriyaḥ ।।

paṇalābhakṛtāśeṣadharmaḥ svalpaprado atha saḥ ।
abhūd gṛhī sudattākhyo gṛhaṃ hi svaplamucyate ।।

kadāciddarśanāyātaṃ bhagavān purataḥ sthitam ।
taṃ svalpadānanāmnaiva lajjitaṃ dayayāvadat ।।

alpadānaṃ gṛhapaterna lajjāṃ kartumarhasi ।
yāti śraddhārpito dānakaṇaḥ kanakaśailatām ।।

purā bahutaraṃ dattaṃ velamena dvijanmanā ।
śraddhāvirahasāmānyānna tathā vṛddhimāyayau ।।

yaḥ sarvaṃ bhojayedbhaktyā jambudvīpagataṃ janam ।
yaścaikaṃ bodhisaṃyuktaṃ tasya puṇyaṃ tato adhikam ।।

iti vākyaṃ bhagavatastathyaṃ śrutvābhinandya ca ।
nijagehaṃ gṛhapatiḥ prayayau praṇipatya tam ।।

dīpaṃ datvā paṭhan rātrau tatar buddhānuśāsanam ।
daṇḍāya rājapuruṣaiḥ sa nīto agnipravartanāt ।।

daṇḍasya saṃbhavādbaddhaṃ bandhanāgāravartinam ।
taṃ draṣṭumāyayurdevā rātrau śakrabrahmādayaḥ ।।

sa tairdhanaṃ gṝhāṇeti prārthito nāgrahīdyadā ।
tadā dharmopadeśo ayaṃ pravṛttastsya mandire ।।

rājāpi tatprabhāveṇa dṛṣṭvā prajvālitaṃ puram ।
muktvā taṃ bandhanāgārānna dadarśa jalaṃ kkacit ।।

sa gataḥ sugataṃ draṣṭuṃ kadācittatpuraḥ sthitaḥ ।
nṛpaṃ jinapraṇāmāya prāptaṃ paścād vyalokayat ।।

agre bhagavataścakre praṇayaṃ na sa bhūpateḥ ।
jagatpūjyasya purataḥ pūjāmarhati nāparaḥ ।।

jinamāmantrya nṛpatiḥ praṇataḥ svapuraṃ gataḥ ।
vivāsanaṃ gṛhapaterādideśa nijāt purāt ।।

prasādinī sudattasya devatā nṛpatiṃ tataḥ ।
kṣudrajantubhirutsṛṣṭaiścakre daṃśaviṣākulam ।।

sa trastastairnṛpaḥ prāptaḥ sāmātyāntaḥ purānugaḥ ।
gatvā prasādayāmāsa sudattam jinaśāsanāt ।।

iti sa satatapratyāsattyā parāmṛtanirbharaṃ
bhagavaduditaṃ śāntiṃ bheje sudattagṛhādhipaḥ ।
svamiva labhate vighnayāsapravāsavivarjitaṃ
vimalamanasāmantevāsī vivekamahānidhim ।।

iti kṣemendravicaritāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ gṛhapatisudattāvadānaṃ caturstriśaḥ pallavaḥ ।।

ghoṣīlāvadānam ।

phalaṃ samānaṃ labhate sa dāturyāti kṣaṇaṃ dānasahāyatāṃ yaḥ ।
paropakārapraṇayodyatānāṃ nāpuṇyakarmā sacivatvameti ।।

ramye purā bhagavati śrāvastyāṃ jetakānane ।
anāthapiṇḍadārāmavihārādhirate jine ।।

kauśāmbyāṃ vatsanṛpatirbabhūvodayanābhidhaḥ ।
gāyatyadyāṣi yatkīrtirvidyādharavadhūjanaḥ ।।

abhavadviṣaye tasya karmāntākarajīvanaḥ ।
gṛhasthaḥ sudhano nāma dhanādhānavicakṣaṇaḥ ।।

nṛpaḥ kadāciṃdāsthāne taṃ kāryārthinamāgatam ।
vacasaiva parijñāya jagād vihitādaraḥ ।।

jānāmyahaṃ gṛhapate hiraṇyopacitasvaram ।
vipulaḥ saṃcayajñasya suvarṇanidhirasti te ।।

ityuktaḥ sasmitaṃ rājñā sa tamūce kṛtāñjaliḥ ।
satyamastyeva me rājan gṛhe kāñcanasaṃcayaḥ ।।

sadvṛttacintānirate deve vātsalyapeśale ।
kiṃ vā nāsti janāsyāsya pitari tvayi goptari ।।

dhanino yāntyadhanatāṃ nidhanaṃ yānti cādhanāḥ ।
vyāghratām yāti dedbhūbhṛdāmiṣāghrāṇanirghṛṇaḥ ।।

niḥsaṅkairarjyate vittamarjitaṃ ca vibhajyate ।
vibhaktaṃ bhujyate spaṣṭaṃ janairdharmadhane nṛpe ।।

upapannaṃ vacaḥ śrutvā dhīmatastasya bhūpatiḥ ।
tamūce daśanodyotaiḥ prasādaṃ darśayanniva ।।

matimān kāryasacivastvaṃ me bhavitumarhasi ।
dhīdhūryaistvadvidhaireva dhāryate dharaṇībharaḥ ।।

iti rājavacaḥ śrutvā śudhanastamabhāṣata ।
n avayaṃ rājasevāsu sabhāmaṇḍalapaṇḍitāḥ ।।

svācchandyodyānavicchedaḥ sunidrāsukhavikrayaḥ ।
sevā hi puṃsāṃ saṃsāraduḥkhadainyabhayaṃkaraḥ ।।

īśvarairmastakanyastacaraṇaḥ kṛtakṛtyatām ।
pādapīṭha ivāyāti sevako ahaṃ sthitaḥ sadā ।।

sevāyāsaprayāsena prāptānāmapi saṃpadām ।
saṃbhogaḥ piśunāsaṅgī prabhubhrūbhangabhaṅguraḥ ।।

etāśca nāvatiṣṭhante prayatnena dhṛtā api ।
darpogradurgrahagrāhadurgrahā nṛpasaṃpadaḥ ।।

kṣaṇaṃ navanavāśliṣaviśeṣapraṇayodyatāḥ ।
avācavāraramaṇīramaṇīyā vibhūtayaḥ ।।

ityuktapratiṣedho api sa rājñā sacivaḥ kṛtaḥ ।
atikrāmati ko nāma prabhaviṣṇoḥ samīhitam ।।

prāptaprauḍhapadaṃ rājñā nītaṃ sarvādhikāritām ।
vidveṣadūṣitāḥ sarve mantriṇastaṃ na sehire ।।

dharmajijñāsayā rājñā piśunapreritena saḥ ।
naivākarodasatkāryaṃ niyukto api puna punaḥ ।।

āghātaṃ prekṣitaḥ so atha mithyākopena bhūbhujā ।
tathāpyadharmasaṃyuktaṃ na śāsanamatanyata ।।

ekajanmasukhāyaiva bahujanmaśatārditam ।
na sādhuninditaṃ karma karomīti jagāda saḥ ।।

bhayadharmopadhāśuddhaḥ pratimuktaḥ sa bhūbhujā ।
dānasatramavicchinnamakarodakhilārthinām ।।

sarvatra viśrute tasya dānasatre yaśasvinah ।
kalpavṛkṣādaraḥ puṃsāṃ paraṃ pratanutāṃ yayau ।।

atrāntare munigaṇāstīrthārthā dakṣiṇāpathāt ।
āgatā kṛcchrakāntāramaviśan nirjanaṃ vanam ।।

tatra tṛṣṇāturāḥ sarve mūrcchitāḥ śayanāśritāḥ ।
ayācanta jalaṃ mohāduccairniścetanānapi ।।

devagandharvanāgebhyaḥ kaścidyo atra dayāmbudhiḥ ।
sthitaḥ prayacchatu jalaṃ so asmākamiti te abruvan ।।

tataḥ sa ratnakeyūrakkanatkaṅkaṇasaddhvaniḥ ।
bhujasthamemabhṛṅgārastarumadhyādviniryayau ।।

te tasmādamṛtāsvādaṃ pāṇipadmāvanāmitāt ।
ākaṇṭhaṃ salilaṃ pītvā jahṛṣurlabdhajīvitāḥ ।।

prārthitaḥ punarabhyetya papracchuste savismayāḥ ।
adṛśyavṛkṣanilayādudbhūtaṃ ko bhavāniti ।।

so abravīdviśrutayaśāḥ śrāvastyāmāśayaḥ śriyaḥ ।
anāthapiṇḍado nāma sarvado asti gṛhādhipaḥ ।।

saucikena mayā pūrvaṃ tadgṛhāntikavāsinā ।
bhujamudyabhya tadveśma darśitaṃ nityamarthinām ।।

tena puṇyena devatvaṃ prāpto atra viharāmyaham ।
bāhurmam vibhātyeṣa dakṣiṇaḥ so arthidakṣiṇaḥ ।।

te tamāmantrya munayaḥ punaḥ saṃprasthitā vane ।
kṣudhitāḥ snigdhasacchāyaṃ dadṛśuḥ pādapaṃ param ।।

tamapyuccairayācanta bhojanaṃ tadvadeva te ।
uccacāra ca gambhīrā vāṇī vismayakāriṇī ।।

atra puṣkariṇītīre droṇyāṃ divyānnabhojanam ।
saṃpūrṇamasti tadgatvā bhujyatāṃ yadabhīpsitam ।।

iti tena samādiṣṭaṃ bhuktvā te divyabhojanam ।
ko bhavaniti papracchustaṃ divyatarusaṃśrayam ।।

so apyācacakṣe śrāvastyāṃ gṛhastho anāthapiṇḍadaḥ ।
asti tasyāhamabhavaṃ brāhmaṇaḥ saṃghahojane ।।

caturaḥ paricaryāyāṃ dadhikumbhapracārakaḥ ।
tadbhojanānte saṃprāpte svalpaśeṣānnabhojanaḥ ।।

bhikṣuṇāṃ gauraveccāraṃ dṛṣṭvāhaṃ rājabhojanam ।
ātmanaścānnamakṣāramabhavaṃ khinnamānasaḥ ।।

anāthapiṇḍadagirā bhojane gauravāśayā ।
tato mayāṣṭāṅgayuktaṃ gṛhītaṃ poṣadhaṃ vratam ।।

asamāptavratenātha bhuktaṃ laulyānmayā niśi ।
tenāhamabhavaṃ loke vijñātaḥ khaṇḍapoṣadhaḥ ।।

khaṇḍenāpi vratenāhaṃ devaputratvamāgataḥ ।
iti te tadvacaḥ śrutvā munayo vismitā yayuḥ ।।

acintayan vrajantaste tīvreṇa tapasā vayam ।
suciraṃ kevalaṃ kliṣṭāṃ nādyāpi kuśalaspṛśaḥ ।।

adhunā poṣadhaṃ prāptuṃ vratameva yatāmahe ।
nirapāyasukhopāye svahite kasya nādaraḥ ।।

iti saṃcintayantaste kauśāmbīmabhito gatāḥ ।
sudhanasya gṛhaṃ prāpurviśrutaṃ gṛhamedhinaḥ ।।

tatra tena kṛtātithyā nivedyāsmai tadadbhutam ।
anāthapiṇḍadaṃ draṣṭuṃ tenaiva sahitā yayuḥ ।।

śrāvastyām te samāsādya pūjitāstena sādaram ।
asmai nyavedayan sarvaṃ yathādṛṣṭaṃ yathāśrutam ।।

sa tān vratārthina sarvān suhṛdaṃ sudhanaṃ ca tam ।
nināya dharmasacivaḥ prīto bhagavato antikam ।।

bhagavānapi tadvākyāccakre teṣāmanugraham ।
satyadarśanasaṃbuddhā yena te sugatiṃ yayuḥ ।।

teṣu yāteṣu sudhanaṃ pakṣapātādrayā dṛśā ।
vilokya bhagavān samyag vidadhe jñānabhājanam ।।

satyasaṃdarśanāvāptaviśeṣakuśalodayaḥ ।
gatvā jināya kauśāmbyām sa vihāramakārayat ।।

yasmādbhagavatādiṣṭastasmin yātaḥ sahāyatām ।
bhikṣuścundābhidhastasmāt so abhūccundavihārabhūḥ ।।

rādhābhidhā tadā dāsī vihāraparicārikā ।
dayayā bhagavānasyāḥ śīrṇavastraṃ samagrahīt ।।

adāsī syāmiti śraddhāpraṇidhānārpitastayā ।
sa cīvaro bhagavataḥ prayayāvekavarṇatām ।।

sudhanasyojjvalaṃ dṛṣṭvāṃpuṇyasaṃbhāramadbhutam ।
bhikṣubhirbhagavān pṛṣṭastatpūrvodayamabhyadhāt ।।

sundhānākhyo gṛhapatirvārāṇasyāmabhūtpurā ।
nodārakuznjarasyābhūd yasya dānaparikṣayaḥ ।।

anāvṛṣṭihate kāle tasya dvādaśavārṣike ।
avāritamabhūcchatramavicchinnānnamarthinām ।।

tasya padmākaro nāma koṣāgārapatirgṛhe ।
dānasāhāyyakaṃ cakre sahasthā hi samṛddhayaḥ ।।

pratyekabuddhasaṃghasya bhaktakālanivedakah ।
dharmadūtābhidhastasya mantrī dhīmānapasthitaḥ ।।

karmavyākṣepatastasya jāte kālavyatikrame ।
kadācit kukurasteṣāṃ kālasaṃjñāṃ vyadhātpuraḥ ।।

sundhāno adya sa evāhaṃ koṣṭhiko anāthapiṇḍadaḥ ।
saṃghasya dharmadūto yaḥ sa evodayano nṛpaḥ ।।

saṃjñānideśako yaśca kukuraḥ sudhano api saḥ ।
rājñā ghoṣeṇa vijñāto ghoṣilāparanāmabhṛt ।।

caritamityucitaṃ bhavabhedinā bhagavatā kathitaṃ kila bhikṣavaḥ ।
sukṛtasaurabhasārasudhārasaṃ sumanasā śravaṇāñjalibhiḥ papuḥ ।।

iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ ghoṣilāvadānaṃ pañcatriṃśaḥ pallavaḥ ।।

pūrṇāvadānam ।

vibudhasarasiḥ padmaiḥ śobhite paṅkajinyā śuciparisarajātaṃ spṛśyate na sthale abjam ।
sahajaparicitānāṃ nityamantargatānām bhavati sitaguṇānām kāraṇaṃ naiva jātiḥ ।।

śrāvastyāṃ sarvasattvānāṃ svastidhyānaparāyaṇe ।
jinakalpadrume jetavanārāmasthite purā ।।

śūrpārakākhye nagare ratnasaṃcayasāgaraḥ ।
bhavo nāmābhavatsārthaparirmatimatāṃ varaḥ ।।

bhavilo bhavabhadraśca bhavanandī ca viśrutāḥ ।
ketakyāṃ tasya jāyāyāṃ babhūvustanayāstrayaḥ ।।

rogayogādupagaraḥ sa kadācinmumūrṣutām ।
pāruṣyād bhṛśamudvignaiḥ patnīputrairupekṣitaḥ ।।

bhaktyā dāsī tu tasyaikā paricaryāparā param ।
mallikākhyābhavattasyāḥ sevayā svāsthyamāyayau ।।

snehopakārapraṇataḥ kṛtajñaḥ sa tayānvitaḥ ।
ṛtau saṃgamamabhyetya tasyāḥ putramajījanat ।।

yadā tajjanmani pituḥ sarvārthāḥ pūrṇatām yayuḥ ।
sa tadā pūrṇanāmābhūdbālaḥ pūrṇendusundaraḥ ।।

jyeṣṭhāstrayaḥ kṛtidvāhā yayurabdhiṃ dhanārthinaḥ ।
pūrṇastu bhāṇḍaśālāyāṃ pituścakre dhanārjanam ।।

tataḥ pratinivṛttāste prāptārthaḥ sāgarātpunaḥ ।
gaṇanāṃ hemalakṣāṇāṃ kṛtvā svamudire puram ।।

samudragamane teṣām yāvānāsīddhanāgamaḥ ।
pūrṇasya svagṛhe paṇyaurbabhūvābhyadhikastataḥ ।।

taddṛṣṭvā janakasteṣāṃ vṛddhaḥ paryantavāsare ।
tamūcehitamāyatyāṃ tṛṣṇā naikakṣayodayaḥ ।।

dṛṣṭaṃ bhavadbhiḥ sāmudralābhe kṛtapariśramaiḥ ।
pūrṇenoārjitaṃ vittamakleśena mahīyasā ।।

śubhakarmavipākena bhavantyarthā dhanārthinām ।
hastāt palāyate anyasya prāpnoti patitaṃ paraḥ ।।

sanmārgasyāparityāgād yuktāyuktavivecanāt ।
deśakālaparijñānātsatāṃ sarvatra saṃpadaḥ ।।

bhavanti svagṛhe śanyāḥ sudhiyo dharmabhāginaḥ ।
gatvā ratnākaraṃ cānye labhante prāṇasaṃśayam ।।

yatnena boddhavyā sadbhiḥ dhanasyopaniṣtparā ।
adrohaśuddhabuddhīnāṃ svādhīnānāṃ dhanācchriyaḥ ।।

rakṣaṇīyo bhavadbhiśca bhedaḥ satatasaṃhateḥ ।
bhinnāt skhalati kalyāṇaṃ kulāt kumbhādivodakam ।।

athābhinnendhanasyāgnernaśyante sadṛśāstviṣaḥ ।
tathā vipulavaṃśasya bhinnajñātervibhūtayāḥ ।।

bhrātṝṇāṃ saṃtato bhedaḥ kathaṃ nāma nivartate ।
adhyāpitānāṃ patnībhirdveṣavidyāṃ sadā niśi ।।

unnatānāṃ svavaśānāṃ dvaidhaṃ tāvanna jāyate ।
yāvatkuṭhāradhāreva yoṣidviśati nāntaram ।।

bhrāturarthānuvādena guruṃ pāruṣyakutsayā ।
mitramekābhilāṣeṇa nayanti dvaidhatāṃ striyaḥ ।।

tadvadanti hasantyo api bhrūvilāsena yoṣitaḥ ।
yatprayāti suhṛtsnehamūlonmūlanahetutām ।।

hitamuktveti putrāṇāṃ bhūtaye abhimataṃ bhavaḥ ।
anityatāpariyuktaḥ kāle nidhanamāyayau ।।

avibhakte dhane śaktā deśāntaradhanārjane ।
jyeṣṭhā babhūvuḥ pūrṇastu gṛhe vittamacintayat ।।

kālena gṛhamāptānām vastrāśanavivādinām ।
strīmantradattakarṇānāṃ bhedasteṣāmajāyata ।।

vitte vibhajyamāne ath atairvidveṣavaśīkṛteḥ ।
dāsīsuto ayamtyuktvā nītaḥ pūrṇo niraṃśatām ।।

so api pūrṇaśanaḥ kāle śītasaṃkucitaṃ pathi ।
dadarśa grīṣmatāpr api vivaśaṃ dārubhārakam ।।

ādāya dārumūlyena sa tasmāddārubhārakam ।
divyacandanamadrākṣīddahanasyāpi śītadam ।।

sukṛtenaiva mahatā tena labdhamahādhanaḥ ।
sa sevyaḥ sārthavāhānāṃ pūjyo abhūtpṛthivīpateḥ ।।

ratnākaraṃ sa ṣaṭkṛtvaḥ prayātaḥ sarvado arthinām ।
cakāra sarvavaṇījāṃ taraśulkādyanugraham ।।

srhāvastīvāsibhiḥ sārthavaṇigbhiḥ punararthitaḥ ।
yayau pravahaṇārūḍhaḥ samudradvīpamāśu saḥ ।।

pratyāvṛtte pravahaṇe so atha śuśrāva gāyatām ।
vaṇijāṃ sthāvirāḥ śailagāthāḥ sugatasaṃśrayāḥ ।।

kasyaitā iti te tena pṛṣṭāḥ sarve babhāṣire ।
etā bhagavatā gītā gāthā buddhena dhīmatā ।।

iti buddhābhidhāmeva śrutvā harṣamavāpa saḥ ।
puṃsāṃ svavāsanārūḍhaṃ vyaktimāyātyudīritam ।।

tairvistareṇa kathitāmākarṇya bhagavatkathām ।
so abhavattadgatamanāstaddarśanasamutsukaḥ ।।

sa śanairgṛhamāgatya tyaktvā sarvaparicchadam ।
anāthapiṇḍadaṃ draṣṭuṃ śrāvastyāṃ suhṛdaṃ yayau ।।

abhilāṣaṃ nivedyāsmai pravrajyāyāṃ jitendriyaḥ ।
jagāma sahitastena bhaktyā bhagavato antikam ।।

dṛṣṭvaiva tatra sarvajñaṃ mohadhvāntadivākaram ।
tatpādadarśanenaiva mene sa kṛtakṛtyatām ।।

vijñāya tasya bhagavān saṃkalpaṃ tamabhāṣata ।
daśanajyotsnayā kurvan vivekavimalā diśaḥ ।।

ehi bhikṣi nirāśaṅke nirvipakṣe kṣayojjhite ।
ākhyāte dharmavinaye brahmacaryāṃ carepsitam ।।

iti prasādaśīlena jinenodīrite purah ।
pravrajyā sahasaivāsya papātālakṣitā tanau ।।

tataḥ sa śatrau mitre ca praśamāt samatāṃ śritaḥ ।
śāstuḥ śāsanamādāya praṇipatya jagāma tam ।।

śroṇāparāntakaṃ nāma deśaṃ śrūrajanāśrayam ।
svayaṃ parīkṣituṃ kṣāntiṃ janena sa samāyayau ।।

tato dṛṣṭvā tamāyāntaṃ mṛgayāyāmamaṅgalam ।
lubdhakaścāpamākṛṣya hantuṃ kridhāt samādravat ।।

nirvikāraṃ nirudvegaṃ sa taṃ vigatasādhvasam ।
prahareti bruvāṇaṃ ca dṛṣṭvaiva śamamāptavān ।।

śāmyatastasya sahasā prasādī lubdhakasya saḥ ।
dharmaṃ dideśa yenāsau bodhiṃ prāpa sahānugaiḥ ।।

sa tatra sugatārhāṇāṃ sarvopaskarasaṃpadām ।
śatāni paznca ramyāṇāṃ vihārāṇāmakārayat ।।

pūrṇo api jñānasaṃpūrṇaḥ prāptistridaśapūjyatām ।
vairāgyalakṣmyā yukto abhūnmunīnāṃ spṛhaṇīyayā ।।

atha tasyāgrajo bhrātā bhavilaḥ kṣīṇavittatām ।
kālenopagataḥ prāyāt samduraṃ draviṇāśayā ।।

tataḥ pravahaṇārūḍhaḥ so anukūlaiḥ samīraṇaiḥ ।
gośīrṣacandanavanaṃ prāpitaḥ svalpavāsaraiḥ ।।

kuṭhārikaśataistasmin pañcabhiśchettumudyate ।
taccandanavanaṃ divyaṃ bhujaṅgagaṇāsaṃkulam ।।

tatsvāmī yakṣasenānāṃ maheśvaraṃ iti śrutaḥ ।
kopādudasṛjad ghoraṃ kālikākhyaṃ mahānilam ।।

marutā mahatā tena prāpitāḥ prāṇasaṃśayam ।
cakrandurvaṇijaḥ sarve śarvaśakramukhān surān ।।

tānārtarāvamukharān bhavilaḥ sārthanāyakaḥ ।
uvāca saṃcintya ciraṃ paścāttāpasamākulaḥ ।।

pūrṇaḥ kanīyān bhrātā sa hitaiṣī māṃ purāvadat ।
bahukleśo hyalpasukhaḥ kka gantavyastvayāmbudhiḥ ।।

akṛtvā dhīmatastasya vacanaṃ satyadarśinaḥ ।
cyuto ahaṃ dhanalobhena ghore asmin vyasanārṇave ।।

śrutvaitadvaṇijaḥ sarve prabhāvaṃ lokaviśrutam ।
pūrṇasya manasā dhyātvā tameva śaraṇaṃ yayuḥ ।।

namastubhyaṃ jagatkleśaviṣadhoṣāpahāriṇe ।
pūrṇayodīrṇakaruṇāsudhāsaṃpūrṇacetase ।।

ityekasvararāveṇa teṣāṃ saṃpūrite ambare ।
kṣaṇena gatvā tadvṛttaṃ pūrṇaḥ prāha svadevatāḥ ।।

śroṇāparāntakagataḥ śrutvā teṣāṃ sa viplavam ।
vyomnā samādhisaṃnaddhaḥ prāpa pravahaṇaṃ kṣaṇāt ।।

tasmin paryaṅkabandhanena sthito merurivācalah ।
pralayottālavegasya gatiṃ vāhorjahāra sah ।।

pūrṇena pavanaṃ ruddhaṃ jñātvā yakṣagaṇāgraṇīḥ ।
taṃ prasādya yayau tyaktvā tebhyaścandanakānanam ।।

pūrṇaprasādādādāya bhavilaścandanadrumān ।
hṛṣṭastenaiva sahitaḥ śūrpāraṃ svapuraṃ yayau ।।

pūrṇo ath saṃmate bhrātustatra gośīrṣacandanaiḥ ।
cakre candanamālākhyaṃ prāsādaṃ sugato acitam ।।

tatra pūrṇena bhagavān dhyātastūrṇaṃ vihāysā ।
samāyayau jetavanādullaṅghya śatayojanīm ।।

āgacchato bhagavataḥ puraḥprasṛtayā jagat ।
dehakāntyā kapiśitaṃ sarvaṃ himamivābhavat ।।

puropāntanivāsinyastaṃ vilokya gṛhāṅganāḥ ।
tīvracittaprasādena praśamonmukhatāṃ yayuḥ ।।

kuśalopacitāṃ tāsāṃ bhagavān satyadeśanām ।
cakre bhavādṛtāṃ kāntāstāh prāpuḥ kuśalaṃ yayuḥ ।।

ṛddhyā bhagavatastatra caityaṃ paurāṅganābhidham ।
tābhirvihitamadyāpi vandante caityavandakāḥ ।।

munīnāṃ bhagavān kṛtvā tathā valkalino muneḥ ।
pravrajyānugrahaṃ śuddhāṃ vidadhe dharmadeśanām ।।

tataścandanamālākhyaṃ prāsādaṃ bhagavān jinaḥ ।
praviśya sphāṭikaṃ cakre janasaṃghabharakṣamam ।।

atha ratnāsanāsīnaḥ sa tatra karuṇānidhiḥ ।
vidadhe sarvasattvānāṃ śāntyai nirvāṇadeśanām ।।

atrāntare sānucarau munīndrau kṛṣṇāgautamau ।
abhyetya dharmaśravaṇeśāstuḥ śāsanamāpatuḥ ।।

tatra kṛtvātha bhagavān prāsādasya pratigraham ।
punarjetavanaṃ gacchannudyayau saha bhikṣubhiḥ ।।

vrahan mārīcilokasthām maudgalyāyanamātaram ।
sagdirā cāryasatye tāṃ dharmamārge nyaveśayat ।।

atha jetavanaṃ prāptaṃ bhagavantaṃ savismayāḥ ।
pūrṇasya puṇyaṃ papracchurbhikṣavaḥ so apyabhāṣata ।।

kāśyapasya purā samyaksaṃbuddhasyānyajanmani ।
vihārādhikṛtaḥ pūrṇaḥ saṃghopasthāyako abhavat ।।

sa kadācidasaṃmṛṣṭāṃ dṛṣṭvā vaihārikīṃ bhuvam ।
prāha pravrajitaṃ tīvraṃ krodhādupadhivārikam ।।

dṛptasyopadhivāro adya vihāro asminnamārjitaḥ ।
kasya dāsīsutasyeti bruvāṇastamabhartsayat ।।

tena pāruṣyapāpena bhuktvā narakadurgatim ।
dāsīsuto abhavat pūrṇaḥ pañca janmaśatāni saḥ ।।

saṃghopāsanamevāsya puṇyāyābhūnmahīyasā ।
arhattvaṃ yena niḥśeṣabhavakleśojjhitaḥ śritaḥ ।।

iti prabhāvaṃ kathitaṃ jinena pūrṇasya puṇyopacayapraṇitam ।
śrutvādbhutaṃ saṃsadi bhikṣusaṃghaḥ puṇyaprasaṃśābhirato babhūva ।।

iti kṣemendraviracitāyām bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyām pūrṇāvadānaṃ ṣaṭtriṃśaḥ pallavaḥ ।।

mūkapaṅgvavadānam ।

ākiṃcanyasukhāya niḥspṛhatayā vairāgyalakṣmījuṣaḥ
sarvaṃ yānti vihāya kāyasacivāḥ santaḥ praśāntyai vanam ।
tatrāpi vrataḍambare parikarārambhāya cet saṃcayas
tatkaḥ kośaparicchadopakaraṇairgehe aparādhaḥ kṛtaḥ ।।

jine jetavanārāmavihārābhirate purā ।
śākyarājakumārāṇāṃ pravrajyāsaṃjuṣāṃ puraḥ ।।

citracīvarasatpātrayogapaṭṭādisaṃcayam ।
prabhūtataramālokya bhagavān samacintayat ।।

aho bataiṣāṃ nādyāpi bandhaheturnivartate ।
abhimānamayaḥ kāye priyaḥ parikaragrahaḥ ।।

kāye kāyapariṣkārastasyopakaraṇāvalī ।
tasyāḥ parikarādānamaho nu bandhaśṛnkhalā ।।

iti saṃcintya bhagavān naikāntavihitasthitiḥ ।
kāruṇyādupasannānāṃ kuśalāya samudyataḥ ।।

māsatrayamupasthānaṃ kartavyaṃ yena kenacit ।
adarśanāya bhikṣūṇāmakaroditi saṃvidam ।।

pravṛtte niyame tasmin bhikṣurāraṇyakavrataḥ ।
āyayāvupasenākhyaḥ kāryārthaṃ tanucīvaraḥ ।।

pravāritaḥ sa saṃprāpya dhanyaḥ sugatadarśanam ।
kṛtakṛtyaḥ kṣasṇaṃ sthitvā pratasthe praṇipatya tam ।।

vrajantametya papracchurbhikṣavaḥ parivārya tam ।
tavārya darśanamaho dattaṃ bhagavatā katham ।।

māsatrayaṃ darśane asya niyamaḥ śāsanena yaḥ ।
sa kathaṃ bhavatā bhagnaḥ saṃghasyonmārgagāminā ।।

śrutvā tadvacanaṃ teṣāmupasenaḥ smitottaram ।
tānuce n amayā kaścit kṛtaḥ samayaviplavaḥ ।।

ahamukto bhagavatā darśanāvasare svayam ।
āraṇyakasya me bhikṣorniṣedho nāsti darśane ।।

paricchadopakaraṇatyāganirmuktabandhanāḥ ।
avāryadarśanā vṛkṣamūlikāḥ pāṃśukūlikāḥ ।।

idamadya paraṃ prātariti ye saṃcaye ratāḥ ।
pātravīcaravargeṣu teṣāṃ nāstīha darśanam ।।

pāthobhiḥ prasarattuṣāraśiśiraistṛṣṇāturāste paraṃ
te nityaṃ ca nidhānadhāmni vivṛte apyanyādalaṃ durgatāḥ ।
teṣāṃ candanapādapādupanataḥ saṃtāpakaḥ pāvako
yaireṣa praśamavratopakaraṇe baddho abhimānagrahaḥ ।।

ityuktamupasenena śrutvā te śākyabhikṣavaḥ ।
vailakṣyakṣayitotsāhāḥ sahasaiva vyacintayan ।।

etadbhagavatādiṣṭamasmānuddhiśya nāparān ।
vicitracīvaracayaprāvārā vayameva yat ।।

viratecchāḥ priyāh śāsturmahecchā vayamapriyāḥ ।
tasmādicchāṃ parityajya bhavāmastasya saṃmatāḥ ।।

iti saṃcintya te sarve cārucīvarasaṃcayam ।
prāvṛtyābhyadhikaṃ tyaktvā yayurbhagavato antikam ।।

icchāvirāme bhagavān vyadhātteṣāmanugraham ।
jñānavajreṇa satkāyadṛṣṭiśailaṃ bibheda yaḥ ।।

śākyarājakumārāṇāṃ śrotaḥprāptiphalaspṛśām ।
bhikṣubhiḥ pūrvavṛttāntaṃ pṛṣṭaḥ prāha tathāgataḥ ।।

vārāṇasyāmabhūtpūrvaṃ brahmadatto mahīpatiḥ ।
dānārdrahasto yadbāhuḥ kṣmāmadhāddigdvipopamaḥ ।।

tasya brahmāvatī muktālateva guṇaśālinī ।
kīrtiḥ satpuruṣasyeva viśrutā vanitābhavat ।।

pratibimbopamaṃ patyuḥ sā sutaṃ vimalāśayā ।
jalakrīḍāgatā kāle suṣuve divyalakṣaṇam ।।

udakākhyaḥ sa bālo abhūt saṃjātaḥ salilāntare ।
vardhamānaḥ pitustulyaṃ yauvarājyānorathaiḥ ।।

śatāni pañcāmātyānāṃ tasya janmadinaṃ samam ।
avāpustulyarūpāṇāṃ putrāṇām śatapañcakam ।।

nijaṃ jātismaraḥ smṛtvā prāgvṛttaṃ sa śiśuḥ śanaiḥ ।
acintayat prāptakālaṃ hitaṃ sukṛtamātmanaḥ ।।

ṣaṣṭivarṣāṇi kṛtvā tu yauvarājyamahaṃ purā ।
abhavaṃ kṛcchrasaṃtaptaściraṃ narakasaṃkaṭe ।।

janmanyasminnapi punaryauvarājyamupasthitam ।
sarvathā prārthyamāno api na kariṣyāmi pātakam ।।

iti saṃcintya sa ciraṃ rājabhogaparāṅmukhaḥ ।
piturudvegajananīmagrahīt paṅgumūkatām ।।

sarvalakṣaṇayukto api rājavṛtterabhājanam ।
sa mūkapaṅgurnāmābhūd bandhūnāṃ duḥkhavardhanaḥ ।।

prāpteṣu mantriputreṣu śastraśāstrabalodayam ।
rājaputraḥ pravṛddho api nodatiṣṭhanna cāvadat ।।

pṛṣṭastataḥ kṣitīśena vaidyāstaddoṣabheṣajam ।
avadan vaikalyaṃ rājan rājasūnorna dṛśyate ।।

abhyāsādyadi jāto asya doṣo api sukhasevinaḥ ।
tadeṣa bhayasaṃvegāduttiṣṭhati ca vakti ca ।।

iti vaidyairabhihitaṃ tathetyuktvā kṣitīśvaraḥ ।
mithyaiva vadhyavasudhāṃ bhayāya vyasṛjatsutam ।।

sa bhartsyamānah puruṣaistamuvāca rathasthitam ।
api kaścidvasatyasyāṃ vārāṇasyāṃ na vā janaḥ ।।

iti tadvacanaṃ śrutvā tairnītaḥ sa nṛpāntikam ।
tatra pitrārthyamāno api mūka evābhavat punaḥ ।।

punarvadhyabhuvaṃ nītaḥ śavaṃ dṛṣṭvā jagād saḥ ।
astyeṣa jīvati śavaḥ kiṃ vā sarvātmanā mṛtaḥ ।।

śrutvaitat taiḥ pituḥ pārśve nyasto maunaṃ vyadhātpunaḥ ।
punarvadhabhayāccaiva nītaḥ provāca tān pathi ।।

rāśirya eṣa dhānyasya sa hi bhukto anubhujyate ।
ityuktavākyo api punarnoce kiṃcit pitu paraḥ ।।

tataḥ khyātapratikṣepe tasyādiṣṭe mahībhujā ।
so avadadvaradānena vacmi pradbhyāṃ vrajāmi ca ।।

athāsya rājñā hṛṣṭena varadāne pratiśrute ।
sa padbhyāṃ svayamabhyetya spaṣṭaṃ pitaramabravīt ।।

nāhaṃ paṅgurna mūko ahaṃ naiva cāhaṃ jaḍāśayaḥ ।
kiṃtu janmāntarakleśaṃ smṛtvā vaihvalyamāśritaḥ ।।

yauvarājyasukhaṃ bhuktvā ṣaṣṭivarṣāṇyahaṃ purā ।
ṣaṣṭivarṣasahasrāṇi nyavasaṃ narakodare ।।

rājabhītyā mayā tasmāt kṛteyaṃ mūkapaṅgutā ।
pravrajyayā brahmacaryaṃ carāmyeṣa varo mama ।।

iti tenoktamākarṇya tamuvāca mahīpatiḥ ।
amūka ityāptadhṛtirvirakta iti duḥkhitaḥ ।।

dharmamūlamidaṃ rājyaṃ putra na tyaktumarhasi ।
yajñadānaprajātrāṇaiḥ puṇyapūrṇā nṝpaśriyaḥ ।।

ekaputrastvayā putra parityāgarasādaham ।
nidrādaridratām nītaḥ śokaśayyāsamāśrayaḥ ।।

saṃpūrṇacandrarucirāṃ vyaktamauktikahāsinīm ।
kathaṃ saṃpadamutsṛjya pravrajyābhimatā tava ।।

kathaṃ śayyāḥ parityajya prājyarājyasukhocitāḥ ।
vanāntavāsavyasanī sevase pāṃśulāḥ sthalīḥ ।।

kāntālīlāmukuramaṇimanmandirīṃ rājadhānīm
etāṃ tyaktvānanu vanabhuvaḥ saṃpatadvyāghraghorāḥ ।
sarvaprītyai jaradajagarāśvāsavipluṣṭapatrāḥ
kliṣṭacchāyāh praviralalatāstāḥ kathaṃ te bhavanti ।।

pituḥ śrutveti vacanaṃ rājaputrastamabravīt ।
dantakāntādhararuciṃ vairāgyaṃ grāhayanniva ।।

śītalā nirmalajalāh saṃtoṣaśaśiśītalāḥ ।
vane vairāgyasubhagā bhuvaḥ kasya na vallabhāḥ ।।

paradārā iva kṣiprasukhāvarjitadurjanāḥ ।
narakapratyayāyāme sāpāyā na priyāḥ priyāḥ ।।

dhyānaṃ mantraḥ parijñānamindriyāṇāṃ canirjayaḥ ।
rājñāṃ hiṃsāprayatnena yogo ayaṃ narakapradaḥ ।।

hasantyaḥ saṃsāraṃ kusumakalilāḥ kānanabhuvaḥ
svabhāvena prītiṃ vidadhati budhānāṃ śamamayīm ।
