dṛḍhaṃ cintāśrāṇtā vyajanapavanocchvāsabahulā
vibhūtirbhūpānāṃ śiraḥsaktāmanityatām ।।

anujānīhi māṃ tāta vrajāmyeṣa tapovanam ।
jānīhi sarvabhāvānāṃ śiraḥsaktāmanityatām ।।

iti putravacaḥ śrutvā tattatheti vicintayan ।
uvācopacitāścaryastaṃ manīṣī mahīpatiḥ ।।

vivekavimalaṃ putra tvamicchāsi sa cedvanam ।
hitvāme saṃśayaṃ tāvat paścādyuktiṃ kariṣyasi ।।

vrajatā badhyavaśudhāṃ tiryaguktaṃ tvayā vacaḥ ।
pracuraṃ tadabhiprāyaṃ vaktumarhasi tattvataḥ ।।

iti kṣitibhujā pṛṣṭaḥ so abravīttanmayoditam ।
vasatyatra na kaścit tvā madvadhādyo nivartayet ।।

sukṛtī jīvati śavaḥ sa pāpastu mṛto amṛtaḥ ।
prāk puṇyaṃ bhakṣyate mūlāt sadhanairdhānyarāśivat ।।

ityāśayānmayā tāta taduktaṃ vacanaṃ priyam ।
।।

iti śrutvā kṣitipatistaṃ pariṣvajya sādaraḥ ।
ucitaṃ kriyatām putra kuśalāyetyabhāṣataḥ ।।

tataḥ sa pitrānujñātaḥ sāśrunetreṇa kānanam ।
prayayau mantriputrāṇāṃ sahitaḥ pañcabhiḥ śataiḥ ।।

maharṣerantike tatra pravrajyāṃ prāpya sānugah ।
teṣāṃ kālena so apaśyat kuṇḍavalkalasaṃcayam ।।

tataḥsa saṃcayadveṣī tadadarśanasaṃvidā ।
ekākī vijane tasthau kaṃcit kālaṃmahāmatiḥ ।।

darśanābhāṣaṇe baddhaniyamo api yadṛcchayā ।
prāptaṃ svāgatamityuktvā papraccha kuśalaṃ mṛgam ।।

punaśca pūjitaṃ dṛṣṭvā muniṃ tena mṛgavratam ।
amātyatanayāḥ sarve vilakṣāḥ samacintayan ।।

mṛgo mṛgavrataścāyaṃ pūjitau niṣparigrahau ।
etāvanajinau daṇḍasaṃbḥārāḍambarojjhitau ।।

etadarthamanenāsmaddarśane niyamaḥ kṛtaḥ ।
vratopakaraṇavyagrānnūnamasyāpi vārayet ।।

iti saṃcintya sarvaṃ te vratopacārasaṃcayam ।
nadyāṃ prakṣipya vārāyāṃ yayuḥ śuddhāstadantikam ।।

tyaktvā gṛhabhūvaṃ teṣāmāśayānuśayocitām ।
sa dhātuṃ prakṛtiṃ jñātvā vidadhe dharmadeśanām ।।

rājaputraḥ sa evāhaṃ śākyāste mantrisūnavaḥ ।
punastyāgopadeśo ayamadyāpyeṣāṃ mayā kṛtaḥ ।।

iti śākyakumāravṛttametat kathitaṃ bhikṣugaṇaḥ svayaṃ jinena ।
avadhārya parāmapūjayat tāṃ karuṇāmāśritavatsalasya tasya ।।

iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ mūkapaṅgvavadānaṃ nāma saptatriṃśaḥ pallavaḥ ।।

kṣānyavadānam ।

te jayanti dhṛtiśīlinaḥ paraṃ nirvikārarucisūcitādbhutāḥ ।
śeṣavat pṛthulabhāranirvyathāḥ ye vahanti sukṛtakṣamāḥ kṣamām ।।

purā purā puṇyaviparyayeṇa ripuḥ prajānāṃ janitaprakampaḥ ।
udunbanāmā nibiḍopatāpairyakṣa kṣayāyaiva kṛtakṣaṇo abhūt ।।

akālakālaṃ tamanāthabandhurlokānukampī bhagavān prasahya ।
śikṣopadeśaṃ śaraṇaṃ prapannaṃ śamābhidhāyī vinaye nyayuṅkta ।।

tasmin praśānte bhuvanopatāpe draṣṭuṃ prahṛṣṭaḥ sugataṃ sametya ।
saṃcāriṇaṃ nākapatiḥ praṇamya tatkālajātasmitamityuvāca ।।

kasmādakasmāt smitacandralekhā mukhāmbuje bhāti tavādbhuteyam ।
akāraṇaṃ sattvasudhāsamudrā na lokasāmānyatayām hasanti ।।

śrutveti vākyaṃ tridaśeśvarasya tat taṃ sarvadarśī bhagavān babhāṣe ।
asmin pradeśe nijapūrvavṛttaṃ smṛtvā smtaṃ jātamidaṃ mamendraṃ ।।

purā muniḥ kṣāniratirvane asminnuvāsa nirvāsitaroṣadoṣaḥ ।
yo abhūdbhuvo rāgarajaḥsvabhāve vidveṣavānindurivāravinde ।।

athottarāśādhipatirvasante vanāntarālokanakautukena ।
sāntaḥpuraḥ kelisukhāya kāmī tadāśramopāntamahīmavāpa ।।

rāgī kalirnāma sa bhūmipālaḥ pādaprahārairvadanāsavaiśca ।
lebhe vilāseṣu nitambinīnāmaśokaśobhāṃ bakulaśriyaṃ ca ।।

diśastapolopapṛthuprakopabhrūbhaṅgavṛndairiva tāpasānām ।
tatra bhramadbhirbhramarairbabhūvuḥ kāmāgnidhūmairiva sāndhakārāh ।।

līlāvilolāḥ pavanākulālīstanāvanamrāḥ stabakā latānām ।
raktādharāḥ pāṭalapallavānām prāpurvilāsaṃ lalanā latānām ।।

rājāṅganāḥ kautukavibhrameṇa vane carantyastamṛṣiṃ vilokya ।
acañcaladhyānasamādhisaktaṃ vimuktarāgaṃ parivārya tasthuḥ ।।

taddeśamabhyetya nareśvaro atha dṛṣṭvā vabhūbhiḥ parivāritaṃ tam ।
īrṣyāprakopānaladurnirīkṣyaḥ ciccheda tasyāśu sa pāṇipādam ।।

chinnāṅgavargo api sa nirvikāraścukopa bhūpāya na nāma dhīraḥ ।
nyavārayat krūrataraṃ ca tasmai gandharvayakṣoragadevasaṃgham ।।

tataḥ prayāte nṛpatau puraṃ svāṃ sametya sarve munayo vanebhyaḥ ।
taṃ tatra kṛtāvayavaṃ vilokya kṣāntā api krodhadhutā babhūvuḥ ।।

śāpapradānābhimukhān nivārya kṣantavyamityeva sa tānuvāca ।
kṣāmāsamāliṅgitamānasānām kopakriyābhiḥ kriyate na saṅgaḥ ।।

vikāravego api na pāṇipādacchede mamābhūd yadi vītamanyoḥ ।
satyena tenākṣatadeha eva syāmityavādīt sa punaḥ prasādī ।।

tataḥ kṣaṇāt saṃgatapāṇipādaṃ rūḍhavraṇaṃ pretya sadodayena ।
apūjayat kṣāntiguṇaṃ stavena taṃ devatā sattvasitaiśca puṣpaiḥ ।।

rājāpi tatkilbiṣakālakūṭavisphoṭasaṃghaṭṭavinaṣṭaceṣṭaḥ ।
pūrotkaṭāvartavivartamānaḥ saṃvartapākaṃ narakaṃ jagāma ।।

yo abhūtpurā kṣāntiratirmaharṣiḥ so ahaṃ kaliryaśca sa devadattaḥ ।
atītavṛttasmaraṇena śakra nākāraṇaṃ jātamidaṃ smitaṃ me ।।

iti bhagavataḥ śrutvā vākyaṃ sa vismayamānasaḥ
pramadavikacavyaktotsāhā vahannayanāvalīḥ ।
taraṇikiraṇasparśeneva sphuṭaḥ kamalākaras
tridaśavasatiṃ prītaḥ prāyāt patistridivaikasām ।।

iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ kṣāntyavadānamaṣṭatriṃśaḥ pallavaḥ ।।

kapilāvadānam ।

atyantamunnatimatāṃ mahatāṃ vināśadoṣasya durjanasamāgama eva hetuḥ ।
kūladrumāḥ kila phalaprasavaiḥ sahaiva sadyaḥ patanti jalasaṃgatibhinnamūlāḥ ।।

rucirāgāraśālinyām vaiśālyāṃ bhagavān purā ।
valgumatyāstaṭe nadyā vicacāra tathāgataḥ ।।

tasyāḥ kaivartasarthena gambhīre ambhasi dustare ।
kadācid ghoramakaraḥ kṣiptvā jālaṃ samuddhṛtaḥ ।।

aṣṭādaśaśirāḥ siḥsadviraprakharānanaḥ ।
nṛṇāṃ sahasrairākṛṣṭaḥ parvatākāravigrahaḥ ।।

taṃ dṛṣṭvā tatra vitrastāh srastākarṣaṇarajjavaḥ ।
āścaryaniścaladṛśo na tasthurna yayuḥ kṣaṇam ।।

gaṇanāṃ gahanāścaryaviśeṣaśataśālinām ।
saṃsāre karmavaicitrye vikārāṇāṃ karoti kaḥ ।।

atrāntare tamuddeśaṃ bhagavān bhūtabhāvanaḥ ।
jinah samāyayau sarvajanatrāṇakṛtakṣaṇah ।।

savṛddhabālalalanaṃ janaṃ kautukasaṃgatam ।
dṛṣṭvā tatrākarottīre bhagavānāsanagraham ।।

bhikṣusaṃghaiḥ parivṛtaṃ dṛṣṭvā tatra tathāgatam ।
jano abhūdunmukhaḥ sarvaḥ pratyāvṛttaḥ ivodadhiḥ ।।

taṃ vilokyaiva vinatāḥ kaivartāḥ prāṇibandhanam ।
viśālajālaṃ sahasā saṃsāramiva tatyajuḥ ।।

matsyakumbhīnakrādisaṃsāraṃ tadgirāmbhasi ।
tyaktvā te viratāṭopā babhūvuḥ kilbiṣadviṣaḥ ।।

tairnyastaṃ bhagavān dṛṣṭvā mahākamaramagrataḥ ।
taṃ jagāda sṛjan dantakāntyaiva karuṇānadīm ।।

api tvaṃ kapilaḥ putra kiṃ n asmarasi duṣkṛtam ।
vacoduścaritasyāyaṃ paripāko anubhūyate ।।

sāpyakalyāṇamitraṃ te jananī kkādya vartate ।
sarvajñenetyabhihitaḥ smṛtvā jātimuvāca saḥ ।।

vibho bhavāmi kapilaḥ smarāmi nijaduṣkṛtam ।
vacoduścaritasyāyaṃ paripāko anubhūyate ।।

yātā me narakaṃ mātā narakādeśinī purā ।
ityuktvā makarastatra ruroda paruṣasvaram ।।

taṃ śokasāgare magnaṃ babhāṣe bhagavān punaḥ ।
akāle kiṃ karomyadya tiryagyonigatasya te ।।

apuṇyaprārambhe rabhasahasitollāsavihite
pramattānāṃ yāte narakaparipākapraṇayitām ।
aśānteḥ saṃtāpaṃ ruditaśaraṇāni pratiniśaṃ
bhṛśaṃ kleśāveśairdiśati viṣatulyairanuśayaḥ ।।

kṣaṇaṃ duḥkhakṣayāyaiva mayi cittaṃ prasādaya ।
prasannamānasaḥ kāle yāsyasi tridaśālayam ।।

śṛṇu vatsa hitaṃ cedaṃ vicārya kuru cetasi ।
anityāḥ sarvasaṃskārāḥ śāntinirvāṇamakṣayam ।।

ityājñayāḥ bhagavatastasmin yāte prasannatām ।
janasaṃghaḥ sa suciraṃ babhūvāścaryaniścalaḥ ।।

āryānandaḥ praṇayinā janenābhyarthitastataḥ ।
tatpūrvavṛttaṃ papraccha bhagavantaṃ kṛtāñjaliḥ ।।

sa tena pṛṣṭaḥ provāca vimapajñānalocanaḥ ।
asyākuśalaśīlasya vṛttāntaḥ śrūyatāmayam ।।

bhadrakākhye purā kalpe varṣāyutayugāyuṣi । jane babhūva bhagavān kāśyapākhyastathāgataḥ।।

kṛkirnāma mahīpālaḥ kalpaśāla ivārthinām ।
abhavat samaye tasmin vārāṇasyāṃ bahupradaḥ ।।

kadācidvibudhāsthāne sahasrākṣamivāparam ।
āsīnaṃ vādisiṃhākhyastaṃ vidvānāyayau dvijaḥ ।।

avilambitasaṃprāptadarśanāsanasatkṛtiḥ ।
sa dattāśīrnarapatiṃ śiṣyaśreṇivṛto abhyadhāt ।।

svasti svastimate budhādhipasabhāsīnāya tubhyaṃ vibho
lubdhāḥ saccaritāmṛte tava paraṃ saṃdarśane rāgiṇaḥ ।
sadveṣāḥ parabhūpanāmni mukharāste sudguṇodīraṇe
kasmātsarvaguṇāśrayeṇa bhavatā duṣairvayaṃ yojitāḥ ।।

yadyācakā api nirantararatnavarṣe nānārthisārthaparipūrakatām prayānti ।
sarvaṃ bhavānupamapuṇyanidhe vadānya nirdainyadānavibhavasya vijṛmbhitaṃ te ।।

rājan kiṃcitparicitaguṇaiḥ sevayā sadgurubhyaḥ
prāpto asmābhirvibudhavijayī ko api vidyāṃśaleśaḥ ।
asyāṃ vidvatkamalabharasaumyaprabhāyāṃ sabhāyāṃ
tasyotkarṣaṃ katipayapadaṃ pratyayaṃ darśayāmaḥ ।।

nijaguṇagaṇane dhīrlajjate sajjanānāṃ mukharayati tathāpi prauḍhavādābhilāṣaḥ ।
iyati jagati rājan kṣipramānviṣyatām me prativacanaruciśedasti kaścidvipaścit ।।

saṃdarbhagarbhagambhīramiti tasyotkaṭaṃ vacaḥ ।
śrutvā kṣitipatiḥ kṣipraṃ vilakṣaḥ samacintayat ।।

aprāptapratimallo ayaṃ yadi yāyānmadoddhataḥ ।
tadeṣa mam adeśasya yaśaḥkhaṇḍanadiṇḍimaḥ ।।

guṇāpamānakṛd yatra mūrkho bhavati bhūpatiḥ ।
na karoti janastatra vidyārjanapariśramam ।।

vivekavimalāloke dharmārāme mahīpatau ।
loke vidyāḥ pravartante sadācārakriyā iva ।।

tasmādasya prayatnena kartavyo madanigraha ।
vidyādaridratā deśe doṣa eva viśāṃpateḥ ।।

iti saṃcintya nṛpatirvipraṃ karvaṭavāsinam ।
ānināya mahāmatyairanviṣaya viduṣāṃ gurum ।।

abhūbhṛtsabhāmupādhyāya pretya taṃ tarkakarkaśam ।
cakāra vādisiṃhasya darpakesarakartanam ।।

tasya tena jitasyāśu vijitāśeṣavādinaḥ ।
maunasūtraṃ samāpede lajjiteva sarasvatī ।।

ārūḍhāḥ śubhramahasaṃ nakṣatrāṇāmivodayāḥ ।
uparyupari dṛśyante guṇotkarṣā manīṣiṇām ।।

vādisiṃhaṃ visṛjyātha datvā bhūri dhanaṃ nṛpaḥ ।
dadau dvijāya jayine karvaṭaṃ nagaropamam ।।

labdharājagajāśvo atha carukeyūrakaṅkaṇaḥ ।
upādhyāyaḥ svabhavanaṃ praviveśa saha śriyā ।।

bhujairjitā bhūmibhujāṃ vaṇijāṃ sāgarārjitāḥ ।
vidyāvatāṃ virājante guṇotkarṣarjitāḥ śriyaḥ ।।

kālena śrīmatastasya putrajanmotsavo abhavat ।
sukhe api sukhasaṃpattirlakṣaṇaṃ puṇyakarmaṇām ।।

kapilo nāma sa śiśustejaḥpiṅgaśiroruhaḥ ।
vardhamānamatirvidvān piturabhyadhiko abhavat ।।

kule mahati vaiduṣyaṃ vibhavodbhavaḥ ।
vibhave satsutotkarṣaḥ phalaṃ sukṛtaśākhinaḥ ।।

kadācidvyādhisaṃyogātpratyāsannatanukṣayaḥ ।
vijane putramāhūya so avadat putravatsalaḥ ।।
bālye guṇārjanaṃ putra paralokasukhārjanam ।।
uttamarṇa iva prāpte kāle sugaṇitāvadhau ।
adhunā vivaśaḥ kkāhaṃ kka sā vidyā kka taddhanam ।।

guṇapuṣpe sukhaphale baddhamūle dhanairjane ।
vane vajra ivākālakālaḥ patatiḥ duḥsahaḥ ।।

kṣapayati sakalābhirjanma vidyākalābhiḥ kṣaṇikasukhanimittaṃ saṃnidhatte ca vittam ।
paśuśiśuṣu manuṣyaḥ prīyate mohaśiṣyaḥ tanuvirahamūrhūrte sarvamanyat sa cānyaḥ ।।

idaṃ tu te hitaṃ vacmi snehamohavaśīkṛtaḥ ।
saṃsārasāraśaraṇaṃ vatsa vetsi bahuśrutaḥ ।।

santaḥ praṇamyāḥ paruṣaṇ na vācyaṃ kāryaḥ prayatnena paropakāraḥ ।
pāpāvapāte satataṃ hi puṃsāmetāni puṇyānyavalambanāni ।।

alobhaśobhābharaṇā vibhūtiradveṣasaktiḥ svasukheṣvamohaḥ ।
mūlatraye asmin kuśaladrumasya vasatyaśeṣākhilasatphataśrīḥ ।।

yāvattapati tīkṣṇāṃśurasmin bhuvanamaṇḍale ।
tāvattvatsadṛśaḥ putra vidvān vādī na vidyate ।।

bhikṣubhistu na kartavyastvayā vādaḥ kadācanah ।
gambhīrajñānadurbodhaprabuddhā bauddhabuddhayaḥ ।।

purā bhikṣurmayā pṛṣṭaḥ padasyārthaṃ jahāsa mām ।
praśnaṃ kartuṃ na jānīṣe vidvāniti jagāda ca ।।

tasmād bhikṣuvivādaste paraṃ pāṇḍityapīḍanam ।
balaprabhāvakāmo hi giriṃ mūrdhnāṃ na tāḍayet ।।

ityuktvā tanayaṃ vipraḥ paralokabhuvaṃ yayau ।
kāyāvasathapānthānāṃ dehinām na cirasthitiḥ ।।

vāgmī kālena kapilaḥ khaṇḍitākhilapaṇḍitaḥ ।
nṛpādbahugrṇaṃ prāpa dhanamānamahodayam ।।

tataḥ kadācidekānte kapilaṃ kācarābhidhā ।
saṃprāptaṃ vādisāmrājyaṃ jagāda jananī śanaiḥ ।।

vādidarpacchidā putra digdvīpajayinā tvayā ।
durjanāḥ śramaṇāḥ kasmāddarpāndhāḥ parivarjitāḥ ।।

parotkarṣādhirūḍhasya pratipakṣe kṣamārateḥ ।
akṣamo ayamiti vyaktaṃ kṣaṇena kṣīyate yaśaḥ ।।

iti māturvacaḥ śrutvā so avadad biduṣo vacaḥ ।
na vādaḥ śramaṇaiḥ kāryaḥ pitrāhamiti vāritaḥ ।।

iyaṃ durjīvikāsmākam patrālambanavādinām ।
kriyate guṇamānyānāṃ mānamlānirmukhe yayā ।।

dhigetaccaṇḍapāṇḍityaṃ guruvidveṣaduḥsaham ।
mahatāṃ sukhabhaṅgāya sadā tasmin samudyamaḥ ।।

yasyāṃ na mayā sā buddhiḥ sā śrīrlobhaṃ nihanti yā ।
darpo na yasya vidyā sā śaktiryā ca kṣamāvatī ।।

evameva na kartavyaḥ parairvidveṣavigrahaḥ ।
kiṃ mātarjagatām pūjyabhikṣubhiḥ khyātalakṣmabhiḥ ।।

vijetuṃ na ca te śakyāḥ praṃānapariniṣṭhitāḥ ।
pratipakṣairavikṣiptaṃ yeṣāṃ nairātmyaśāsanam ।।

iti putravacaḥ śrutvā kupitā tamuvāca sā ।
abhūttava pitā nūnaṃ pāpaśramaṇacetakaḥ ।।

mahati brāhmaṇakule jātaḥ prājño bahuśrutaḥ ।
bhikṣapakṣe nipatitaḥ kathaṃ tvamapi tādṛśaḥ ।।

pṛthupramāṇakhaṅgena kuru śramaṇanigraham ।
avidāryābhrasaṃghātaṃ tīrkṣṇāṃśurna virājate ।।

it sa prerito māturgirā tadbhaktiyantritaḥ ।
bhikṣūṇāmāśramapadaṃ śanairgantuṃ samudyayau ।।

vrajan sa saṃmukhāyātaṃ bhikṣuṃ jijñāsayā pathi ।
granthasāraṃ pramāṇaṃ ca papraccha samayocitam ।।

sa tena pṛṣṭaḥ provāca gāḍhaśabdārthanirṇayam ।
lakṣatrayapramāṇaṃ na śastraṃ tīrthikadurlabham ।।

kutaḥ pāre ativartante kka ca vartmātivartate ।
sukhaduḥkhe ca lokasya kkacit samabhibandhataḥ ।।

iti gambhīraśabdārthaṃ śāsturbhagavato vacaḥ ।
anupāsitasarvajñairjñāyate na yathā tathā ।।

etadākarṇya kapilaḥ ślokagāmbhīryavismitaḥ ।
yayau bhagavataḥ puṇyaṃ kāśyapasya tapovanam ।।

tathā bhikṣugaṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā prasannahṛdayānanaḥ ।
acintayat tadaśraddhāṃ vihāya gatamatsaraḥ ।।

eteṣāṃ dveṣakāluṣyāt krauryaṃ kaḥ kartumarhati ।
yeṣāṃ saṃdarśanenaiva vaimalyaṃ labhate manaḥ ।।

iti saṃcintya sa ciraṃ tadvivādaparāṅmukhaḥ ।
dūrādhvakhinnaḥ svagṛhaṃ gatvā provāca mātaram ।।

mithyaivāhaṃ tvayā mātaḥ preritaḥ kalikarmaṇi ।
ajayāḥ śramaṇā loke gūḍhārthagranthavādinaḥ ।।

ślokamātraṃ mayā śrutvā bhikṣorekasya vartmani ।
ajñātārthena vailakṣyāt suciraṃ vīkṣitāṃ kṣitiḥ ।।

tadgrantheṣvakṝtābhyāsastān vaktuṃ kah pragalbhate ।
kathayanti svaśastraṃ te na hi pravrajitādṛte ।।

iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā jananī tamabhāṣata ।
āyāsitāhaṃ bhavatā garbhabhāreṇa kevalam ।।

saṃgharṣamarṣaśūnyena dainyāt sarvapraṇāminā ।
dharṣaṇānirvimarṣeṇa kriyate puruṣeṇa kim ।।

loke sakalaratnānāṃ tejasaiva mahārghatā ।
ko hyarthaḥ puruṣaprāṇaistejojīvanavarjitaiḥ ।।

mithyā tadgranthalābḥāya pravrajyā gṛhyate na kim ।
mūrdhni kṛtteṣu jāyante kiṃ keśeṣu kuśaḥ punaḥ ।।

iti māturgirā tasya manaḥ kaluṣatāṃ yayau ।
sahasā kālavātālīrajoruddhamivāmbaram ।।

tataḥ sa kūṭapraśamapraṇayī bhikṣukānanam ।
gatvā gṛhītvā pravrajyāṃ śāstraṃ saugatamāptavān ।।

kālena dharmakathakaḥ sa vidvān guṇagauravāt ।
siṃhāsanaṃ samāruhya vidadhe dharmadeśanām ।।

jananyā preritastasyāṃ deśanāyāṃ krameṇa saḥ ।
bhikṣudharmaviruddhārthaṃ avktuṃ samupacakrame ।।

dharmaprahāravyathitairbhikṣubhiḥ sa pade pade ।
nivāryamāṇastānūce kṛtvā vikṛtamānanam ।।

ajñātvā darpamukharairayathā bahuvādibhiḥ ।
bhavadbhiḥ sthūladantoṣṭhairvyākhyā mama visūditā ।।

yūyaṃ gardabhamarkaṭoṣṭravadanā dvīpyāsyapaśvānanā
mārjāraiṇavarāhakukkuramukhā durdarśavakrkraḥ param ।
sahyā maunajuṣo api naiva vikaṭāṭopaṃ raṭantaḥ kimu
bhrūbhaṅgairiti bhikṣusaṃghamasakṛnnirbhartsayan so abhyadhāt ।।

tasya vākyaśaraistīkṣṇairvikṛttā iva bhikṣavaḥ ।
anuktvaiva prativacastyaktvā taṃ yayuranyataḥ ।।

tena vākpātakenātha paścāttāpamupāgataḥ ।
tatyāja jananīmeva pravrajyām na tu tāṃ dvijaḥ ।।

śramaṇairme hṛtaḥ putra iti sā vipralāpinī ।
unmādinī tanuṃ tyaktvā prapede narakasthitim ।।

tataḥ kālena kapilaḥ svayaṃ kalitakilbiṣaḥ ।
dehānte vākyapāruṣyādimāṃ makaratāṃ gataḥ ।।

tānyetāni mukhānyasya yānyūce bhikṣubhartsane ।
phalaṃ sadṛśarūpaṃ hi karmabījāt prajāyate ।।

ityuktvā tatra bhagavān dharmamādiśya śāśvatam ।
janasyānugrahaṃ cakre nānābodhividhāyakam ।।

tataḥ prayāte svapadaṃ jine tanmayamānasaḥ ।
kamaraḥ projjhitāhārastyaktvā dehaṃ divaṃ yayau ।।

cāturmahārājikeṣu deveṣu viśadadyutiḥ ।
śrīmān sa jātaḥ sugate kṣaṇaṃ cittaprasādanāt ।।

tataḥ pūrṇenduvadanaḥ sragvī rucirakuṇḍalah ।
sa sākāra ivānandaḥ sugataṃ draṣṭumāyayau ।।

prakīrṇadivyakusumaḥ kirīṭaspṛṣṭabhūtalaḥ ।
prabhāpūritadikcakrastaṃ bhaktyā praṇanāma saḥ ।।

cakre tasyopaviṣṭasya bhagavān dharmadeśanām ।
yayā srotaḥphalaṃ prāpya satyadarśī jagāma saḥ ।।

tṛṇamiva gurukāyo apyuddhṛtaḥ pāpapaṅkād
iti sa jananikāyaḥ so api duḥkhājjinena ।
vyasananipatitānāṃ līlayā puṇyaśīlā
nikhilamatulamūlaṃ kleśamunmūlayanti ।।

iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ kapilavadānaṃ nāma ekonacatvāriṃśaḥ pallavaḥ ।।

udrāyaṇāvadānam ।

tulyameva puruṣeṇa bhujyate kāyabhājanagataṃ śubhāśubham ।
dehināṃ vividhakarmajaṃ phalaṃ na hyabhuktamupayāti saṃkṣayam ।।

bhagavān sugataḥ pūrvaṃ pure rājagṛhābhidhe ।
kalandakanivāsākhye vijahāra vanāntare ।।

bimbisāraḥ kṣitipatistatrābhūdviśrutaḥ śriyā ।
ākaraḥ saravratnānāṃ ratnākaram ivāparaḥ ।।

babhūva samaye tasmin raurukākhye pure nṛpaḥ ।
śrīmānudrāyaṇo nāma yaśaścandramahodadhiḥ ।।

tasya candraprabhā nāma patnī candrānanābhavat ।
śikhaṇḍī yuvarājaśca sūnurvikramakarkaśaḥ ।।

hiruko bhirukaśceti tasyāmātyau babhūvatuḥ ।
gaṇanīyau na vinaye yayuḥ śukrabṛhaspatī ।।

jātā bhūmibhujaḥ prītirlekhakhatviṣastayoḥ ।
raverdūrasthitasyāpi kamalākarayoriva ।।

apūrvaratnanicayapreṣaṇairbahuśastayoḥ ।
paripūrṇaṃ paraṃ prāpa sakhyaṃ prema vidhānataḥ ।।

dūrasthāpi paraṃ prītiḥ satāṃ kīrtirivākṣayā ।
saṃsaktāpi khalaprītistṛṇajvāleva na sthirā ।।

kadāciddivyaratnāṅkaṃ kavacaṃ kāñcanojjvalam ।
prāhiṇod bimbisārāya sāramudrāyaṇo nṛpaḥ ।।

viṣahsastrāgnirakṣārhaṃ vicitraratnakaṃ ca tat ।
suhṛtpreṣitamādāya provāca saciavān nṛpaḥ ।।

idaṃ me prahitaṃ tena saujanyamiva bhūbhujā ।
sarva rakṣākṣamaṃ varma gāḍhapremanivedakam ।।

na paśyāmyasya sadṛśaṃ pratideyaṃ tathādhikam ।
alpapratikriyā śalyamupakārāpakārayoḥ ।।

ucitaṃ cintyatāṃ kiṃcit preṣaṇīyamato adhikam ।
sarvairbhadbhirityuktvā nṝpaścintākulo abhavat ।।

atha dhīmān mahāmātyaściraṃ dhyātvā tamabravīt ।
varṣakārābhidho vipraḥ sarvavidyāsu pāragaḥ ।।

ato bahuguṇaṃ rāgannekamevāstyupāyanam ।
tasya saṃpreṣane yatnaḥ kriyatāṃ yadi śakyate ।।

ya eṣa bhagavān buddhaḥ sthitastvadviṣayāntike ।
devānāmādarasthānaṃ paṭastatpratimānvitaḥ ।।

aśeṣalokakalyāṇakalikākalpapādapaḥ ।
citre svapne atha saṃkalpe pṛthupuṇyaiḥ sa dṛśyate ।।

iti mantrivacaḥ śrutvā tathetyuktvā mahīpatiḥ ।
gatvā bhagavate namrastamevārthaṃ nyavedayat ।।

anujñātastatastena nṛpaścitrakarān varān ।
ādideśāśu bhagavatpratimollekhakarmaṇi ।।

jinasyālokayantaste mūrti rūpavśīkṛtāḥ ।
yayuḥ pramāṇagrahaṇe pragalbhā apyaśaktatām ।।

saṃkrāntāṃ nimalapaṭe chāyāṃ bhagavatastataḥ ।
suvarṇabhāvanābhikhyāṃ te śanaiḥ samapūrayan ।।

prāḥiṇodatha bhūpālastaṃ buddhapratimāpaṭam ।
jagannayanapuṇyānāṃ mūrtānāmiva saṃcayam ।।

bimbisārasya hastāṅkalekhāmudrāyaṇo nṛpaḥ ।
paṭasya purataḥ prāptām hṛṣṭaḥ svayamavācayat ।।

sugatacaraṇapadmanyāsapuṇyopakaṇṭhāt
tridaśapuraviśeṣānmāgadhodāraradeśāt ।
kuśalakalitamūrtirbhūpatirbimbisāraḥ
kṣititalatilakaṃ tvāṃ dharmabandhurbravīti ।।

etatte prahitaṃ hitaṃ bhavamahāmohāmaye bheṣajaṃ
rājadveṣaviṣāpahaṃ bhagavato bimbaṃ śaśāṅkatviṣaḥ ।
tṛṣṇāpacchamanaṃ prasannamadhuraṃ tvannetrapātrārpitaṃ
dhanyaḥ puṇyarasāyanaṃ piba haṭhādākaṇṭhamutkaṇṭhitaḥ ।।

sanmārge viniyojanaṃ sguṇagaṇādhāne sadādhyāpanaṃ
durvyāpāranivāraṇam thirasukhaprāptau paripreraṇam ।
nirvyājopakṛtau nirantaratayā sarvātmanā vartanaṃ
kartavyaṃ kimataḥ paraṃ priyahitaṃ kalyāṇamitraiḥ satām ।।

iti lekhārthamāsvādya suhṛtpremāmṛtocitam ।
rājā gajādhirūḍhasya paṭasya prayayau puraḥ ।।

abhinandya tamānandāt sāmātyaḥ sapurohitaḥ ।
hemasiṃhāsanotsaṅge sa prasārya nyaveśayat ।।

lāvaṇyapuṇyanilayaṃ dṛṣṭvā tatsaugataṃ vapuḥ ।
namo namah prabuddhāyetyavadajagatījanaḥ ।।

buddhābhidhānaṃ śrutvaiva pulakālaṃkṛtākṛtiḥ ।
puṣpavarṣe surairmukte vismito abhūnmahīpati ।।

puṇyaṃ bhagavataḥ śrutvā sa tatra caritāmṛtam ।
payodānādasotkaṇṭhanīlakaṇṭhatulāṃ yayau ।।

dvādaśāṅgaṃ paṭasyādha sānulomaviparyayam ।
pratītyasamutpādaṃ ca dṛṣṭvā mohaṃ mumoca saḥ ।।

srotaḥprāptiphalenaivaṃ dṛṣṭasatyo atha bhūpatiḥ ।
dideśa pratisaṃdeśaṃ sakhyurbhikṣurvisarjanaiḥ ।।

bimbisārastatastasmai kṛtvā bhagavato arthanām ।
kātyāyanaṃ ca vyasṛjat śailākhyām cāpi bhikṣuṇīm ।।

udrāyaṇasya nṝpaterāryaḥ kātyāyano atha saḥ ।
pūjāvidhāyinastatra vidadhe dharmadeśanām ।।

dharmadeśanayā tasya saṃgataḥ sumahān janaḥ ।
srotaḥsakṛdanāgāmiphalārhatpadamāptavān ।।

tasmin gṛhapatī khyātau tiṣyapuṣyābhidhau pure ।
śāntyai pravrajya tasyāgre parinirvṛtimāpatuḥ ।।

kālena vihitai stūpau dehānte jñātibhistayoḥ ।
tannāmacihnāvadyāpi vandante caityavandakāḥ ।।

devyāścandraprabhāyāśca śaolākhyā sāpi bhikṣuṇī ।
krameṇāntaḥpure cakre satataṃ dharmadeśanām ।।

kadācidatha bhūpālah krīḍagāragatāṃ priyām । tāmajñāsīnnimittajñaḥ saptāhāvadhijīvitām ।। 
jñātasaṃsāracaritastatastāṃ vaśudhādhipaḥ ।
anujajñe śubhapadaṃ prātuṃ pravrajyayā puraḥ ।।

svākhyāte dharmavinmaye bhikṣukyā nṛpatergirā ।
devī pravrajitā dehaṃ dine tatyāja saptame ।।

cāturmahārājikeṣu deveṣu sahasaiva sā ।
prayātā devakanyātvaṃ jagāma jinakānanam ।।

tatra pūrṇenduvadanā divyābharaṇabhūṣitā ।
dṛṣṭvā śākyamuniṃ hṛṣṭā sā papātāsya pādayoḥ ।।

prakīrṇadivyapuṣpāyāstasyāścakre tathāgataḥ ।
dharmopapādanaṃ yena dṛṣṭasatyā jagāma sā ।।

sā gatvā nagaraṃ patyurvyomnā mūrtirivaindavī ।
vibodhya niśi suptasya cakre bodhiprakāśanam ।।

yātāyāṃ svapadaṃ tasyāṃ prabhāte vasudhādhipaḥ ।
pravrajyābhimukhaḥ putramabhiṣicya śikhaṇḍinam ।।

prajātrāṇāya nikṣipya taṃ mahāmātyayostataḥ ।
nṛpaterbimbisārasya suhṛdaḥ sa yayau puram ।।

bimbisārastamāyātaṃ vigatacchatracāmaram ।
nṛpopacāraiḥ praṇataḥ prītipūtairapūjayat ।।

viśrāntamāsanāsīnaṃ sa tamūce savismayaḥ ।
hṛṣṭhaḥ saṃdarśanenāsya śrīviyogena duḥkhitaḥ ।।

rājannanantasāmantamauliviśrāntaśāsanaḥ ।
pākaśāsanatulyastvaṃ kathamevamupāgataḥ ।।

abhinnavakrkraprakṛterguptamantrasya dhīmataḥ ।
pareṇa rājyaharaṇaṃ vīra saṃbhāvyate na te ।।

iti pṛṣṭaḥ sa suhṛdā sasmitastamabhāṣata ।
rājan vṛddhivibhūtirme na priyā sarvagāminī ।।

viṣayāsvādavaimukhyād vitṛṣṇena mayā svayam ।
utsṛṣṭamiva saṃtyaktamaiśvaryaṃ bhogabhājanam ।।

tvayā kalyāṇamitreṇa sugatapratimāpaṭaḥ ।
yo asau hitāya prahitaḥ s avairāgyagururmamaḥ ।।

adhunā tvatprasādena gatvā bhagavato antike ।
icchāmyavāptuṃ pravrajyāmagārādanagārikaḥ ।।

iti sakhyurvacaḥ śrutvā tattatheti vicintya ca ।
sādarastadvivekena bimbisārastamabravīt ।।

dhanyo bahumataścāsi satāṃ tvaṃ pṛthivīpate ।
kathaṃ saṃsāravimukhī jātā te matirīdṛśī ।।

saṃtoṣavibhavo bhogasubhagaḥ śobhase param ।
lakṣaṇaṃ śuddhasattvānāṃ vairājyābharaṇaṃ manah ।।

kiṃ sāmrājyamahaujasā sarajasā duḥsādhanaiḥ sādhanaiḥ
kiṃ bhogaiḥ kṣaṇabhojanaiḥ kulaṣadaiḥ kiṃ sattvaduḥkhaiḥ sukhaiḥ ।
saṃsāroparamāya cetasi satāṃ janmāntaropārjitaṃ
vairāgyaṃ kurute padaṃ yadi mahāmohaprarohāpaham ।।

yena prāṇamanaḥpriyā vasumatī saṃtyajyate līlayā
trailokyābhimate api yaḥ smarasukhe vaimukhyadīkṣāguruḥ ।
saṃmohavysanāturaṃ jagadidaṃ yenānukampāspadaṃ
puṇyaiḥ ko api sa jāyate matimatāṃ saṃsāravāmaḥ śamah ।।

ityuktvā bimbisārastaṃ nītvā veṇuvanāśramam ।
sapraṇāmaṃ bhagavate tadvṛttāntaṃ nyavedayat ।।

udrāyaṇo api sugatākāraṃ suciracintitam ।
vilokya harṣādātmānaṃ kṛtakṛtyamamanyata ।।

parṇāmavyagraśirasā saṃsāracchedini tanau ।
papāta bhagavaddṛṣṭistasya pravrajyayā saha ।।

bhikṣubhāvamathāsādya pātrapāṇiḥ sa cīvarī ।
nagare piṇḍapātārthī cakāra janavismayam ।।

prajāḥ śikhaṇḍī dharmeṇa pālayitvā prasannadhīḥ ।
yātaḥ kālena kāluṣyamadharmābhirato abahvat ।।

kaluṣaṃ kāñcanarucivyaktavidyudvilāsinī ।
na kasya kurute lakṣmīrmeghamāleva mānasam ।।

anāyattaṃ mahāmātyau hiruko bhirukaśca tam ।
adharmakarmanirataṃ kruddhau tatyajatuḥ prabhum ।।

tatpade vihitau rājñā sacivau daṇḍamugdarau ।
cittānuvṛttikuśalau svairaṃ saktaṃ tamūcatuḥ ।।

prajārañjanasaṃsaktā rājadaurjanyavādinaḥ ।
svayaśaḥkhyāpanāyaiva jāyante dhūrtamantriṇaḥ ।।

na dharmaṃ na sukhaṃ nārthaṃ na kīrti na ca jīvitam ।
gaṇayanti prabhorarthe te bhṛtyā bhavyabhaktayaḥ ।।

nākhaṇḍitā nākṣayitā nātaptā nāpyapīḍitāḥ ।
kurvantyarthakriyā rājñastilatulyāḥ kila prajāḥ ।।

iti bruvāṇau tau rājñā niyuktau rājyacintane ।
lobhāt pravṛttau durnītau hantuṃ niḥśaraṇāḥ prajāḥ ।।

nirvicāre durācāre kumatau pṛthivīpatau ।
luptasatye mahāmātye prajānāṃ jīvitaṃ kutaḥ ।।

udrāyaṇo athācireṇa kadācid vaṇijaṃpathi ।
nijadeśāgataṃ vārtāṃ papraccha nṛparāṣṭrayoḥ ।।

so avadaddeva kuśalī sutastava mahīpatiḥ ।
kiṃ tu sanmantrirahitaḥ kumantrivaśamāgataḥ ।।

tatra prajānāṃ vitatopatāpaḥ ko api pravṛttaḥ prabhuśāsanena ।
yenādya tatkutsitadeśajanma divāniśaṃ śocati pauralokaḥ ।।

yatra dhvāntaṃ sṛjati taraṇiryatra candro agnivarṣī
yatrodeti prakaṭamamṛtādutkaṭaḥ kālakūṭaḥ ।
yatra trātā harati nṛpatirjīvavṛttiṃ prajānāṃ
tatrākrandaṃ prasṝtavipulopaplavaṃ kaḥ śṛṇoti ।।

ityāsaktanṛpāyāsakhinnasyārtimayaṃ vacaḥ ।
duḥsahaṃ vaṇijaḥ śrutvā sa tamūce kṛpānidhiḥ ।।

dadgirā tvamito gatvā tūrṇamāśvāsaya prajāḥ ।
sthāpayiṣyāmyahaṃ dharme svayametya śikhaṇḍinam ।।

ityuktastena sānandaḥ svadeśaṃ śanakairvaṇik ।
gatvā prajānāṃ vidadhe svairamāśvāsanaṃ puraḥ ।।

pravāde prasṛte tasminnamātyau daṇḍamudgarau ।
atītabhūpāgamanatrastau bhūpatimūcatuḥ ।।

sarvatra śrūyate deva pravādaḥ sādhuninditaḥ ।
vṛddhaḥ pravrajito rājā rājyārthī yatnavāniti ।।

tīvravrataparikliṣṭaḥ saṃbhogābhimukhādaraḥ ।
lajjāṃ pravrajyayā sārdhaṃ tyaktvā sa punareṣyati ।।

rājannapakkavairāgyāstyajanti sahasaiva yat ।
tat pūrvābhyadhikaṃ teṣāṃ prayāti priyatāṃ punaḥ ।।

lokasthitiviruddheṣu viṣayeṣu viśeṣataḥ ।
spṛhā saṃjāyate jantorapathyeṣviva rogiṇaḥ ।।

sukhotsekātparityaktaṃ prahastamupāgatam ।
prāyaḥ sarvaṃ bhavatyeva jaḍasyāmramiva priyam ।।

tasmādbhavantamutsārya pratāpanidhimāsanāt ।
kṣīṇaḥ śaśīva sthaviraḥ sa rājyaṃ bhoktumicchati ।।

cīvarodvignagātrasya varavastrābhilāṣiṇaḥ ।
jātāsya muṇḍite mūrdhni ratnāṅkamukuṭaspṛhā ।।

ratnaharmyeṣu navatāsaṃbhogavibhavodbhavam ।
tyaktvā vilāsamāyāsaṃ vanavāsaṃ saheta kaḥ ।।

mṛduśayanasukhārhā ye kathaṃ śerate te
hariṇakharakhurodyatkatkaṇṭakāsu sthalīṣu ।
madhu vidhukaraśītaṃ yairnipītaṃ kathaṃ te
vanajagajamadoṣṇaṃ tiktamambhaḥ pibanti ।।

adhunaiva tavāsannapraveśaviṣamasthiteḥ ।
ādyaṃmataṃ nyāyavidāṃ rājaputra nipātanam ।।

tasmādanāgato rājā pūrvaṃ vadhyastava prabho ।
dīpaṃ hanti pataṅgo hi na dagdhaścetsamāpatan ।।

tayoriti girā kṣipramabhūd bhūpatirākūlaḥ ।
khalameghaiḥ kaluṣatāṃ nītaṃ kasya na mānasam ।।

sa tau babhāṣe sāśaṅkaḥ krakacakrūratāṃ gataḥ ।
bādhaḥ sādhāraṇaścāyaṃ yuvayormama cāgrataḥ ।।

bhavadbhyāmeva vinayopāyaviśrāntayā dhiyā ।
vicārya kāryatātparyaṃ yad yuktaṃ tadvidhīyatām ।।

iti rājñā kṛtotsāhau tau visṛjyāśu ghātakān ।
udrāyaṇasyāgrapathaṃ vadhāyaiva babandhatuḥ ।।

so apiprajñāparitrāṇe niyoktuṃ putramudyataḥ ।
bhagavantaṃ samabhyetya vrajāmīti vyajijñapat ।।

sarvajñenābhyanujñātaḥ svakṛtaṃ bhujyatāmiti ।
karmapāśasamākṛṣṭaḥ sa yayau rorukaṃ puram ।।

tasmādvrajantaṃ nirvyājamācāramiva durjanāḥ ।
duṣṭāmātyaprayuktāste jagnurvartmani ghātakāḥ ।।

tasya cāīvarapātrādīn gṛhītvā nihatasya te ।
vyadevayan kṛtaṃ prītyau rājākāryamamātyayoḥ ।।

tataḥ pāpaprahṛṣṭābhyāṃ nṛpastābhyāṃ pradarśitam ।
dṛṣṭvā mumoha sahasā raktāktaṃ cīvaraṃ pituḥ ।।

sa labdhasaṃjñaḥ śanakaiḥ śuśoca na tathā gurum ।
yathā patitamātmānaṃ ghore narakagahvare ।।

so avadadvatsa saṃprāptaṃ phalaṃ khalajanānmayā ।
aiśvaryamadhulubdhena pāpapātamapaśyatā ।।

aho bata nirālambe ghore narakasaṃkaṭe ।
unnatārohiṇāṃ sadyaḥ pātakaṃ khalasaṃgatam ।।

kṛtametanmahatpāpaṃ duṣṭāmātyadhiyā mayā ।
patitasya mamedānīṃ pāvako api na pāvakah ।।

tulyaṃ pituścārhatasya vadhe kā mama niṣkṛtiḥ ।
pītaṃ yatra mayaikasmin pātre sadahanaṃviṣam ।।

vṛddhe pitari niḥsaṅke śamaṃ pravrajyayāśrite ।
svacitta niśitaṃ śastraṃ lobhādvyāpāritaṃ mayā ।।

yatsaṃcintitameva kampajanakaṃ śrotuṃ nayat śakyate
dṛṣṭaṃ yacca karoti śokakalanāṃ niścetanānāmapi ।
yatra krairyamapi prayāti mṛdutāṃ tīvrānutāpāgninā
tatrāpi prasaranti nirghṛṇadhiyām nistriṃśatīkṣṇāḥ kriyāḥ ।।

ityuktvā duḥkahsaṃtaptaḥ pralāpamukharānanaḥ ।
nyavārayattayoḥ kopātpraveśaṃ duṣṭamantriṇoḥ ।।

guṇāntaraṃ parijñāya bhirukaṃ hirukaṃ ca saḥ ।
ānināya prasādyāśu purāṇau sacivau pituḥ ।।

tataścintākṛśe rājñi śokāt pāṇḍuratām gate ।
svairaṃ tajjananīmetya duṣṭāmātyāvavocatām ।।

devi tvatanayaḥ śrīmān svabhāvasaralāśayaḥ ।
rājyarakṣāṃ na jānāti svajanocchedakarkaśām ।।

pitā pravrajito apyasya rājyaṃ hartumupāgataḥ ।
āvābhyāṃ praśamaṃ nītastatra kā nāma vācyatā ।।

nīcatantropapannaścet kramo ayamaśubhakramaḥ ।
rājyābhilāṣiṇo bhikṣostasyāpi sa kathaṃ kramaḥ ।।

āvāṃ pitṛvadhakridhād vāritau bhūbhujā padāt ।
svayamadyāpi śokena kiṃ mithyā pariśuṣyate ।।

sukṛtaṃ kṛtamāvābhyām prabhorduḥkhakṛśāṅgatā ।
bhavanti sarvabhāveṣu bhṛjyā evāparādhinaḥ ।।

gataṃ śocati kiṃ rājā yatkṛtaṃ kṛtameva tat ।
upekṣyate tvayā devi kasmāccintākṛśaḥ sutaḥ ।।

tābhyāmityuditaṃ śrutvā sā rājajananī śanaiḥ ।
ūce taralikā nāma tadvākyavihitādarā ।।

ānantaryamidaṃ karma dvayornarakapātakam ।
yuṣmanmatādupanataṃ rājñaḥ pūrvakṛtena vā ।।

ahaṃ tu vārayāmyasya śokaṃ pitṛvadhodbhavam ।
arhadvadhodbhavaṃ duḥkhaṃ bhavadbhyāmapi vāryatāṃ ।।

iti tau svairamādiśya sā gatvā pārthivāntikam ।
tamuvāca śucākrāntaṃ parikṣīṇamivoḍupam ।।

dharmādharmamayaṃ putra rājyaṃ rājñāṃ bahucchalam ।
pāpānāṃ śaṅkayā tasmin kiṃ śucā pariśuṣyasi ।।

piturvadhāt pratapto asi yadi nāma gurupriyaḥ ।
tatrocyate samutsṛjya lajjāṃ tvadduḥkhasaṃkaṭe ।।

svairaṃ jātastvamanyena na sa taddharmataḥ pitā ।
svecchāhārasukhāḥ putra striyo hi nirapatrpāḥ ।।

ityapriyamapi śrutvā rājā tadvacanaṃ rahaḥ ।
pitṛvaiśasapāpograduḥkhasaṃtāpamatyajat ।।

prakurvantyastādrerudayagiriṇā kleśakalanāṃ
kṣaṇāt kṣoṇīkṣmābhṛdvighaṭanavonodaṃ vidadhati ।
sṛjantyetā vahniṃ sapadi salilāttacca dahanād
aśādhyaṃ nārīṇāṃ na hi bhavati kiṃcitrtribhuvane ।।

atha so arhadvadhenaiva śalyatulyena pīḍitaḥ ।
nṛpaḥ papraccha dharmajñānniṣkṛtiṃ tasya karmaṇaḥ ।।

tatastau duṣṭasacivau tiṣyapuṣyākhyacaityayoḥ ।
mārjārapotau dhṛtvāntaḥsaktāvāmiṣaśikṣayā ।।

niṣiddhāvapi dhāṣṭaryena praviśya nṛpateḥ sabhām ।
tamūcatustīvratāpasaṃtāpapraśamārthinam ।।

deva mithyaiva bhavatā cittamāyāsyate bhṛśam ।
sarvakalyāṇā loke asmin nārhantaḥ santi te matāḥ ।।

yadi satyaṃ bhaveyuste nabhaso rājahaṃsavat ।
ṛddhimantaḥ kathaṃ teṣāmanyena vadhasaṃbhavaḥ ।।

na santi tasmādarhantaḥ kutastadvadhapātakam ।
sīmāvivādaḥ kastatr yatra grāmo na vidyate ।।

tiṣyapuṣyau gṛhapatī yāvarhatpadamāpatuḥ ।
mārjārāvantare jātau tāvevādy asvacaityayoḥ ।।

prakaṭau tau ca dṛśyete pratyakṣaṃ kasya saṃśayaḥ ।
pratyayo yadi nāstyeva svayaṃ kiṃ na nirīkṣyate ।।

ityuktvā bhūpateḥ kṛtvā khalau dolākulaṃ manaḥ ।
jagmatuḥ sahitau tena caityasaṃdarśanāya tau ।।

apūrvakautukāveśāt tatra saṃghaṭite jane ।
vilokanodyate rājño sāmātye duṣṭamantriṇau ।।

āmiṣābhyāsasaṃbaddhatiṣyapuṣyābhidhānayoḥ ।
dhūrtau cakraturāhvānaṃ śanairbālabiḍālayoḥ ।।

tau tiṣyapuṣyāvarhantau mārjārau stho yuvāṃ yadi ।
pradakṣīṇaṃ vā kriyatāṃ tena satyena caityayoḥ ।।

māṃsadānakṣaṇe tābhyāmiti vācamudīritau ।
tūrṇaṃ nirgatya mārjārau cakratustau pradakṣiṇam ।।

taddṛṣṭvā sahasāvāptapratyaye sānuge nṛpe ।
yāte durjanamāyaiva jagajjayamahīṃ yayau ।।

muṣṭau vāyuṃ dṛṣadi kamalaṃ citramākāśadeśe
jihvāgre ca pracuraracanāsṛṣṭisaṃhāralīlāḥ ।
kiṃ vā nānyat paśuśiśudhiyāṃ mohanāyendrajālaṃ
mūrtaṃ dhurtāḥ kṣaṇaparicitapratyayaṃ darśayanti ।।

niṣpratyayaparo rājā tataḥ saugatadarśane ।
āryakātyāyanasyāgre śraddhāpūjāmavārayat ।।

rājadhānyāṃ niṣiddho atha bahireva sasānugaḥ ।
vineyakṛpayā tatra tasthau śailā ca bhikṣuṇī ।।

tataḥ kadācidāyāntaṃ dṛṣṭvā kātyāyanaḥ puraḥ ।
nṛpatiṃ janasaṃpātādavamānabhayād yayau ।।

preṣitaṃ pūrvamantribhyāṃ vrajantamavalokya tam ।
duṣṭāmātyau narapatiṃ dīrghavairāvavocatām ।।

rājannamaṅgalanidhirmuṇḍo ayaṃ viśiraḥ pathi ।
dṛṣṭo adya bhikṣurasmābhirna vidmaḥ kiṃ bhaviṣyati ।।

na paśyāmi mukhaṃ rājñaḥ pāpasyeti bhaṇatyasau ।
tathā hi kṣaṇamekānte gatvā dūramitaḥ sthitaḥ ।।

śrutvaitaddurjanāmarṣāduvācānucarān nṛpaḥ ।
eṣa dūrasthitaḥ pāṃśumuṣṭibhiḥ pūryatāmiti ।।

pūryamāṇaḥ sa taiḥ pāṃśumuṣṭibhirduṣṭaceṭakaiḥ ।
divyāṃ kuṭīṃ praveśena parihārāya nirmame ।।

amarṣakopitāḥ sarpāḥ vyāghrā vā pītalohitāḥ ।
śānterāyānti mṛdutāṃ nat u bhūpaticeṭakāḥ ।।

tataḥ prayāte nṛpatau pāṃśurāśiśatāvṛtam ।
duḥkhādūcaturabhyetya hiruko bhirukaśca tam ।।

ārya kṛcchramavāpto asi rājñā krūreṇa duṣkṛtaiḥ ।
locanāni dhigasmākaṃ yairidaṃ dṛśyate pureḥ ।।

mohāndhaḥ pātakaśvabhre durjanaiḥ pātito nṛpaḥ ।
karmaṇo vayamapyasya darśanāt pāpabhāginaḥ ।।

bhūriyam bhūripāpārtā tyājyā prājyamatestava ।
duḥsahaḥ khalasaṃvāsaḥ tyāgaḥ kasya na saṃmataḥ ।।

prayāti na śamaḥ śamaṃ kṣayamupaiti naiva kṣamā
bhavanti na ca buddhayaḥ paruṣaroṣadoṣaspṛśaḥ ।
vasanti na vimānanā manasi śalyatulyāḥ satāṃ
na duṣṭajanavarjanādaparamāsti loke sukham ।।

aiśvaryaṃ guṇināmadhonipatanāyāsaprayāsapradaṃ
gāmbhīryaṃ timirākāraṃ praviśatāṃ prāṇāpahaṃ prāṇinām ।
naṣṭā sāpi nikṛṣṭduṣṭkuṭilavyālairupādeyatā
kūpasyeva khalasya nāsti tadaho doṣāliyuktaṃ yataḥ ।।

tayoriti vacaḥ śrutvā mahākātyāyano avadat ।
na nikāre api me kopaḥ karmaṇo gatirīdṛśī ।।

etāvadeva me duḥkhaṃ yanmūḍhasya mahīpateḥ ।
khalasaṃgamadoṣeṇa bhayaṃ mahadupasthitam ।।

prathame hi mahāvāyuḥ pureasya nipatiṣyati ।
dvitīye puṣpavṛṣṭiśca vastravṛṣṭistataḥ pare ।।

rūpyavṛṣṭiścaturthe ca hemavṛṣṭiśca pañcame ।
ratnavṛṣṭistataḥ ṣaṣṭhe pāṃśuvṛṣṭiśca saptame ।।

tayā sabandhurāṣṭro asay na bhaviṣyati bhūpatiḥ ।
tasmād bhavadbhyāṃ gantavyaṃ ratnānyādāya bhūyase ।।

iti tadvacanaṃ śrutvā viniścitya tatheti tau ।
hirukaḥ śyāmakaṃ putraṃ tasyopasthāpakaṃ vyadhāt ।।

bhirukaśca sutāṃ śyāmāvatīmādāya pāṇinā ।
abhyetya bhikṣukīṃ śailāṃ praṇayādidamabravīt ।।

ārye bhavatyā me kanyā ghoṣilasya gṛhaprabhoḥ ।
gṛhe samarpaṇīyeyamāsannapratipannayā ।।

evamuktvārpayitvā tāvamātyau jagmaturgṛham ।
śailāpi kanyāmādāya prayayau ghoṣilālayam ।।

tataḥ krameṇa tadabhūdyathoktaṃ bhikṣuṇā pure ।
jñānadīpavatī prajñā yathātattvaṃ hi paśyati ।।

ṣaṣṭhe ahni ratnavarṣe atha patite ratnapūritām ।
yayaturnāvamādāya tāvamātyāvalakṣitau ।।

tau dakṣiṇāṃ diśaṃ gatvā cakraturnagaradvayam ।
hiruko hirukākhyānaṃ bhirukākhyaṃ tathāparaḥ ।।

pare ahni pāṃśuvarṣeṇamahatā patatā nṛpaḥ ।
sabandhurāṣṭraḥ pralayṃ prayayau narakātithiḥ ।।

sadaṇḍimudgare rājñi yāte kilbiṣaśeṣatām ।
taṃ mantriputramādāya vyomnā kātyāyano yayau ।।

tamevānugatā prītyā nabhasā puradevatā ।
tadājñayā khavacanīkarvaṭe vidadhe sthitim ।।

bhikṣupuṇyānubhāvena bhāgyairmantrisutasya ca ।
adhiṣṭhānena devyāśca śrīmattadabahvat puram ।।

tatrātha devatā cakre caityaṃ kātyāyanasya sā ।
suravatyāṃ yadadyāpi vandante caityavandakāḥ ।।

mantrisūnumathādāya lagnaṃ cīvarakarṇike ।
lambanaṃ sa yayau vyomnā deśaṃ kātyāyanaḥ param ।।

lambate lambate ko ayamityukte vismayājjanaiḥ ।
babhūvuste janāstatra lambakā iti viśrutāḥ ।।

atrāntare divaṃ yāte tatrāputre mahīpatau ।
sa kṛtaḥ śyāmako rājā lakṣaṇajñistadājñayā ।।

gatvā bhokkānakaṃ nāma diśā kātyāyanastataḥ ।
jananyāstatra saṃśuddhāṃ vidasdhe dharmadeśanām ।।

sā dṛṣṭasatyā putrasya yaṣṭīmādāya sādaram ।
vandyamādyapi mahatī yaṣṭicaityamakārayat ।।

śrāvastīmatha sotkaṇṭhaḥ prāpya kātyāyanaḥ śanaiḥ ।
jinaṃ vilokya sānandaścakre tatpādavandanam ।।

udrāyaṇasutakathām tatra tena niveditām ।
ākarṇya bhikṣubhiḥ pṛṣṭaḥ sarvajñastānabhāṣata ।।

lubdhakah kālapāśākhyaḥ karvaṭopāntakānane ।
sakūṭāṃ mṛgabandhāya nidadhe vāgurām puraḥ ।।

yantraṃ pāśāvṛtaṃ datvā yāte tasmin yadṛśchayā ।
pratyekabuddhastaṃ deśaṃ prāpya viśrāntimāptavān ।।

tasya puṇyānubhāvena bandhaṃ na viviśurmṛgāḥ ।
na hi śuddhātmanāmagre prāpnotyakuśalaṃ janah ।।

lubdhako api tato abhyetya pāśānālokya nirmṛgān ।
pratyekabuddhaṃ krodhāndho viṣadigdheṣuṇāvadhīṭ ।।

tasya sāyakaviddhasya jvalajjvalanatejsaḥ ।
prabhāvamadbhutaṃ dṛṣṭvā pādayornipapāta saḥ ।।

akāryakaraṇodvegasaṃtāpādatha lubdhakaḥ ।
nininda śocannātmānaṃ saṃtyajya śaravāgurāḥ ।।

parinirvāṇamāptasya tasyāsthīni nidhāya saḥ ।
chatradhvajādisaṃbhāraiḥ stūpaṃ cakre sadārcitam ।।

lubdhakastena puṇyena babhūvodrāyaṇo nṛpaḥ ।
vadhāt pratyekabuddhasya bahuśo vadhamāptavān ।।

nandanāmno gṛhapatermadalekhābhidhā sutā ।
babhūva dhanadhanyādisphūtiḥ karvaṭavāsinaḥ ।।

sā kadācinmadotsiktāḥ gṛhamārjanareṇubhiḥ ।
pratyekabuddhamāyāntaṃ pathi mohādavākirat ।।

tasminneva dine tasyāściracintābhirarthitaḥ ।
varaḥ stanabharārtāyā varaṇārthī samāyayau ।।

mūdhni pratyekabuddhasya pāṃśumuṣṭiunipātanāt ।
pratyāsannavivāhāhamiti bhrātaramāha sā ।।

tatastasyāh pravādena cikṣipurvaraṇāptaye ।
mūrdhni pratyekabuddhasya rajāṃsi prauḍhakanyakāḥ ।।

guṇākārapravṛttena prayayena vimohitāḥ ।
nirvicārya pravartante viruddheṣvapi vastuṣu ।।

pravṛttapātakācāre tasmin buddhabudhābhidhau ।
nivāraṇaṃ gṛhapatī karmaṇastasya cakratuḥ ।।

saiva kanyā narapatiḥ śikhaṇḍī pāpabhāgabhūt ।
pravādakartā tadbhrātā bhikṣuḥ katyāyano apyayam ।।

jātau gṛhapatī rūḍhaduṣṭācāranivāraṇāt ।
puripatāpānnirmuktau hiruko bhirukaśca tau ।।

iti bhagavataḥ śrutvā vākyaṃ vicārya ca bhikṣavaḥ
phalapariṇatiṃ jñātvā citrām śubhāśubhakarmaṇām ।
khalajanavacastulyaṃ śatruṃ vicārasamaṃ guruṃ
sukṛtasadṛśaṃ bandhuṃ loke na kiṃcana menire ।।

iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāmudrāyaṇāvadānaṃ catvāriṃśaḥ pallavaḥ ।।

kapilāvadānam ।

yadbhūpālaviśāladānabibhavaprodbhūtapuṇyādhikaṃ
dānasyātikṛśasya satphalabharamapnotyalaṃ durgataḥ ।
śuddhasyaiva vivṛddhadharmadhavalaśraddhāsamṛdhyānvitaṃ
niḥsaṃsāravijṛmbhitaṃ taducitaṃ cittasya vittasya ca ।।

jine jetavanārāmavihāriṇi mahādhanah ।
dhīrābhidhānaḥ śrāvastyāmabhūd gṛhapatiḥ purāḥ ।।

tasya paṇḍitanāmabhūt putraḥ sukṛtapaṇḍitaḥ ।
akhaṇḍitayaśaḥpuṇyadānālaṃkāramaṇḍitaḥ ।।

sa bāla eva bhikṣūṇām rājārhairvastrabhojanaiḥ ।
śāriputrapradhānānāṃ cakārātithisatkriyām ।।

tataḥ kadācidakṣīṇādurbhikṣakṣayite jane ।
yācyayācakatulyatve piṇḍicchedo athināmabhūt ।।

bhikṣūṇāṃ saṃkaṭe tasmin kāle paramadāruṇe ।
paṇḍitaḥ sugatāhūtaḥ pratasthe jetakānanam ।।

taṃ vrajantaṃ turaṅgeṇa kāñcanādāmaśobhinam ।
ūcurviṭāḥ samabhyetya guṇotsāhāsahiṣṇavaḥ ।।

arthisārthārthanākalpavṛkṣastvaṃ dikṣu viśrutaḥ ।
śatāni pañca saṃprāptāstvāmuddiśyāśayā vayam ।।

alaṃkārāṃśukayugaṃ pratyekaṃ naḥ samīhitam ।
adhunaivāvilambena dīyatām yadi śakyate ।।

ityuktastaiḥ sadācāraḥ so avatīrya turaṅgamāt ।
sādhu pūjāṃ vidhāyaiṣāṃ dhīmān kṣaṇamacintayat ।।

bhagavantamadṛṣṭvaiva gacchāmi svagṛhaṃ yadi ।
āsannāmṛtapānasya taṃ vighnaṃ kathamutaśe ।।

adatvā priyamarthibhyo vrajāmi yadi nistrapah ।
kathaṃ karomi dānasya tāṃ svayaṃ vratakhaṇḍanām ।।

iti cintayatastasya bhittvā bhūmiṃ samudgataḥ ।
nāgarājaḥ svayaṃ śeṣaḥ prādādarthisamīhitam ।।

dattāni nāgarājena vastrāṇyābharaṇāni ca ।
sa tebhyaḥ pratipādyāśu yayau niḥśalyatāmiva ।।

te api dṛṣṭvā tadāścaryaṃ puṇyāṃ sugatabhāvanām ।
sarvārthasaṃpatsiddhīnāṃ jananīmeva menire ।।

jātacittaprasādāste tenaiva sahitāstataḥ ।
bhagavantaṃ yayurdraṣṭuṃ vinaṣṭadveṣakalmaṣāḥ ।।

bhagavantamathālokya kumāraḥ praṇatānanaḥ ।
tatpādapadmarajasā dhanyaścakre lalāṭikām ।।

hāraṃ punaścaraṇayoḥ śāstuḥ śaśikarojjvalam ।
vinyasya praṇatānagre sa tānasmai nyavedayat ।।

dharmadeśanayā teṣāṃ bhagavān jñānavajrabhṛt ।
bhittvā satkāyadṛṣṭyadriṃ srotaḥprāptiphalaṃ vyadhāt ।।

dṛṣṭasatyeṣu yāteṣu tatasteṣu praṇamya tam ।
kumāraṃpaṇḍitaṃ prītyā bhagavān svayamabhyadhāt ।।

vatsa puṇyairavāpto asi paryāptiṃ sukṛtaśriyām ।
durbhikṣesvapi bhikṣūṇāṃ kuru bhojyādhivāsanām ।।

parigraho me bhikṣūṇāṃ śatānyarhatrayodaśa ।
anye cānviṣya kṛcchrārtāḥ saṃvibhajyāstvayā pure ।।

iti śrutvā bhagavataḥ paṇḍitaḥ pramadākulaḥ ।
bhaktyā saṃghasya vidadhe yāvajjīvaṃ nimantraṇam ।।

tataḥ svagṛhamabhyetya rājārhaibhikṣusaṃmataiḥ ।
saṃbuddhapramukhaṃ saṃghaṃ sadā bhojyairapūjayat ।।

daridrānadaridrāṃśca yācyānapi ca yācakān ।
anukampyān sa vidadhe dānenānyānukampinah ।।

śeṣān kṛpaṇasaṃghātān so anviṣya karuṇāmbudhiḥ ।
ratnarāśiṃ dadau tebhyo daurgatyatimirāpaham ।।

sa ratnanikarasteṣāṃ jagāmāṅgārarāśitām ।
nṛṇāṃ bhāgyāni ratnāni maṇayaḥ prasthajātayaḥ ।।

te tamūcuḥ samabhyetya svapnadṛṣṭadhanā iva ।
ratnanāmnā tvayāsmākaṃ sa datto aṅgārasaṃcayaḥ ।।

dhanalābhena mahatā sadyaḥ prāptonnatirjanah ।
tatsaṃkṣayāt kṣaṇenaiva paribhraṣṭo na jīvati ।।

iti teṣāṃ vacaḥ śrutvā paṇḍitaḥ karuṇānidhiḥ ।
tānūce puṇyadīnānāṃ ratnānyāyāntyaratnatām ।।

yuṣmābhirna kṛtaḥ pūrvaṃ mohāt sukṛtasaṃcayaḥ ।
tenāyaṃ ratnarāśirvaḥ prayāto aṅgārasāratām ।।

ratnāni yatnanihitānyapi yānti dūraṃ puṇyakṣayādupanayanti ca bhāgyayogāt ।
vittārjanaṃ patitaśokanimittameva vittaṃ hi cittamucitaṃ sukṛtapravṛttam ।।

tasmād bhavadbhirbhojyāya bhikṣusaṃgho adhivāsyatām ।
bhogasaṃbhārasaṃpattimahaṃ saṃpādayāmi vaḥ ।।

ityuktāstena taddattavittabhojanasaṃpadā ।
te buddhapramukhaṃ saṃghaṃ dinamekamapūjayan ।।

saṃghaṃ yathāvadabhyarcya praṇīdhānamakāri taiḥ ।
m ākadācana dāridyraṃ syādasmākamiti kṣaṇam ।।

tataste paṇḍitagirā gatvā dadṝśuragrataḥ ।
tamevāṅgāranikaraṃ prayātaṃ ratnarāśitām ।।

bhavane paṇḍitasyātha kumārasya prabhavataḥ ।
vivṛtānāṃ nidhānānāṃ nirvighnaṃ śatamudyayau ।।

sa prasenajite rājñe dharmajñaḥ sthitirakṣaṇāt ।
dadau nidhānaṣaḍbhāgaṃ sa cāsyāṅgāratāmagāt ।।

kumārasyaiva sukṛtairbhogyo ayaṃ nidhisaṃcayaḥ ।
ityantarīkṣādvacanaṃ tataḥ śuśrāva bhūpatiḥ ।।

kumārasyaiva vacasā tānnidhīnnirdhitāṃ punaḥ ।
prāptāṃ vilokya sāścaryaḥ prahiṇottadgṛhaṃ nṛpaḥ ।।

tatastadakhilaṃ vittaṃ vitīrya vipulāśayaḥ ।
kumāraḥ saṃpadāṃ cakre sthitiṃ durgataveśmasu ।।

atha niḥsārasaṃsāravicāravirataspṛhaḥ ।
anityatāṃ sa saṃcintyaḥ dīraḥ pitarabravīt ।।

anujānīhi māṃ tāvat gantuṃ tāta patovanam ।
imā janmaśatocchiṣṭāḥ kliṣṭā mama vibhūtayaḥ ।।

trailokyasaṃpatsaṃprāptiryasmin vrajati bhogyatām ।
tadidaṃ sarvabhūtānāmāyurbhājanamalpakam ।।

śīte yasya karomi saṃtatamṛdusparśāṃśukaurgūhanaṃ
saṃtāpe racayāmi yasya śiśiraśrīkhaṇḍacarcārcanam ।
yasyārthe viṣaśastravahnibhujagavrātātparaṃ me bhayaṃ
prāptaḥ so apyamapāyataḥ parihṛte apyāyāti kāyaḥ kṣayam ।।

bhogādviraktaḥ pravrajyāmādāya dayitāṃ vane ।
viharāmi haran cintāṃ cintātaptasya cetasaḥ ।।

ityuktvā sa parityajya viṣayasnehabandhanam ।
kṛtābhyuopagamaḥ pitrā śāriputrāśamaṃ yayau ।।

tatra pravrajitastena pātrapāṇiḥ sacīvaraḥ ।
tasyaivānucaro bhūtvā vicacāra yatavfataḥ ।।

sa dṛṣṭvā karṣakairdhārāṃ kṣetrāt kṣetrapravartitām ।
nirdiṣṭena pathā yāntīṃ vismayādityacintayat ।।

aho vihitamārgeṇa gacchatāmapyacetasām ।
jalānāṃ karmasaṃsiddhardṛśyate natu dehinām ।।

saṃcintyeti vrajannagre dṛṣṭvā yaṣṭīkṛtaṃ śaram ।
prataptamiṣukāreṇa pradadhyau dhīmatāṃ varaḥ ।।

tāpāt praguṇatāmete yānti niścetanāḥ śarāḥ ।
na tu saṃsārasaṃtaptā api vakrāḥ śarīriṇaḥ ।।

iti dhyāyan vilokyāgre takṣṇā śakaṭacakratām ।
nītāni dṛḍharūpāṇi punaścintāṃ samāyayau ।।

aho nu ghaṭanāyogād yānti karmaṇyatāṃ kṣaṇāt ।
niścetanānid ārūṇi na cittāni śarīriṇām ।।

it caṃcintya saṃyātaḥ sudharmaniyamādaraḥ ।
vatsalaṃ pitaraṃ putra ivācāryamuvāca saḥ ।।

ārya eva prayātvadya piṇḍapātāya matkṛte ।
ahaṃ tu bhavatādiṣṭaṃ cintayāmi nijavratam ।।

ityupādhyāyamabhyarthya bhaktakṛtyāya paṇḍitaḥ ।
tasmin yāte tadādiṣṭaṃ vihārāgāramāviśat ।।

tatra yaṣṭīkṛtatanuḥ kṛtvā pratimukhīṃ smṛtim ।
sa pradadhyau nijaṃ dharmaṃ baddhaparyaṅkaniścalaḥ ।।

tasmin samādhisaṃnaddhe vasudhā sadharādharā ।
vicacālākhilāmbhodhijalaloladukūlinī ।।

śakrastaṃ dhyānanirataṃ jñātvā nirvighnasiddhaye ।
dideśa dikṣu rakṣāyai dikpālān sendubhāskarān ।।

bhagavānatha sarvajñastasya siddhimupasthitām ।
pākāt kuśalamūlānāṃ jñātvā kṣaṇamacintayat ।।

āsannārhatpadasyāsya śāriputraḥ sametya cet ।
dvāramuddhāṭayenmadhye vighna eṣa na saṃśayaḥ ।।

tasmādāgacchatastasya gatvā svayamahaṃ puraḥ ।
karomi kālahārāya nānāpraśnāśrayāḥ kathāḥ ।।

iti saṃcintya bhagavān svayaṃ taddiśamāgataḥ ।
bhikṣorāgacchatasyasya vjlambaṃ kathayākarot ।।

suraprabhāvānniḥśabde nabhogatavihaṃgame ।
loke nirvātadīpasya tulyatāṃ prāpa paṇḍitaḥ ।।

srotaḥ prāptiphalādūrdhvaṃ sakṛdāgāmyavāpya saḥ ।
anāgāmiphalaṃ prāpya tato arhatphalamāptavān ।।

tataḥ kathānte sugate prayāte nijamāśramam ।
śāriputraḥ praviśyarkamiva śiṣyaṃ vyalokayat ।।

taṃ dṛṣṭvā sahasottīrṇaṃ viśīrṇabhavabandhanam ।
siddhiṃ yugaśataprāpyāṃ tasya tām praśaśaṃsa saḥ ।।

tāṃ tasyārhatpadaprāptiṃ śrutvā jagati viśrutām ।
bhikṣubhirbhagavāṇ pṛṣṭastatkathāmabravījjinah ।।

bhagavān kāśyapaḥ pūrvaṃ vārāṇasyāṃ tathāgataḥ ।
saha bhikṣūsahasrāṇāṃ viṃśatyā puravāsibhiḥ ।।

śraddhāpraṇītaiḥ śucibhiḥ sarvabhogyairmanonugaiḥ ।
uvāsa pūjitah kaṃcit kālaṃ sattvahitodyataḥ ।।

bhikṣupūjāpare tatra vartamāne gṛhe gṛhe ।
acintyayadviniḥśvasya durgato nāma durgataḥ ।।

dhiṅ māmatīva dāridyrāt nīcaṃ niṣkuśalakriyam ।
naiko api mandabhāgyena yena bhikṣurnimantritaḥ ।।

tyājyā janasya sakalavyavahārabāhyāḥ vākyapramāṇapadasaṃdhiṣu naiva yogyāḥ ।
naṣṭakriyā vigatakārakatarkahīnāḥ śabdā ivārtharahitāḥ puruṣā bhavanti ।।

iti cintānalākrāntaṃ ninditaṃ dhanahīnataḥ ।
taṃ samāhūya ko apyetya sukṛtaprerako abhyadhāt ।।

kṣīṇārthenāpi bhavatā janmāntaraśubhāptaye ।
yathākathaṃcideko api bhikṣuḥ kiṃ na nimantritaḥ ।।

ityuktastena saṃsaktaśalyaḥ punarivāhataḥ ।
bhiokṣubhojanavaikalyāt sa bhṛdhaṃ vyathito abhavat ।।

kathaṃcitkṣḥutparikṣāmaḥ sa gatvā śreṣṭhimandiram ।
yatnena prāpa mūlyāṃśaṃ dārupāṭanakarmaṇā ।।

kṛtvā tatraiva tadbhāryā śuddhataṇḍulakhaṇḍanam ।
tadaṃśabhṛtimūlyāptaṃ bhaktyā bhartre nyavedayat ।।

samudyatasya tasyātha bhikṣubhojanasiddhaye ।
śuddhaye śuddhasattvasya śakro abhūdanusādhakah ।।

divyavarṇarasāmode bhojye śakreṇa sādhite ।
prītyā pracchannarūpeṇa bhikṣuṃ lekhe na durgataḥ ।।

vibhūtimohitairgūḍhaiḥ pūrvaṃ puranivāsibhiḥ ।
saṃghe nimantrite duḥkhāt durgato martumudyayau ।।

kṛpayā tasya bhagavān svayamabhyetya kāśyapaḥ ।
śuddhisiddhiṃ parijñāya cakre bhojyapratigraham ।।

aho ahaṃ bhavato bhojyaṃ prayacchāmīti bhūbhujā ।
prayatnāt prārtito apyarthaṃ naivāmanyata durgataḥ ।।

guṇadraviṇasaṃpūrṇaḥ syāṃ daridraprasādanaḥ ।
bhagavantamathābhyarcya praṇīdhānaṃ cakāra saḥ ।।

svāśramaṃ kāśyape yāte surendre ca divaṃ gate ।
durgatasya gṛhaṃ sarvaṃ divyaratnaipūrayat ।।

viśvakarmā tatastasya vidadhe śakraśāsanāt ।
bhavanaṃ rucirodyānaṃ ratnastambhavibhūṣitam ।।

saṃprāptavimalaiśvaryaḥ sahitaṃ sarvabhikṣubhiḥ ।
saptāhaṃ vibhavairbhogaiḥ sa kāśyapamapūjayat ।।

kṣutkṣāmāṅganamarthibhiḥ parihṛtadvāraṃ rudaddārakaṃ
gehaṃ niścalakajjalānyapi sthalīkoṇasvananmakṣikam ।
cullīsuptabiḍālabālamaparaṃ yasyābhavadrauravaṃ
śrīstasyaiva nṛpaspṛhāspadatayāścaryaṃ na kasya svayam ।।

tena dānaprabhāveṇa sudhāśuddhena durgataḥ ।
janmāntare paṇḍitatāmavāpyārhattvamāgataḥ ।।

iti paṇḍitapūrvajanmavṛttaṃ kathitaṃ sarvavidā guṇādareṇa ।
avadhārya viśuddhadānapuṇyaṃ kuśalārhaṃ praśaśaṃsa bhikṣusaṃghaḥ ।।

iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ kapilāvadānaṃ nāmaikacatvāriṃśaḥ pallavaḥ ।।

kanakavarṇāvadānam ।

sattvena sūryarucayastamasi sphuranti dharmeṇa ratnanicayā nabhasaḥ tapanti ।
dhairyeṇa sarvavipadaḥ praśamaṃ vrajanti dānena bhogasubhagāḥ kakubho bhavanti ।।

bhagavān sugataḥ pūrvaṃ śrāvastyāṃ jetakānane ।
kuśalānāṃ prapānnānāṃ vidadhe dharmadeśanām ।।

pūrvakalpāntarajane vatsarāṣṭāyutāyuṣi ।
śrīmān kanakavarṇākhyo babhūva pṛthivīpatiḥ ।।

kanakākhyā purī tasya śakrasyevāmarāvatī ।
sarvalokeśvarasyāpi vasatirvallabhābhavat ।।

nāyakārhaṃ yaśaḥśubhraṃ cāruvṛttaguṇocitam ।
hṝdaye yaḥ prajākāryaṃ muktāhāramivāvahat ।।

prajākarmavipākena pure paramadāruṇā ।
avṛṣṭirabhavat tatra sarvabhūtabhayapradā ।।

sā dhairyahāriṇī sarvalokasaṃtāpakāriṇī ।
avṛṣṭiḥ prayayau bhūbhṛnmānasāyāsahetutām ।।

kuṇṭhasarvapratīkāraḥ sa cintāstimitaṃ puraḥ ।
uvāca suciraṃ dhyātvā pradhānāmātyamaṇḍalam ।।

avarṣopanipāto ayaṃ prajānāṃ niṣpratikriyaḥ ।
karoti me yatnakṛtaṃ niṣphalaṃ paripālanam ।।

nivṛttavarṣāḥ kakubho bhavantyabhrāśca svacchakāḥ ।
pravṛttabāṣpavarṣāśca prajāḥ pāpena bhūbhujām ।।

trāṇaṃ mahābhayādrājā prajānāṃ na karoti yaḥ ।
tasya spaṣṭaṃ naṭasyeva kirīṭamukuṭagrahaḥ ।।
tadā kṝtayugaṃ loke yadā rājā prajāhitaḥ ।।
durbhikṣakṣayitāḥ pṛthutarakleśāvalīvihvalāḥ ।
hāhākāraviśṛṅkhalāḥ khalatarairatyarditā vallabhaiḥ
śocantyaḥ pralayaṃ prayāntaśaraṇāḥ pāpairnṛpāṇāṃ prajāḥ ।।

tasmātsamastakoṣeṇa rakṣaṇīyā mayā prajāḥ ।
rājñāṃ prajāparitrāṇapuṇyaṃ ratnamayo nidhiḥ ।।

ityuktvā sarvalokasya saṃcintya koṣṭhakoṣayoḥ ।
sa nināya nijaṃ sarvaṃ sadā bhogyopabhogyatām ।।

tataḥ kālena tasyogradurbhikṣeṇānnasaṃcayaḥ ।
yayau mahāvyayādekapuruṣāśanaśeṣatām ।।

tasminnavasare vyomnā samabhyetya raviprabhaḥ ।
pratyekabuddhastasyātha vidadhe bhojanārthanām ।।

niyame saṃśaye tasminnātmanaḥ prāṇadhāraṇe ।
nirvikalpya sa tatasrvaṃ dadau tasmai prasannadhīḥ ।।

svaprāṇavṛttiṃ tenāsau kṛtvātithyaprasādinā ।
prayayau nabahsā tasya prasaṃśan sattvaśīaltām ।।

athodyayau vyaomamahādvipasya nīlālimāleva sadambulekhā ।
meghāvalī paścimadikpralambā kapolakālāgurumañjarīva ।।

tataḥ samastaṃ gaganāntarālamutphullanīlotpalakānanābham ।
ācchādyamānaṃ sarasairbabhāse bhṛṅgapravandhauriva meghasaṃghaiḥ ।।

tataḥ papātākhilabhojyavṛṣṭiriṣṭā prajānāṃ bhuvi sapta rātrīḥ ।
dhānyādivṛṣṭistadanantaraṃ ca ratnadivṛṣṭiśca tataḥ krameṇa ।।

iti sa kanakavarṇaḥ kṣmāpatirbhūpatīnāṃ mukuṭamaṇirivoccairbhrājamānaḥ prajānām ।
akṛta sukṛtasaṃpatprīṇitah prāṇarakṣāṃ prabhavati hi parārthe sajjanānāṃ prabhāvaḥ ।।

bhūpatiḥ kanakavarṇa eṣa yaḥ so ahameva vapuṣātmanādhunā ।
ityudīrya bhagavān jinaḥ satāṃ dhīmatāṃ vyadhita dharmadeśanām ।।

iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ kanakavarṇāvadānaṃ nāma dvicatvāriṃśaḥ pallavaḥ ।।

hiraṇyapāṇyavadānam ।

sarvopakārapraṇayī prabhāvaḥ sarvopajīvyā mahatī vibhūtiḥ ।
puṇyāṅkurārhasya phalaṃ viśālapalārhametat prathamaṃ hi puṣpam ।।

jine jetavanārāmavihārābhigate purā ।
śrāvastyāṃ devasenākhyaḥ śrīmānāsīdgṛhādhipaḥ ।।

hiraṇṃyapāṇistasyābhūtputraḥ satputramāninaḥ ।
yasya hemamayaṃ jātaṃ pāṇidvitayamadbhutam ।।

rūpyalakṣadvayaṃ tasya prātaḥ prātaḥ karadvaye ।
prādurāsītsa tenābhūdarthināṃ kalpapādapaḥ ।।

tasya vyaktavivekena paripākena bhūyasā ।
kāle kuśalamūlānāṃ jine bhaktirajāyata ।।

atha jetavana gatvā bahgavantaṃ tathāgatam ।
sa dṛṣṭvā vidadhe tasya sānandaḥ pādavandanam ।।

bhagavānapi saṃṣāratāpapraśamacandikām ।
sudhāsakhīṃ dideśāsmai dṛśaṃ kuśalavṛtikām ।।

sa śāsturdarśanenaiva saṃmohatimitojjhita ।
babhāse suryakiraṇaprabuddhakamalopamaḥ ।।

bhagavān vidadhe tasya tataḥ saddharmadeśanām ।
yayā dharmamayaṃ cakṣurakṣuṇṇālokamudyayau ।।

prākpuṇyapariṇāmena jātavairāgyavāsanaḥ ।
praṇamya vimalaprajñaḥ sa sarvajñamabhāṣataḥ ।।

śaraṇya śaraṇāptasya bhagavan bhavahāriṇī ।
aśeṣakleśanāśāya pravrajyā me vidhīyatām ।।

capalaṃ prāṇināmāyuṣtato api navayauvanam ।
vidyudvilāsacapalāstato apyetā vibhūtayaḥ ।।

iti tasya bruvāṇasya sugatānugrahoditā ।
papāta vitarajasaḥ pravrajyā vapuṣi svayam ।।

raktacīvarasuvyaktāṃ bibhrāṇaḥ sa viraktatām ।
pātragraheṇa tatyāja punaḥ saṃsārapātratām ।।

tasya tāmadbhutāṃ siddhiṃ pratyakṣaṃ vīkṣyaṃ bhikṣavaḥ ।
tatpūrvavṛttaṃ papracchurbhagavantaṃ sa cābravīt ।।

vārāṇasyāṃ purā rājā kṛkirnāma tathāgate ।
kāśyapākhye bhagavati prayāti parinirvṛtim ।।

śarīramasya samkṛtya stūpaṃ ratnamayaṃ vyadhāt ।
svargāvagāhanaprauḍhaṃ mūrtaṃ puṇyamivonnatam ।।

tasminnāropyamāṇāyāṃ yaṣṭayāṃ pūjāparigrahe ।
kitavaḥ kandalo nāma nidadhe rūpakadvayam ।।

cittaprasādaśuddhena tena puṇyena bhūyasā ।
hiraṇyapāṇiḥ prāpto adya mahatāṃ spṝhaṇīyatām ।।

bhavati vibhavastyāgodāraḥ samagraguṇo bhuvi
prasaratiḥ yaśaḥ śuklaṃ loke sudhāṃśusahodaram ।
pariṇatipade puṇyaṃ dhatte yadalpamanalpatāṃ
vimalamanasaḥ śraddhāśuddhaṃ tadeva vijṛmbhitam ।।

iti prabhāvaṃ kathitaṃ jinena puṇyānubhāvasya hiraṇyapāṇeḥ ।
śrutvaiva harṣādaravismayānāṃ sa bhikṣusaṃghaḥ praṇayī babhūva ।।

iti kṣemandraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ hiraṇyapāṇyavadānaṃ tricatvāriṃśaḥ pallavaḥ ।।

ajātaśatrupitṛdrohāvadānam ।

durjanaduḥsahaviṣadharabhīṣaṇataratimirapatitānām ।
ālambanajananaṃ bhavabhayaharaṇaṃ jinasmaraṇam ।।

pure rājagṛhābhikhye bhagavān bhūbhṛtaḥ purā ।
kaṭake gṛdhrakūṭasya vijahāra tathāgataḥ ।।

tasminnavasare rājā bimbisāraḥ sutapriyaḥ ।
ajātaśatruṇā tatra putreṇa krūrakāriṇā ।।

suhṛdaḥ pāvakasyeva devadattasya saṃmatam ।
ghorāndhabandhanāgāraṃ niḥsaṃcāraṃ praveśitaḥ ।।

patnyā praveśitaṃ tasya bandhane gūḍhabhojanam ।
jñātvā sa tatkṣayākāṅkṣī kṣutkṣāmasya nyavārayat ।।

rūkṣaḥ kṛśo atimalinaḥ so abhavat pṛthivīpatiḥ ।
akālakālameghārtaḥ kṛṣṇapakṣa ivoḍupaḥ ।।

saṃkīrṇavāsasaṃtāpātprāyaḥ peśalacetasām ।
karotyāliṅganaṃ prauḍhā gāḍhapraṇayinī vipat ।।

sa samuddhiśya śokārtaḥ sugatādhyuṣitāṃ diśam ।
kṛtāñjalirnataśirāḥ kṣāmasvaramabhāṣata ।।

nāmastubhyaṃ bhagavate mahārhāya mahārhate ।
dīnoddharaṇasaṃnaddhasamyaksaṃbodhibodhicetase ।।

namaste ghorasaṃsāramakarākarasetave ।
jināya janatājanmakleśapraśamahetave ।।

namo nityaprabuddhāya sarvasattvaikabandhave ।
viśuddhadhānme buddhāya karuṇāmṛtasindhave ।।

iti bhaktisudhāṃ śiktvā sugataśravaṇocitām ।
puṇyapuṣpaprasavinīṃ sa cakre stutimañjarīm ।।

sarvajñastasya vijñāya kāyakleśaśamayīṃ daśām ।
bandhanāgāravivarālokairāpyāyanam vyadhāt ।।

ajātaśatrustadvṛttaṃ jñātvā śaṅkākulaḥ pituḥ ।
nyavārayadbandhagṛhe susūkṣmavivarāṇyapi ।।

tatastasya tadādeśāt cakrurbandhanarakṣiṇaḥ ।
kṣureṇa gāḍhabaddhasya pādayostadvikartanam ।।

sa tīvravaiśasakleśavyathitah pārthivaḥ param ।
namo buddhāya buddhāyetyārtasaṃkrandanaṃ vyadhāt ।।

bhagavānatha sarvajñaḥ puraḥ pratyakṣatāṃ gataḥ ।
śakradattāsanāsīnaḥ kāruṇyāttamabhāṣataḥ ।।

rājan kiṃ kriyate krūrakarmaṇāṃ gatirīdṛśī ।
śubhāśubhasamudbhūtaṃ na bhuktaṃ kṣiyate phalam ।।

rāgadveṣaviṣāsakte nānāvyasanaduḥsahe ।
evaṃvidhaiva niḥsāre saṃsāre duḥkhasāratā ।।

saṃkleśakalile kāle vipatsaṃpadvisaṃkaṭe ।
dhairyameva paritrāṇaṃ vairāgyaṃ ca nirākulam ।।

saṃsāraghoragahanāntaravardhamānaiḥ duḥkhānalavyatikaraprasṛtairasiktāḥ ।
dhūmodgamairiva punaḥ sukṛtocitānāṃ bāṣpāmbubindukalilā na dṛśo bhavanti ।।

bhajasva dhairyaṃ duḥkhe asmin bhogāśāṃ tyaja bhūpate ।
pariṇāmavirodhinyaḥ sarvāḥ saṃsāravṛttayaḥ ।।

adhunaiva tavāsannā dehātte kuśalasthitiḥ ।
ityuktvā taṃ samāśvasya bhagavān svapadaṃ yayau ।।

bimbisāro api dehānte tasminneva kṣaṇe divi ।
abhūjjinarṣabho nāma śrīmān vaiśravaṇātmajaḥ ।।

ajātaśatrurjanakaṃ jñātvā vigatajīvitam ।
śarīramasya satkṛtya nininda nijaduṣkṛtam ।।

tasyātitīvrapāpārtaṃ cittaṃ durvṛttadūṣitam ।
paścāttāpāgnipatanaṃ prāyaścittamivākarot ।।

so avadadbata saṃmohādaiśvaryamadalubdhadhīḥ ।
durvṛttapātakaśvabhre patito ahamadhomukhaḥ ।।

śrutaprajñādaridrāṇāṃ nijanidrāsukhāpahā ।
cintā dahati gātrāṇi khalamantrānuvartinām ।।

patitasyāvasannasya pāpapaṅke pramādinah ।
anālambasya saṃtrāṇaṃ jinasaṃsmaraṇaṃ mama ।।

iti saṃcintya suciraṃ sa gatvā sugatāntikam ।
jugupsamānaḥ kukṛtātparaṃ saṃkocamāyayau ।।

tatrāpavitramātmānaṃ manyamānaḥ sapatrapaḥ ।
praṇanāma jinaṃ dūrāt pāpasparśabhayādiva ।।

sāśrunetraḥ paritrāṇaṃ sa sarvajñaṃ vyajijñapat ।
sakampaḥ kāyasaṃsaktaṃ vidhunvanniva duṣkṛtam ।।

bhagavan kṛtapāyo ahamāsannanarakānalaḥ ।
uttaptaḥ karuṇāsindhuṃ tvāmeva śaraṇaṃ gataḥ ।।
māmiyaṃ śoṇaparyantā dṛṣṭiste puṣkaraprabhā ।।
khalamantrapravṛttena durvṛttena pramādinā ।
mayā vibhavalubdhena pāpena nihataḥ pitā ।।

iti pralāpinastasya vacaḥ śrutvā tathāgataḥ ।
sasarha tatpāparajaḥśuddhyai puṇyasarasvatīm ।।

rājanna cintitaḥ pāpaḥ khaleneva svakarmaṇā ।
preritastvaṃ pitṛvadhe patitaḥ pāpasaṃkaṭe ।।

duḥkhaṃ tattena bhoktavyaṃ prāptavyaṃ kilbiṣaṃ tvayā ।
tava tasya ca bhūpāla tulyaiṣā bhavitavyatā ।।

nijakaṇṭhasamutkīrṇāṃ lalāṭapaṭavartinī ।
śilāśakalalekheva niścalā niyatirnṛṇām ।।

kurvatā kaluṣaṃ karma khalapreraṇayā tvayā ।
pratyāsannāmṛtaśreyaḥ svahastena tiraskṛtam ।।

adyāpi yadi te pāpaṃ hantuṃ prāptuṃ ca saṃpadam ।
vāñchāsti tatkuru matiṃ puṇye pāpaśamātmani ।।

dīpavṛttyā sukhaṃ sūte jīvayatyujjvalaṃ yaśah ।
amṛtasya prakāro ayaṃ suvṛttaḥ satsamāgamaḥ ।।

paścāttāpāgnupātena sādhunā saṃgamena ca ।
saṃkīrtanena dānena pāpaṃ naśyati dehinām ।।

pātraṃ pavitrayati naiva guṇān kṣiṇoti snehaṃ na saṃharati naiva malaṃ prasūte ।
doṣāvasānaruciraścalatāṃ na dhatte satsaṃgamaḥ sukṛtasadmani ko api dīpaḥ ।।

guṇigaṇavipaddīkṣādakṣaḥ kṣapākṣaṇasaṃnibhaḥ
sakalanayanavyāpārāṇāṃ janeṣu nirodhakaḥ ।
asamaviṣamāyāsāvāsaḥ prakāśaparikṣayāt
sṛjati hi mahāmohāgdāḍhaṃ tamaḥ khalasaṃgamaḥ ।।

pratyekabuddhastvaṃ rājan kālena kṣīṇakilbiṣaḥ ।
bhaviṣyasi vivekena kṛtālekaḥ śanaiḥ śanaiḥ ।।

iti tasya dayāśvāsaṃ cakāra bahgavān jinah ।
patiteṣvadhikaṃ santaḥ karuṇāsnigdhalocanāḥ ।।

tataḥ praṇamya sugataṃ prayātaḥ svapadaṃ nṛpaḥ ।
mahataḥ pāpabhārasya viveda laghutāmiva ।।

tasmin prayāte sarvajñaḥ pṛṣṭastatkarma kautukāt ।
bhikṣubhiḥ kṣitipālasya pūrvavṛttamabhāṣata ।।

vārāṇasyāṃ nirāyāsavilāsavyavasāyinaḥ ।
catvāraḥ śreṣṭhitanayā babhūvuḥ śrīviśṛṅkhalāḥ ।।

te kadācit sukhakṣībā mithaḥ kalikathāsthitāḥ ।
pratyekabuddhamāyāntaṃ dadṛśuryauvanoddhatāḥ ।।

taṃ dṛṣṭvā jātavidveṣāḥ śamasaṃyamanindakāḥ ।
jyeṣṭhaḥ sundarako nāma bhrātṝn provāca sasmitaḥ ।।

ayaṃ cīvarapātrāṅkaḥ pānena gatajīvitaḥ ।
kṣibo vidhīyate bhikṣurityayaṃ me manorathaḥ ।।

ityukte cāpalāt tena dvitīyaḥ kundarābhidhaḥ ।
uvāca bhikṣuṃ kṣiptvemaṃ hantumicchāmyahaṃ jale ।।

tatastṛtīyo apyavadat pāpaḥ sundarakābhidhaḥ ।
eṣa bhikṣurvaraṃ tasyāṃ vīthyāṃ nikṣipyate javāt ।।

caturtho apyavadat krūramatiḥ kandarakābhidhaḥ ।
bhikṣoḥ kṣureṇa kriyate niścarma caraṇadvayam ।।

iti teṣāṃ bruvāṇānāṃ kaluṣo abhūnmanorathaḥ ।
yena janmāntare prāpuste svecchāsadṛśaṃ phalam ।।

dhanaṃ paśyati lobhāndhaḥ kridhāndhaḥ śatrumeva ca ।
kāmāndhah kāminīmeva darpāndhastu na kiṃcana ।।

dhanidbhūtavikārāṇāṃ prayātyaniyatātmanām ।
madamandavicārāṇāmānandaḥ kleśabandhatām ।।

krudhyantyakāraṇamakāraṇamutpatanti snihyantyakāraṇamakāraṇamāmananti ।
mohāhatāḥ khalu hitāhitanirvicārāḥ tṛptāḥ paraṃ nṛpaśavaḥ samadā bhavanti ।।

jyeṣṭhaḥ śreṣṭhisutaḥ pāpātsa evāparajanmani ।
śāriryānābhidhaḥ śākyaḥ pītvā madyaṃ vyapadyata ।।

dvitīyo api mahānnāma śākyastoye kṣayaṃ gataḥ ।
tṛtīyaśca svaputreṇa vyasto rājā prasenajit ।।

bimbisāraścaturtho asau dhṛtaḥ putreṇa bandhane ।
prayuktaṃ dhanavatkarma bhujyate hi savṛddhikam ।।

mohāhatairiha hi sadbhirasadbhireṣāṃ niḥśarma karma sahasaiva viḍambyate yat । bāṣpāmbupūrṇanayanairanayopanītaḥmastokaśokavivaśairanubhūyate atra ।।

sugatakathitametat pūrvajanmapravṛttaṃ viṣaviṣamavipākaṃ bimbisārasya vṛttam ।
vibudhasadasi bhikṣuḥ spaṣṭamākarṇya mene vyasanaśatanimittaṃ dūṣitaṃ cittameva ।।

iti kṣemendraviracitāyām bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāmajātaśatrupitṛdrodāvadānaṃ nāma catuścatvāriṃśaḥ pallavaḥ ।।

kṛtajñāvadānam ।

andhīkṛto api svadṛśā tamasā khalena lakṣmīvihāravirahe vinipātito api ।
kaṣṭāṃ daśāmiva niśāmativāhya padmaḥ svāmeva saṃpadamupaiti punarguṇāḍhyaḥ ।।

śrāvastyāṃ sugate jetavanodyānavihāriṇi ।
devadattaḥ paridveṣavyādhivyāpto vyacintayat ।।

tulyaḥ samāno me bhrātā manuṣyaḥ śākyavaṃśajaḥ ।
prāptaḥ puṇyaprabhāveṇa trijagatpūjyatāṃ jinaḥ ।।

jīvitodvṛttaye tasmāt taysya yatnaṃ karomyaham ।
na hyanastaṃgate bhānau paratejaḥ prakāśate ।।

vijñānenānubhāvena vidyayā tapasā śriyā ।
paraprakarṣaṃ sahate na hi mānonnataṃ manah ।।

viṣaṃ nijanakhāgreṣu dhṛtvā tasya praṇāmakṛt ।
saṃcārayāmi vapuṣi nediṣṭhaḥ pādapīḍaṇaiḥ ।।

iti saṃcintya kaluṣaṃ vidveṣavivaśaḥ khalah ।
sa tiṣyapramukhānetya bāndhavānidamabhyadhāt ।।

krūraḥ kṛtāpakāro ahaṃ sugatasyādya pādayoḥ ।
saralasya prasādāya ptāmi gurupātakah ।।

iti bruvāṇastaiḥ sarvaiḥ sudattānumataiḥ saha ।
jinaṃ jetavanāsīnaṃ draṣṭuṃ duṣṭamatiryayau ।।

bhagavantaṃ vilokyābhūttatra yāvatsa sarvaśaḥ ।
tāvaddagdho ahamityuccairutkṣiptacaraṇo avadat ।।

huiṃsāsaṃkalpapāpena vrajreṇeva samāhataḥ ।
saśarīraṃ kṣaṇe tasmin narakāgnau papāta saḥ ।।

sarvajñaḥ sahasā dṛṣṭvā taṃ ghoranarake cyutam ।
uvāca śrutatadvṛttavismitāṃ bhikṣusaṃsadam ।।

eṣa kilbiṣadoṣeṇa patitaḥ kleśasaṃkaṭe ।
tīvram hi timira sūte sarvathā malinaṃ manaḥ ।।

nagaryāmatighoṣāyāṃ ratisomasya bhūpateḥ ।
kṛtajñaścākṛtajñaśca purā putrau babhūvatuḥ ।।

kṛtajñaḥ kṛpayārthibhyaḥ kalpavṛkṣaḥ ivāniśam ।
nijaṃ vimucya pradadau ratnābharaṇasaṃcayam ।।

avibhaktaṃ piturdravyaṃ sarvaṃ sādhāraṇaṃ tayoḥ ।
vadannityakṛtajñpo api ten adattaḥ jahat tat ।।

tataḥ ślādhyāya vacasā matighoṣābhodho nṛpaḥ ।
janakalyānikāṃ nāma kṛtajñāya sutāṃ dadau ।।

svayamevārjitaṃ vittaṃ dātuṃ jātamanorathaḥ ।
āruroham pravahaṇaṃ kṛtajño atha mahodadhau ।।

ratnārjanodyataṃ yāntaṃ taṃ dveṣaspardhitādaraḥ ।
tamevānuyayau lobhādakṛtajño api durjanaḥ ।।

saṃpūrṇaṃ vaṇijāṃ sārthaiḥ tataḥ pravahaṇaṃ śanaiḥ ।
ānukūlyena matutāmavāpa dvīpamīpsitam ।।

tasmin pratinivṛtte atha svadeśaṃ gantumudyate ।
ratnarāśibhirāpūrṇasaṃklape svadeśaṃ gantumudyate ।।

kṛtajñaḥ pṛthivīmūlyaṃ ratnānāṃ śatapaḥñcakam ।
ādāya granthipaṭṭena babandhāṃśukapallave ।।

ratnabhārapariśrāntaṃ tataḥ pravahaṇaṃ mahat ।
abhajyata mahāvātairaiśvaryamiva durnayaiḥ ।।

tataḥ phalakavāhastaṃ kṛtajñaḥ prāptajīvitaḥ ।
akṛtajñaṃ nimajjantaṃ pṛṣṭhena samatārayat ।।

tāritaḥ kṛpayā bhrātrā sa ghoramakarākarāt ।
apaśyadañcale tasya ruciraṃ ratnasaṃcayam ।।

sa tasya ratnalobhena dveṣena ca vaśīkṛtaḥ ।
samudratīre śrāntasya bhrāturdrohamacintayat ।।

tasya nidrānilīnasya śastreṇotpāṭya locanam ।
gṛhītvā ratnanicayaṃ kṛtaghnaḥ sa yayau javāt ।।

krūreṇāṅgīkṛtastena rāhuṇeva divākara ।
lokopakāravihato duḥkhitaḥ so apyacintayat ।।

adhunārthipradāne arthe vyarthībhūte manorathe ।
kiṃ mamāndhasya vandhyena jīvitena prayojanam ।।

aprāptaviṣayāḥ prāṇā na prayānti yadi kṣayam ।
tadasaṃgatayo yogāḥ kleśaynti kṣyakṣamāḥ ।।

kṣaṇe dhane jane dveṣamānavaikalyavihvale ।
pūjye puṃsāṃ samenaiva śeṣasya ca yaśovyayaḥ ।।

iti saṃcintya sa śanairvrajansārthena tāritaḥ ।
avāpa nagaropāntaṃ matighoṣasya bhūpateḥ ।।

gopālabhavane tatra sa kaṃcitkālamāsthitaḥ ।
udyānayātrāgatayā rājaputryā vilokitah ।।

taṃ dṛṣṭvāndhamapi vyaktarājalakśaṇalakṣitam ।
prāgjanmapremabandhena sābhilāṣā babhūva sā ।।

tataḥ svayaṃvaravidhiṃ sā kṛtvā śāsanātpituḥ ।
rājñāṃ madhye ca mānyānāṃ vavre vigatalocanam ।।

bhūmipālān parityajya vṛto andhaḥ pāpayā tvayā ।
uktveti pitrā kopena nirastā śuśubhe na sā ।।

udyāne sā nidhāyāndhaṃ yatnenāhṛtya bhojanam ।
sadā tasmai dadau premapraṇayopacitādarā ।।

kadācittāṃ cirāyātāmāhārāvasare gate ।
uvāca rājatanayaḥ paraṃ mlānānanaḥ kṣudhā ।।

asamīkṣitakāriṇā tvayā kevalacāpalāt ।
vṛto ahamandhaḥ saṃtyajya nṛpān vipulalocanān ।।

paścāttāpena nūnaṃ tvaṃ mayi paryuṣitādarā ।
adhunā tāṇḍavaṃ premṇah pradarśayitumudyatā ।।

andhasaṃdarśanodvignā surūpālokanonmukhī ।
āhārakāle atikrānte cireṇeha tvamāgatā ।।

ityuktvā paruṣaṃ tena kampamānā lateva sā ।
uvāca guñjanmadhupaśreṇīmadhuravādinī ।।

nātha mithyaiva me śankāṃ na kopātkartumarhasi ।
vāgbāṇapātaṃ sahate na cetaḥ prītipeśalaṃ ।।

tvāmeca devatāṃ jāne yadyahaṃ śuddhamānas ā ।
tena satyena sālokamekaṃ nayanamastu te ।।

ityukte sattvaśālinyā tayā tasyāśu locanam ।
utphullakamalākāramekaṃ vimalatām yayau ।।

tasyāh satyaprabhāveṇa saṃjātapṛthuvismayah ।
satyapratyayasotsāhaṃ kṛtajñastāmabhāṣata ।।

bhrātrā tenākṛtajñna pāṭite locanadvaye ।
tasmin vikāro vairaṃ vā na nikāro apyabhūnmama ।।

svacchaṃ tenāstu satyena dvitīyamapi locanam ।
ityukte takṣaṇenāsya spaṣṭaṃ cakṣuralakṣyata ।।

ataḥ kathitavṛttāntaṃ kṛtajñamucitaṃ patim ।
prahṛṣṭā janakalyāṇī gatvā pitre nyavedayat ।।

pūjitaḥ śvaśureṇātha sa ratnagajavājibhiḥ ।
śriyeva kāntayā sārdhaṃ jagāma nagaraṃ pituḥ ।।

sa tatra pitrā hṛṣṭena caraṇālīnaśekharaḥ ।
janānurāgasubhage yaivarājye pade dhṛtaḥ ।।

akṛtajño api nirlajjastaṃ prasādayituṃ śaṭhaḥ ।
vicintya pādapatane tasya drohaṃ samāyayau ।।

unmanā hantumāyātaḥ sa taṃ kuṭulaceṣṭitaḥ ।
hāhā dagdho asmi dagdho asmītyuktvaiva narake apatat ।।

sa eva devadatto asau kṛtajño apyahameva ca ।
janmāntarānubandhena dveṣo asya na nivartate ।।

sarvajñabhāṣitamiti pracuropakāraṃ taddevadattacaritaṃ paritāpakāri ।
janmāntaropacitapātakasaṃnibaddhaṃ śrutvā babhūva vimanā iva bhikṣusaṃghaḥ ।।

iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ kṛtajñāvadānaṃ pañcacatvāriṃśaḥ pallavaḥ ।।

śālistambāvadānam ।

dānaikatānamanasāṃ pṛthusattvabhājāmutsāhamānaguṇabhogavibhūṭipūtaḥ ।
prākuṇyasaṃcayamayaḥ kuśalabhidhānaḥ kāle phalatyavikalaḥ kila kalpavṛkṣaḥ ।।

kosalendrasya bhūbhartuḥ śrāvastyām bhagavān purā ।
vijahāra va rodyāne saha bhikṣagaṇairjinaḥ ।।

ādimadhyāṇtakalyāṇaṃ bahvābhibhavasādhakam ।
saṃdideśa sa saddharmaṃ trailokyakuśalodyataḥ ।।

atrāṇtare nāgarājaputrāḥ sāgaravāsinah ।
catvāraḥ sugatodīrṇaṃ saddharmaṃ paramāmṛtam ।।

abhiratyākhyayā svasrā preritāḥ śrotumāgatāḥ ।
te balātibala-śvāsa-mahāśvāsābhidhāḥ samam ।।

krakucchandasya sudhiyaḥ kāle bhagavataḥ pura ।
kanakākhyasya ca muneḥ kāśyapasya ca yatnataḥ ।।

ājagmuḥ śrīsukhāsaktāḥ śrotumaprārthitā api ।
tatpuṇyapariṇāmena prāptāḥ śākyamuneḥ purā ।।

teṣu praṇamya śāstāraṃ caraṇālīnamauliṣu ।
vidhāya mānuṣaṃ rūpamupaviṣṭeṣu parṣadi ।।

saddharmamāyayau śrotuṃ kosalendraḥ prasenajit ।
lakṣmīmandasmitacchāyaṃ nivārya cchatracāmaram ।।

śāstuḥ pādapraṇāmāya viśatastasya saṃsadi ।
avakāśaṃ natāścakruḥ sarve nṛpatigauravāt ।।

tasyābhinandyamānasya varṣāśramagurornṛbhiḥ ।
nāgarājasutāścakrurnāvakāśaṃ na satkṛtam ।।

tasyābhinandyamānasya varṇāśramagurornṛbhiḥ ।
nāgarājasutāścakrurnāvakāśaṃ na satkṛtam ।।

sa saṃjñayā samādiśya nijaṃ parijanaṃ puraḥ ।
gamane nigraham teṣāṃ nirvikāra ivābhavat ।।

bhagavānapi sarvajñastasya jñātvā ca niścayam ।
dharmopadeśaparyante provāca racitasmitaḥ ।।

na vidveṣarajaḥpūrṇamanomalinadarpaṇe ।
bhāti dharmopadeśasya pratibimbapratigrahaḥ ।।

avihitasamatānāṃ kopamohāhatānāṃ kṛśamapi kuśalāṃśaṃ nopadeśaḥ karoti ।
na hi vahutaradoṣe śuddhihīne śarīre vrajati hatamatīnām bheṣajaṃ bheṣajatvama ।।

iti yuktaṃ bhagavatā hitamuktaṃ mahīpatiḥ ।
śrutvāpi na ca tatyāja nāgeṣu vimanaskatām ।।

bhagavantaṃ praṇamyātha prayāte svapadaṃ nṛpe ।
nāgāstatsainikābaddhamārge vyomapathā yayuḥ ।।

te vicintya svabhavane kṣmāsaṃkṣayakṛtakṣaṇāḥ ।
ghoranirghātameghaughagrastalokāḥ samāyayuḥ ।।

teṣāṃ vyavasitaṃ jñātvā sarvajñaḥ pakṣapātinām ।
rakṣḥākṣamaṃ kṣitipatermaudgalyāyanamādiśat ।।

atha nāgagaṇotsṛṣṭā vajravṛṣṭirmahīpatau ।
bhūbhartustatprabhāveṇa prayayau puṣpavṛṣṭitām ।।

śastrāstravṛṣṭirnibiḍakṣiptā tairatha duḥsahā ।
maudgalyāyanasaṃkalpādyayau rājārhabhojyatām ।।

tatprabhāvātprayāteṣu bhognotsāheṣu bhogiṣu ।
gatvā vavande sugataṃ nṛpatirvītaviplavaḥ ।।

sa maudgalyāyanasyārghyamucitaṃ bhogasaṃpadā ।
bhaktisaṃskārasubhagaṃ vidadhe jianśāsanāt ।।

tataḥ svargocitām bhikṣurvibhūtiṃ vīkṣya bhūpateḥ ।
papraccha kautukavaśāt sarvajñaṃ caritāñjaliḥ ।।

bhagavan kasya puṇyasya prabhāveṇa prasenajit ।
sarvairvirājitaṃ bhogaiḥ prājyaṃ rājyamavāptavān ।।

ikṣustambavadetasya śālistambaśca jāyate ।
divyapānānnasaṃpattiḥ phalaṃ tatkasya karmaṇaḥ ।।

iti pṛṣṭaḥ praṇayinā bhikṣuṇā bhagavān jinaḥ ।
uvāca śrūyatāṃ rājñaḥ kāraṇaṃ bhogasaṃpadām ।।

kosale asmin janapade khaṇḍākhyaguḍakarṣakaḥ ।
dadau pratyekabuddhāya pūrvamikṣurasaudanam ।।

bhuktenekṣurasānnena tena vātagadārditaḥ ।
pratyekabuddhastatpuṇyaiḥ prasannaḥ susthatāṃ yayau ।।

rājā prasenajit so ayaṃ puṇyavān guḍakarṣakah ।
tena puṇyaprabhāveṇa bhogabhāgī virājate ।।

upakāraḥ kṛtajñānāṃ nikāraḥ krūracetasām ।
sukṛtāṃśaśca śādhūnāmaplo apyāyātyanalpatām ।।

sarvajñeneti kathite pūrvapuṇye mahīpateḥ ।
babhūva sukṛtotkarṣe bhikṣurāścaryaniścalah ।।

atha bhaktyā bhagavataḥ kṛtvā rājādhivāsanām ।
upaninye svayaṃ tāṃ tāṃ surārhāṃ bhogasaṃpadam ।।

paropacārai rucirairarcite kāñcanāsane ।
sukhopaviṣṭaṃ provāca naranāthastathāgatam ।।

bhagavan me bhavadbhaktivibhaktasukṛtaśriyaḥ ।
cayah kuśalamūlānāmanirmuktyai bhaviṣyati ।।

vinayātpārthiveneti pūrṇapuṇyābhimāninā ।
pṛṣṭaḥ smitasitālokaṃ jagāda sugataḥ sṛjan ।।

rājan saṃsāramārgo ayamanādinidhanodbhavaḥ ।
helālaṅghyaḥ kathaṃ puṃsāmaprāpya kleśasaṃkṣayam ।।

ciraparicitaiścakrāvartairasaktagatāgatiḥ
prakṛtigahanaḥ saṃsāro ayaṃ sukhena na laṅghyate ।
asati hi vinā yogābhyāsaṃ kṣaye kila karmaṇāṃ
sphuṭaphalatatirdharmo apyasminnibandhanatām gataḥ ।।

sarvato vinivṛttasya dānābhyāsena bhūyasā ।
mamāpi dharmasaṃsāro babhūva bhūrijanmakṛt ।।

dhaniko nāma dhanavān vārāṇasyāmabhūtpurā ।
tāpāpahaḥ phalasphīṭaśchāyāvṛkṣa ivārthinām ।।

durbhikṣakṣapite loke viṣamakleśavihvale ।
bhojyaṃ pratyekabuddhānāṃ so arthitaḥ pañcabhiḥ śataiḥ ।।

sa teṣāṃ parabhogārhaṃ durbhikṣāvadhi bhojanam ।
akalpayadanalpaśrīḥ koṣṭhāgārī gatasmayaḥ ।।

śatapañcakasaṃghātairbhoktuṃ tasya gṛhaṃ tataḥ ।
kramātpratyekabuddhānām sahasradvayamāyayau ।।

tasya tatpuṇyavāsena jāto labdhaphalaśriyā ।
durbhikṣadānajanito ratnakośastadākṣayaḥ ।।

sukhaṃ sanātanaṃ puṇyabhogyatvaṃ praṇidhānataḥ ।
śāstustataḥ pareṇāyaṃ samyaksaṃbodhimāpitaḥ ।।

puṇyena pāpena ca veṣṭiteyaṃ saṃsāriṇāṃ karmaphalapravṛttiḥ ।
sitāsitā bandhanarajjureṣā tatsaṃkṣaye mokṣapathaṃ vadanti ।।

iti kṣitīśaḥ kathitaṃ jinena mohavyapāyena niśamya mokṣam ।
kleśakṣayārhaṃ śamameva matvā puṇyābhimānaṃ śithilīvakāra ।।

iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ śālistambāvadānaṃ nāma ṣaṭcatvāriṃśaḥ pallavaḥ ।।

sarvārthasiddhāvadānam ।

svārthapravṛttau vigataspṛhāṇāṃ paropakāre satatodyatānām ।
kleśeṣvabhītā vyasanairanītā vighnairapīḍākarameti siddhiḥ ।।

śrāvastyāṃ bhagavān pūrvaṃ jino jetavanasthitaḥ ।
dharmākhyānaprasaṅgena bhikṣusaṃghamabhāṣata ।।

āsīdakhilabhūpālamaulilālitaśāsanah ।
siddhārtho nāma sukṛtī sārvabhaumo mahīpatiḥ ।।

sāgarākhyasya nāgasya sūnurjaladhivāsinah ।
sarvārthasiddhaḥ putratvaṃ prayayau tasya bhūpateḥ ।।

sa bhādrakalpiko bodhisattvaḥ sattvojjvalaprabhaḥ ।
jātamātraḥ kṣititalaṃ cakre pūrṇaṃ svaṛddhibhiḥ ।।

tasya pravardhamānasya dharmasyeva samudyayau ।
samastabhuvanavyāpi vibudhābhyarcitaṃ yaśaḥ ।।

sa kadācidvarodyāne syandanena yuvā vrajan ।
dadarśa vṛddhapuruṣaṃ devatānirmitaṃ puraḥ ।।

taṃ vilokya jarājīrṇaṃ jātavairāgyavāsanah ।
saṃsāramiva niḥsāraṃ sa śarīvamamanyata ।।

udyānayātrāvirataḥ śanaiḥ pratinivṛtya saḥ ।
dāridyravidrutacchāyānadrākṣīt kṛpaṇān pathi ।।

dṛṣṭvā tānasukhakleṣṭān karuṇākṛṣṭamānasaḥ ।
acintayadaho duḥkhaṃ sahante bhuvi durgatāḥ ।।

adānaprabhavaṃ duḥkhaṃ vadantīti visaṃgatāḥ ।
pṛthivyāṃ ratnapūrṇāyāṃ parapiṇḍopajīvinaḥ ।।

idamevāvisaṃvādi cihnaṃ kaluṣakarmaṇām ।
dīnāṃ yadete yācante puruṣaṃ puruṣāḥ param ।।

aho duṣkṛtameteṣāmavadhūtāḥ pade pade ।
yadete mārgaṇodvignā bhikṣitvāpi bubhukṣitāḥ ।।

iti saṃcintya suciraṃ viścakleśakṣayodyataḥ ।
yadaridraṃ jagatkartuṃ ratnārthī jaladhiṃ yayau ।।

kathacidiva saṃsaktaḥ sa pitrā dṛḍhaniścayaḥ ।
smāruhya pravahaṇaṃ ratnadvīpamavāptavān ।।

tatra pravahaṇārūḍhān vaṇijaḥ sahayāyinaḥ ।
so abravītkriyatām kāmaṃ yuṣmābhirmaṇisaṃgrahaṃ ।।

etaiḥ sāmānyaratnaistu mama nāsti prayojanam ।
kośe mahānti bhāsvanti santi ratnottamāni naḥ ।।

kiṃ tu cintāmaṇiprāptyai vipulo ayaṃ mamodyamaḥ ।
tena vidrutadāridyrāṃ kartumicchāmi modenīm ।।

śrutaṃ mayā nāgarājaḥ sāgarākhyo mahodadhau ।
vasatyasti gṛhe tasya cintitārthaprado maṇiḥ ।।

vilaṅghya viṣamaṃ mārgaṃ tamādātuṃ vrajāmyaham ।
nāsti dhairyasahāyānām durgamaṃ vyavasāyinām ।।

na ca madvirahe kiṃcid vyasanaṃ vo bhaviṣyati ।
satyameva parārtho ayaṃ yadi me sukṛtodyamaḥ ।।

ityuktvā tān samāmantrya pratasthe sthiraniścayaḥ ।
mahatīṃ dhṛtimālambya sattvavān pārthivātmajaḥ ।।

gulphamātreṇa saptāhaṃ gatvā gaṅgamavartmanā ।
jānudaghnena saptāhaṃ saptāhaṃ pauruṣeṇa ca ।।

catvāri saptarātrāṇi tataḥ puṣkariṇījalaiḥ ।
gatvā dṛṣṭiviṣān ghorān dadarśa phaṇinaḥ puraḥ ।।

maitrīyuktena manasā kṛtvā tānatha nirviṣān ।
krūrakopairvṛtaṃ yakṣairyakṣadvīpamavāpa saḥ ।।

tatra maitreṇa manasā vītakrodhān vidhāya tān ।
śuśrāva tairabhihitaṃ vipulotsāhavismitaiḥ ।।

kumāra sphīṭasattvena tathā vīryeṇacāmunā ।
nāgarājasya bhavanaṃ samāhitamavāpya tam ।।

kālena samyaksaṃbuddhaḥ sarvajñastvaṃ bhaviṣyasi ।
śrāvakāśca bhaviṣyāmo vayaṃ tvadanuyāyinaḥ ।।

prasannairiti tairuktamabhinandya nṛpātmajaḥ ।
rakṣevarāvṛtaṃ prāpa rākṣasadvīpamutkaṭam ।।

tathaiva vigatakrūravikāraistaiḥ sa pūjitaḥ ।
bhūjotkṣepeṇa nikṣiptaḥ kṣaṇānnāgendrasadmāni ।।

sa tatra dīptavibhave divyotsāsasukhocitaḥ ।
aśṛṇoddīrghaduḥkhārtisūcakaṃ rodanadhvanim ।।

sa tamākarṇya sodvegaḥ prakṛtyaiva dayārdradhīḥ ।
kimetaditi papraccha dṛṣṭvāgre nāgakanyakām ।।

sā taṃ babhāṣe saṃsaktaśokoṣmapiśunairmuhuḥ ।
mlānayantīṃ svaniśvāsaurbimbādharadalatviṣam ।।

guṇāvān nāgarājasya putraḥ kamalalocanaḥ ।
jyoṣṭhaḥ sarvārthasiddhākhyaḥ priyaḥ pañcatvamāgataḥ ।।

tataḥ pratigatānande vinivṛttasukhotsave ।
dhanena rodanenāsminna bhavedbhavane sthitiḥ ।।

iti tasyā vacaḥ śrutvā so antaḥ paricitāṃ vahan ।
svadeśadarśanaprāpto nāgarājāntikaṃ yayau ।।

nāgarājastamāyāntaṃ parijñāya priyāsakhaḥ ।
ehyehi putreti vadan babhūvānandavihvalaḥ ।।

martyajanmakathām tena svaṃ cāgamanakāraṇam ।
śrutvā niveditaṃ nāgaḥ pariṣvajya jagāda tam ।।

cintāmaṇirayaṃ putra mama maulivibhūṣaṇam ।
gṛhyatām tava saṃkalpaṃ na vandhyaṃ kartumutsahe ।।

deyaḥ kṛtajagatkṛtyo mamaivāyaṃ punastvayā ।
ityuktvāsmai dadau divyacūḍaṃ ratna vimucya saḥ ।।
hṛṣṭaḥ praṇamya nāgendraṃ yayau pravahaṇāntikam ।।
samudradevatā tatra taṃ dṛṣṭvā śrutatatkathā ।
uvāca kīdṛśaḥ sādho prāptaścintāmaṇīstvayā ।।

।।

।।

samudre patitaṃ dṛṣṭvā ratnaṃ kṛcchratarārjitam ।
sa jagāda dṛḍhodyogavaiphalyodveganiścalaḥ ।।

aho guṇocitākārā praṇayānmṛduvādinī ।
vidveṣakaluṣaṃ karma kṛtvā tvaṃ na vilajjase ।।

parotkarṣeṣu saṃgharṣaśokakleśamupaiti yaḥ ।
śītalā api tasyaitā jvālāvalayitā diśaḥ ।।

paritsāhaḥ priyo yasya tasya sattvamahodadheḥ ।
karpūradhavalaṃ dhatte trilokītilakaṃ yaśaḥ ।।

devi prayaccha me ratnamasmādvirama pātakāt ।
apavādalatāṃ karma na sādhoradhirohhati ।।

lobhātpramādāddveṣādvā ratnaṃ cenna prayacchasi ।
śoṣayāmyeṣa jaladhiṃ tadimaṃ te samāśrayam ।।

ityuktvā pyasakṛttena sā ratne na dadau yadā ।
sa tadā svaprabhāveṇa śoṣāyābdheḥ samudyayau ।।

dhyātamātraṃ sahasrākṣavacasā viśvakarmaṇā ।
nirmitaṃ sahasā tasya patramāvirabhutkare ।।

sa tenāgastyaculukākāreṇāmbhaḥ payonidheḥ ।
antarīkṣe samutkṣipya cikṣepa kṣamaṇodyataḥ ।।

kṛte bhūbhāgaśeṣe abdhau tenātyadbhutakāriṇā ।
suranirbhartsitā bhītā devatāsmai maṇīṃ dadau ।।

nirvyājaṃ sāhasaṃ dīptiṃ ratnānāmiva tattvataḥ ।
prabhāvaṃ vetti mahatāṃ mantrāṇāṃ tapasāṃ ca kaḥ ।।

sphārastāvadapāravārivirasavyāpārahelābalāt
kallolāvaliyantritāmbaratayā ratnākaraḥ śrūyate ।
gambhīraḥ punaraprameyamahimā ko api prabhāvaḥ satāṃ
yasmin vismayadhāmni cintanavidhāvante plavante dhiyaḥ ।।

tataścintāmaṇiṃ buddhvā nijasārthena saṃgataḥ ।
rājasūnuḥ svanagaraṃ prāpa pūrṇamanorathaḥ ।।

kṛtakṛtyaḥ prahṛṣṭenaḥ sa pitrā tatra pūjitaḥ ।
dhvajāgre ratnamādhāya jagāda janasaṃsadi ।।

parārtha eva yatno ayaṃ nātmārtho yadi me kkacit ।
tena satyena loko aya sarvaṃ yātvadaridratām ।।

ityukte sattvanidhinā tena dīnadayālunā ।
ratnavṛṣṭiraparyantā nipapāta mahītale ।।

tena ratnasamūhena dikṣu sarvāsu bhāsvatā ।
yayau janasya dāridyramayaṃ niḥśeṣatāṃ tamaḥ ।।

āśāpāśavatāṃ balāptraviśatāṃ bāhyāṅgaṇaṃ śrīmatāṃ
dvāḥsthāghātavatām muhurvicalatāṃ dvārodare sīdatām ।
dīrghairniḥśvasitaiḥ śucā nipatitāṃ dehakṣayaṃ kāṅkṣatāṃ
dīnānāṃ maṇirāśiraśmiśabalaḥ śrīsaṃgamaḥ ko apyabhūt ।।

tacchāsanāduraganāyakameva yāte cintāmaṇau vigatadainyajane ca loke ।
sarvatra dānarasikasya janasya cetaḥ sarvārthisārthaviratākulitaṃ babhūva ।।

sarvārthasiddhaḥ kṣitipālasūnuḥ yo abhūtsa evāhamihānyadehaḥ ।
śrutvetivṛttaṃ kathitaṃ jinena te bhikṣavastanmayatāmavāpuḥ ।।

iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ sarvārthasiddhāvadānaṃ satpacatvāriṃśaḥ pallavaḥ ।।

hastakāvadānam ।

mattebhakumbhoccakucābhirāmāḥ karpūrahārāṃśuvilāsahāsāḥ ।
prītipradāḥ puṇyavatāṃ bhavanti prauḍhā yuvatyaśca vibhūtayaśca ।।

tathāgate bhagavati śrāvastyāṃ vanacāriṇi ।
abhavatsuprabuddhākhyaḥ śrīmān gṛhapatiḥ purā ।।

babhūva hastako nāma tasyātidayitaḥ sutaḥ ।
pūrvārjitānāṃ puṇyānāṃ sākāra iva saṃcayaḥ ।।

tasya janmadine jātaścāmīkaramayo mahān ।
ekībhūta ivāścaryavrajaḥ pravarakuñcaraḥ ।।

sa gajendraḥ kumāraśca tatpituśca manorathaḥ ।
lokakautukakośāśca pūrṇatāṃ tyulyamāyayuḥ ।।

sa śaśīva śiśuḥ kāle kalānilayatāṃ gataḥ ।
ruruce rucimān sarvalokalocanabāndhavaḥ ।।

sa śanaiḥ pūritābhogabhujastambhavibhūṣaṇam ।
lebhe manobhavārambhabhavanaṃ navayauvanam ।।

kadācidatha bhūbhartuḥ sa prasenajitaḥ sutām ।
tanucīvaracihnena sahajena virājitām ।।

kanyāṃ cīvarakanyākhyāṃ lāvaṇyalalitānanām ।
udyānadarśanāyātāṃ dadarśāyatalocanām ।।

akliṣṭarūpāmālokya tāmaparyuṣitadyutim ।
vismayasmarayostulyamāyayau sahasā vaśam ।।

so acintayadaho kāntamidamatyadbhutaṃ vapuḥ ।
yasmin bhāti mukhavyājādadoṣaviśadaḥ śaśī ।।

lāvaṇyamapratimameva bibhati tanvī bandhūkabandhuradharo madhurasvabhāvaḥ ।
drohodyataḥ sarasavidrumapallavānāṃ bimbaprabhāprasabhabhramavandhyakāraḥ ।।

vakrkraṃ na kṣamate madaṃ śaśamṛtaḥ kleśnāti kāntiḥ sudhām
utphullotpalakānanasya kurute dṛṣṭiḥ prabhābhrtsanam ।
manye manmathasaṃgamocitatanoḥ sāptnyabhītipradā
līlāyāsyāḥ sahasā vilāsalaharīśoṣaṃ vidhatte rateḥ ।।

udvṛtte kaṭhine parodharayuge naśyadviveke ciraṃ
yasyā doṣamaye apyaho guṇavatā hāreṇa baddhā sthitiḥ ।
yaccāsminnavalambate ambujadhiyā rolambarekhā mukhe
lolākṣyāḥ kimapi praśāntanayane līnaṃ munīnāṃ manaḥ ।।

iti cintayatastasya vapuḥ puṣpaśaropamam ।
vilokya bhūpatisutā babhūvāścaryaniścalā ।।

hṛte lajjāṃśuke tasyāḥ smareṇa smitakāriṇā ।
pratyagrapulakākīrṇaṃ vapuḥ spaṣṭamadṛśyata ।।

ruddhā navābhilāṣeṇa vailakṣyeṇa nivartitā ।
manastatraiva nikṣipya sā śūnyeva śanairyayau ।।

rājadhānīṃ samāsādya lajjāvismayamanmathaiḥ ।
mīliteva nilīneva proṣiteva babhūva sā ।।

kumāro api svabhavane samudbhūtamanobhāvḥ ।
tāmevendumukhīmagre saṃkalpairalikhanmuhuḥ ।।

sa tāṃ mānasasarvasvaṃ smaravidyāmiva smaran ।
pradadhyau kurlabhām matvā tanayām cakravartinaḥ ।।

janmāntare tanuryasya tapaḥparicitā ciram ।
dhanyaḥ sa tāmavāpnoti latāṃ sukṛtaśākhinaḥ ।।

ramyapradānapuṇyena taddarśanamavāpyate ।
na jāne tāni puṇyāni yeṣāṃ tatsaṃgamaḥ phalam ।।

tadvakrkraśītakiraṇasmaraṇotsavena
tasyāśca durlabhatayā virahoṣmaṇā me ।
no vedmi kiṃ dhṛtiriyaṃ kimayaṃ vimohaḥ
kiṃ jīvitaṃ kimasubhiḥ sahaḥ viprayogaḥ ।।

tadvakrkrabjajitaḥ prasahra bhajate kṣaiṇyaṃ kṣapāvallabhaḥ
tadbhūvibhramalajjitaṃ ca vinatiṃ dhate dhanurmānmatham ।
tasyāh pallavapeśaladyutimuṣā śoṣādhareṇārditaṃ
nūnaṃ prāpya parājayaṃ vanamahīṃ bimba samālambate ।।

iti pūrṇenduvadanāvadanadhyānaniścalah ।
niśāṃ nināya saṃtyaktaḥ serṣyayeva sanidrayā ।।

kanyādarśanavṛttāntaṃ tatastena niveditam ।
śrutvā pitāsya saṃkrantacintāparicito abhavat ।।

sa tamūce vayaṃ putra rājño asya puravāsinah ।
sa kathaṃ te duhitaraṃ cakravartī pradāsyati ।।

aśakyaṃ naiva kurvanti samīhante na durlabham ।
asaṃbhāvyaṃ na bhāṣante mānakāmā manīṣiṇaḥ ।।

cūtacampakavallīṣu svādhīnāsu nirādaraḥ ।
cintayan pārijātasya latām śuṣyati ṣaṭpadaḥ ।।

tava tasyāśca saṃbandhaḥ prājganmavihito yadi ।
tadavaśyaṃ bhavatyeva niṣprayatnaphalodayah ।।

āśāpāśairanākṛṣṭaṃ vicārairakadarthitam ।
prayatnabhārairaśrāntaṃ vidhatte bhavitavyatā ।।

ityākarṇya piturvākyaṃ tattatheti vicintayan ।
na cetaḥ kanyakānītaṃ samānetuṃ śaśāka saḥ ।।

sa gatvā dantayugalaṃ yayāce hemakuñcaram ।
navasaṃdarśane rājñaḥ prītiyogyamupāyanam ।।

puṇyabandhena kariṇā dattaṃ dantayugaṃ tataḥ ।
sa hemamayamādāya draṣṭuṃ bhūmipatiṃ yayau ।।

sa ratnaruciraṃ prāpya bhavanaṃ pṛthivīpateḥ ।
praviśyaḥ praṇataḥ prītyai hemadantadvayaṃ dadau ।।

bhūbhujā viśrutaguṇaḥ prasādenābhinanditaḥ ।
varaṃ gṛhāṇetyuktaśca sa na jagrāha kiṃcana ।।

tasyādīnadyuteścakre mānamabhyadhikaṃ nṛpaḥ ।
aucityacārucaritaḥ priyaḥ kasya na niḥspṛhaḥ ।।

sa sadā darśane rājñaḥ kāñcanāṅgāni dantinaḥ ।
punarjātanavāṅgena dattāṇi prīyate dadau ।।

tamuvāca mahīpālaḥ sevāpraṇayayantritaḥ ।
dūtīṃ manaḥprasādaya vadanadyutimudvahan ।।

prabhūtahemasaṃbhārāṃ gurvīṃ sovāmimāmaham ।
na sahe prauravārgo hi bhavaṇīyo mahībhṛtām ।।

saṃvibhajya janānītaiḥ kā prītirmama kāñcanaiḥ ।
tavānarghaguṇā mūrtiriyameva mama priyā ।।

lobhaḥ puruṣaratneṣu bhūṣaṇārheṣu śobhate ।
rājñāṃ kośeṣu sīdanti hemaratnāśmasaṃcayāḥ ।।

samīhitatamaṃ tubhyaṃ kiṃ prayacchāmi kathyatām ।
niḥśeṣakośadānena na nāmānuśayo astu me ।।

rājñṃ dṛkpātapātreṇa prāpyante yadi na śriyaḥ ।
tadanarthaṃ gatārthinyā ko athaḥ pārthivasevayā ।।

ityuktaḥ kṣitipālena kumāraḥ kalitāñjaliḥ ।
tamabhāṣata bhūpāla dātumarhati ko aparaḥ ।।

anarthitena ratnāni vibudhebhyaḥ prayacchatā ।
tadunnidraṃ samudrasya mudritaṃ bhavatā yaśaḥ ।।

mahatāpi prayatnena pūryate na mahāśayaḥ ।
alpakānāṃ tadairśvaryaṃ dāridyaṃ tanmahīyasām ।।

kiṃ tu tvadbhujaguptānāṃ dharmamārgeṇa jīvatāṃ ।
janānāṃ nāsti dāridyaṃ draviṇaṃ yena mṛgyate ।।

dhanārthino na tu vayaṃ na ca sevādhikāriṇaḥ ।
dhanaṃ dhanaṃ dhanadhiyāṃ māna eva manasvinām ।।

mīladguṇena parameśvarasevanena nurmūlatām sumanasāṃ sahasā gatānām ।
dainyātpunaḥ kṛpaṇapaṇyapathe cyutānāṃ na sparśamātramapi sādhujanaḥ karoti ।।

arthitvānmaraṇam varaṃ tanubhṛtām dainyāvasannātmanāṃ
arthī sarvajanāvamānavasatiḥ satkārayogyaḥ śavaḥ ।
kumbhastāvadadhah prayāti guṇavān kūpāvatāre paraṃ
yāvanmohatamaḥpraveśavivaśaḥ prāpto arthitā lambate ।।

sāmānyā dhanasaṃpadaḥ krayakṛṣiprāpyā sadā dhīmatāṃ
saṃtoṣo yadi nāsti tatkimaparā bhūmirnidhānāvṛtā ।
santyevātiśayaprasādaniratāstā hemaratnakriyāḥ
kasyeṣṭaḥ priyasaṃgamāya vapuṣāṃ sevāmayo vikrayaḥ ।।

ityapāradhiyastasya vacaḥ śrutvā mahīpatiḥ ।
gṝhyatāmaparaṃ kiṃcidityabhāṣata sādaraḥ ।।

aucityacaturālāpaḥ karkaśo api nṛpāṃ priyaḥ ।
kṛpaṇaścāṭukāro api karṇaśūlāya kevalaḥ ।।

aurdāryaparituṣṭena sa rājñabhyarthitaḥ param ।
tamūce yadu tuṣṭo asi sutā mahyaṃ pradīyatām ।।

ityukte tena nṛpatiḥ saṃdehāndolitāśayaḥ ।
prātarvaktāhamityuktvā kṣaṇaṃ kṣmātalamaikṣata ।।

sa kumāraṃ visṛjyātha pradhānāmātyamabravīt ।
prasādarabhasenaiva kṛtaṃ vākcāpalaṃ mayā ।।

cakravartikulotpannā kanyā puṇyapaṇocitā ।
kathaṃ sāmānyapaurāya guṇamātreṇa dīyate ।।

dadāmīti pratiśrutya paścādanuśayākulaḥ ।
kathaṃ sarādhano bhūtvā bhaviṣyāmyarthiniṣphalaḥ ।।

kathaṃ prāptasya tasyāhaṃ prātardraṣṭ mukhaṃ puraḥ ।
priyo apyapriyatāṃ yātaḥ sa me durlabhayecchayā ।।

nūnaṃ guṇopapanno api prakṛtyaiva śarīriṇām ।
vakti yāvanna dehīti tāvadgavati vallabhah ।।

iti bhūmipateḥ śrutvāḥ vaco dolāvalambinaḥ ।
tamuvāca mahāmātyaḥ saṃcintyāvasarocitam ।।

anālocitaparyantāḥ pratyagrasarasādarāḥ ।
svabhāvarabhasā eva bhavanti prabhubuddhayaḥ ।।

aśakyārthanayā tena lubdheneva guṇodayaḥ ।
rājasevāpravṛttena hemahastī vināśitaḥ ।।

vācyo asau bhavatā svairaṃ kanyārthī punarāgataḥ ।
hemahastinamāruhya prāptaḥ prāpsyasi me sutām ।।

tenotkṛttaḥ svahastena kutastasya sa kuñjaraḥ ।
na cāsau tadvirahitaḥ punarāyāti lajjayā ।।

ityamātyasya vacasā nṛpatiryuktimāśritaḥ ।
prāptaṃ kumāramanyedyustadevābhimukho avadat ।।

kumāro api gṝhaṃ gatvā vivāhocitamaṅgalaiḥ ।
haumadviradamāruhya svajanena sajāyayau ।।

svarṇavāraṇasaṃrūḍhaṃ tamāyāntaṃ mahīpatiḥ ।
vilokyāścaryavibhavaṃ mene puṇyavatāṃ varam ।।

kautukādatha bhūpālastaṃ gajaṃ hemavigraham ।
āruroha mahotsāhaḥ sumerumiva vajrabhṛt ।।

ārūḍhe pṛthivīpāle na cacāla sa kuñjaraḥ ।
prasarsarpa kumāreṇa punaścālaṃkṛtāsanaḥ ।।

taṃ jñātvā nṛpatirdevaṃ tatprabhāveṇa vismitaḥ ।
dhanyo asmīti vadan kanyāṃ dadau tasmai smaraśriyam ।।

abhyarcya kanyāratnena nṛpatiḥ puruṣottamam ।
harṣotsavasamuddhūtaḥ sudhāsindhurivābabhau ।।

tataḥ kumāre dayitāmādāya svagṛhaṃ gate ।
saphalo abhūdanaṅgasya kārmukākarṣaṇaśramaḥ ।।

nave vayasi bhogārhe navakāntāsamāgame ।
tasyābhūdvibhavodāraḥ sadā navanavotsavaḥ ।।

tataḥ kadācidbhūpālaḥ kṛtakṛtyaḥ prasenajit ।
puṇyaprabhāvaṃ jāmātuḥ kalayan samacintayat ।।

aho divyaḥ prabhāvo asau kumārasya pradṛśyate ।
na hi sāmānyapuṇyānāṃ pāko bhavati tadvidhaḥ ।।

kulaṃ lakṣmīharmyaṃ hṛtaśaśimadā rūpalaharī
vayaḥ saṃbhogārhaṃ guṇaparicayo bhūṣaṇacayaḥ ।
yaśaḥ puṇyodyānaprasṛtakusumollāsaruciraṃ
na vidmaḥ kasyāyaṃ kuśalapariṇāmasya vibhavaḥ ।।

iti saṃcintya suciraṃ sa saṃjātakutūhalaḥ ।
sarvajñadarśanāvaddhamāruroha manoratham ।।

sa jātātaramāhūya sutāṃ ca sacivaiḥ saha ।
bhagavantaṃ yayau draṣṭuṃ manasā prathamaṃ gataḥ ।।

yāte dṛṣṭipathaṃ jetavane saṃtyajya vāhanam ।
upasṛtyaḥ nṛpaḥ padbhyāṃ bhagavantaṃ vyalokayat ।।

sa taṃ praṇamya tatpādapadmabhūtiśikhāmaṇiḥ ।
sutāṃ jāmātaraṃ cāsmai namro nāmnā nyavedayat ।।

upaviṣṭeṣu sarveṣu praṇāmānatamauliṣu ।
papraccha rājā sarvajñaṃ bhagavantaṃ kṛtāñjaliḥ ।।

ayaṃ guṇagaopetaḥ kumāraḥ śrīmatāṃ varaḥ ।
haimeva dantināyāto bhagavan kena karmaṇā ।।

iyaṃ cīvarakanyā ca matsutāsya navā vadhūḥ ।
kena puṇyaprabhāveṇa jīvitādadhivallabhā ।।

iti pṛṣṭaḥ kṣitīśena sarvavidbhagavān jinaḥ ।
tamūce bhūpate puṃsāṃ puṇyodbhūtā vibhūtayaḥ ।।

yadudāro yaducito yad bhrājiṃṣṇu yadadbhutam ।
spṛhaṇīyaṃ ca yalloke tattatpuṇyasamudbahvam ।।

vipaśvī bhagavān pūrvaṃ sugataḥ saha bhikṣubhiḥ ।
cacāra lokakṛpayā rājño bandhumataḥ pure ।।

tasminnavasare tatra kumāryā saha dārakaḥ ।
vikrīḍāvartmani puraḥ kṛtvā dārumayaṃ gajam ।।

tau vilokya samāyāntaṃ dhmātajambūnadadyutim ।
phullapadmadalākārakaruṇāsnigdhalocanam ।।

bhagavantaṃ samudbhūtatadbhaktisarasonmukhau ।
krīḍāgajaṃ nivedyāsmai praṇatau tasthatuḥ puraḥ ।।

bhagavānapi sarvajñastayorjñātvā manoratham ।
dayayā caraṇasparśaṃ vidadhe dārudantinaḥ ।।

samyak cittaprasādena dṛṣṭau bhagavatātha tau ।
praṇīdhānaṃ vivāhāya cakraturdārakau mithaḥ ।।

kulaprabhāvavibhavairbhūyājjanma mamocitam ।
vāhanaṃ hemadantī ca kumārasyetyabhūnmatiḥ ।।

dṛṣṭvā bhagavataḥ kanyā saṃsaktre cārucīvare ।
janmacīvarayuktāṃ syāmahametacintayat ।।

sa eṣa praṇidhānena jātasteneha hastakaḥ ।
iyaṃ cīvarakanyā ca tanucīvaralakṣaṇa ।।

iti kṣrutvā kṣitipatistadvṛttaṃ sugato aditam ।
mukuṭaspṛṣṭatatpādapadmaḥ svabhavanaṃ yayau ।।

yāte savismayaṃ rājñi kumāraḥ saha jāyayā ।
kathyamānaṃ bhagavatā dharmaṃ śuśrāva śuddhadhīḥ ।।

tatastau jātavairāgyau kṣīṇasaṃsāravāsanau ।
pravrajyayā jitakleśau śuddhāṃ bodhimavāpatuḥ ।।

vitatasukṛtapuṇyābhyāsayogena puṃsāṃ bhavati kuśalabhājāṃ dharmakāmārthasaṃpat ।
abhimatamatha bhuktvā tatphalaṃ sadārāste vighanagaganakāntiṃ śāntimante bhajante ।।

iti kṣemandraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ hastakāvadānamaṣṭacatvāriṃśaḥ pallavaḥ ।।
